# Sutta Nipāta

## Vagga 1 ^vagga1-0

### Uragasutta (Sutta Nipāta 1.1) ^snp1-1-0

Yo uppatitaṁ vineti kodhaṁ, ^snp1-1-1-1

Visaṭaṁ sappavisaṁva osadhehi; ^snp1-1-1-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-1-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇaṁ. ^snp1-1-1-4

Yo rāgamudacchidā asesaṁ, ^snp1-1-2-1

Bhisapupphaṁva saroruhaṁ vigayha; ^snp1-1-2-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-2-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇaṁ. ^snp1-1-2-4

Yo taṇhamudacchidā asesaṁ, ^snp1-1-3-1

Saritaṁ sīghasaraṁ visosayitvā; ^snp1-1-3-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-3-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇaṁ. ^snp1-1-3-4

Yo mānamudabbadhī asesaṁ, ^snp1-1-4-1

Naḷasetuṁva sudubbalaṁ mahogho; ^snp1-1-4-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-4-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇaṁ. ^snp1-1-4-4

Yo nājjhagamā bhavesu sāraṁ, ^snp1-1-5-1

Vicinaṁ pupphamivā udumbaresu; ^snp1-1-5-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-5-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇaṁ. ^snp1-1-5-4

Yassantarato na santi kopā, ^snp1-1-6-1

Itibhavābhavatañca vītivatto; ^snp1-1-6-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-6-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇaṁ. ^snp1-1-6-4

Yassa vitakkā vidhūpitā, ^snp1-1-7-1

Ajjhattaṁ suvikappitā asesā; ^snp1-1-7-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-7-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇaṁ. ^snp1-1-7-4

Yo nāccasārī na paccasārī, ^snp1-1-8-1

Sabbaṁ accagamā imaṁ papañcaṁ; ^snp1-1-8-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-8-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇaṁ. ^snp1-1-8-4

Yo nāccasārī na paccasārī, ^snp1-1-9-1

Sabbaṁ vitathamidanti ñatva loke; ^snp1-1-9-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-9-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇaṁ. ^snp1-1-9-4

Yo nāccasārī na paccasārī, ^snp1-1-10-1

Sabbaṁ vitathamidanti vītalobho; ^snp1-1-10-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-10-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇaṁ. ^snp1-1-10-4

Yo nāccasārī na paccasārī, ^snp1-1-11-1

Sabbaṁ vitathamidanti vītarāgo; ^snp1-1-11-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-11-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇaṁ. ^snp1-1-11-4

Yo nāccasārī na paccasārī, ^snp1-1-12-1

Sabbaṁ vitathamidanti vītadoso; ^snp1-1-12-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-12-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇaṁ. ^snp1-1-12-4

Yo nāccasārī na paccasārī, ^snp1-1-13-1

Sabbaṁ vitathamidanti vītamoho; ^snp1-1-13-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-13-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇaṁ. ^snp1-1-13-4

Yassānusayā na santi keci, ^snp1-1-14-1

Mūlā ca akusalā samūhatāse; ^snp1-1-14-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-14-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇaṁ. ^snp1-1-14-4

Yassa darathajā na santi keci, ^snp1-1-15-1

Oraṁ āgamanāya paccayāse; ^snp1-1-15-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-15-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇaṁ. ^snp1-1-15-4

Yassa vanathajā na santi keci, ^snp1-1-16-1

Vinibandhāya bhavāya hetukappā; ^snp1-1-16-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-16-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇaṁ. ^snp1-1-16-4

Yo nīvaraṇe pahāya pañca, ^snp1-1-17-1

Anigho tiṇṇakathaṅkatho visallo; ^snp1-1-17-2

So bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṁ, ^snp1-1-17-3

Urago jiṇṇamivattacaṁ purāṇanti. ^snp1-1-17-4

Uragasuttaṁ paṭhamaṁ. ^snp1-1-17-5

### Dhaniyasutta (Sutta Nipāta 1.2) ^snp1-2-0

“Pakkodano duddhakhīrohamasmi, ^snp1-2-1-1

(iti dhaniyo gopo) ^snp1-2-1-2

Anutīre mahiyā samānavāso; ^snp1-2-1-3

Channā kuṭi āhito gini, ^snp1-2-1-4

Atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva”. ^snp1-2-1-5

“Akkodhano vigatakhilohamasmi, ^snp1-2-2-1

(iti bhagavā) ^snp1-2-2-2

Anutīre mahiyekarattivāso; ^snp1-2-2-3

Vivaṭā kuṭi nibbuto gini, ^snp1-2-2-4

Atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva”. ^snp1-2-2-5

“Andhakamakasā na vijjare, ^snp1-2-3-1

(iti dhaniyo gopo) ^snp1-2-3-2

Kacche rūḷhatiṇe caranti gāvo; ^snp1-2-3-3

Vuṭṭhimpi saheyyumāgataṁ, ^snp1-2-3-4

Atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva”. ^snp1-2-3-5

“Baddhāsi bhisī susaṅkhatā, ^snp1-2-4-1

(iti bhagavā) ^snp1-2-4-2

Tiṇṇo pāragato vineyya oghaṁ; ^snp1-2-4-3

Attho bhisiyā na vijjati, ^snp1-2-4-4

Atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva”. ^snp1-2-4-5

“Gopī mama assavā alolā, ^snp1-2-5-1

(iti dhaniyo gopo) ^snp1-2-5-2

Dīgharattaṁ saṁvāsiyā manāpā; ^snp1-2-5-3

Tassā na suṇāmi kiñci pāpaṁ, ^snp1-2-5-4

Atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva”. ^snp1-2-5-5

“Cittaṁ mama assavaṁ vimuttaṁ, ^snp1-2-6-1

(iti bhagavā) ^snp1-2-6-2

Dīgharattaṁ paribhāvitaṁ sudantaṁ; ^snp1-2-6-3

Pāpaṁ pana me na vijjati, ^snp1-2-6-4

Atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva”. ^snp1-2-6-5

“Attavetanabhatohamasmi, ^snp1-2-7-1

(iti dhaniyo gopo) ^snp1-2-7-2

Puttā ca me samāniyā arogā; ^snp1-2-7-3

Tesaṁ na suṇāmi kiñci pāpaṁ, ^snp1-2-7-4

Atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva”. ^snp1-2-7-5

“Nāhaṁ bhatakosmi kassaci, ^snp1-2-8-1

(iti bhagavā) ^snp1-2-8-2

Nibbiṭṭhena carāmi sabbaloke; ^snp1-2-8-3

Attho bhatiyā na vijjati, ^snp1-2-8-4

Atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva”. ^snp1-2-8-5

“Atthi vasā atthi dhenupā, ^snp1-2-9-1

(iti dhaniyo gopo) ^snp1-2-9-2

Godharaṇiyo paveṇiyopi atthi; ^snp1-2-9-3

Usabhopi gavampatīdha atthi, ^snp1-2-9-4

Atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva”. ^snp1-2-9-5

“Natthi vasā natthi dhenupā, ^snp1-2-10-1

(iti bhagavā) ^snp1-2-10-2

Godharaṇiyo paveṇiyopi natthi; ^snp1-2-10-3

Usabhopi gavampatīdha natthi, ^snp1-2-10-4

Atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva”. ^snp1-2-10-5

“Khilā nikhātā asampavedhī, ^snp1-2-11-1

(iti dhaniyo gopo) ^snp1-2-11-2

Dāmā muñjamayā navā susaṇṭhānā; ^snp1-2-11-3

Na hi sakkhinti dhenupāpi chettuṁ, ^snp1-2-11-4

Atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva”. ^snp1-2-11-5

“Usabhoriva chetva bandhanāni, ^snp1-2-12-1

(iti bhagavā) ^snp1-2-12-2

Nāgo pūtilataṁva dālayitvā; ^snp1-2-12-3

Nāhaṁ punupessaṁ gabbhaseyyaṁ, ^snp1-2-12-4

Atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva”. ^snp1-2-12-5

Ninnañca thalañca pūrayanto, ^snp1-2-13-1

Mahāmegho pavassi tāvadeva; ^snp1-2-13-2

Sutvā devassa vassato, ^snp1-2-13-3

Imamatthaṁ dhaniyo abhāsatha. ^snp1-2-13-4

“Lābhā vata no anappakā, ^snp1-2-14-1

Ye mayaṁ bhagavantaṁ addasāma; ^snp1-2-14-2

Saraṇaṁ taṁ upema cakkhuma, ^snp1-2-14-3

Satthā no hohi tuvaṁ mahāmuni. ^snp1-2-14-4

Gopī ca ahañca assavā, ^snp1-2-15-1

Brahmacariyaṁ sugate carāmase; ^snp1-2-15-2

Jātimaraṇassa pāragū, ^snp1-2-15-3

Dukkhassantakarā bhavāmase”. ^snp1-2-15-4

“Nandati puttehi puttimā, ^snp1-2-16-1

(iti māro pāpimā) ^snp1-2-16-2

Gomā gohi tatheva nandati; ^snp1-2-16-3

Upadhī hi narassa nandanā, ^snp1-2-16-4

Na hi so nandati yo nirūpadhi”. ^snp1-2-16-5

“Socati puttehi puttimā, ^snp1-2-17-1

(iti bhagavā) ^snp1-2-17-2

Gomā gohi tatheva socati; ^snp1-2-17-3

Upadhī hi narassa socanā, ^snp1-2-17-4

Na hi so socati yo nirūpadhī”ti. ^snp1-2-17-5

Dhaniyasuttaṁ dutiyaṁ. ^snp1-2-17-6

### Khaggavisāṇasutta (Sutta Nipāta 1.3) ^snp1-3-0

“Sabbesu bhūtesu nidhāya daṇḍaṁ, ^snp1-3-1-1

Aviheṭhayaṁ aññatarampi tesaṁ; ^snp1-3-1-2

Na puttamiccheyya kuto sahāyaṁ, ^snp1-3-1-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-1-4

“Saṁsaggajātassa bhavanti snehā, ^snp1-3-2-1

Snehanvayaṁ dukkhamidaṁ pahoti; ^snp1-3-2-2

Ādīnavaṁ snehajaṁ pekkhamāno, ^snp1-3-2-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-2-4

“Mitte suhajje anukampamāno, ^snp1-3-3-1

Hāpeti atthaṁ paṭibaddhacitto; ^snp1-3-3-2

Etaṁ bhayaṁ santhave pekkhamāno, ^snp1-3-3-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-3-4

“Vaṁso visālova yathā visatto, ^snp1-3-4-1

Puttesu dāresu ca yā apekkhā; ^snp1-3-4-2

Vaṁsakkaḷīrova asajjamāno, ^snp1-3-4-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-4-4

“Migo araññamhi yathā abaddho, ^snp1-3-5-1

Yenicchakaṁ gacchati gocarāya; ^snp1-3-5-2

Viññū naro seritaṁ pekkhamāno, ^snp1-3-5-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-5-4

“Āmantanā hoti sahāyamajjhe, ^snp1-3-6-1

Vāse ṭhāne gamane cārikāya; ^snp1-3-6-2

Anabhijjhitaṁ seritaṁ pekkhamāno, ^snp1-3-6-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-6-4

“Khiḍḍā ratī hoti sahāyamajjhe, ^snp1-3-7-1

Puttesu ca vipulaṁ hoti pemaṁ; ^snp1-3-7-2

Piyavippayogaṁ vijigucchamāno, ^snp1-3-7-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-7-4

“Cātuddiso appaṭigho ca hoti, ^snp1-3-8-1

Santussamāno itarītarena; ^snp1-3-8-2

Parissayānaṁ sahitā achambhī, ^snp1-3-8-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-8-4

“Dussaṅgahā pabbajitāpi eke, ^snp1-3-9-1

Atho gahaṭṭhā gharamāvasantā; ^snp1-3-9-2

Appossukko paraputtesu hutvā, ^snp1-3-9-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-9-4

“Oropayitvā gihibyañjanāni, ^snp1-3-10-1

Sañchinnapatto yathā koviḷāro; ^snp1-3-10-2

Chetvāna vīro gihibandhanāni, ^snp1-3-10-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-10-4

“Sace labhetha nipakaṁ sahāyaṁ, ^snp1-3-11-1

Saddhiṁ caraṁ sādhuvihāridhīraṁ; ^snp1-3-11-2

Abhibhuyya sabbāni parissayāni, ^snp1-3-11-3

Careyya tenattamano satīmā”. ^snp1-3-11-4

“No ce labhetha nipakaṁ sahāyaṁ, ^snp1-3-12-1

Saddhiṁ caraṁ sādhuvihāridhīraṁ; ^snp1-3-12-2

Rājāva raṭṭhaṁ vijitaṁ pahāya, ^snp1-3-12-3

Eko care mātaṅgaraññeva nāgo”. ^snp1-3-12-4

“Addhā pasaṁsāma sahāyasampadaṁ, ^snp1-3-13-1

Seṭṭhā samā sevitabbā sahāyā; ^snp1-3-13-2

Ete aladdhā anavajjabhojī, ^snp1-3-13-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-13-4

“Disvā suvaṇṇassa pabhassarāni, ^snp1-3-14-1

Kammāraputtena suniṭṭhitāni; ^snp1-3-14-2

Saṅghaṭṭamānāni duve bhujasmiṁ, ^snp1-3-14-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-14-4

“Evaṁ dutīyena sahā mamassa, ^snp1-3-15-1

Vācābhilāpo abhisajjanā vā; ^snp1-3-15-2

Etaṁ bhayaṁ āyatiṁ pekkhamāno, ^snp1-3-15-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-15-4

“Kāmā hi citrā madhurā manoramā, ^snp1-3-16-1

Virūparūpena mathenti cittaṁ; ^snp1-3-16-2

Ādīnavaṁ kāmaguṇesu disvā, ^snp1-3-16-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-16-4

“Ītī ca gaṇḍo ca upaddavo ca, ^snp1-3-17-1

Rogo ca sallañca bhayañca metaṁ; ^snp1-3-17-2

Etaṁ bhayaṁ kāmaguṇesu disvā, ^snp1-3-17-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-17-4

“Sītañca uṇhañca khudaṁ pipāsaṁ, ^snp1-3-18-1

Vātātape ḍaṁsasarīsape ca; ^snp1-3-18-2

Sabbānipetāni abhisambhavitvā, ^snp1-3-18-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-18-4

“Nāgova yūthāni vivajjayitvā, ^snp1-3-19-1

Sañjātakhandho padumī uḷāro; ^snp1-3-19-2

Yathābhirantaṁ viharaṁ araññe, ^snp1-3-19-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-19-4

“Aṭṭhānataṁ saṅgaṇikāratassa, ^snp1-3-20-1

Yaṁ phassaye sāmayikaṁ vimuttiṁ; ^snp1-3-20-2

Ādiccabandhussa vaco nisamma, ^snp1-3-20-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-20-4

“Diṭṭhīvisūkāni upātivatto, ^snp1-3-21-1

Patto niyāmaṁ paṭiladdhamaggo; ^snp1-3-21-2

Uppannañāṇomhi anaññaneyyo, ^snp1-3-21-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-21-4

“Nillolupo nikkuho nippipāso, ^snp1-3-22-1

Nimmakkho niddhantakasāvamoho; ^snp1-3-22-2

Nirāsayo sabbaloke bhavitvā, ^snp1-3-22-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-22-4

“Pāpaṁ sahāyaṁ parivajjayetha, ^snp1-3-23-1

Anatthadassiṁ visame niviṭṭhaṁ; ^snp1-3-23-2

Sayaṁ na seve pasutaṁ pamattaṁ, ^snp1-3-23-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-23-4

“Bahussutaṁ dhammadharaṁ bhajetha, ^snp1-3-24-1

Mittaṁ uḷāraṁ paṭibhānavantaṁ; ^snp1-3-24-2

Aññāya atthāni vineyya kaṅkhaṁ, ^snp1-3-24-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-24-4

“Khiḍḍaṁ ratiṁ kāmasukhañca loke, ^snp1-3-25-1

Analaṅkaritvā anapekkhamāno; ^snp1-3-25-2

Vibhūsanaṭṭhānā virato saccavādī, ^snp1-3-25-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-25-4

“Puttañca dāraṁ pitarañca mātaraṁ, ^snp1-3-26-1

Dhanāni dhaññāni ca bandhavāni; ^snp1-3-26-2

Hitvāna kāmāni yathodhikāni, ^snp1-3-26-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-26-4

“Saṅgo eso parittamettha sokhyaṁ, ^snp1-3-27-1

Appassādo dukkhamettha bhiyyo; ^snp1-3-27-2

Gaḷo eso iti ñatvā matīmā, ^snp1-3-27-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-27-4

“Sandālayitvāna saṁyojanāni, ^snp1-3-28-1

Jālaṁva bhetvā salilambucārī; ^snp1-3-28-2

Aggīva daḍḍhaṁ anivattamāno, ^snp1-3-28-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-28-4

“Okkhittacakkhu na ca pādalolo, ^snp1-3-29-1

Guttindriyo rakkhitamānasāno; ^snp1-3-29-2

Anavassuto apariḍayhamāno, ^snp1-3-29-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-29-4

“Ohārayitvā gihibyañjanāni, ^snp1-3-30-1

Sañchannapatto yathā pārichatto; ^snp1-3-30-2

Kāsāyavattho abhinikkhamitvā, ^snp1-3-30-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-30-4

“Rasesu gedhaṁ akaraṁ alolo, ^snp1-3-31-1

Anaññaposī sapadānacārī; ^snp1-3-31-2

Kule kule appaṭibaddhacitto, ^snp1-3-31-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-31-4

“Pahāya pañcāvaraṇāni cetaso, ^snp1-3-32-1

Upakkilese byapanujja sabbe; ^snp1-3-32-2

Anissito chetva sinehadosaṁ, ^snp1-3-32-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-32-4

“Vipiṭṭhikatvāna sukhaṁ dukhañca, ^snp1-3-33-1

Pubbeva ca somanassadomanassaṁ; ^snp1-3-33-2

Laddhānupekkhaṁ samathaṁ visuddhaṁ, ^snp1-3-33-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-33-4

“Āraddhaviriyo paramatthapattiyā, ^snp1-3-34-1

Alīnacitto akusītavutti; ^snp1-3-34-2

Daḷhanikkamo thāmabalūpapanno, ^snp1-3-34-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-34-4

“Paṭisallānaṁ jhānamariñcamāno, ^snp1-3-35-1

Dhammesu niccaṁ anudhammacārī; ^snp1-3-35-2

Ādīnavaṁ sammasitā bhavesu, ^snp1-3-35-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-35-4

“Taṇhakkhayaṁ patthayamappamatto, ^snp1-3-36-1

Aneḷamūgo sutavā satīmā; ^snp1-3-36-2

Saṅkhātadhammo niyato padhānavā, ^snp1-3-36-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-36-4

“Sīhova saddesu asantasanto, ^snp1-3-37-1

Vātova jālamhi asajjamāno; ^snp1-3-37-2

Padumaṁva toyena alippamāno, ^snp1-3-37-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-37-4

“Sīho yathā dāṭhabalī pasayha, ^snp1-3-38-1

Rājā migānaṁ abhibhuyya cārī; ^snp1-3-38-2

Sevetha pantāni senāsanāni, ^snp1-3-38-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-38-4

“Mettaṁ upekkhaṁ karuṇaṁ vimuttiṁ, ^snp1-3-39-1

Āsevamāno muditañca kāle; ^snp1-3-39-2

Sabbena lokena avirujjhamāno, ^snp1-3-39-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-39-4

“Rāgañca dosañca pahāya mohaṁ, ^snp1-3-40-1

Sandālayitvāna saṁyojanāni; ^snp1-3-40-2

Asantasaṁ jīvitasaṅkhayamhi, ^snp1-3-40-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-40-4

“Bhajanti sevanti ca kāraṇatthā, ^snp1-3-41-1

Nikkāraṇā dullabhā ajja mittā; ^snp1-3-41-2

Attaṭṭhapaññā asucī manussā, ^snp1-3-41-3

Eko care khaggavisāṇakappo”. ^snp1-3-41-4

Khaggavisāṇasuttaṁ tatiyaṁ. ^snp1-3-41-5

### Kasibhāradvājasutta (Sutta Nipāta 1.4) ^snp1-4-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp1-4-1-1

ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā magadhesu viharati dakkhiṇāgirismiṁ ekanāḷāyaṁ brāhmaṇagāme. ^snp1-4-1-2

Tena kho pana samayena kasibhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa pañcamattāni naṅgalasatāni payuttāni honti vappakāle. ^snp1-4-1-3

Atha kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṁ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya yena kasibhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa kammanto tenupasaṅkami. ^snp1-4-1-4

Tena kho pana samayena kasibhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa parivesanā vattati. ^snp1-4-1-5

Atha kho bhagavā yena parivesanā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā ekamantaṁ aṭṭhāsi. ^snp1-4-1-6

Addasā kho kasibhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṁ piṇḍāya ṭhitaṁ. ^snp1-4-2-1

Disvāna bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp1-4-2-2

“ahaṁ kho, samaṇa, kasāmi ca vapāmi ca; kasitvā ca vapitvā ca bhuñjāmi. ^snp1-4-2-3

Tvampi, samaṇa, kasassu ca vapassu ca; kasitvā ca vapitvā ca bhuñjassū”ti. ^snp1-4-2-4

“Ahampi kho, brāhmaṇa, kasāmi ca vapāmi ca; kasitvā ca vapitvā ca bhuñjāmī”ti. ^snp1-4-3-1

“Na kho pana mayaṁ passāma bhoto gotamassa yugaṁ vā naṅgalaṁ vā phālaṁ vā pācanaṁ vā balībadde vā. ^snp1-4-3-2

Atha ca pana bhavaṁ gotamo evamāha: ^snp1-4-3-3

‘ahampi kho, brāhmaṇa, kasāmi ca vapāmi ca; kasitvā ca vapitvā ca bhuñjāmī’”ti. ^snp1-4-3-4

Atha kho kasibhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṁ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi: ^snp1-4-4-1

“Kassako paṭijānāsi, ^snp1-4-5-1

na ca passāma te kasiṁ; ^snp1-4-5-2

Kasiṁ no pucchito brūhi, ^snp1-4-5-3

yathā jānemu te kasiṁ”. ^snp1-4-5-4

“Saddhā bījaṁ tapo vuṭṭhi, ^snp1-4-6-1

paññā me yuganaṅgalaṁ; ^snp1-4-6-2

Hirī īsā mano yottaṁ, ^snp1-4-6-3

sati me phālapācanaṁ. ^snp1-4-6-4

Kāyagutto vacīgutto, ^snp1-4-7-1

āhāre udare yato; ^snp1-4-7-2

Saccaṁ karomi niddānaṁ, ^snp1-4-7-3

soraccaṁ me pamocanaṁ. ^snp1-4-7-4

Vīriyaṁ me dhuradhorayhaṁ, ^snp1-4-8-1

yogakkhemādhivāhanaṁ; ^snp1-4-8-2

Gacchati anivattantaṁ, ^snp1-4-8-3

yattha gantvā na socati. ^snp1-4-8-4

Evamesā kasī kaṭṭhā, ^snp1-4-9-1

Sā hoti amatapphalā; ^snp1-4-9-2

Etaṁ kasiṁ kasitvāna, ^snp1-4-9-3

Sabbadukkhā pamuccatī”ti. ^snp1-4-9-4

Atha kho kasibhāradvājo brāhmaṇo mahatiyā kaṁsapātiyā pāyasaṁ vaḍḍhetvā bhagavato upanāmesi: ^snp1-4-10-1

“bhuñjatu bhavaṁ gotamo pāyasaṁ. ^snp1-4-10-2

Kassako bhavaṁ; ^snp1-4-10-3

yañhi bhavaṁ gotamo amatapphalaṁ kasiṁ kasatī”ti. ^snp1-4-10-4

“Gāthābhigītaṁ me abhojaneyyaṁ, ^snp1-4-11-1

Sampassataṁ brāhmaṇa nesa dhammo; ^snp1-4-11-2

Gāthābhigītaṁ panudanti buddhā, ^snp1-4-11-3

Dhamme satī brāhmaṇa vuttiresā. ^snp1-4-11-4

Aññena ca kevalinaṁ mahesiṁ, ^snp1-4-12-1

Khīṇāsavaṁ kukkuccavūpasantaṁ; ^snp1-4-12-2

Annena pānena upaṭṭhahassu, ^snp1-4-12-3

Khettaṁ hi taṁ puññapekkhassa hotī”ti. ^snp1-4-12-4

“Atha kassa cāhaṁ, bho gotama, imaṁ pāyasaṁ dammī”ti? ^snp1-4-13-1

“Na khvāhaṁ taṁ, brāhmaṇa, passāmi sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya, yassa so pāyaso bhutto sammā pariṇāmaṁ gaccheyya, aññatra tathāgatassa vā tathāgatasāvakassa vā. ^snp1-4-13-2

Tena hi tvaṁ, brāhmaṇa, taṁ pāyasaṁ appaharite vā chaḍḍehi appāṇake vā udake opilāpehī”ti. ^snp1-4-13-3

Atha kho kasibhāradvājo brāhmaṇo taṁ pāyasaṁ appāṇake udake opilāpesi. ^snp1-4-14-1

Atha kho so pāyaso udake pakkhitto cicciṭāyati ciṭiciṭāyati sandhūpāyati sampadhūpāyati. ^snp1-4-14-2

Seyyathāpi nāma phālo divasaṁ santatto udake pakkhitto cicciṭāyati ciṭiciṭāyati sandhūpāyati sampadhūpāyati; ^snp1-4-14-3

evamevaṁ so pāyaso udake pakkhitto cicciṭāyati ciṭiciṭāyati sandhūpāyati sampadhūpāyati. ^snp1-4-14-4

Atha kho kasibhāradvājo brāhmaṇo saṁviggo lomahaṭṭhajāto yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavato pādesu sirasā nipatitvā bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp1-4-15-1

“abhikkantaṁ, bho gotama, abhikkantaṁ, bho gotama. ^snp1-4-15-2

Seyyathāpi, bho gotama, nikkujjitaṁ vā ukkujjeyya, paṭicchannaṁ vā vivareyya, mūḷhassa vā maggaṁ ācikkheyya, andhakāre vā telapajjotaṁ dhāreyya, ‘cakkhumanto rūpāni dakkhantī’ti; evamevaṁ bhotā gotamena anekapariyāyena dhammo pakāsito. ^snp1-4-15-3

Esāhaṁ bhavantaṁ gotamaṁ saraṇaṁ gacchāmi dhammañca bhikkhusaṅghañca, ^snp1-4-15-4

labheyyāhaṁ bhoto gotamassa santike pabbajjaṁ, labheyyaṁ upasampadan”ti. ^snp1-4-15-5

Alattha kho kasibhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavato santike pabbajjaṁ, alattha upasampadaṁ. ^snp1-4-16-1

Acirūpasampanno kho panāyasmā bhāradvājo eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto nacirasseva—yassatthāya kulaputtā sammadeva agārasmā anagāriyaṁ pabbajanti, tadanuttaraṁ—brahmacariyapariyosānaṁ diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja vihāsi. ^snp1-4-16-2

“Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā”ti abbhaññāsi. ^snp1-4-16-3

Aññataro ca panāyasmā bhāradvājo arahataṁ ahosīti. ^snp1-4-16-4

Kasibhāradvājasuttaṁ catutthaṁ. ^snp1-4-16-5

### Cundasutta (Sutta Nipāta 1.5) ^snp1-5-0

“Pucchāmi muniṁ pahūtapaññaṁ, ^snp1-5-1-1

(iti cundo kammāraputto) ^snp1-5-1-2

Buddhaṁ dhammassāmiṁ vītataṇhaṁ; ^snp1-5-1-3

Dvipaduttamaṁ sārathīnaṁ pavaraṁ, ^snp1-5-1-4

Kati loke samaṇā tadiṅgha brūhi”. ^snp1-5-1-5

“Caturo samaṇā na pañcamatthi, ^snp1-5-2-1

(cundāti bhagavā) ^snp1-5-2-2

Te te āvikaromi sakkhipuṭṭho; ^snp1-5-2-3

Maggajino maggadesako ca, ^snp1-5-2-4

Magge jīvati yo ca maggadūsī”. ^snp1-5-2-5

“Kaṁ maggajinaṁ vadanti buddhā, ^snp1-5-3-1

(iti cundo kammāraputto) ^snp1-5-3-2

Maggakkhāyī kathaṁ atulyo hoti; ^snp1-5-3-3

Magge jīvati me brūhi puṭṭho, ^snp1-5-3-4

Atha me āvikarohi maggadūsiṁ”. ^snp1-5-3-5

“Yo tiṇṇakathaṅkatho visallo, ^snp1-5-4-1

Nibbānābhirato anānugiddho; ^snp1-5-4-2

Lokassa sadevakassa netā, ^snp1-5-4-3

Tādiṁ maggajinaṁ vadanti buddhā. ^snp1-5-4-4

Paramaṁ paramanti yodha ñatvā, ^snp1-5-5-1

Akkhāti vibhajate idheva dhammaṁ; ^snp1-5-5-2

Taṁ kaṅkhachidaṁ muniṁ anejaṁ, ^snp1-5-5-3

Dutiyaṁ bhikkhunamāhu maggadesiṁ. ^snp1-5-5-4

Yo dhammapade sudesite, ^snp1-5-6-1

Magge jīvati saññato satīmā; ^snp1-5-6-2

Anavajjapadāni sevamāno, ^snp1-5-6-3

Tatiyaṁ bhikkhunamāhu maggajīviṁ. ^snp1-5-6-4

Chadanaṁ katvāna subbatānaṁ, ^snp1-5-7-1

Pakkhandī kuladūsako pagabbho; ^snp1-5-7-2

Māyāvī asaññato palāpo, ^snp1-5-7-3

Patirūpena caraṁ sa maggadūsī. ^snp1-5-7-4

Ete ca paṭivijjhi yo gahaṭṭho, ^snp1-5-8-1

Sutavā ariyasāvako sapañño; ^snp1-5-8-2

Sabbe netādisāti ñatvā, ^snp1-5-8-3

Iti disvā na hāpeti tassa saddhā; ^snp1-5-8-4

Kathaṁ hi duṭṭhena asampaduṭṭhaṁ, ^snp1-5-8-5

Suddhaṁ asuddhena samaṁ kareyyā”ti. ^snp1-5-8-6

Cundasuttaṁ pañcamaṁ. ^snp1-5-8-7

### Parābhavasutta (Sutta Nipāta 1.6) ^snp1-6-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp1-6-1-1

ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. ^snp1-6-1-2

Atha kho aññatarā devatā abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṁ jetavanaṁ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ aṭṭhāsi. ^snp1-6-1-3

Ekamantaṁ ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavantaṁ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi: ^snp1-6-1-4

“Parābhavantaṁ purisaṁ, ^snp1-6-2-1

mayaṁ pucchāma gotama; ^snp1-6-2-2

Bhavantaṁ puṭṭhumāgamma, ^snp1-6-2-3

kiṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-2-4

“Suvijāno bhavaṁ hoti, ^snp1-6-3-1

suvijāno parābhavo; ^snp1-6-3-2

Dhammakāmo bhavaṁ hoti, ^snp1-6-3-3

dhammadessī parābhavo”. ^snp1-6-3-4

“Iti hetaṁ vijānāma, ^snp1-6-4-1

paṭhamo so parābhavo; ^snp1-6-4-2

Dutiyaṁ bhagavā brūhi, ^snp1-6-4-3

kiṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-4-4

“Asantassa piyā honti, ^snp1-6-5-1

sante na kurute piyaṁ; ^snp1-6-5-2

Asataṁ dhammaṁ roceti, ^snp1-6-5-3

taṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-5-4

“Iti hetaṁ vijānāma, ^snp1-6-6-1

dutiyo so parābhavo; ^snp1-6-6-2

Tatiyaṁ bhagavā brūhi, ^snp1-6-6-3

kiṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-6-4

“Niddāsīlī sabhāsīlī, ^snp1-6-7-1

anuṭṭhātā ca yo naro; ^snp1-6-7-2

Alaso kodhapaññāṇo, ^snp1-6-7-3

taṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-7-4

“Iti hetaṁ vijānāma, ^snp1-6-8-1

tatiyo so parābhavo; ^snp1-6-8-2

Catutthaṁ bhagavā brūhi, ^snp1-6-8-3

kiṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-8-4

“Yo mātaraṁ pitaraṁ vā, ^snp1-6-9-1

jiṇṇakaṁ gatayobbanaṁ; ^snp1-6-9-2

Pahu santo na bharati, ^snp1-6-9-3

taṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-9-4

“Iti hetaṁ vijānāma, ^snp1-6-10-1

catuttho so parābhavo; ^snp1-6-10-2

Pañcamaṁ bhagavā brūhi, ^snp1-6-10-3

kiṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-10-4

“Yo brāhmaṇaṁ samaṇaṁ vā, ^snp1-6-11-1

Aññaṁ vāpi vanibbakaṁ; ^snp1-6-11-2

Musāvādena vañceti, ^snp1-6-11-3

Taṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-11-4

“Iti hetaṁ vijānāma, ^snp1-6-12-1

Pañcamo so parābhavo; ^snp1-6-12-2

Chaṭṭhamaṁ bhagavā brūhi, ^snp1-6-12-3

Kiṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-12-4

“Pahūtavitto puriso, ^snp1-6-13-1

Sahirañño sabhojano; ^snp1-6-13-2

Eko bhuñjati sādūni, ^snp1-6-13-3

Taṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-13-4

“Iti hetaṁ vijānāma, ^snp1-6-14-1

Chaṭṭhamo so parābhavo; ^snp1-6-14-2

Sattamaṁ bhagavā brūhi, ^snp1-6-14-3

Kiṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-14-4

“Jātitthaddho dhanatthaddho, ^snp1-6-15-1

Gottatthaddho ca yo naro; ^snp1-6-15-2

Saññātiṁ atimaññeti, ^snp1-6-15-3

Taṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-15-4

“Iti hetaṁ vijānāma, ^snp1-6-16-1

Sattamo so parābhavo; ^snp1-6-16-2

Aṭṭhamaṁ bhagavā brūhi, ^snp1-6-16-3

Kiṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-16-4

“Itthidhutto surādhutto, ^snp1-6-17-1

Akkhadhutto ca yo naro; ^snp1-6-17-2

Laddhaṁ laddhaṁ vināseti, ^snp1-6-17-3

Taṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-17-4

“Iti hetaṁ vijānāma, ^snp1-6-18-1

Aṭṭhamo so parābhavo; ^snp1-6-18-2

Navamaṁ bhagavā brūhi, ^snp1-6-18-3

Kiṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-18-4

“Sehi dārehi asantuṭṭho, ^snp1-6-19-1

Vesiyāsu padussati; ^snp1-6-19-2

Dussati paradāresu, ^snp1-6-19-3

Taṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-19-4

“Iti hetaṁ vijānāma, ^snp1-6-20-1

Navamo so parābhavo; ^snp1-6-20-2

Dasamaṁ bhagavā brūhi, ^snp1-6-20-3

Kiṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-20-4

“Atītayobbano poso, ^snp1-6-21-1

Āneti timbarutthaniṁ; ^snp1-6-21-2

Tassā issā na supati, ^snp1-6-21-3

Taṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-21-4

“Iti hetaṁ vijānāma, ^snp1-6-22-1

Dasamo so parābhavo; ^snp1-6-22-2

Ekādasamaṁ bhagavā brūhi, ^snp1-6-22-3

Kiṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-22-4

“Itthiṁ soṇḍiṁ vikiraṇiṁ, ^snp1-6-23-1

Purisaṁ vāpi tādisaṁ; ^snp1-6-23-2

Issariyasmiṁ ṭhapeti, ^snp1-6-23-3

Taṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-23-4

“Iti hetaṁ vijānāma, ^snp1-6-24-1

Ekādasamo so parābhavo; ^snp1-6-24-2

Dvādasamaṁ bhagavā brūhi, ^snp1-6-24-3

Kiṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ”. ^snp1-6-24-4

“Appabhogo mahātaṇho, ^snp1-6-25-1

Khattiye jāyate kule; ^snp1-6-25-2

So ca rajjaṁ patthayati, ^snp1-6-25-3

Taṁ parābhavato mukhaṁ. ^snp1-6-25-4

Ete parābhave loke, ^snp1-6-26-1

Paṇḍito samavekkhiya; ^snp1-6-26-2

Ariyo dassanasampanno, ^snp1-6-26-3

Sa lokaṁ bhajate sivan”ti. ^snp1-6-26-4

Parābhavasuttaṁ chaṭṭhaṁ. ^snp1-6-26-5

### Vasalasutta (Sutta Nipāta 1.7) ^snp1-7-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp1-7-1-1

ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. ^snp1-7-1-2

Atha kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṁ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya sāvatthiṁ piṇḍāya pāvisi. ^snp1-7-1-3

Tena kho pana samayena aggikabhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa nivesane aggi pajjalito hoti āhuti paggahitā. ^snp1-7-1-4

Atha kho bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ sapadānaṁ piṇḍāya caramāno yena aggikabhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa nivesanaṁ tenupasaṅkami. ^snp1-7-1-5

Addasā kho aggikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṁ dūratova āgacchantaṁ. ^snp1-7-2-1

Disvāna bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp1-7-2-2

“tatreva, muṇḍaka; ^snp1-7-2-3

tatreva, samaṇaka; ^snp1-7-2-4

tatreva, vasalaka, tiṭṭhāhī”ti. ^snp1-7-2-5

Evaṁ vutte, bhagavā aggikabhāradvājaṁ brāhmaṇaṁ etadavoca: ^snp1-7-3-1

“jānāsi pana tvaṁ, brāhmaṇa, vasalaṁ vā vasalakaraṇe vā dhamme”ti? ^snp1-7-3-2

“Na khvāhaṁ, bho gotama, jānāmi vasalaṁ vā vasalakaraṇe vā dhamme; ^snp1-7-3-3

sādhu me bhavaṁ gotamo tathā dhammaṁ desetu, yathāhaṁ jāneyyaṁ vasalaṁ vā vasalakaraṇe vā dhamme”ti. ^snp1-7-3-4

“Tena hi, brāhmaṇa, suṇāhi, sādhukaṁ manasi karohi; bhāsissāmī”ti. ^snp1-7-3-5

“Evaṁ, bho”ti kho aggikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavato paccassosi. ^snp1-7-3-6

Bhagavā etadavoca: ^snp1-7-3-7

“Kodhano upanāhī ca, ^snp1-7-4-1

pāpamakkhī ca yo naro; ^snp1-7-4-2

Vipannadiṭṭhi māyāvī, ^snp1-7-4-3

taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-4-4

Ekajaṁ vā dvijaṁ vāpi, ^snp1-7-5-1

yodha pāṇaṁ vihiṁsati; ^snp1-7-5-2

Yassa pāṇe dayā natthi, ^snp1-7-5-3

taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-5-4

Yo hanti parirundhati, ^snp1-7-6-1

gāmāni nigamāni ca; ^snp1-7-6-2

Niggāhako samaññāto, ^snp1-7-6-3

taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-6-4

Gāme vā yadi vā raññe, ^snp1-7-7-1

yaṁ paresaṁ mamāyitaṁ; ^snp1-7-7-2

Theyyā adinnamādeti, ^snp1-7-7-3

taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-7-4

Yo have iṇamādāya, ^snp1-7-8-1

cujjamāno palāyati; ^snp1-7-8-2

Na hi te iṇamatthīti, ^snp1-7-8-3

taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-8-4

Yo ve kiñcikkhakamyatā, ^snp1-7-9-1

panthasmiṁ vajantaṁ janaṁ; ^snp1-7-9-2

Hantvā kiñcikkhamādeti, ^snp1-7-9-3

taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-9-4

Attahetu parahetu, ^snp1-7-10-1

dhanahetu ca yo naro; ^snp1-7-10-2

Sakkhipuṭṭho musā brūti, ^snp1-7-10-3

taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-10-4

Yo ñātīnaṁ sakhīnaṁ vā, ^snp1-7-11-1

dāresu paṭidissati; ^snp1-7-11-2

Sāhasā sampiyena vā, ^snp1-7-11-3

taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-11-4

Yo mātaraṁ pitaraṁ vā, ^snp1-7-12-1

jiṇṇakaṁ gatayobbanaṁ; ^snp1-7-12-2

Pahu santo na bharati, ^snp1-7-12-3

taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-12-4

Yo mātaraṁ pitaraṁ vā, ^snp1-7-13-1

Bhātaraṁ bhaginiṁ sasuṁ; ^snp1-7-13-2

Hanti roseti vācāya, ^snp1-7-13-3

Taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-13-4

Yo atthaṁ pucchito santo, ^snp1-7-14-1

Anatthamanusāsati; ^snp1-7-14-2

Paṭicchannena manteti, ^snp1-7-14-3

Taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-14-4

Yo katvā pāpakaṁ kammaṁ, ^snp1-7-15-1

Mā maṁ jaññāti icchati; ^snp1-7-15-2

Yo paṭicchannakammanto, ^snp1-7-15-3

Taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-15-4

Yo ve parakulaṁ gantvā, ^snp1-7-16-1

Bhutvāna sucibhojanaṁ; ^snp1-7-16-2

Āgataṁ nappaṭipūjeti, ^snp1-7-16-3

Taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-16-4

Yo brāhmaṇaṁ samaṇaṁ vā, ^snp1-7-17-1

Aññaṁ vāpi vanibbakaṁ; ^snp1-7-17-2

Musāvādena vañceti, ^snp1-7-17-3

Taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-17-4

Yo brāhmaṇaṁ samaṇaṁ vā, ^snp1-7-18-1

Bhattakāle upaṭṭhite; ^snp1-7-18-2

Roseti vācā na ca deti, ^snp1-7-18-3

Taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-18-4

Asataṁ yodha pabrūti, ^snp1-7-19-1

Mohena paliguṇṭhito; ^snp1-7-19-2

Kiñcikkhaṁ nijigīsāno, ^snp1-7-19-3

Taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-19-4

Yo cattānaṁ samukkaṁse, ^snp1-7-20-1

Pare ca mavajānāti; ^snp1-7-20-2

Nihīno sena mānena, ^snp1-7-20-3

Taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-20-4

Rosako kadariyo ca, ^snp1-7-21-1

Pāpiccho maccharī saṭho; ^snp1-7-21-2

Ahiriko anottappī, ^snp1-7-21-3

Taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-21-4

Yo buddhaṁ paribhāsati, ^snp1-7-22-1

Atha vā tassa sāvakaṁ; ^snp1-7-22-2

Paribbājaṁ gahaṭṭhaṁ vā, ^snp1-7-22-3

Taṁ jaññā vasalo iti. ^snp1-7-22-4

Yo ve anarahaṁ santo, ^snp1-7-23-1

Arahaṁ paṭijānāti; ^snp1-7-23-2

Coro sabrahmake loke, ^snp1-7-23-3

Eso kho vasalādhamo; ^snp1-7-23-4

Ete kho vasalā vuttā, ^snp1-7-23-5

Mayā yete pakāsitā. ^snp1-7-23-6

Na jaccā vasalo hoti, ^snp1-7-24-1

Na jaccā hoti brāhmaṇo; ^snp1-7-24-2

Kammunā vasalo hoti, ^snp1-7-24-3

Kammunā hoti brāhmaṇo. ^snp1-7-24-4

Tadamināpi jānātha, ^snp1-7-25-1

Yathāmedaṁ nidassanaṁ; ^snp1-7-25-2

Caṇḍālaputto sopāko, ^snp1-7-25-3

Mātaṅgo iti vissuto. ^snp1-7-25-4

So yasaṁ paramaṁ patto, ^snp1-7-26-1

Mātaṅgo yaṁ sudullabhaṁ; ^snp1-7-26-2

Āgacchuṁ tassupaṭṭhānaṁ, ^snp1-7-26-3

Khattiyā brāhmaṇā bahū. ^snp1-7-26-4

Devayānaṁ abhiruyha, ^snp1-7-27-1

Virajaṁ so mahāpathaṁ; ^snp1-7-27-2

Kāmarāgaṁ virājetvā, ^snp1-7-27-3

Brahmalokūpago ahu; ^snp1-7-27-4

Na naṁ jāti nivāresi, ^snp1-7-27-5

Brahmalokūpapattiyā. ^snp1-7-27-6

Ajjhāyakakule jātā, ^snp1-7-28-1

Brāhmaṇā mantabandhavā; ^snp1-7-28-2

Te ca pāpesu kammesu, ^snp1-7-28-3

Abhiṇhamupadissare. ^snp1-7-28-4

Diṭṭheva dhamme gārayhā, ^snp1-7-29-1

Samparāye ca duggati; ^snp1-7-29-2

Na ne jāti nivāreti, ^snp1-7-29-3

Duggatyā garahāya vā. ^snp1-7-29-4

Na jaccā vasalo hoti, ^snp1-7-30-1

Na jaccā hoti brāhmaṇo; ^snp1-7-30-2

Kammunā vasalo hoti, ^snp1-7-30-3

Kammunā hoti brāhmaṇo”ti. ^snp1-7-30-4

Evaṁ vutte, aggikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp1-7-31-1

“abhikkantaṁ, bho gotama …pe… ^snp1-7-31-2

upāsakaṁ maṁ bhavaṁ gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaṁ saraṇaṁ gatan”ti. ^snp1-7-31-3

Vasalasuttaṁ sattamaṁ. ^snp1-7-31-4

### Mettasutta (Sutta Nipāta 1.8) ^snp1-8-0

“Karaṇīyamatthakusalena, ^snp1-8-1-1

Yanta santaṁ padaṁ abhisamecca; ^snp1-8-1-2

Sakko ujū ca suhujū ca, ^snp1-8-1-3

Sūvaco cassa mudu anatimānī. ^snp1-8-1-4

Santussako ca subharo ca, ^snp1-8-2-1

Appakicco ca sallahukavutti; ^snp1-8-2-2

Santindriyo ca nipako ca, ^snp1-8-2-3

Appagabbho kulesvananugiddho. ^snp1-8-2-4

Na ca khuddamācare kiñci, ^snp1-8-3-1

Yena viññū pare upavadeyyuṁ; ^snp1-8-3-2

Sukhino va khemino hontu, ^snp1-8-3-3

Sabbasattā bhavantu sukhitattā. ^snp1-8-3-4

Ye keci pāṇabhūtatthi, ^snp1-8-4-1

Tasā vā thāvarā vanavasesā; ^snp1-8-4-2

Dīghā vā ye va mahantā, ^snp1-8-4-3

Majjhimā rassakā aṇukathūlā. ^snp1-8-4-4

Diṭṭhā vā ye va adiṭṭhā, ^snp1-8-5-1

Ye va dūre vasanti avidūre; ^snp1-8-5-2

Bhūtā va sambhavesī va, ^snp1-8-5-3

Sabbasattā bhavantu sukhitattā. ^snp1-8-5-4

Na paro paraṁ nikubbetha, ^snp1-8-6-1

Nātimaññetha katthaci na kañci; ^snp1-8-6-2

Byārosanā paṭighasañña, ^snp1-8-6-3

Nāññamaññassa dukkhamiccheyya. ^snp1-8-6-4

Mātā yathā niyaṁ puttam ^snp1-8-7-1

Āyusā ekaputtamanurakkhe; ^snp1-8-7-2

Evampi sabbabhūtesu, ^snp1-8-7-3

Mānasaṁ bhāvaye aparimāṇaṁ. ^snp1-8-7-4

Mettañca sabbalokasmi, ^snp1-8-8-1

Mānasaṁ bhāvaye aparimāṇaṁ; ^snp1-8-8-2

Uddhaṁ adho ca tiriyañca, ^snp1-8-8-3

Asambādhaṁ averamasapattaṁ. ^snp1-8-8-4

Tiṭṭhaṁ caraṁ nisinno va, ^snp1-8-9-1

Sayāno yāvatāssa vitamiddho; ^snp1-8-9-2

Etaṁ satiṁ adhiṭṭheyya, ^snp1-8-9-3

Brahmametaṁ vihāramidhamāhu. ^snp1-8-9-4

Diṭṭhiñca anupaggamma, ^snp1-8-10-1

Sīlavā dassanena sampanno; ^snp1-8-10-2

Kāmesu vinaya gedhaṁ, ^snp1-8-10-3

Na hi jātuggabbhaseyya punaretī”ti. ^snp1-8-10-4

Mettasuttaṁ aṭṭhamaṁ. ^snp1-8-10-5

### Hemavatasutta (Sutta Nipāta 1.9) ^snp1-9-0

“Ajja pannaraso uposatho, ^snp1-9-1-1

(iti sātāgiro yakkho) ^snp1-9-1-2

Dibbā ratti upaṭṭhitā; ^snp1-9-1-3

Anomanāmaṁ satthāraṁ, ^snp1-9-1-4

Handa passāma gotamaṁ”. ^snp1-9-1-5

“Kacci mano supaṇihito, ^snp1-9-2-1

(iti hemavato yakkho) ^snp1-9-2-2

Sabbabhūtesu tādino; ^snp1-9-2-3

Kacci iṭṭhe aniṭṭhe ca, ^snp1-9-2-4

Saṅkappassa vasīkatā”. ^snp1-9-2-5

“Mano cassa supaṇihito, ^snp1-9-3-1

(iti sātāgiro yakkho) ^snp1-9-3-2

Sabbabhūtesu tādino; ^snp1-9-3-3

Atho iṭṭhe aniṭṭhe ca, ^snp1-9-3-4

Saṅkappassa vasīkatā”. ^snp1-9-3-5

“Kacci adinnaṁ nādiyati, ^snp1-9-4-1

(iti hemavato yakkho) ^snp1-9-4-2

Kacci pāṇesu saññato; ^snp1-9-4-3

Kacci ārā pamādamhā, ^snp1-9-4-4

Kacci jhānaṁ na riñcati”. ^snp1-9-4-5

“Na so adinnaṁ ādiyati, ^snp1-9-5-1

(iti sātāgiro yakkho) ^snp1-9-5-2

Atho pāṇesu saññato; ^snp1-9-5-3

Atho ārā pamādamhā, ^snp1-9-5-4

Buddho jhānaṁ na riñcati”. ^snp1-9-5-5

“Kacci musā na bhaṇati, ^snp1-9-6-1

(iti hemavato yakkho) ^snp1-9-6-2

Kacci na khīṇabyappatho; ^snp1-9-6-3

Kacci vebhūtiyaṁ nāha, ^snp1-9-6-4

Kacci samphaṁ na bhāsati”. ^snp1-9-6-5

“Musā ca so na bhaṇati, ^snp1-9-7-1

(iti sātāgiro yakkho) ^snp1-9-7-2

Atho na khīṇabyappatho; ^snp1-9-7-3

Atho vebhūtiyaṁ nāha, ^snp1-9-7-4

Mantā atthañca bhāsati”. ^snp1-9-7-5

“Kacci na rajjati kāmesu, ^snp1-9-8-1

(iti hemavato yakkho) ^snp1-9-8-2

Kacci cittaṁ anāvilaṁ; ^snp1-9-8-3

Kacci mohaṁ atikkanto, ^snp1-9-8-4

Kacci dhammesu cakkhumā”. ^snp1-9-8-5

“Na so rajjati kāmesu, ^snp1-9-9-1

(iti sātāgiro yakkho) ^snp1-9-9-2

Atho cittaṁ anāvilaṁ; ^snp1-9-9-3

Sabbamohaṁ atikkanto, ^snp1-9-9-4

Buddho dhammesu cakkhumā”. ^snp1-9-9-5

“Kacci vijjāya sampanno, ^snp1-9-10-1

(iti hemavato yakkho) ^snp1-9-10-2

Kacci saṁsuddhacāraṇo; ^snp1-9-10-3

Kaccissa āsavā khīṇā, ^snp1-9-10-4

Kacci natthi punabbhavo”. ^snp1-9-10-5

“Vijjāya ceva sampanno, ^snp1-9-11-1

(iti sātāgiro yakkho) ^snp1-9-11-2

Atho saṁsuddhacāraṇo; ^snp1-9-11-3

Sabbassa āsavā khīṇā, ^snp1-9-11-4

Natthi tassa punabbhavo”. ^snp1-9-11-5

“Sampannaṁ munino cittaṁ, ^snp1-9-12-1

Kammunā byappathena ca; ^snp1-9-12-2

Vijjācaraṇasampannaṁ, ^snp1-9-12-3

Dhammato naṁ pasaṁsati”. ^snp1-9-12-4

“Sampannaṁ munino cittaṁ, ^snp1-9-13-1

Kammunā byappathena ca; ^snp1-9-13-2

Vijjācaraṇasampannaṁ, ^snp1-9-13-3

Dhammato anumodasi. ^snp1-9-13-4

Sampannaṁ munino cittaṁ, ^snp1-9-14-1

Kammunā byappathena ca; ^snp1-9-14-2

Vijjācaraṇasampannaṁ, ^snp1-9-14-3

Handa passāma gotamaṁ”. ^snp1-9-14-4

“Eṇijaṅghaṁ kisaṁ vīraṁ, ^snp1-9-15-1

Appāhāraṁ alolupaṁ; ^snp1-9-15-2

Muniṁ vanasmiṁ jhāyantaṁ, ^snp1-9-15-3

Ehi passāma gotamaṁ. ^snp1-9-15-4

Sīhaṁvekacaraṁ nāgaṁ, ^snp1-9-16-1

Kāmesu anapekkhinaṁ; ^snp1-9-16-2

Upasaṅkamma pucchāma, ^snp1-9-16-3

Maccupāsappamocanaṁ. ^snp1-9-16-4

Akkhātāraṁ pavattāraṁ, ^snp1-9-17-1

Sabbadhammāna pāraguṁ; ^snp1-9-17-2

Buddhaṁ verabhayātītaṁ, ^snp1-9-17-3

Mayaṁ pucchāma gotamaṁ”. ^snp1-9-17-4

“Kismiṁ loko samuppanno, ^snp1-9-18-1

(iti hemavato yakkho) ^snp1-9-18-2

Kismiṁ kubbati santhavaṁ; ^snp1-9-18-3

Kissa loko upādāya, ^snp1-9-18-4

Kismiṁ loko vihaññati”. ^snp1-9-18-5

“Chasu loko samuppanno, ^snp1-9-19-1

(hemavatāti bhagavā) ^snp1-9-19-2

Chasu kubbati santhavaṁ; ^snp1-9-19-3

Channameva upādāya, ^snp1-9-19-4

Chasu loko vihaññati”. ^snp1-9-19-5

“Katamaṁ taṁ upādānaṁ, ^snp1-9-20-1

Yattha loko vihaññati; ^snp1-9-20-2

Niyyānaṁ pucchito brūhi, ^snp1-9-20-3

Kathaṁ dukkhā pamuccati”. ^snp1-9-20-4

“Pañca kāmaguṇā loke, ^snp1-9-21-1

Manochaṭṭhā paveditā; ^snp1-9-21-2

Ettha chandaṁ virājetvā, ^snp1-9-21-3

Evaṁ dukkhā pamuccati. ^snp1-9-21-4

Etaṁ lokassa niyyānaṁ, ^snp1-9-22-1

Akkhātaṁ vo yathātathaṁ; ^snp1-9-22-2

Etaṁ vo ahamakkhāmi, ^snp1-9-22-3

Evaṁ dukkhā pamuccati”. ^snp1-9-22-4

“Ko sūdha tarati oghaṁ, ^snp1-9-23-1

Kodha tarati aṇṇavaṁ; ^snp1-9-23-2

Appatiṭṭhe anālambe, ^snp1-9-23-3

Ko gambhīre na sīdati”. ^snp1-9-23-4

“Sabbadā sīlasampanno, ^snp1-9-24-1

Paññavā susamāhito; ^snp1-9-24-2

Ajjhattacintī satimā, ^snp1-9-24-3

Oghaṁ tarati duttaraṁ. ^snp1-9-24-4

Virato kāmasaññāya, ^snp1-9-25-1

Sabbasaṁyojanātigo; ^snp1-9-25-2

Nandībhavaparikkhīṇo, ^snp1-9-25-3

So gambhīre na sīdati”. ^snp1-9-25-4

“Gambhīrapaññaṁ nipuṇatthadassiṁ, ^snp1-9-26-1

Akiñcanaṁ kāmabhave asattaṁ; ^snp1-9-26-2

Taṁ passatha sabbadhi vippamuttaṁ, ^snp1-9-26-3

Dibbe pathe kamamānaṁ mahesiṁ. ^snp1-9-26-4

Anomanāmaṁ nipuṇatthadassiṁ, ^snp1-9-27-1

Paññādadaṁ kāmālaye asattaṁ; ^snp1-9-27-2

Taṁ passatha sabbaviduṁ sumedhaṁ, ^snp1-9-27-3

Ariye pathe kamamānaṁ mahesiṁ. ^snp1-9-27-4

Sudiṭṭhaṁ vata no ajja, ^snp1-9-28-1

Suppabhātaṁ suhuṭṭhitaṁ; ^snp1-9-28-2

Yaṁ addasāma sambuddhaṁ, ^snp1-9-28-3

Oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṁ. ^snp1-9-28-4

Ime dasasatā yakkhā, ^snp1-9-29-1

Iddhimanto yasassino; ^snp1-9-29-2

Sabbe taṁ saraṇaṁ yanti, ^snp1-9-29-3

Tvaṁ no satthā anuttaro. ^snp1-9-29-4

Te mayaṁ vicarissāma, ^snp1-9-30-1

Gāmā gāmaṁ nagā nagaṁ; ^snp1-9-30-2

Namassamānā sambuddhaṁ, ^snp1-9-30-3

Dhammassa ca sudhammatan”ti. ^snp1-9-30-4

Hemavatasuttaṁ navamaṁ. ^snp1-9-30-5

### Āḷavakasutta (Sutta Nipāta 1.10) ^snp1-10-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp1-10-1-1

ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā āḷaviyaṁ viharati āḷavakassa yakkhassa bhavane. ^snp1-10-1-2

Atha kho āḷavako yakkho yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp1-10-1-3

“nikkhama, samaṇā”ti. ^snp1-10-1-4

“Sādhāvuso”ti bhagavā nikkhami. ^snp1-10-1-5

“Pavisa, samaṇā”ti. ^snp1-10-1-6

“Sādhāvuso”ti bhagavā pāvisi. ^snp1-10-1-7

Dutiyampi kho …pe… ^snp1-10-2-1

tatiyampi kho āḷavako yakkho bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp1-10-2-2

“nikkhama, samaṇā”ti. ^snp1-10-2-3

“Sādhāvuso”ti bhagavā nikkhami. ^snp1-10-2-4

“Pavisa, samaṇā”ti. ^snp1-10-2-5

“Sādhāvuso”ti bhagavā pāvisi. ^snp1-10-2-6

Catutthampi kho āḷavako yakkho bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp1-10-3-1

“nikkhama, samaṇā”ti. ^snp1-10-3-2

“Na khvāhaṁ taṁ, āvuso, nikkhamissāmi. ^snp1-10-3-3

Yaṁ te karaṇīyaṁ, taṁ karohī”ti. ^snp1-10-3-4

“Pañhaṁ taṁ, samaṇa, pucchissāmi. ^snp1-10-4-1

Sace me na byākarissasi, cittaṁ vā te khipissāmi, hadayaṁ vā te phālessāmi, pādesu vā gahetvā pāragaṅgāya khipissāmī”ti. ^snp1-10-4-2

“Na khvāhaṁ taṁ, āvuso, passāmi sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya yo me cittaṁ vā khipeyya hadayaṁ vā phāleyya pādesu vā gahetvā pāragaṅgāya khipeyya. ^snp1-10-5-1

Api ca tvaṁ, āvuso, puccha yadākaṅkhasī”ti. ^snp1-10-5-2

Atha kho āḷavako yakkho bhagavantaṁ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi: ^snp1-10-5-3

“Kiṁ sūdha vittaṁ purisassa seṭṭhaṁ, ^snp1-10-6-1

Kiṁ su suciṇṇaṁ sukhamāvahāti; ^snp1-10-6-2

Kiṁ su have sādutaraṁ rasānaṁ, ^snp1-10-6-3

Kathaṁjīviṁ jīvitamāhu seṭṭhaṁ”. ^snp1-10-6-4

“Saddhīdha vittaṁ purisassa seṭṭhaṁ, ^snp1-10-7-1

Dhammo suciṇṇo sukhamāvahāti; ^snp1-10-7-2

Saccaṁ have sādutaraṁ rasānaṁ, ^snp1-10-7-3

Paññājīviṁ jīvitamāhu seṭṭhaṁ”. ^snp1-10-7-4

“Kathaṁ su tarati oghaṁ, ^snp1-10-8-1

kathaṁ su tarati aṇṇavaṁ; ^snp1-10-8-2

Kathaṁ su dukkhamacceti, ^snp1-10-8-3

kathaṁ su parisujjhati”. ^snp1-10-8-4

“Saddhāya tarati oghaṁ, ^snp1-10-9-1

appamādena aṇṇavaṁ; ^snp1-10-9-2

Vīriyena dukkhamacceti, ^snp1-10-9-3

paññāya parisujjhati”. ^snp1-10-9-4

“Kathaṁ su labhate paññaṁ, ^snp1-10-10-1

kathaṁ su vindate dhanaṁ; ^snp1-10-10-2

Kathaṁ su kittiṁ pappoti, ^snp1-10-10-3

kathaṁ mittāni ganthati; ^snp1-10-10-4

Asmā lokā paraṁ lokaṁ, ^snp1-10-10-5

kathaṁ pecca na socati”. ^snp1-10-10-6

“Saddahāno arahataṁ, ^snp1-10-11-1

dhammaṁ nibbānapattiyā; ^snp1-10-11-2

Sussūsaṁ labhate paññaṁ, ^snp1-10-11-3

appamatto vicakkhaṇo. ^snp1-10-11-4

Patirūpakārī dhuravā, ^snp1-10-12-1

uṭṭhātā vindate dhanaṁ; ^snp1-10-12-2

Saccena kittiṁ pappoti, ^snp1-10-12-3

dadaṁ mittāni ganthati. ^snp1-10-12-4

Yassete caturo dhammā, ^snp1-10-13-1

saddhassa gharamesino; ^snp1-10-13-2

Saccaṁ dhammo dhiti cāgo, ^snp1-10-13-3

sa ve pecca na socati. ^snp1-10-13-4

Iṅgha aññepi pucchassu, ^snp1-10-14-1

puthū samaṇabrāhmaṇe; ^snp1-10-14-2

Yadi saccā damā cāgā, ^snp1-10-14-3

khantyā bhiyyodha vijjati”. ^snp1-10-14-4

“Kathaṁ nu dāni puccheyyaṁ, ^snp1-10-15-1

Puthū samaṇabrāhmaṇe; ^snp1-10-15-2

Yohaṁ ajja pajānāmi, ^snp1-10-15-3

Yo attho samparāyiko. ^snp1-10-15-4

Atthāya vata me buddho, ^snp1-10-16-1

Vāsāyāḷavimāgamā; ^snp1-10-16-2

Yohaṁ ajja pajānāmi, ^snp1-10-16-3

Yattha dinnaṁ mahapphalaṁ. ^snp1-10-16-4

So ahaṁ vicarissāmi, ^snp1-10-17-1

Gāmā gāmaṁ purā puraṁ; ^snp1-10-17-2

Namassamāno sambuddhaṁ, ^snp1-10-17-3

Dhammassa ca sudhammatan”ti. ^snp1-10-17-4

Āḷavakasuttaṁ dasamaṁ. ^snp1-10-17-5

### Vijayasutta (Sutta Nipāta 1.11) ^snp1-11-0

Caraṁ vā yadi vā tiṭṭhaṁ, ^snp1-11-1-1

nisinno uda vā sayaṁ; ^snp1-11-1-2

Samiñjeti pasāreti, ^snp1-11-1-3

esā kāyassa iñjanā. ^snp1-11-1-4

Aṭṭhinahārusaṁyutto, ^snp1-11-2-1

tacamaṁsāvalepano; ^snp1-11-2-2

Chaviyā kāyo paṭicchanno, ^snp1-11-2-3

yathābhūtaṁ na dissati. ^snp1-11-2-4

Antapūro udarapūro, ^snp1-11-3-1

yakanapeḷassa vatthino; ^snp1-11-3-2

Hadayassa papphāsassa, ^snp1-11-3-3

vakkassa pihakassa ca. ^snp1-11-3-4

Siṅghāṇikāya kheḷassa, ^snp1-11-4-1

sedassa ca medassa ca; ^snp1-11-4-2

Lohitassa lasikāya, ^snp1-11-4-3

pittassa ca vasāya ca. ^snp1-11-4-4

Athassa navahi sotehi, ^snp1-11-5-1

asucī savati sabbadā; ^snp1-11-5-2

Akkhimhā akkhigūthako, ^snp1-11-5-3

kaṇṇamhā kaṇṇagūthako. ^snp1-11-5-4

Siṅghāṇikā ca nāsato, ^snp1-11-6-1

mukhena vamatekadā; ^snp1-11-6-2

Pittaṁ semhañca vamati, ^snp1-11-6-3

kāyamhā sedajallikā. ^snp1-11-6-4

Athassa susiraṁ sīsaṁ, ^snp1-11-7-1

matthaluṅgassa pūritaṁ; ^snp1-11-7-2

Subhato naṁ maññati bālo, ^snp1-11-7-3

avijjāya purakkhato. ^snp1-11-7-4

Yadā ca so mato seti, ^snp1-11-8-1

Uddhumāto vinīlako; ^snp1-11-8-2

Apaviddho susānasmiṁ, ^snp1-11-8-3

Anapekkhā honti ñātayo. ^snp1-11-8-4

Khādanti naṁ suvānā ca, ^snp1-11-9-1

siṅgālā ca vakā kimī; ^snp1-11-9-2

Kākā gijjhā ca khādanti, ^snp1-11-9-3

ye caññe santi pāṇino. ^snp1-11-9-4

Sutvāna buddhavacanaṁ, ^snp1-11-10-1

Bhikkhu paññāṇavā idha; ^snp1-11-10-2

So kho naṁ parijānāti, ^snp1-11-10-3

Yathābhūtañhi passati. ^snp1-11-10-4

Yathā idaṁ tathā etaṁ, ^snp1-11-11-1

Yathā etaṁ tathā idaṁ; ^snp1-11-11-2

Ajjhattañca bahiddhā ca, ^snp1-11-11-3

Kāye chandaṁ virājaye. ^snp1-11-11-4

Chandarāgaviratto so, ^snp1-11-12-1

Bhikkhu paññāṇavā idha; ^snp1-11-12-2

Ajjhagā amataṁ santiṁ, ^snp1-11-12-3

Nibbānaṁ padamaccutaṁ. ^snp1-11-12-4

Dvipādakoyaṁ asuci, ^snp1-11-13-1

Duggandho parihīrati; ^snp1-11-13-2

Nānākuṇapaparipūro, ^snp1-11-13-3

Vissavanto tato tato. ^snp1-11-13-4

Etādisena kāyena, ^snp1-11-14-1

Yo maññe uṇṇametave; ^snp1-11-14-2

Paraṁ vā avajāneyya, ^snp1-11-14-3

Kimaññatra adassanāti. ^snp1-11-14-4

Vijayasuttaṁ ekādasamaṁ. ^snp1-11-14-5

### Munisutta (Sutta Nipāta 1.12) ^snp1-12-0

Santhavāto bhayaṁ jātaṁ, ^snp1-12-1-1

niketā jāyate rajo; ^snp1-12-1-2

Aniketamasanthavaṁ, ^snp1-12-1-3

etaṁ ve munidassanaṁ. ^snp1-12-1-4

Yo jātamucchijja na ropayeyya, ^snp1-12-2-1

Jāyantamassa nānuppavecche; ^snp1-12-2-2

Tamāhu ekaṁ muninaṁ carantaṁ, ^snp1-12-2-3

Addakkhi so santipadaṁ mahesi. ^snp1-12-2-4

Saṅkhāya vatthūni pamāya bījaṁ, ^snp1-12-3-1

Sinehamassa nānuppavecche; ^snp1-12-3-2

Sa ve munī jātikhayantadassī, ^snp1-12-3-3

Takkaṁ pahāya na upeti saṅkhaṁ. ^snp1-12-3-4

Aññāya sabbāni nivesanāni, ^snp1-12-4-1

Anikāmayaṁ aññatarampi tesaṁ; ^snp1-12-4-2

Sa ve munī vītagedho agiddho, ^snp1-12-4-3

Nāyūhatī pāragato hi hoti. ^snp1-12-4-4

Sabbābhibhuṁ sabbaviduṁ sumedhaṁ, ^snp1-12-5-1

Sabbesu dhammesu anūpalittaṁ; ^snp1-12-5-2

Sabbañjahaṁ taṇhakkhaye vimuttaṁ, ^snp1-12-5-3

Taṁ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti. ^snp1-12-5-4

Paññābalaṁ sīlavatūpapannaṁ, ^snp1-12-6-1

Samāhitaṁ jhānarataṁ satīmaṁ; ^snp1-12-6-2

Saṅgā pamuttaṁ akhilaṁ anāsavaṁ, ^snp1-12-6-3

Taṁ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti. ^snp1-12-6-4

Ekaṁ carantaṁ munimappamattaṁ, ^snp1-12-7-1

Nindāpasaṁsāsu avedhamānaṁ; ^snp1-12-7-2

Sīhaṁva saddesu asantasantaṁ, ^snp1-12-7-3

Vātaṁva jālamhi asajjamānaṁ; ^snp1-12-7-4

Padmaṁva toyena alippamānaṁ, ^snp1-12-7-5

Netāramaññesamanaññaneyyaṁ; ^snp1-12-7-6

Taṁ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti. ^snp1-12-7-7

Yo ogahaṇe thambhorivābhijāyati, ^snp1-12-8-1

Yasmiṁ pare vācāpariyantaṁ vadanti; ^snp1-12-8-2

Taṁ vītarāgaṁ susamāhitindriyaṁ, ^snp1-12-8-3

Taṁ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti. ^snp1-12-8-4

Yo ve ṭhitatto tasaraṁva ujju, ^snp1-12-9-1

Jigucchati kammehi pāpakehi; ^snp1-12-9-2

Vīmaṁsamāno visamaṁ samañca, ^snp1-12-9-3

Taṁ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti. ^snp1-12-9-4

Yo saññatatto na karoti pāpaṁ, ^snp1-12-10-1

Daharo majjhimo ca muni yatatto; ^snp1-12-10-2

Arosaneyyo na so roseti kañci, ^snp1-12-10-3

Taṁ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti. ^snp1-12-10-4

Yadaggato majjhato sesato vā, ^snp1-12-11-1

Piṇḍaṁ labhetha paradattūpajīvī; ^snp1-12-11-2

Nālaṁ thutuṁ nopi nipaccavādī, ^snp1-12-11-3

Taṁ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti. ^snp1-12-11-4

Muniṁ carantaṁ virataṁ methunasmā, ^snp1-12-12-1

Yo yobbane nopanibajjhate kvaci; ^snp1-12-12-2

Madappamādā virataṁ vippamuttaṁ, ^snp1-12-12-3

Taṁ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti. ^snp1-12-12-4

Aññāya lokaṁ paramatthadassiṁ, ^snp1-12-13-1

Oghaṁ samuddaṁ atitariya tādiṁ; ^snp1-12-13-2

Taṁ chinnaganthaṁ asitaṁ anāsavaṁ, ^snp1-12-13-3

Taṁ vāpi dhīrā muni vedayanti. ^snp1-12-13-4

Asamā ubho dūravihāravuttino, ^snp1-12-14-1

Gihī dāraposī amamo ca subbato; ^snp1-12-14-2

Parapāṇarodhāya gihī asaññato, ^snp1-12-14-3

Niccaṁ munī rakkhati pāṇine yato. ^snp1-12-14-4

Sikhī yathā nīlagīvo vihaṅgamo, ^snp1-12-15-1

Haṁsassa nopeti javaṁ kudācanaṁ; ^snp1-12-15-2

Evaṁ gihī nānukaroti bhikkhuno, ^snp1-12-15-3

Munino vivittassa vanamhi jhāyatoti. ^snp1-12-15-4

Munisuttaṁ dvādasamaṁ. ^snp1-12-15-5

Uragavaggo paṭhamo. ^snp1-12-15-6

Tassuddānaṁ ^snp1-12-16-0

Urago dhaniyo ceva, ^snp1-12-16-1

visāṇañca tathā kasi; ^snp1-12-16-2

Cundo parābhavo ceva, ^snp1-12-16-3

vasalo mettabhāvanā. ^snp1-12-16-4

Sātāgiro āḷavako, ^snp1-12-17-1

Vijayo ca tathā muni; ^snp1-12-17-2

Dvādasetāni suttāni, ^snp1-12-17-3

Uragavaggoti vuccatīti. ^snp1-12-17-4

## Vagga 2 ^vagga2-0

### Ratanasutta (Sutta Nipāta 2.1) ^snp2-1-0

Yānīdha bhūtāni samāgatāni, ^snp2-1-1-1

Bhummāni vā yāni va antalikkhe; ^snp2-1-1-2

Sabbeva bhūtā sumanā bhavantu, ^snp2-1-1-3

Athopi sakkacca suṇantu bhāsitaṁ. ^snp2-1-1-4

Tasmā hi bhūtā nisāmetha sabbe, ^snp2-1-2-1

Mettaṁ karotha mānusiyā pajāya; ^snp2-1-2-2

Divā ca ratto ca haranti ye baliṁ, ^snp2-1-2-3

Tasmā hi ne rakkhatha appamattā. ^snp2-1-2-4

Yaṁ kiñci vittaṁ idha vā huraṁ vā, ^snp2-1-3-1

Saggesu vā yaṁ ratanaṁ paṇītaṁ; ^snp2-1-3-2

Na no samaṁ atthi tathāgatena, ^snp2-1-3-3

Idampi buddhe ratanaṁ paṇītaṁ; ^snp2-1-3-4

Etena saccena suvatthi hotu. ^snp2-1-3-5

Khayaṁ virāgaṁ amataṁ paṇītaṁ, ^snp2-1-4-1

Yadajjhagā sakyamunī samāhito; ^snp2-1-4-2

Na tena dhammena samatthi kiñci, ^snp2-1-4-3

Idampi dhamme ratanaṁ paṇītaṁ; ^snp2-1-4-4

Etena saccena suvatthi hotu. ^snp2-1-4-5

Yaṁ buddhaseṭṭho parivaṇṇayī suciṁ, ^snp2-1-5-1

Samādhimānantarikaññamāhu; ^snp2-1-5-2

Samādhinā tena samo na vijjati, ^snp2-1-5-3

Idampi dhamme ratanaṁ paṇītaṁ; ^snp2-1-5-4

Etena saccena suvatthi hotu. ^snp2-1-5-5

Ye puggalā aṭṭha sataṁ pasatthā, ^snp2-1-6-1

Cattāri etāni yugāni honti; ^snp2-1-6-2

Te dakkhiṇeyyā sugatassa sāvakā, ^snp2-1-6-3

Etesu dinnāni mahapphalāni; ^snp2-1-6-4

Idampi saṅghe ratanaṁ paṇītaṁ, ^snp2-1-6-5

Etena saccena suvatthi hotu. ^snp2-1-6-6

Ye suppayuttā manasā daḷhena, ^snp2-1-7-1

Nikkāmino gotamasāsanamhi; ^snp2-1-7-2

Te pattipattā amataṁ vigayha, ^snp2-1-7-3

Laddhā mudhā nibbutiṁ bhuñjamānā; ^snp2-1-7-4

Idampi saṅghe ratanaṁ paṇītaṁ, ^snp2-1-7-5

Etena saccena suvatthi hotu. ^snp2-1-7-6

Yathindakhīlo pathavissito siyā, ^snp2-1-8-1

Catubbhi vātehi asampakampiyo; ^snp2-1-8-2

Tathūpamaṁ sappurisaṁ vadāmi, ^snp2-1-8-3

Yo ariyasaccāni avecca passati; ^snp2-1-8-4

Idampi saṅghe ratanaṁ paṇītaṁ, ^snp2-1-8-5

Etena saccena suvatthi hotu. ^snp2-1-8-6

Ye ariyasaccāni vibhāvayanti, ^snp2-1-9-1

Gambhīrapaññena sudesitāni; ^snp2-1-9-2

Kiñcāpi te honti bhusaṁ pamattā, ^snp2-1-9-3

Na te bhavaṁ aṭṭhamamādiyanti; ^snp2-1-9-4

Idampi saṅghe ratanaṁ paṇītaṁ, ^snp2-1-9-5

Etena saccena suvatthi hotu. ^snp2-1-9-6

Sahāvassa dassanasampadāya, ^snp2-1-10-1

Tayassu dhammā jahitā bhavanti; ^snp2-1-10-2

Sakkāyadiṭṭhī vicikicchitañca, ^snp2-1-10-3

Sīlabbataṁ vāpi yadatthi kiñci. ^snp2-1-10-4

Catūhapāyehi ca vippamutto, ^snp2-1-11-1

Chaccābhiṭhānāni abhabba kātuṁ; ^snp2-1-11-2

Idampi saṅghe ratanaṁ paṇītaṁ, ^snp2-1-11-3

Etena saccena suvatthi hotu. ^snp2-1-11-4

Kiñcāpi so kamma karoti pāpakaṁ, ^snp2-1-12-1

Kāyena vācā uda cetasā vā; ^snp2-1-12-2

Abhabba so tassa paṭicchadāya, ^snp2-1-12-3

Abhabbatā diṭṭhapadassa vuttā; ^snp2-1-12-4

Idampi saṅghe ratanaṁ paṇītaṁ, ^snp2-1-12-5

Etena saccena suvatthi hotu. ^snp2-1-12-6

Vanappagumbe yatha phussitagge, ^snp2-1-13-1

Gimhānamāse paṭhamasmiṁ gimhe; ^snp2-1-13-2

Tathūpamaṁ dhammavaraṁ adesayi, ^snp2-1-13-3

Nibbānagāmiṁ paramaṁ hitāya; ^snp2-1-13-4

Idampi buddhe ratanaṁ paṇītaṁ, ^snp2-1-13-5

Etena saccena suvatthi hotu. ^snp2-1-13-6

Varo varaññū varado varāharo, ^snp2-1-14-1

Anuttaro dhammavaraṁ adesayi; ^snp2-1-14-2

Idampi buddhe ratanaṁ paṇītaṁ, ^snp2-1-14-3

Etena saccena suvatthi hotu. ^snp2-1-14-4

Khīṇaṁ purāṇaṁ nava natthi sambhavaṁ, ^snp2-1-15-1

Virattacittāyatike bhavasmiṁ; ^snp2-1-15-2

Te khīṇabījā avirūḷhichandā, ^snp2-1-15-3

Nibbanti dhīrā yathāyaṁ padīpo; ^snp2-1-15-4

Idampi saṅghe ratanaṁ paṇītaṁ, ^snp2-1-15-5

Etena saccena suvatthi hotu. ^snp2-1-15-6

Yānīdha bhūtāni samāgatāni, ^snp2-1-16-1

Bhummāni vā yāni va antalikkhe; ^snp2-1-16-2

Tathāgataṁ devamanussapūjitaṁ, ^snp2-1-16-3

Buddhaṁ namassāma suvatthi hotu. ^snp2-1-16-4

Yānīdha bhūtāni samāgatāni, ^snp2-1-17-1

Bhummāni vā yāni va antalikkhe; ^snp2-1-17-2

Tathāgataṁ devamanussapūjitaṁ, ^snp2-1-17-3

Dhammaṁ namassāma suvatthi hotu. ^snp2-1-17-4

Yānīdha bhūtāni samāgatāni, ^snp2-1-18-1

Bhummāni vā yāni va antalikkhe; ^snp2-1-18-2

Tathāgataṁ devamanussapūjitaṁ, ^snp2-1-18-3

Saṅghaṁ namassāma suvatthi hotūti. ^snp2-1-18-4

Ratanasuttaṁ paṭhamaṁ. ^snp2-1-18-5

### Āmagandhasutta (Sutta Nipāta 2.2) ^snp2-2-0

“Sāmākaciṅgūlakacīnakāni ca, ^snp2-2-1-1

Pattapphalaṁ mūlaphalaṁ gavipphalaṁ; ^snp2-2-1-2

Dhammena laddhaṁ satamasnamānā, ^snp2-2-1-3

Na kāmakāmā alikaṁ bhaṇanti. ^snp2-2-1-4

Yadasnamāno sukataṁ suniṭṭhitaṁ, ^snp2-2-2-1

Parehi dinnaṁ payataṁ paṇītaṁ; ^snp2-2-2-2

Sālīnamannaṁ paribhuñjamāno, ^snp2-2-2-3

So bhuñjasī kassapa āmagandhaṁ. ^snp2-2-2-4

Na āmagandho mama kappatīti, ^snp2-2-3-1

Icceva tvaṁ bhāsasi brahmabandhu; ^snp2-2-3-2

Sālīnamannaṁ paribhuñjamāno, ^snp2-2-3-3

Sakuntamaṁsehi susaṅkhatehi; ^snp2-2-3-4

Pucchāmi taṁ kassapa etamatthaṁ, ^snp2-2-3-5

Kathaṁpakāro tava āmagandho”. ^snp2-2-3-6

“Pāṇātipāto vadhachedabandhanaṁ, ^snp2-2-4-1

Theyyaṁ musāvādo nikativañcanāni ca; ^snp2-2-4-2

Ajjhenakuttaṁ paradārasevanā, ^snp2-2-4-3

Esāmagandho na hi maṁsabhojanaṁ. ^snp2-2-4-4

Ye idha kāmesu asaññatā janā, ^snp2-2-5-1

Rasesu giddhā asucibhāvamassitā; ^snp2-2-5-2

Natthikadiṭṭhī visamā durannayā, ^snp2-2-5-3

Esāmagandho na hi maṁsabhojanaṁ. ^snp2-2-5-4

Ye lūkhasā dāruṇā piṭṭhimaṁsikā, ^snp2-2-6-1

Mittadduno nikkaruṇātimānino; ^snp2-2-6-2

Adānasīlā na ca denti kassaci, ^snp2-2-6-3

Esāmagandho na hi maṁsabhojanaṁ. ^snp2-2-6-4

Kodho mado thambho paccupaṭṭhāpanā, ^snp2-2-7-1

Māyā usūyā bhassasamussayo ca; ^snp2-2-7-2

Mānātimāno ca asabbhi santhavo, ^snp2-2-7-3

Esāmagandho na hi maṁsabhojanaṁ. ^snp2-2-7-4

Ye pāpasīlā iṇaghātasūcakā, ^snp2-2-8-1

Vohārakūṭā idha pāṭirūpikā; ^snp2-2-8-2

Narādhamā yedha karonti kibbisaṁ, ^snp2-2-8-3

Esāmagandho na hi maṁsabhojanaṁ. ^snp2-2-8-4

Ye idha pāṇesu asaññatā janā, ^snp2-2-9-1

Paresamādāya vihesamuyyutā; ^snp2-2-9-2

Dussīlaluddā pharusā anādarā, ^snp2-2-9-3

Esāmagandho na hi maṁsabhojanaṁ. ^snp2-2-9-4

Etesu giddhā viruddhātipātino, ^snp2-2-10-1

Niccuyyutā pecca tamaṁ vajanti ye; ^snp2-2-10-2

Patanti sattā nirayaṁ avaṁsirā, ^snp2-2-10-3

Esāmagandho na hi maṁsabhojanaṁ. ^snp2-2-10-4

Na macchamaṁsānamanāsakattaṁ, ^snp2-2-11-1

Na naggiyaṁ na muṇḍiyaṁ jaṭājallaṁ; ^snp2-2-11-2

Kharājināni nāggihuttassupasevanā, ^snp2-2-11-3

Ye vāpi loke amarā bahū tapā; ^snp2-2-11-4

Mantāhutī yaññamutūpasevanā, ^snp2-2-11-5

Sodhenti maccaṁ avitiṇṇakaṅkhaṁ. ^snp2-2-11-6

Sotesu gutto viditindriyo care, ^snp2-2-12-1

Dhamme ṭhito ajjavamaddave rato; ^snp2-2-12-2

Saṅgātigo sabbadukkhappahīno, ^snp2-2-12-3

Na lippati diṭṭhasutesu dhīro”. ^snp2-2-12-4

Iccetamatthaṁ bhagavā punappunaṁ, ^snp2-2-13-1

Akkhāsi naṁ vedayi mantapāragū; ^snp2-2-13-2

Citrāhi gāthāhi munī pakāsayi, ^snp2-2-13-3

Nirāmagandho asito durannayo. ^snp2-2-13-4

Sutvāna buddhassa subhāsitaṁ padaṁ, ^snp2-2-14-1

Nirāmagandhaṁ sabbadukkhappanūdanaṁ; ^snp2-2-14-2

Nīcamano vandi tathāgatassa, ^snp2-2-14-3

Tattheva pabbajjamarocayitthāti. ^snp2-2-14-4

Āmagandhasuttaṁ dutiyaṁ. ^snp2-2-14-5

### Hirisutta (Sutta Nipāta 2.3) ^snp2-3-0

Hiriṁ tarantaṁ vijigucchamānaṁ, ^snp2-3-1-1

Tavāhamasmi iti bhāsamānaṁ; ^snp2-3-1-2

Sayhāni kammāni anādiyantaṁ, ^snp2-3-1-3

Neso mamanti iti naṁ vijaññā. ^snp2-3-1-4

Ananvayaṁ piyaṁ vācaṁ, ^snp2-3-2-1

yo mittesu pakubbati; ^snp2-3-2-2

Akarontaṁ bhāsamānaṁ, ^snp2-3-2-3

parijānanti paṇḍitā. ^snp2-3-2-4

Na so mitto yo sadā appamatto, ^snp2-3-3-1

Bhedāsaṅkī randhamevānupassī; ^snp2-3-3-2

Yasmiñca seti urasīva putto, ^snp2-3-3-3

Sa ve mitto yo parehi abhejjo. ^snp2-3-3-4

Pāmujjakaraṇaṁ ṭhānaṁ, ^snp2-3-4-1

pasaṁsāvahanaṁ sukhaṁ; ^snp2-3-4-2

Phalānisaṁso bhāveti, ^snp2-3-4-3

vahanto porisaṁ dhuraṁ. ^snp2-3-4-4

Pavivekarasaṁ pitvā, ^snp2-3-5-1

Rasaṁ upasamassa ca; ^snp2-3-5-2

Niddaro hoti nippāpo, ^snp2-3-5-3

Dhammapītirasaṁ pivanti. ^snp2-3-5-4

Hirisuttaṁ tatiyaṁ. ^snp2-3-5-5

### Maṅgalasutta (Sutta Nipāta 2.4) ^snp2-4-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp2-4-1-1

ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. ^snp2-4-1-2

Atha kho aññatarā devatā abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṁ jetavanaṁ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ aṭṭhāsi. ^snp2-4-1-3

Ekamantaṁ ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavantaṁ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi: ^snp2-4-1-4

“Bahū devā manussā ca, ^snp2-4-2-1

maṅgalāni acintayuṁ; ^snp2-4-2-2

Ākaṅkhamānā sotthānaṁ, ^snp2-4-2-3

brūhi maṅgalamuttamaṁ”. ^snp2-4-2-4

“Asevanā ca bālānaṁ, ^snp2-4-3-1

paṇḍitānañca sevanā; ^snp2-4-3-2

Pūjā ca pūjaneyyānaṁ, ^snp2-4-3-3

etaṁ maṅgalamuttamaṁ. ^snp2-4-3-4

Patirūpadesavāso ca, ^snp2-4-4-1

pubbe ca katapuññatā; ^snp2-4-4-2

Attasammāpaṇidhi ca, ^snp2-4-4-3

etaṁ maṅgalamuttamaṁ. ^snp2-4-4-4

Bāhusaccañca sippañca, ^snp2-4-5-1

vinayo ca susikkhito; ^snp2-4-5-2

Subhāsitā ca yā vācā, ^snp2-4-5-3

etaṁ maṅgalamuttamaṁ. ^snp2-4-5-4

Mātāpitu upaṭṭhānaṁ, ^snp2-4-6-1

puttadārassa saṅgaho; ^snp2-4-6-2

Anākulā ca kammantā, ^snp2-4-6-3

etaṁ maṅgalamuttamaṁ. ^snp2-4-6-4

Dānañca dhammacariyā ca, ^snp2-4-7-1

ñātakānañca saṅgaho; ^snp2-4-7-2

Anavajjāni kammāni, ^snp2-4-7-3

etaṁ maṅgalamuttamaṁ. ^snp2-4-7-4

Āratī viratī pāpā, ^snp2-4-8-1

majjapānā ca saṁyamo; ^snp2-4-8-2

Appamādo ca dhammesu, ^snp2-4-8-3

etaṁ maṅgalamuttamaṁ. ^snp2-4-8-4

Gāravo ca nivāto ca, ^snp2-4-9-1

santuṭṭhi ca kataññutā; ^snp2-4-9-2

Kālena dhammassavanaṁ, ^snp2-4-9-3

etaṁ maṅgalamuttamaṁ. ^snp2-4-9-4

Khantī ca sovacassatā, ^snp2-4-10-1

samaṇānañca dassanaṁ; ^snp2-4-10-2

Kālena dhammasākacchā, ^snp2-4-10-3

etaṁ maṅgalamuttamaṁ. ^snp2-4-10-4

Tapo ca brahmacariyañca, ^snp2-4-11-1

Ariyasaccāna dassanaṁ; ^snp2-4-11-2

Nibbānasacchikiriyā ca, ^snp2-4-11-3

Etaṁ maṅgalamuttamaṁ. ^snp2-4-11-4

Phuṭṭhassa lokadhammehi, ^snp2-4-12-1

Cittaṁ yassa na kampati; ^snp2-4-12-2

Asokaṁ virajaṁ khemaṁ, ^snp2-4-12-3

Etaṁ maṅgalamuttamaṁ. ^snp2-4-12-4

Etādisāni katvāna, ^snp2-4-13-1

Sabbattha maparājitā; ^snp2-4-13-2

Sabbattha sotthiṁ gacchanti, ^snp2-4-13-3

Taṁ tesaṁ maṅgalamuttaman”ti. ^snp2-4-13-4

Maṅgalasuttaṁ catutthaṁ. ^snp2-4-13-5

### Sūcilomasutta (Sutta Nipāta 2.5) ^snp2-5-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp2-5-1-1

ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā gayāyaṁ viharati ṭaṅkitamañce sūcilomassa yakkhassa bhavane. ^snp2-5-1-2

Tena kho pana samayena kharo ca yakkho sūcilomo ca yakkho bhagavato avidūre atikkamanti. ^snp2-5-1-3

Atha kho kharo yakkho sūcilomaṁ yakkhaṁ etadavoca: ^snp2-5-1-4

“eso samaṇo”ti. ^snp2-5-1-5

“Neso samaṇo, samaṇako eso. ^snp2-5-1-6

Yāvāhaṁ jānāmi yadi vā so samaṇo, yadi vā so samaṇako”ti. ^snp2-5-1-7

Atha kho sūcilomo yakkho yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavato kāyaṁ upanāmesi. ^snp2-5-2-1

Atha kho bhagavā kāyaṁ apanāmesi. ^snp2-5-2-2

Atha kho sūcilomo yakkho bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp2-5-2-3

“bhāyasi maṁ, samaṇā”ti? ^snp2-5-2-4

“Na khvāhaṁ taṁ, āvuso, bhāyāmi; ^snp2-5-2-5

api ca te samphasso pāpako”ti. ^snp2-5-2-6

“Pañhaṁ taṁ, samaṇa, pucchissāmi. ^snp2-5-3-1

Sace me na byākarissasi, cittaṁ vā te khipissāmi, hadayaṁ vā te phālessāmi, pādesu vā gahetvā pāragaṅgāya khipissāmī”ti. ^snp2-5-3-2

“Na khvāhaṁ taṁ, āvuso, passāmi sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya yo me cittaṁ vā khipeyya hadayaṁ vā phāleyya pādesu vā gahetvā pāragaṅgāya khipeyya. ^snp2-5-4-1

Api ca tvaṁ, āvuso, puccha yadākaṅkhasī”ti. ^snp2-5-4-2

Atha kho sūcilomo yakkho bhagavantaṁ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi: ^snp2-5-4-3

“Rāgo ca doso ca kutonidānā, ^snp2-5-5-1

Aratī ratī lomahaṁso kutojā; ^snp2-5-5-2

Kuto samuṭṭhāya manovitakkā, ^snp2-5-5-3

Kumārakā dhaṅkamivossajanti”. ^snp2-5-5-4

“Rāgo ca doso ca itonidānā, ^snp2-5-6-1

Aratī ratī lomahaṁso itojā; ^snp2-5-6-2

Ito samuṭṭhāya manovitakkā, ^snp2-5-6-3

Kumārakā dhaṅkamivossajanti. ^snp2-5-6-4

Snehajā attasambhūtā, ^snp2-5-7-1

Nigrodhasseva khandhajā; ^snp2-5-7-2

Puthū visattā kāmesu, ^snp2-5-7-3

Māluvāva vitatāvane. ^snp2-5-7-4

Ye naṁ pajānanti yatonidānaṁ, ^snp2-5-8-1

Te naṁ vinodenti suṇohi yakkha; ^snp2-5-8-2

Te duttaraṁ oghamimaṁ taranti, ^snp2-5-8-3

Atiṇṇapubbaṁ apunabbhavāyā”ti. ^snp2-5-8-4

Sūcilomasuttaṁ pañcamaṁ. ^snp2-5-8-5

### Kapilasutta (dhammacariyasutta) (Sutta Nipāta 2.6) ^snp2-6-0

Dhammacariyaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, ^snp2-6-1-1

Etadāhu vasuttamaṁ; ^snp2-6-1-2

Pabbajitopi ce hoti, ^snp2-6-1-3

Agārā anagāriyaṁ. ^snp2-6-1-4

So ce mukharajātiko, ^snp2-6-2-1

vihesābhirato mago; ^snp2-6-2-2

Jīvitaṁ tassa pāpiyo, ^snp2-6-2-3

rajaṁ vaḍḍheti attano. ^snp2-6-2-4

Kalahābhirato bhikkhu, ^snp2-6-3-1

Mohadhammena āvuto; ^snp2-6-3-2

Akkhātampi na jānāti, ^snp2-6-3-3

Dhammaṁ buddhena desitaṁ. ^snp2-6-3-4

Vihesaṁ bhāvitattānaṁ, ^snp2-6-4-1

avijjāya purakkhato; ^snp2-6-4-2

Saṅkilesaṁ na jānāti, ^snp2-6-4-3

maggaṁ nirayagāminaṁ. ^snp2-6-4-4

Vinipātaṁ samāpanno, ^snp2-6-5-1

gabbhā gabbhaṁ tamā tamaṁ; ^snp2-6-5-2

Sa ve tādisako bhikkhu, ^snp2-6-5-3

pecca dukkhaṁ nigacchati. ^snp2-6-5-4

Gūthakūpo yathā assa, ^snp2-6-6-1

sampuṇṇo gaṇavassiko; ^snp2-6-6-2

Yo ca evarūpo assa, ^snp2-6-6-3

dubbisodho hi sāṅgaṇo. ^snp2-6-6-4

Yaṁ evarūpaṁ jānātha, ^snp2-6-7-1

bhikkhavo gehanissitaṁ; ^snp2-6-7-2

Pāpicchaṁ pāpasaṅkappaṁ, ^snp2-6-7-3

pāpaācāragocaraṁ. ^snp2-6-7-4

Sabbe samaggā hutvāna, ^snp2-6-8-1

abhinibbajjiyātha naṁ; ^snp2-6-8-2

Kāraṇḍavaṁ niddhamatha, ^snp2-6-8-3

kasambuṁ apakassatha. ^snp2-6-8-4

Tato palāpe vāhetha, ^snp2-6-9-1

Assamaṇe samaṇamānine; ^snp2-6-9-2

Niddhamitvāna pāpicche, ^snp2-6-9-3

Pāpaācāragocare. ^snp2-6-9-4

Suddhā suddhehi saṁvāsaṁ, ^snp2-6-10-1

Kappayavho patissatā; ^snp2-6-10-2

Tato samaggā nipakā, ^snp2-6-10-3

Dukkhassantaṁ karissathāti. ^snp2-6-10-4

Dhammacariyasuttaṁ chaṭṭhaṁ. ^snp2-6-10-5

### Brāhmaṇadhammikasutta (Sutta Nipāta 2.7) ^snp2-7-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp2-7-1-1

ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. ^snp2-7-1-2

Atha kho sambahulā kosalakā brāhmaṇamahāsālā jiṇṇā vuḍḍhā mahallakā addhagatā vayoanuppattā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṁsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṁ sammodiṁsu. ^snp2-7-1-3

Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdiṁsu. Ekamantaṁ nisinnā kho te brāhmaṇamahāsālā bhagavantaṁ etadavocuṁ: ^snp2-7-1-4

“sandissanti nu kho, bho gotama, etarahi brāhmaṇā porāṇānaṁ brāhmaṇānaṁ brāhmaṇadhamme”ti? ^snp2-7-1-5

“Na kho, brāhmaṇā, sandissanti etarahi brāhmaṇā porāṇānaṁ brāhmaṇānaṁ brāhmaṇadhamme”ti. ^snp2-7-1-6

“Sādhu no bhavaṁ gotamo porāṇānaṁ brāhmaṇānaṁ brāhmaṇadhammaṁ bhāsatu, sace bhoto gotamassa agarū”ti. ^snp2-7-1-7

“Tena hi, brāhmaṇā, suṇātha, sādhukaṁ manasi karotha, bhāsissāmī”ti. ^snp2-7-1-8

“Evaṁ, bho”ti kho te brāhmaṇamahāsālā bhagavato paccassosuṁ. ^snp2-7-1-9

Bhagavā etadavoca: ^snp2-7-1-10

“Isayo pubbakā āsuṁ, ^snp2-7-2-1

saññatattā tapassino; ^snp2-7-2-2

Pañca kāmaguṇe hitvā, ^snp2-7-2-3

attadatthamacārisuṁ. ^snp2-7-2-4

Na pasū brāhmaṇānāsuṁ, ^snp2-7-3-1

na hiraññaṁ na dhāniyaṁ; ^snp2-7-3-2

Sajjhāyadhanadhaññāsuṁ, ^snp2-7-3-3

brahmaṁ nidhimapālayuṁ. ^snp2-7-3-4

Yaṁ nesaṁ pakataṁ āsi, ^snp2-7-4-1

dvārabhattaṁ upaṭṭhitaṁ; ^snp2-7-4-2

Saddhāpakatamesānaṁ, ^snp2-7-4-3

dātave tadamaññisuṁ. ^snp2-7-4-4

Nānārattehi vatthehi, ^snp2-7-5-1

sayanehāvasathehi ca; ^snp2-7-5-2

Phītā janapadā raṭṭhā, ^snp2-7-5-3

te namassiṁsu brāhmaṇe. ^snp2-7-5-4

Avajjhā brāhmaṇā āsuṁ, ^snp2-7-6-1

ajeyyā dhammarakkhitā; ^snp2-7-6-2

Na ne koci nivāresi, ^snp2-7-6-3

kuladvāresu sabbaso. ^snp2-7-6-4

Aṭṭhacattālīsaṁ vassāni, ^snp2-7-7-1

(komāra) Brahmacariyaṁ cariṁsu te; ^snp2-7-7-2

Vijjācaraṇapariyeṭṭhiṁ, ^snp2-7-7-3

Acaruṁ brāhmaṇā pure. ^snp2-7-7-4

Na brāhmaṇā aññamagamuṁ, ^snp2-7-8-1

napi bhariyaṁ kiṇiṁsu te; ^snp2-7-8-2

Sampiyeneva saṁvāsaṁ, ^snp2-7-8-3

saṅgantvā samarocayuṁ. ^snp2-7-8-4

Aññatra tamhā samayā, ^snp2-7-9-1

utuveramaṇiṁ pati; ^snp2-7-9-2

Antarā methunaṁ dhammaṁ, ^snp2-7-9-3

nāssu gacchanti brāhmaṇā. ^snp2-7-9-4

Brahmacariyañca sīlañca, ^snp2-7-10-1

ajjavaṁ maddavaṁ tapaṁ; ^snp2-7-10-2

Soraccaṁ avihiṁsañca, ^snp2-7-10-3

khantiñcāpi avaṇṇayuṁ. ^snp2-7-10-4

Yo nesaṁ paramo āsi, ^snp2-7-11-1

Brahmā daḷhaparakkamo; ^snp2-7-11-2

Sa vāpi methunaṁ dhammaṁ, ^snp2-7-11-3

Supinantepi nāgamā. ^snp2-7-11-4

Tassa vattamanusikkhantā, ^snp2-7-12-1

Idheke viññujātikā; ^snp2-7-12-2

Brahmacariyañca sīlañca, ^snp2-7-12-3

Khantiñcāpi avaṇṇayuṁ. ^snp2-7-12-4

Taṇḍulaṁ sayanaṁ vatthaṁ, ^snp2-7-13-1

Sappitelañca yāciya; ^snp2-7-13-2

Dhammena samodhānetvā, ^snp2-7-13-3

Tato yaññamakappayuṁ. ^snp2-7-13-4

Upaṭṭhitasmiṁ yaññasmiṁ, ^snp2-7-14-1

Nāssu gāvo haniṁsu te; ^snp2-7-14-2

Yathā mātā pitā bhātā, ^snp2-7-14-3

Aññe vāpi ca ñātakā; ^snp2-7-14-4

Gāvo no paramā mittā, ^snp2-7-14-5

Yāsu jāyanti osadhā. ^snp2-7-14-6

Annadā baladā cetā, ^snp2-7-15-1

Vaṇṇadā sukhadā tathā; ^snp2-7-15-2

Etamatthavasaṁ ñatvā, ^snp2-7-15-3

Nāssu gāvo haniṁsu te. ^snp2-7-15-4

Sukhumālā mahākāyā, ^snp2-7-16-1

Vaṇṇavanto yasassino; ^snp2-7-16-2

Brāhmaṇā sehi dhammehi, ^snp2-7-16-3

Kiccākiccesu ussukā; ^snp2-7-16-4

Yāva loke avattiṁsu, ^snp2-7-16-5

Sukhamedhitthayaṁ pajā. ^snp2-7-16-6

Tesaṁ āsi vipallāso, ^snp2-7-17-1

Disvāna aṇuto aṇuṁ; ^snp2-7-17-2

Rājino ca viyākāraṁ, ^snp2-7-17-3

Nāriyo samalaṅkatā. ^snp2-7-17-4

Rathe cājaññasaṁyutte, ^snp2-7-18-1

Sukate cittasibbane; ^snp2-7-18-2

Nivesane nivese ca, ^snp2-7-18-3

Vibhatte bhāgaso mite. ^snp2-7-18-4

Gomaṇḍalaparibyūḷhaṁ, ^snp2-7-19-1

Nārīvaragaṇāyutaṁ; ^snp2-7-19-2

Uḷāraṁ mānusaṁ bhogaṁ, ^snp2-7-19-3

Abhijjhāyiṁsu brāhmaṇā. ^snp2-7-19-4

Te tattha mante ganthetvā, ^snp2-7-20-1

Okkākaṁ tadupāgamuṁ; ^snp2-7-20-2

Pahūtadhanadhaññosi, ^snp2-7-20-3

Yajassu bahu te vittaṁ; ^snp2-7-20-4

Yajassu bahu te dhanaṁ. ^snp2-7-20-5

Tato ca rājā saññatto, ^snp2-7-21-1

Brāhmaṇehi rathesabho; ^snp2-7-21-2

Assamedhaṁ purisamedhaṁ, ^snp2-7-21-3

Sammāpāsaṁ vājapeyyaṁ niraggaḷaṁ; ^snp2-7-21-4

Ete yāge yajitvāna, ^snp2-7-21-5

Brāhmaṇānamadā dhanaṁ. ^snp2-7-21-6

Gāvo sayanañca vatthañca, ^snp2-7-22-1

Nāriyo samalaṅkatā; ^snp2-7-22-2

Rathe cājaññasaṁyutte, ^snp2-7-22-3

Sukate cittasibbane. ^snp2-7-22-4

Nivesanāni rammāni, ^snp2-7-23-1

Suvibhattāni bhāgaso; ^snp2-7-23-2

Nānādhaññassa pūretvā, ^snp2-7-23-3

Brāhmaṇānamadā dhanaṁ. ^snp2-7-23-4

Te ca tattha dhanaṁ laddhā, ^snp2-7-24-1

Sannidhiṁ samarocayuṁ; ^snp2-7-24-2

Tesaṁ icchāvatiṇṇānaṁ, ^snp2-7-24-3

Bhiyyo taṇhā pavaḍḍhatha; ^snp2-7-24-4

Te tattha mante ganthetvā, ^snp2-7-24-5

Okkākaṁ puna mupāgamuṁ. ^snp2-7-24-6

Yathā āpo ca pathavī ca, ^snp2-7-25-1

Hiraññaṁ dhanadhāniyaṁ; ^snp2-7-25-2

Evaṁ gāvo manussānaṁ, ^snp2-7-25-3

Parikkhāro so hi pāṇinaṁ; ^snp2-7-25-4

Yajassu bahu te vittaṁ, ^snp2-7-25-5

Yajassu bahu te dhanaṁ. ^snp2-7-25-6

Tato ca rājā saññatto, ^snp2-7-26-1

Brāhmaṇehi rathesabho; ^snp2-7-26-2

Nekā satasahassiyo, ^snp2-7-26-3

Gāvo yaññe aghātayi. ^snp2-7-26-4

Na pādā na visāṇena, ^snp2-7-27-1

Nāssu hiṁsanti kenaci; ^snp2-7-27-2

Gāvo eḷakasamānā, ^snp2-7-27-3

Soratā kumbhadūhanā; ^snp2-7-27-4

Tā visāṇe gahetvāna, ^snp2-7-27-5

Rājā satthena ghātayi. ^snp2-7-27-6

Tato devā pitaro ca, ^snp2-7-28-1

Indo asurarakkhasā; ^snp2-7-28-2

Adhammo iti pakkanduṁ, ^snp2-7-28-3

Yaṁ satthaṁ nipatī gave. ^snp2-7-28-4

Tayo rogā pure āsuṁ, ^snp2-7-29-1

Icchā anasanaṁ jarā; ^snp2-7-29-2

Pasūnañca samārambhā, ^snp2-7-29-3

Aṭṭhānavutimāgamuṁ. ^snp2-7-29-4

Eso adhammo daṇḍānaṁ, ^snp2-7-30-1

Okkanto purāṇo ahu; ^snp2-7-30-2

Adūsikāyo haññanti, ^snp2-7-30-3

Dhammā dhaṁsanti yājakā. ^snp2-7-30-4

Evameso aṇudhammo, ^snp2-7-31-1

Porāṇo viññugarahito; ^snp2-7-31-2

Yattha edisakaṁ passati, ^snp2-7-31-3

Yājakaṁ garahatī jano. ^snp2-7-31-4

Evaṁ dhamme viyāpanne, ^snp2-7-32-1

Vibhinnā suddavessikā; ^snp2-7-32-2

Puthū vibhinnā khattiyā, ^snp2-7-32-3

Patiṁ bhariyāvamaññatha. ^snp2-7-32-4

Khattiyā brahmabandhū ca, ^snp2-7-33-1

Ye caññe gottarakkhitā; ^snp2-7-33-2

Jātivādaṁ nirākatvā, ^snp2-7-33-3

Kāmānaṁ vasamanvagun”ti. ^snp2-7-33-4

Evaṁ vutte, te brāhmaṇamahāsālā bhagavantaṁ etadavocuṁ: ^snp2-7-34-1

“abhikkantaṁ, bho gotama …pe… ^snp2-7-34-2

upāsake no bhavaṁ gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupete saraṇaṁ gate”ti. ^snp2-7-34-3

Brāhmaṇadhammikasuttaṁ sattamaṁ. ^snp2-7-34-4

### Dhamma (nāvā) sutta (Sutta Nipāta 2.8) ^snp2-8-0

Yasmā hi dhammaṁ puriso vijaññā, ^snp2-8-1-1

Indaṁva naṁ devatā pūjayeyya; ^snp2-8-1-2

So pūjito tasmi pasannacitto, ^snp2-8-1-3

Bahussuto pātukaroti dhammaṁ. ^snp2-8-1-4

Tadaṭṭhikatvāna nisamma dhīro, ^snp2-8-2-1

Dhammānudhammaṁ paṭipajjamāno; ^snp2-8-2-2

Viññū vibhāvī nipuṇo ca hoti, ^snp2-8-2-3

Yo tādisaṁ bhajati appamatto. ^snp2-8-2-4

Khuddañca bālaṁ upasevamāno, ^snp2-8-3-1

Anāgatatthañca usūyakañca; ^snp2-8-3-2

Idheva dhammaṁ avibhāvayitvā, ^snp2-8-3-3

Avitiṇṇakaṅkho maraṇaṁ upeti. ^snp2-8-3-4

Yathā naro āpagamotaritvā, ^snp2-8-4-1

Mahodakaṁ salilaṁ sīghasotaṁ; ^snp2-8-4-2

So vuyhamāno anusotagāmī, ^snp2-8-4-3

Kiṁ so pare sakkhati tārayetuṁ. ^snp2-8-4-4

Tatheva dhammaṁ avibhāvayitvā, ^snp2-8-5-1

Bahussutānaṁ anisāmayatthaṁ; ^snp2-8-5-2

Sayaṁ ajānaṁ avitiṇṇakaṅkho, ^snp2-8-5-3

Kiṁ so pare sakkhati nijjhapetuṁ. ^snp2-8-5-4

Yathāpi nāvaṁ daḷhamāruhitvā, ^snp2-8-6-1

Phiyena rittena samaṅgibhūto; ^snp2-8-6-2

So tāraye tattha bahūpi aññe, ^snp2-8-6-3

Tatrūpayaññū kusalo mutīmā. ^snp2-8-6-4

Evampi yo vedagu bhāvitatto, ^snp2-8-7-1

Bahussuto hoti avedhadhammo; ^snp2-8-7-2

So kho pare nijjhapaye pajānaṁ, ^snp2-8-7-3

Sotāvadhānūpanisūpapanne. ^snp2-8-7-4

Tasmā have sappurisaṁ bhajetha, ^snp2-8-8-1

Medhāvinañceva bahussutañca; ^snp2-8-8-2

Aññāya atthaṁ paṭipajjamāno, ^snp2-8-8-3

Viññātadhammo sa sukhaṁ labhethāti. ^snp2-8-8-4

Nāvāsuttaṁ aṭṭhamaṁ. ^snp2-8-8-5

### Kiṁsīlasutta (Sutta Nipāta 2.9) ^snp2-9-0

“Kiṁsīlo kiṁsamācāro, ^snp2-9-1-1

kāni kammāni brūhayaṁ; ^snp2-9-1-2

Naro sammā niviṭṭhassa, ^snp2-9-1-3

uttamatthañca pāpuṇe”. ^snp2-9-1-4

“Vuḍḍhāpacāyī anusūyako siyā, ^snp2-9-2-1

Kālaññū cassa garūnaṁ dassanāya; ^snp2-9-2-2

Dhammiṁ kathaṁ erayitaṁ khaṇaññū, ^snp2-9-2-3

Suṇeyya sakkacca subhāsitāni. ^snp2-9-2-4

Kālena gacche garūnaṁ sakāsaṁ, ^snp2-9-3-1

Thambhaṁ niraṅkatvā nivātavutti; ^snp2-9-3-2

Atthaṁ dhammaṁ saṁyamaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, ^snp2-9-3-3

Anussare ceva samācare ca. ^snp2-9-3-4

Dhammārāmo dhammarato, ^snp2-9-4-1

Dhamme ṭhito dhammavinicchayaññū; ^snp2-9-4-2

Nevācare dhammasandosavādaṁ, ^snp2-9-4-3

Tacchehi nīyetha subhāsitehi. ^snp2-9-4-4

Hassaṁ jappaṁ paridevaṁ padosaṁ, ^snp2-9-5-1

Māyākataṁ kuhanaṁ giddhi mānaṁ; ^snp2-9-5-2

Sārambhaṁ kakkasaṁ kasāvañca mucchaṁ, ^snp2-9-5-3

Hitvā care vītamado ṭhitatto. ^snp2-9-5-4

Viññātasārāni subhāsitāni, ^snp2-9-6-1

Sutañca viññātasamādhisāraṁ; ^snp2-9-6-2

Na tassa paññā ca sutañca vaḍḍhati, ^snp2-9-6-3

Yo sāhaso hoti naro pamatto. ^snp2-9-6-4

Dhamme ca ye ariyapavedite ratā, ^snp2-9-7-1

Anuttarā te vacasā manasā kammunā ca; ^snp2-9-7-2

Te santisoraccasamādhisaṇṭhitā, ^snp2-9-7-3

Sutassa paññāya ca sāramajjhagū”ti. ^snp2-9-7-4

Kiṁsīlasuttaṁ navamaṁ. ^snp2-9-7-5

### Uṭṭhānasutta (Sutta Nipāta 2.10) ^snp2-10-0

Uṭṭhahatha nisīdatha, ^snp2-10-1-1

ko attho supitena vo; ^snp2-10-1-2

Āturānañhi kā niddā, ^snp2-10-1-3

sallaviddhāna ruppataṁ. ^snp2-10-1-4

Uṭṭhahatha nisīdatha, ^snp2-10-2-1

Daḷhaṁ sikkhatha santiyā; ^snp2-10-2-2

Mā vo pamatte viññāya, ^snp2-10-2-3

Maccurājā amohayittha vasānuge. ^snp2-10-2-4

Yāya devā manussā ca, ^snp2-10-3-1

sitā tiṭṭhanti atthikā; ^snp2-10-3-2

Tarathetaṁ visattikaṁ, ^snp2-10-3-3

khaṇo vo mā upaccagā; ^snp2-10-3-4

Khaṇātītā hi socanti, ^snp2-10-3-5

nirayamhi samappitā. ^snp2-10-3-6

Pamādo rajo pamādo, ^snp2-10-4-1

Pamādānupatito rajo; ^snp2-10-4-2

Appamādena vijjāya, ^snp2-10-4-3

Abbahe sallamattanoti. ^snp2-10-4-4

Uṭṭhānasuttaṁ dasamaṁ. ^snp2-10-4-5

### Rāhulasutta (Sutta Nipāta 2.11) ^snp2-11-0

“Kacci abhiṇhasaṁvāsā, ^snp2-11-1-1

nāvajānāsi paṇḍitaṁ; ^snp2-11-1-2

Ukkādhāro manussānaṁ, ^snp2-11-1-3

kacci apacito tayā”. ^snp2-11-1-4

“Nāhaṁ abhiṇhasaṁvāsā, ^snp2-11-2-1

avajānāmi paṇḍitaṁ; ^snp2-11-2-2

Ukkādhāro manussānaṁ, ^snp2-11-2-3

niccaṁ apacito mayā”. ^snp2-11-2-4

“Pañca kāmaguṇe hitvā, ^snp2-11-3-1

piyarūpe manorame; ^snp2-11-3-2

Saddhāya gharā nikkhamma, ^snp2-11-3-3

dukkhassantakaro bhava. ^snp2-11-3-4

Mitte bhajassu kalyāṇe, ^snp2-11-4-1

pantañca sayanāsanaṁ; ^snp2-11-4-2

Vivittaṁ appanigghosaṁ, ^snp2-11-4-3

mattaññū hohi bhojane. ^snp2-11-4-4

Cīvare piṇḍapāte ca, ^snp2-11-5-1

paccaye sayanāsane; ^snp2-11-5-2

Etesu taṇhaṁ mākāsi, ^snp2-11-5-3

mā lokaṁ punarāgami. ^snp2-11-5-4

Saṁvuto pātimokkhasmiṁ, ^snp2-11-6-1

indriyesu ca pañcasu; ^snp2-11-6-2

Sati kāyagatā tyatthu, ^snp2-11-6-3

nibbidābahulo bhava. ^snp2-11-6-4

Nimittaṁ parivajjehi, ^snp2-11-7-1

subhaṁ rāgūpasañhitaṁ; ^snp2-11-7-2

Asubhāya cittaṁ bhāvehi, ^snp2-11-7-3

ekaggaṁ susamāhitaṁ. ^snp2-11-7-4

Animittañca bhāvehi, ^snp2-11-8-1

Mānānusayamujjaha; ^snp2-11-8-2

Tato mānābhisamayā, ^snp2-11-8-3

Upasanto carissatī”ti. ^snp2-11-8-4

Itthaṁ sudaṁ bhagavā āyasmantaṁ rāhulaṁ imāhi gāthāhi abhiṇhaṁ ovadatīti. ^snp2-11-9-1

Rāhulasuttaṁ ekādasamaṁ. ^snp2-11-9-2

### Nigrodhakappa (vaṅgīsa) sutta (Sutta Nipāta 2.12) ^snp2-12-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp2-12-1-1

ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā āḷaviyaṁ viharati aggāḷave cetiye. ^snp2-12-1-2

Tena kho pana samayena āyasmato vaṅgīsassa upajjhāyo nigrodhakappo nāma thero aggāḷave cetiye aciraparinibbuto hoti. ^snp2-12-1-3

Atha kho āyasmato vaṅgīsassa rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa evaṁ cetaso parivitakko udapādi— ^snp2-12-1-4

parinibbuto nu kho me upajjhāyo udāhu no parinibbutoti? ^snp2-12-1-5

Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso sāyanhasamayaṁ paṭisallānā vuṭṭhito yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho āyasmā vaṅgīso bhagavantaṁ etadavoca— ^snp2-12-1-6

idha mayhaṁ, bhante, rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa evaṁ cetaso parivitakko udapādi— ^snp2-12-1-7

parinibbuto nu kho me upajjhāyo, udāhu no parinibbutoti. ^snp2-12-1-8

Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaṁsaṁ cīvaraṁ katvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṁ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṁ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi: ^snp2-12-1-9

“Pucchāmi satthāramanomapaññaṁ, ^snp2-12-2-1

Diṭṭheva dhamme yo vicikicchānaṁ chettā; ^snp2-12-2-2

Aggāḷave kālamakāsi bhikkhu, ^snp2-12-2-3

Ñāto yasassī abhinibbutatto. ^snp2-12-2-4

Nigrodhakappo iti tassa nāmaṁ, ^snp2-12-3-1

Tayā kataṁ bhagavā brāhmaṇassa; ^snp2-12-3-2

So taṁ namassaṁ acari mutyapekkho, ^snp2-12-3-3

Āraddhaviriyo daḷhadhammadassī. ^snp2-12-3-4

Taṁ sāvakaṁ sakya mayampi sabbe, ^snp2-12-4-1

Aññātumicchāma samantacakkhu; ^snp2-12-4-2

Samavaṭṭhitā no savanāya sotā, ^snp2-12-4-3

Tuvaṁ no satthā tvamanuttarosi. ^snp2-12-4-4

Chindeva no vicikicchaṁ brūhi metaṁ, ^snp2-12-5-1

Parinibbutaṁ vedaya bhūripañña; ^snp2-12-5-2

Majjheva no bhāsa samantacakkhu, ^snp2-12-5-3

Sakkova devāna sahassanetto. ^snp2-12-5-4

Ye keci ganthā idha mohamaggā, ^snp2-12-6-1

Aññāṇapakkhā vicikicchaṭhānā; ^snp2-12-6-2

Tathāgataṁ patvā na te bhavanti, ^snp2-12-6-3

Cakkhuñhi etaṁ paramaṁ narānaṁ. ^snp2-12-6-4

No ce hi jātu puriso kilese, ^snp2-12-7-1

Vāto yathā abbhaghanaṁ vihāne; ^snp2-12-7-2

Tamovassa nivuto sabbaloko, ^snp2-12-7-3

Na jotimantopi narā tapeyyuṁ. ^snp2-12-7-4

Dhīrā ca pajjotakarā bhavanti, ^snp2-12-8-1

Taṁ taṁ ahaṁ vīra tatheva maññe; ^snp2-12-8-2

Vipassinaṁ jānamupāgamumhā, ^snp2-12-8-3

Parisāsu no āvikarohi kappaṁ. ^snp2-12-8-4

Khippaṁ giraṁ eraya vaggu vagguṁ, ^snp2-12-9-1

Haṁsova paggayha saṇikaṁ nikūja; ^snp2-12-9-2

Bindussarena suvikappitena, ^snp2-12-9-3

Sabbeva te ujjugatā suṇoma. ^snp2-12-9-4

Pahīnajātimaraṇaṁ asesaṁ, ^snp2-12-10-1

Niggayha dhonaṁ vadessāmi dhammaṁ; ^snp2-12-10-2

Na kāmakāro hi puthujjanānaṁ, ^snp2-12-10-3

Saṅkheyyakāro ca tathāgatānaṁ. ^snp2-12-10-4

Sampannaveyyākaraṇaṁ tavedaṁ, ^snp2-12-11-1

Samujjupaññassa samuggahītaṁ; ^snp2-12-11-2

Ayamañjalī pacchimo suppaṇāmito, ^snp2-12-11-3

Mā mohayī jānamanomapañña. ^snp2-12-11-4

Parovaraṁ ariyadhammaṁ viditvā, ^snp2-12-12-1

Mā mohayī jānamanomavīra; ^snp2-12-12-2

Vāriṁ yathā ghammani ghammatatto, ^snp2-12-12-3

Vācābhikaṅkhāmi sutaṁ pavassa. ^snp2-12-12-4

Yadatthikaṁ brahmacariyaṁ acarī, ^snp2-12-13-1

Kappāyano kaccissa taṁ amoghaṁ; ^snp2-12-13-2

Nibbāyi so ādu saupādiseso, ^snp2-12-13-3

Yathā vimutto ahu taṁ suṇoma”. ^snp2-12-13-4

“Acchecchi taṇhaṁ idha nāmarūpe, ^snp2-12-14-1

(iti bhagavā) ^snp2-12-14-2

Kaṇhassa sotaṁ dīgharattānusayitaṁ; ^snp2-12-14-3

Atāri jātiṁ maraṇaṁ asesaṁ”, ^snp2-12-14-4

Iccabravī bhagavā pañcaseṭṭho. ^snp2-12-14-5

“Esa sutvā pasīdāmi, ^snp2-12-15-1

Vaco te isisattama; ^snp2-12-15-2

Amoghaṁ kira me puṭṭhaṁ, ^snp2-12-15-3

Na maṁ vañcesi brāhmaṇo. ^snp2-12-15-4

Yathāvādī tathākārī, ^snp2-12-16-1

Ahu buddhassa sāvako; ^snp2-12-16-2

Acchidā maccuno jālaṁ, ^snp2-12-16-3

Tataṁ māyāvino daḷhaṁ. ^snp2-12-16-4

Addasā bhagavā ādiṁ, ^snp2-12-17-1

Upādānassa kappiyo; ^snp2-12-17-2

Accagā vata kappāyano, ^snp2-12-17-3

Maccudheyyaṁ suduttaran”ti. ^snp2-12-17-4

Nigrodhakappasuttaṁ dvādasamaṁ. ^snp2-12-17-5

### Sammāparibbājanīyasutta (Sutta Nipāta 2.13) ^snp2-13-0

“Pucchāmi muniṁ pahūtapaññaṁ, ^snp2-13-1-1

Tiṇṇaṁ pāraṅgataṁ parinibbutaṁ ṭhitattaṁ; ^snp2-13-1-2

Nikkhamma gharā panujja kāme, ^snp2-13-1-3

Kathaṁ bhikkhu sammā so loke paribbajeyya”. ^snp2-13-1-4

“Yassa maṅgalā samūhatā, ^snp2-13-2-1

(iti bhagavā) ^snp2-13-2-2

Uppātā supinā ca lakkhaṇā ca; ^snp2-13-2-3

So maṅgaladosavippahīno, ^snp2-13-2-4

Sammā so loke paribbajeyya. ^snp2-13-2-5

Rāgaṁ vinayetha mānusesu, ^snp2-13-3-1

Dibbesu kāmesu cāpi bhikkhu; ^snp2-13-3-2

Atikkamma bhavaṁ samecca dhammaṁ, ^snp2-13-3-3

Sammā so loke paribbajeyya. ^snp2-13-3-4

Vipiṭṭhikatvāna pesuṇāni, ^snp2-13-4-1

Kodhaṁ kadarīyaṁ jaheyya bhikkhu; ^snp2-13-4-2

Anurodhavirodhavippahīno, ^snp2-13-4-3

Sammā so loke paribbajeyya. ^snp2-13-4-4

Hitvāna piyañca appiyañca, ^snp2-13-5-1

Anupādāya anissito kuhiñci; ^snp2-13-5-2

Saṁyojaniyehi vippamutto, ^snp2-13-5-3

Sammā so loke paribbajeyya. ^snp2-13-5-4

Na so upadhīsu sārameti, ^snp2-13-6-1

Ādānesu vineyya chandarāgaṁ; ^snp2-13-6-2

So anissito anaññaneyyo, ^snp2-13-6-3

Sammā so loke paribbajeyya. ^snp2-13-6-4

Vacasā manasā ca kammunā ca, ^snp2-13-7-1

Aviruddho sammā viditvā dhammaṁ; ^snp2-13-7-2

Nibbānapadābhipatthayāno, ^snp2-13-7-3

Sammā so loke paribbajeyya. ^snp2-13-7-4

Yo vandati manti nunnameyya, ^snp2-13-8-1

Akkuṭṭhopi na sandhiyetha bhikkhu; ^snp2-13-8-2

Laddhā parabhojanaṁ na majje, ^snp2-13-8-3

Sammā so loke paribbajeyya. ^snp2-13-8-4

Lobhañca bhavañca vippahāya, ^snp2-13-9-1

Virato chedanabandhanā ca bhikkhu; ^snp2-13-9-2

So tiṇṇakathaṅkatho visallo, ^snp2-13-9-3

Sammā so loke paribbajeyya. ^snp2-13-9-4

Sāruppaṁ attano viditvā, ^snp2-13-10-1

No ca bhikkhu hiṁseyya kañci loke; ^snp2-13-10-2

Yathātathiyaṁ viditvā dhammaṁ, ^snp2-13-10-3

Sammā so loke paribbajeyya. ^snp2-13-10-4

Yassānusayā na santi keci, ^snp2-13-11-1

Mūlā ca akusalā samūhatāse; ^snp2-13-11-2

So nirāso anāsisāno, ^snp2-13-11-3

Sammā so loke paribbajeyya. ^snp2-13-11-4

Āsavakhīṇo pahīnamāno, ^snp2-13-12-1

Sabbaṁ rāgapathaṁ upātivatto; ^snp2-13-12-2

Danto parinibbuto ṭhitatto, ^snp2-13-12-3

Sammā so loke paribbajeyya. ^snp2-13-12-4

Saddho sutavā niyāmadassī, ^snp2-13-13-1

Vaggagatesu na vaggasāri dhīro; ^snp2-13-13-2

Lobhaṁ dosaṁ vineyya paṭighaṁ, ^snp2-13-13-3

Sammā so loke paribbajeyya. ^snp2-13-13-4

Saṁsuddhajino vivaṭṭacchado, ^snp2-13-14-1

Dhammesu vasī pāragū anejo; ^snp2-13-14-2

Saṅkhāranirodhañāṇakusalo, ^snp2-13-14-3

Sammā so loke paribbajeyya. ^snp2-13-14-4

Atītesu anāgatesu cāpi, ^snp2-13-15-1

Kappātīto aticcasuddhipañño; ^snp2-13-15-2

Sabbāyatanehi vippamutto, ^snp2-13-15-3

Sammā so loke paribbajeyya. ^snp2-13-15-4

Aññāya padaṁ samecca dhammaṁ, ^snp2-13-16-1

Vivaṭaṁ disvāna pahānamāsavānaṁ; ^snp2-13-16-2

Sabbupadhīnaṁ parikkhayāno, ^snp2-13-16-3

Sammā so loke paribbajeyya”. ^snp2-13-16-4

“Addhā hi bhagavā tatheva etaṁ, ^snp2-13-17-1

Yo so evaṁvihārī danto bhikkhu; ^snp2-13-17-2

Sabbasaṁyojanayogavītivatto, ^snp2-13-17-3

Sammā so loke paribbajeyyā”ti. ^snp2-13-17-4

Sammāparibbājanīyasuttaṁ terasamaṁ. ^snp2-13-17-5

### Dhammikasutta (Sutta Nipāta 2.14) ^snp2-14-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp2-14-1-1

ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. ^snp2-14-1-2

Atha kho dhammiko upāsako pañcahi upāsakasatehi saddhiṁ yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho dhammiko upāsako bhagavantaṁ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi: ^snp2-14-1-3

“Pucchāmi taṁ gotama bhūripañña, ^snp2-14-2-1

Kathaṅkaro sāvako sādhu hoti; ^snp2-14-2-2

Yo vā agārā anagārameti, ^snp2-14-2-3

Agārino vā panupāsakāse. ^snp2-14-2-4

Tuvañhi lokassa sadevakassa, ^snp2-14-3-1

Gatiṁ pajānāsi parāyaṇañca; ^snp2-14-3-2

Na catthi tulyo nipuṇatthadassī, ^snp2-14-3-3

Tuvañhi buddhaṁ pavaraṁ vadanti. ^snp2-14-3-4

Sabbaṁ tuvaṁ ñāṇamavecca dhammaṁ, ^snp2-14-4-1

Pakāsesi satte anukampamāno; ^snp2-14-4-2

Vivaṭṭacchadosi samantacakkhu, ^snp2-14-4-3

Virocasi vimalo sabbaloke. ^snp2-14-4-4

Āgañchi te santike nāgarājā, ^snp2-14-5-1

Erāvaṇo nāma jinoti sutvā; ^snp2-14-5-2

Sopi tayā mantayitvājjhagamā, ^snp2-14-5-3

Sādhūti sutvāna patītarūpo. ^snp2-14-5-4

Rājāpi taṁ vessavaṇo kuvero, ^snp2-14-6-1

Upeti dhammaṁ paripucchamāno; ^snp2-14-6-2

Tassāpi tvaṁ pucchito brūsi dhīra, ^snp2-14-6-3

So cāpi sutvāna patītarūpo. ^snp2-14-6-4

Ye kecime titthiyā vādasīlā, ^snp2-14-7-1

Ājīvakā vā yadi vā nigaṇṭhā; ^snp2-14-7-2

Paññāya taṁ nātitaranti sabbe, ^snp2-14-7-3

Ṭhito vajantaṁ viya sīghagāmiṁ. ^snp2-14-7-4

Ye kecime brāhmaṇā vādasīlā, ^snp2-14-8-1

Vuddhā cāpi brāhmaṇā santi keci; ^snp2-14-8-2

Sabbe tayi atthabaddhā bhavanti, ^snp2-14-8-3

Ye cāpi aññe vādino maññamānā. ^snp2-14-8-4

Ayañhi dhammo nipuṇo sukho ca, ^snp2-14-9-1

Yoyaṁ tayā bhagavā suppavutto; ^snp2-14-9-2

Tameva sabbepi sussūsamānā, ^snp2-14-9-3

Taṁ no vada pucchito buddhaseṭṭha. ^snp2-14-9-4

Sabbepime bhikkhavo sannisinnā, ^snp2-14-10-1

Upāsakā cāpi tatheva sotuṁ; ^snp2-14-10-2

Suṇantu dhammaṁ vimalenānubuddhaṁ, ^snp2-14-10-3

Subhāsitaṁ vāsavasseva devā”. ^snp2-14-10-4

“Suṇātha me bhikkhavo sāvayāmi vo, ^snp2-14-11-1

Dhammaṁ dhutaṁ tañca carātha sabbe; ^snp2-14-11-2

Iriyāpathaṁ pabbajitānulomikaṁ, ^snp2-14-11-3

Sevetha naṁ atthadaso mutīmā. ^snp2-14-11-4

No ve vikāle vicareyya bhikkhu, ^snp2-14-12-1

Gāme ca piṇḍāya careyya kāle; ^snp2-14-12-2

Akālacāriñhi sajanti saṅgā, ^snp2-14-12-3

Tasmā vikāle na caranti buddhā. ^snp2-14-12-4

Rūpā ca saddā ca rasā ca gandhā, ^snp2-14-13-1

Phassā ca ye sammadayanti satte; ^snp2-14-13-2

Etesu dhammesu vineyya chandaṁ, ^snp2-14-13-3

Kālena so pavise pātarāsaṁ. ^snp2-14-13-4

Piṇḍañca bhikkhu samayena laddhā, ^snp2-14-14-1

Eko paṭikkamma raho nisīde; ^snp2-14-14-2

Ajjhattacintī na mano bahiddhā, ^snp2-14-14-3

Nicchāraye saṅgahitattabhāvo. ^snp2-14-14-4

Sacepi so sallape sāvakena, ^snp2-14-15-1

Aññena vā kenaci bhikkhunā vā; ^snp2-14-15-2
