Dhammaṁ paṇītaṁ tamudāhareyya, ^snp2-14-15-3

Na pesuṇaṁ nopi parūpavādaṁ. ^snp2-14-15-4

Vādañhi eke paṭiseniyanti, ^snp2-14-16-1

Na te pasaṁsāma parittapaññe; ^snp2-14-16-2

Tato tato ne pasajanti saṅgā, ^snp2-14-16-3

Cittañhi te tattha gamenti dūre. ^snp2-14-16-4

Piṇḍaṁ vihāraṁ sayanāsanañca, ^snp2-14-17-1

Āpañca saṅghāṭirajūpavāhanaṁ; ^snp2-14-17-2

Sutvāna dhammaṁ sugatena desitaṁ, ^snp2-14-17-3

Saṅkhāya seve varapaññasāvako. ^snp2-14-17-4

Tasmā hi piṇḍe sayanāsane ca, ^snp2-14-18-1

Āpe ca saṅghāṭirajūpavāhane; ^snp2-14-18-2

Etesu dhammesu anūpalitto, ^snp2-14-18-3

Bhikkhu yathā pokkhare vāribindu. ^snp2-14-18-4

Gahaṭṭhavattaṁ pana vo vadāmi, ^snp2-14-19-1

Yathākaro sāvako sādhu hoti; ^snp2-14-19-2

Na hesa labbhā sapariggahena, ^snp2-14-19-3

Phassetuṁ yo kevalo bhikkhudhammo. ^snp2-14-19-4

Pāṇaṁ na hane na ca ghātayeyya, ^snp2-14-20-1

Na cānujaññā hanataṁ paresaṁ; ^snp2-14-20-2

Sabbesu bhūtesu nidhāya daṇḍaṁ, ^snp2-14-20-3

Ye thāvarā ye ca tasā santi loke. ^snp2-14-20-4

Tato adinnaṁ parivajjayeyya, ^snp2-14-21-1

Kiñci kvaci sāvako bujjhamāno; ^snp2-14-21-2

Na hāraye harataṁ nānujaññā, ^snp2-14-21-3

Sabbaṁ adinnaṁ parivajjayeyya. ^snp2-14-21-4

Abrahmacariyaṁ parivajjayeyya, ^snp2-14-22-1

Aṅgārakāsuṁ jalitaṁva viññū; ^snp2-14-22-2

Asambhuṇanto pana brahmacariyaṁ, ^snp2-14-22-3

Parassa dāraṁ na atikkameyya. ^snp2-14-22-4

Sabhaggato vā parisaggato vā, ^snp2-14-23-1

Ekassa veko na musā bhaṇeyya; ^snp2-14-23-2

Na bhāṇaye bhaṇataṁ nānujaññā, ^snp2-14-23-3

Sabbaṁ abhūtaṁ parivajjayeyya. ^snp2-14-23-4

Majjañca pānaṁ na samācareyya, ^snp2-14-24-1

Dhammaṁ imaṁ rocaye yo gahaṭṭho; ^snp2-14-24-2

Na pāyaye pivataṁ nānujaññā, ^snp2-14-24-3

Ummādanantaṁ iti naṁ viditvā. ^snp2-14-24-4

Madā hi pāpāni karonti bālā, ^snp2-14-25-1

Kārenti caññepi jane pamatte; ^snp2-14-25-2

Etaṁ apuññāyatanaṁ vivajjaye, ^snp2-14-25-3

Ummādanaṁ mohanaṁ bālakantaṁ. ^snp2-14-25-4

Pāṇaṁ na hane na cādinnamādiye, ^snp2-14-26-1

Musā na bhāse na ca majjapo siyā; ^snp2-14-26-2

Abrahmacariyā virameyya methunā, ^snp2-14-26-3

Rattiṁ na bhuñjeyya vikālabhojanaṁ. ^snp2-14-26-4

Mālaṁ na dhāre na ca gandhamācare, ^snp2-14-27-1

Mañce chamāyaṁ va sayetha santhate; ^snp2-14-27-2

Etañhi aṭṭhaṅgikamāhuposathaṁ, ^snp2-14-27-3

Buddhena dukkhantagunā pakāsitaṁ. ^snp2-14-27-4

Tato ca pakkhassupavassuposathaṁ, ^snp2-14-28-1

Cātuddasiṁ pañcadasiñca aṭṭhamiṁ; ^snp2-14-28-2

Pāṭihāriyapakkhañca pasannamānaso, ^snp2-14-28-3

Aṭṭhaṅgupetaṁ susamattarūpaṁ. ^snp2-14-28-4

Tato ca pāto upavutthuposatho, ^snp2-14-29-1

Annena pānena ca bhikkhusaṅghaṁ; ^snp2-14-29-2

Pasannacitto anumodamāno, ^snp2-14-29-3

Yathārahaṁ saṁvibhajetha viññū. ^snp2-14-29-4

Dhammena mātāpitaro bhareyya, ^snp2-14-30-1

Payojaye dhammikaṁ so vaṇijjaṁ; ^snp2-14-30-2

Etaṁ gihī vattayamappamatto, ^snp2-14-30-3

Sayampabhe nāma upeti deve”ti. ^snp2-14-30-4

Dhammikasuttaṁ cuddasamaṁ. ^snp2-14-30-5

Cūḷavaggo dutiyo. ^snp2-14-30-6

Tassuddānaṁ ^snp2-14-31-0

Ratanāmagandho hiri ca, ^snp2-14-31-1

maṅgalaṁ sūcilomena; ^snp2-14-31-2

Dhammacariyañca brāhmaṇo, ^snp2-14-31-3

nāvā kiṁsīlamuṭṭhānaṁ. ^snp2-14-31-4

Rāhulo puna kappo ca, ^snp2-14-32-1

paribbājaniyaṁ tathā; ^snp2-14-32-2

Dhammikañca viduno āhu, ^snp2-14-32-3

cūḷavagganti cuddasāti. ^snp2-14-32-4

## Vagga 3 ^vagga3-0

### Pabbajjāsutta (Sutta Nipāta 3.1) ^snp3-1-0

“Pabbajjaṁ kittayissāmi, ^snp3-1-1-1

yathā pabbaji cakkhumā; ^snp3-1-1-2

Yathā vīmaṁsamāno so, ^snp3-1-1-3

pabbajjaṁ samarocayi. ^snp3-1-1-4

Sambādhoyaṁ gharāvāso, ^snp3-1-2-1

rajassāyatanaṁ iti; ^snp3-1-2-2

Abbhokāsova pabbajjā, ^snp3-1-2-3

iti disvāna pabbaji. ^snp3-1-2-4

Pabbajitvāna kāyena, ^snp3-1-3-1

pāpakammaṁ vivajjayi; ^snp3-1-3-2

Vacīduccaritaṁ hitvā, ^snp3-1-3-3

ājīvaṁ parisodhayi. ^snp3-1-3-4

Agamā rājagahaṁ buddho, ^snp3-1-4-1

magadhānaṁ giribbajaṁ; ^snp3-1-4-2

Piṇḍāya abhihāresi, ^snp3-1-4-3

ākiṇṇavaralakkhaṇo”. ^snp3-1-4-4

Tamaddasā bimbisāro, ^snp3-1-5-1

pāsādasmiṁ patiṭṭhito; ^snp3-1-5-2

Disvā lakkhaṇasampannaṁ, ^snp3-1-5-3

imamatthaṁ abhāsatha. ^snp3-1-5-4

“Imaṁ bhonto nisāmetha, ^snp3-1-6-1

abhirūpo brahā suci; ^snp3-1-6-2

Caraṇena ca sampanno, ^snp3-1-6-3

yugamattañca pekkhati. ^snp3-1-6-4

Okkhittacakkhu satimā, ^snp3-1-7-1

nāyaṁ nīcakulāmiva; ^snp3-1-7-2

Rājadūtābhidhāvantu, ^snp3-1-7-3

kuhiṁ bhikkhu gamissati”. ^snp3-1-7-4

Te pesitā rājadūtā, ^snp3-1-8-1

piṭṭhito anubandhisuṁ; ^snp3-1-8-2

Kuhiṁ gamissati bhikkhu, ^snp3-1-8-3

kattha vāso bhavissati. ^snp3-1-8-4

Sapadānaṁ caramāno, ^snp3-1-9-1

guttadvāro susaṁvuto; ^snp3-1-9-2

Khippaṁ pattaṁ apūresi, ^snp3-1-9-3

sampajāno paṭissato. ^snp3-1-9-4

Piṇḍacāraṁ caritvāna, ^snp3-1-10-1

Nikkhamma nagarā muni; ^snp3-1-10-2

Paṇḍavaṁ abhihāresi, ^snp3-1-10-3

Ettha vāso bhavissati. ^snp3-1-10-4

Disvāna vāsūpagataṁ, ^snp3-1-11-1

Tayo dūtā upāvisuṁ; ^snp3-1-11-2

Tesu ekova āgantvā, ^snp3-1-11-3

Rājino paṭivedayi. ^snp3-1-11-4

“Esa bhikkhu mahārāja, ^snp3-1-12-1

Paṇḍavassa puratthato; ^snp3-1-12-2

Nisinno byagghusabhova, ^snp3-1-12-3

Sīhova girigabbhare”. ^snp3-1-12-4

Sutvāna dūtavacanaṁ, ^snp3-1-13-1

Bhaddayānena khattiyo; ^snp3-1-13-2

Taramānarūpo niyyāsi, ^snp3-1-13-3

Yena paṇḍavapabbato. ^snp3-1-13-4

Sa yānabhūmiṁ yāyitvā, ^snp3-1-14-1

Yānā oruyha khattiyo; ^snp3-1-14-2

Pattiko upasaṅkamma, ^snp3-1-14-3

Āsajja naṁ upāvisi. ^snp3-1-14-4

Nisajja rājā sammodi, ^snp3-1-15-1

Kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ tato; ^snp3-1-15-2

Kathaṁ so vītisāretvā, ^snp3-1-15-3

Imamatthaṁ abhāsatha. ^snp3-1-15-4

“Yuvā ca daharo cāsi, ^snp3-1-16-1

Paṭhamuppattiko susu; ^snp3-1-16-2

Vaṇṇārohena sampanno, ^snp3-1-16-3

Jātimā viya khattiyo. ^snp3-1-16-4

Sobhayanto anīkaggaṁ, ^snp3-1-17-1

Nāgasaṅghapurakkhato; ^snp3-1-17-2

Dadāmi bhoge bhuñjassu, ^snp3-1-17-3

Jātiṁ akkhāhi pucchito”. ^snp3-1-17-4

“Ujuṁ janapado rāja, ^snp3-1-18-1

Himavantassa passato; ^snp3-1-18-2

Dhanaviriyena sampanno, ^snp3-1-18-3

Kosalesu niketino. ^snp3-1-18-4

Ādiccā nāma gottena, ^snp3-1-19-1

Sākiyā nāma jātiyā; ^snp3-1-19-2

Tamhā kulā pabbajitomhi, ^snp3-1-19-3

Na kāme abhipatthayaṁ. ^snp3-1-19-4

Kāmesvādīnavaṁ disvā, ^snp3-1-20-1

Nekkhammaṁ daṭṭhu khemato; ^snp3-1-20-2

Padhānāya gamissāmi, ^snp3-1-20-3

Ettha me rañjatī mano”ti. ^snp3-1-20-4

Pabbajjāsuttaṁ paṭhamaṁ. ^snp3-1-20-5

### Padhānasutta (Sutta Nipāta 3.2) ^snp3-2-0

“Taṁ maṁ padhānapahitattaṁ, ^snp3-2-1-1

nadiṁ nerañjaraṁ pati; ^snp3-2-1-2

Viparakkamma jhāyantaṁ, ^snp3-2-1-3

yogakkhemassa pattiyā. ^snp3-2-1-4

Namucī karuṇaṁ vācaṁ, ^snp3-2-2-1

bhāsamāno upāgami; ^snp3-2-2-2

‘Kiso tvamasi dubbaṇṇo, ^snp3-2-2-3

santike maraṇaṁ tava. ^snp3-2-2-4

Sahassabhāgo maraṇassa, ^snp3-2-3-1

ekaṁso tava jīvitaṁ; ^snp3-2-3-2

Jīva bho jīvitaṁ seyyo, ^snp3-2-3-3

jīvaṁ puññāni kāhasi. ^snp3-2-3-4

Carato ca te brahmacariyaṁ, ^snp3-2-4-1

Aggihuttañca jūhato; ^snp3-2-4-2

Pahūtaṁ cīyate puññaṁ, ^snp3-2-4-3

Kiṁ padhānena kāhasi. ^snp3-2-4-4

Duggo maggo padhānāya, ^snp3-2-5-1

dukkaro durabhisambhavo’”; ^snp3-2-5-2

Imā gāthā bhaṇaṁ māro, ^snp3-2-5-3

aṭṭhā buddhassa santike. ^snp3-2-5-4

Taṁ tathāvādinaṁ māraṁ, ^snp3-2-6-1

bhagavā etadabravi; ^snp3-2-6-2

“Pamattabandhu pāpima, ^snp3-2-6-3

yenatthena idhāgato. ^snp3-2-6-4

Aṇumattopi puññena, ^snp3-2-7-1

Attho mayhaṁ na vijjati; ^snp3-2-7-2

Yesañca attho puññena, ^snp3-2-7-3

Te māro vattumarahati. ^snp3-2-7-4

Atthi saddhā tathā viriyaṁ, ^snp3-2-8-1

paññā ca mama vijjati; ^snp3-2-8-2

Evaṁ maṁ pahitattampi, ^snp3-2-8-3

kiṁ jīvamanupucchasi. ^snp3-2-8-4

Nadīnamapi sotāni, ^snp3-2-9-1

ayaṁ vāto visosaye; ^snp3-2-9-2

Kiñca me pahitattassa, ^snp3-2-9-3

lohitaṁ nupasussaye. ^snp3-2-9-4

Lohite sussamānamhi, ^snp3-2-10-1

Pittaṁ semhañca sussati; ^snp3-2-10-2

Maṁsesu khīyamānesu, ^snp3-2-10-3

Bhiyyo cittaṁ pasīdati; ^snp3-2-10-4

Bhiyyo sati ca paññā ca, ^snp3-2-10-5

Samādhi mama tiṭṭhati. ^snp3-2-10-6

Tassa mevaṁ viharato, ^snp3-2-11-1

Pattassuttamavedanaṁ; ^snp3-2-11-2

Kāmesu nāpekkhate cittaṁ, ^snp3-2-11-3

Passa sattassa suddhataṁ. ^snp3-2-11-4

Kāmā te paṭhamā senā, ^snp3-2-12-1

Dutiyā arati vuccati; ^snp3-2-12-2

Tatiyā khuppipāsā te, ^snp3-2-12-3

Catutthī taṇhā pavuccati. ^snp3-2-12-4

Pañcamaṁ thinamiddhaṁ te, ^snp3-2-13-1

Chaṭṭhā bhīrū pavuccati; ^snp3-2-13-2

Sattamī vicikicchā te, ^snp3-2-13-3

Makkho thambho te aṭṭhamo. ^snp3-2-13-4

Lābho siloko sakkāro, ^snp3-2-14-1

Micchāladdho ca yo yaso; ^snp3-2-14-2

Yo cattānaṁ samukkaṁse, ^snp3-2-14-3

Pare ca avajānati. ^snp3-2-14-4

Esā namuci te senā, ^snp3-2-15-1

Kaṇhassābhippahārinī; ^snp3-2-15-2

Na naṁ asūro jināti, ^snp3-2-15-3

Jetvā ca labhate sukhaṁ. ^snp3-2-15-4

Esa muñjaṁ parihare, ^snp3-2-16-1

Dhiratthu mama jīvitaṁ; ^snp3-2-16-2

Saṅgāme me mataṁ seyyo, ^snp3-2-16-3

Yañce jīve parājito. ^snp3-2-16-4

Pagāḷhettha na dissanti, ^snp3-2-17-1

Eke samaṇabrāhmaṇā; ^snp3-2-17-2

Tañca maggaṁ na jānanti, ^snp3-2-17-3

Yena gacchanti subbatā. ^snp3-2-17-4

Samantā dhajiniṁ disvā, ^snp3-2-18-1

Yuttaṁ māraṁ savāhanaṁ; ^snp3-2-18-2

Yuddhāya paccuggacchāmi, ^snp3-2-18-3

Mā maṁ ṭhānā acāvayi. ^snp3-2-18-4

Yaṁ te taṁ nappasahati, ^snp3-2-19-1

Senaṁ loko sadevako; ^snp3-2-19-2

Taṁ te paññāya bhecchāmi, ^snp3-2-19-3

Āmaṁ pattaṁva asmanā. ^snp3-2-19-4

Vasīkaritvā saṅkappaṁ, ^snp3-2-20-1

Satiñca sūpatiṭṭhitaṁ; ^snp3-2-20-2

Raṭṭhā raṭṭhaṁ vicarissaṁ, ^snp3-2-20-3

Sāvake vinayaṁ puthū. ^snp3-2-20-4

Te appamattā pahitattā, ^snp3-2-21-1

Mama sāsanakārakā; ^snp3-2-21-2

Akāmassa te gamissanti, ^snp3-2-21-3

Yattha gantvā na socare”. ^snp3-2-21-4

“Satta vassāni bhagavantaṁ, ^snp3-2-22-1

Anubandhiṁ padāpadaṁ; ^snp3-2-22-2

Otāraṁ nādhigacchissaṁ, ^snp3-2-22-3

Sambuddhassa satīmato. ^snp3-2-22-4

Medavaṇṇaṁva pāsāṇaṁ, ^snp3-2-23-1

Vāyaso anupariyagā; ^snp3-2-23-2

Apettha muduṁ vindema, ^snp3-2-23-3

Api assādanā siyā. ^snp3-2-23-4

Aladdhā tattha assādaṁ, ^snp3-2-24-1

Vāyasetto apakkami; ^snp3-2-24-2

Kākova selamāsajja, ^snp3-2-24-3

Nibbijjāpema gotamaṁ”. ^snp3-2-24-4

Tassa sokaparetassa, ^snp3-2-25-1

Vīṇā kacchā abhassatha; ^snp3-2-25-2

Tato so dummano yakkho, ^snp3-2-25-3

Tatthevantaradhāyathāti. ^snp3-2-25-4

Padhānasuttaṁ dutiyaṁ. ^snp3-2-25-5

### Subhāsitasutta (Sutta Nipāta 3.3) ^snp3-3-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp3-3-1-1

eka samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. ^snp3-3-1-2

Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi: ^snp3-3-1-3

“bhikkhavo”ti. ^snp3-3-1-4

“Bhadante”ti te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṁ. ^snp3-3-1-5

Bhagavā etadavoca: ^snp3-3-1-6

“Catūhi, bhikkhave, aṅgehi samannāgatā vācā subhāsitā hoti, na dubbhāsitā, anavajjā ca ananuvajjā ca viññūnaṁ. ^snp3-3-2-1

Katamehi catūhi? ^snp3-3-2-2

Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu subhāsitaṁyeva bhāsati no dubbhāsitaṁ, dhammaṁyeva bhāsati no adhammaṁ, piyaṁyeva bhāsati no appiyaṁ, saccaṁyeva bhāsati no alikaṁ. ^snp3-3-2-3

Imehi kho, bhikkhave, catūhi aṅgehi samannāgatā vācā subhāsitā hoti, no dubbhāsitā, anavajjā ca ananuvajjā ca viññūnan”ti. ^snp3-3-2-4

Idamavoca bhagavā. ^snp3-3-2-5

Idaṁ vatvāna sugato, athāparaṁ etadavoca satthā: ^snp3-3-2-6

“Subhāsitaṁ uttamamāhu santo, ^snp3-3-3-1

Dhammaṁ bhaṇe nādhammaṁ taṁ dutiyaṁ; ^snp3-3-3-2

Piyaṁ bhaṇe nāppiyaṁ taṁ tatiyaṁ, ^snp3-3-3-3

Saccaṁ bhaṇe nālikaṁ taṁ catutthan”ti. ^snp3-3-3-4

Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaṁsaṁ cīvaraṁ katvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṁ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-3-4-1

“paṭibhāti maṁ, bhagavā, paṭibhāti maṁ, sugatā”ti. ^snp3-3-4-2

“Paṭibhātu taṁ, vaṅgīsā”ti bhagavā avoca. ^snp3-3-4-3

Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso bhagavantaṁ sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi: ^snp3-3-4-4

“Tameva vācaṁ bhāseyya, ^snp3-3-5-1

yāyattānaṁ na tāpaye; ^snp3-3-5-2

Pare ca na vihiṁseyya, ^snp3-3-5-3

sā ve vācā subhāsitā. ^snp3-3-5-4

Piyavācameva bhāseyya, ^snp3-3-6-1

yā vācā paṭinanditā; ^snp3-3-6-2

Yaṁ anādāya pāpāni, ^snp3-3-6-3

paresaṁ bhāsate piyaṁ. ^snp3-3-6-4

Saccaṁ ve amatā vācā, ^snp3-3-7-1

esa dhammo sanantano; ^snp3-3-7-2

Sacce atthe ca dhamme ca, ^snp3-3-7-3

āhu santo patiṭṭhitā. ^snp3-3-7-4

Yaṁ buddho bhāsati vācaṁ, ^snp3-3-8-1

Khemaṁ nibbānapattiyā; ^snp3-3-8-2

Dukkhassantakiriyāya, ^snp3-3-8-3

Sā ve vācānamuttamā”ti. ^snp3-3-8-4

Subhāsitasuttaṁ tatiyaṁ. ^snp3-3-8-5

### Pūraḷāsa (sundarikabhāradvāja) sutta (Sutta Nipāta 3.4) ^snp3-4-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp3-4-1-1

ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā kosalesu viharati sundarikāya nadiyā tīre. ^snp3-4-1-2

Tena kho pana samayena sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo sundarikāya nadiyā tīre aggiṁ juhati, aggihuttaṁ paricarati. ^snp3-4-1-3

Atha kho sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo aggiṁ juhitvā aggihuttaṁ paricaritvā uṭṭhāyāsanā samantā catuddisā anuvilokesi: ^snp3-4-1-4

“ko nu kho imaṁ habyasesaṁ bhuñjeyyā”ti? ^snp3-4-1-5

Addasā kho sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṁ avidūre aññatarasmiṁ rukkhamūle sasīsaṁ pārutaṁ nisinnaṁ; ^snp3-4-1-6

disvāna vāmena hatthena habyasesaṁ gahetvā dakkhiṇena hatthena kamaṇḍaluṁ gahetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami. ^snp3-4-1-7

Atha kho bhagavā sundarikabhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa padasaddena sīsaṁ vivari. ^snp3-4-2-1

Atha kho sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo: “muṇḍo ayaṁ bhavaṁ, muṇḍako ayaṁ bhavan”ti tatova puna nivattitukāmo ahosi. ^snp3-4-2-2

Atha kho sundarikabhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa etadahosi: ^snp3-4-2-3

“muṇḍāpi hi idhekacce brāhmaṇā bhavanti, yannūnāhaṁ upasaṅkamitvā jātiṁ puccheyyan”ti. ^snp3-4-2-4

Atha kho sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-4-2-5

“kiṁjacco bhavan”ti? ^snp3-4-2-6

Atha kho bhagavā sundarikabhāradvājaṁ brāhmaṇaṁ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi: ^snp3-4-3-1

“Na brāhmaṇo nomhi na rājaputto, ^snp3-4-4-1

Na vessāyano uda koci nomhi; ^snp3-4-4-2

Gottaṁ pariññāya puthujjanānaṁ, ^snp3-4-4-3

Akiñcano manta carāmi loke. ^snp3-4-4-4

Saṅghāṭivāsī agaho carāmi, ^snp3-4-5-1

Nivuttakeso abhinibbutatto; ^snp3-4-5-2

Alippamāno idha māṇavehi, ^snp3-4-5-3

Akallaṁ maṁ brāhmaṇa pucchasi gottapañhaṁ”. ^snp3-4-5-4

“Pucchanti ve bho brāhmaṇā brāhmaṇebhi, ^snp3-4-6-1

Saha brāhmaṇo no bhavan”ti. ^snp3-4-6-2

“Brāhmaṇo hi ce tvaṁ brūsi, ^snp3-4-7-1

Mañca brūsi abrāhmaṇaṁ; ^snp3-4-7-2

Taṁ taṁ sāvittiṁ pucchāmi, ^snp3-4-7-3

Tipadaṁ catuvīsatakkharaṁ”. ^snp3-4-7-4

“Kiṁ nissitā isayo manujā, ^snp3-4-8-1

Khattiyā brāhmaṇā devatānaṁ; ^snp3-4-8-2

Yaññamakappayiṁsu puthū idha loke”. ^snp3-4-8-3

“Yadantagū vedagū yaññakāle, ^snp3-4-9-1

Yassāhutiṁ labhe tassijjheti brūmi”. ^snp3-4-9-2

“Addhā hi tassa hutamijjhe, ^snp3-4-10-1

(iti brāhmaṇo) ^snp3-4-10-2

Yaṁ tādisaṁ vedagumaddasāma; ^snp3-4-10-3

Tumhādisānañhi adassanena, ^snp3-4-10-4

Añño jano bhuñjati pūraḷāsaṁ”. ^snp3-4-10-5

“Tasmātiha tvaṁ brāhmaṇa atthena, ^snp3-4-11-1

Atthiko upasaṅkamma puccha; ^snp3-4-11-2

Santaṁ vidhūmaṁ anīghaṁ nirāsaṁ, ^snp3-4-11-3

Appevidha abhivinde sumedhaṁ”. ^snp3-4-11-4

“Yaññe ratohaṁ bho gotama, ^snp3-4-12-1

Yaññaṁ yiṭṭhukāmo nāhaṁ pajānāmi; ^snp3-4-12-2

Anusāsatu maṁ bhavaṁ, ^snp3-4-12-3

Yattha hutaṁ ijjhate brūhi me taṁ”. ^snp3-4-12-4

“Tena hi tvaṁ, brāhmaṇa, odahassu sotaṁ; dhammaṁ te desessāmi— ^snp3-4-13-1

Mā jātiṁ pucchī caraṇañca puccha, ^snp3-4-14-1

Kaṭṭhā have jāyati jātavedo; ^snp3-4-14-2

Nīcākulīnopi munī dhitīmā, ^snp3-4-14-3

Ājāniyo hoti hirīnisedho. ^snp3-4-14-4

Saccena danto damasā upeto, ^snp3-4-15-1

Vedantagū vūsitabrahmacariyo; ^snp3-4-15-2

Kālena tamhi habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-4-15-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-4-15-4

Ye kāme hitvā agahā caranti, ^snp3-4-16-1

Susaññatattā tasaraṁva ujjuṁ; ^snp3-4-16-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-4-16-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-4-16-4

Ye vītarāgā susamāhitindriyā, ^snp3-4-17-1

Candova rāhuggahaṇā pamuttā; ^snp3-4-17-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-4-17-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-4-17-4

Asajjamānā vicaranti loke, ^snp3-4-18-1

Sadā satā hitvā mamāyitāni; ^snp3-4-18-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-4-18-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-4-18-4

Yo kāme hitvā abhibhuyyacārī, ^snp3-4-19-1

Yo vedi jātīmaraṇassa antaṁ; ^snp3-4-19-2

Parinibbuto udakarahadova sīto, ^snp3-4-19-3

Tathāgato arahati pūraḷāsaṁ. ^snp3-4-19-4

Samo samehi visamehi dūre, ^snp3-4-20-1

Tathāgato hoti anantapañño; ^snp3-4-20-2

Anūpalitto idha vā huraṁ vā, ^snp3-4-20-3

Tathāgato arahati pūraḷāsaṁ. ^snp3-4-20-4

Yamhi na māyā vasati na māno, ^snp3-4-21-1

Yo vītalobho amamo nirāso; ^snp3-4-21-2

Paṇunnakodho abhinibbutatto, ^snp3-4-21-3

Yo brāhmaṇo sokamalaṁ ahāsi; ^snp3-4-21-4

Tathāgato arahati pūraḷāsaṁ. ^snp3-4-21-5

Nivesanaṁ yo manaso ahāsi, ^snp3-4-22-1

Pariggahā yassa na santi keci; ^snp3-4-22-2

Anupādiyāno idha vā huraṁ vā, ^snp3-4-22-3

Tathāgato arahati pūraḷāsaṁ. ^snp3-4-22-4

Samāhito yo udatāri oghaṁ, ^snp3-4-23-1

Dhammaṁ caññāsi paramāya diṭṭhiyā; ^snp3-4-23-2

Khīṇāsavo antimadehadhārī, ^snp3-4-23-3

Tathāgato arahati pūraḷāsaṁ. ^snp3-4-23-4

Bhavāsavā yassa vacī kharā ca, ^snp3-4-24-1

Vidhūpitā atthagatā na santi; ^snp3-4-24-2

Sa vedagū sabbadhi vippamutto, ^snp3-4-24-3

Tathāgato arahati pūraḷāsaṁ. ^snp3-4-24-4

Saṅgātigo yassa na santi saṅgā, ^snp3-4-25-1

Yo mānasattesu amānasatto; ^snp3-4-25-2

Dukkhaṁ pariññāya sakhettavatthuṁ, ^snp3-4-25-3

Tathāgato arahati pūraḷāsaṁ. ^snp3-4-25-4

Āsaṁ anissāya vivekadassī, ^snp3-4-26-1

Paravediyaṁ diṭṭhimupātivatto; ^snp3-4-26-2

Ārammaṇā yassa na santi keci, ^snp3-4-26-3

Tathāgato arahati pūraḷāsaṁ. ^snp3-4-26-4

Paroparā yassa samecca dhammā, ^snp3-4-27-1

Vidhūpitā atthagatā na santi; ^snp3-4-27-2

Santo upādānakhaye vimutto, ^snp3-4-27-3

Tathāgato arahati pūraḷāsaṁ. ^snp3-4-27-4

Saṁyojanaṁ jātikhayantadassī, ^snp3-4-28-1

Yopānudi rāgapathaṁ asesaṁ; ^snp3-4-28-2

Suddho nidoso vimalo akāco, ^snp3-4-28-3

Tathāgato arahati pūraḷāsaṁ. ^snp3-4-28-4

Yo attano attānaṁ nānupassati, ^snp3-4-29-1

Samāhito ujjugato ṭhitatto; ^snp3-4-29-2

Sa ve anejo akhilo akaṅkho, ^snp3-4-29-3

Tathāgato arahati pūraḷāsaṁ. ^snp3-4-29-4

Mohantarā yassa na santi keci, ^snp3-4-30-1

Sabbesu dhammesu ca ñāṇadassī; ^snp3-4-30-2

Sarīrañca antimaṁ dhāreti, ^snp3-4-30-3

Patto ca sambodhimanuttaraṁ sivaṁ; ^snp3-4-30-4

Ettāvatā yakkhassa suddhi, ^snp3-4-30-5

Tathāgato arahati pūraḷāsaṁ”. ^snp3-4-30-6

“Hutañca mayhaṁ hutamatthu saccaṁ, ^snp3-4-31-1

Yaṁ tādisaṁ vedagunaṁ alatthaṁ; ^snp3-4-31-2

Brahmā hi sakkhi paṭigaṇhātu me bhagavā, ^snp3-4-31-3

Bhuñjatu me bhagavā pūraḷāsaṁ”. ^snp3-4-31-4

“Gāthābhigītaṁ me abhojaneyyaṁ, ^snp3-4-32-1

Sampassataṁ brāhmaṇa nesa dhammo; ^snp3-4-32-2

Gāthābhigītaṁ panudanti buddhā, ^snp3-4-32-3

Dhamme satī brāhmaṇa vuttiresā. ^snp3-4-32-4

Aññena ca kevalinaṁ mahesiṁ, ^snp3-4-33-1

Khīṇāsavaṁ kukkuccavūpasantaṁ; ^snp3-4-33-2

Annena pānena upaṭṭhahassu, ^snp3-4-33-3

Khettañhi taṁ puññapekkhassa hoti”. ^snp3-4-33-4

“Sādhāhaṁ bhagavā tathā vijaññaṁ, ^snp3-4-34-1

Yo dakkhiṇaṁ bhuñjeyya mādisassa; ^snp3-4-34-2

Yaṁ yaññakāle pariyesamāno, ^snp3-4-34-3

Pappuyya tava sāsanaṁ”. ^snp3-4-34-4

“Sārambhā yassa vigatā, ^snp3-4-35-1

Cittaṁ yassa anāvilaṁ; ^snp3-4-35-2

Vippamutto ca kāmehi, ^snp3-4-35-3

Thinaṁ yassa panūditaṁ. ^snp3-4-35-4

Sīmantānaṁ vinetāraṁ, ^snp3-4-36-1

Jātimaraṇakovidaṁ; ^snp3-4-36-2

Muniṁ moneyyasampannaṁ, ^snp3-4-36-3

Tādisaṁ yaññamāgataṁ. ^snp3-4-36-4

Bhakuṭiṁ vinayitvāna, ^snp3-4-37-1

Pañjalikā namassatha; ^snp3-4-37-2

Pūjetha annapānena, ^snp3-4-37-3

Evaṁ ijjhanti dakkhiṇā”. ^snp3-4-37-4

“Buddho bhavaṁ arahati pūraḷāsaṁ, ^snp3-4-38-1

Puññakhettamanuttaraṁ; ^snp3-4-38-2

Āyāgo sabbalokassa, ^snp3-4-38-3

Bhoto dinnaṁ mahapphalan”ti. ^snp3-4-38-4

Atha kho sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-4-39-1

“abhikkantaṁ, bho gotama, abhikkantaṁ, bho gotama. ^snp3-4-39-2

Seyyathāpi, bho gotama, nikkujjitaṁ vā ukkujjeyya, paṭicchannaṁ vā vivareyya, mūḷhassa vā maggaṁ ācikkheyya, andhakāre vā telapajjotaṁ dhāreyya: ‘cakkhumanto rūpāni dakkhantī’ti; evamevaṁ bhotā gotamena anekapariyāyena dhammo pakāsito. ^snp3-4-39-3

Esāhaṁ bhavantaṁ gotamaṁ saraṇaṁ gacchāmi dhammañca bhikkhusaṅghañca. ^snp3-4-39-4

Labheyyāhaṁ bhoto gotamassa santike pabbajjaṁ, labheyyaṁ upasampadan”ti. ^snp3-4-39-5

Alattha kho sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo …pe… ^snp3-4-39-6

arahataṁ ahosīti. ^snp3-4-39-7

Sundarikabhāradvājasuttaṁ catutthaṁ. ^snp3-4-39-8

### Māghasutta (Sutta Nipāta 3.5) ^snp3-5-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp3-5-1-1

ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā rājagahe viharati gijjhakūṭe pabbate. ^snp3-5-1-2

Atha kho māgho māṇavo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṁ sammodi. ^snp3-5-1-3

Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. ^snp3-5-1-4

Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho māgho māṇavo bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-5-1-5

“Ahañhi, bho gotama, dāyako dānapati vadaññū yācayogo; ^snp3-5-2-1

dhammena bhoge pariyesāmi; ^snp3-5-2-2

dhammena bhoge pariyesitvā dhammaladdhehi bhogehi dhammādhigatehi ekassapi dadāmi dvinnampi tiṇṇampi catunnampi pañcannampi channampi sattannampi aṭṭhannampi navannampi dasannampi dadāmi, vīsāyapi tiṁsāyapi cattālīsāyapi paññāsāyapi dadāmi, satassapi dadāmi, bhiyyopi dadāmi. ^snp3-5-2-3

Kaccāhaṁ, bho gotama, evaṁ dadanto evaṁ yajanto bahuṁ puññaṁ pasavāmī”ti? ^snp3-5-2-4

“Taggha tvaṁ, māṇava, evaṁ dadanto evaṁ yajanto bahuṁ puññaṁ pasavasi. ^snp3-5-3-1

Yo kho, māṇava, dāyako dānapati vadaññū yācayogo; ^snp3-5-3-2

dhammena bhoge pariyesati; ^snp3-5-3-3

dhammena bhoge pariyesitvā dhammaladdhehi bhogehi dhammādhigatehi ekassapi dadāti …pe… satassapi dadāti, bhiyyopi dadāti, bahuṁ so puññaṁ pasavatī”ti. ^snp3-5-3-4

Atha kho māgho māṇavo bhagavantaṁ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi— ^snp3-5-3-5

“Pucchāmahaṁ gotamaṁ vadaññuṁ, ^snp3-5-4-1

(iti māgho māṇavo) ^snp3-5-4-2

Kāsāyavāsiṁ agahaṁ carantaṁ; ^snp3-5-4-3

Yo yācayogo dānapati gahaṭṭho, ^snp3-5-4-4

Puññatthiko yajati puññapekkho; ^snp3-5-4-5

Dadaṁ paresaṁ idha annapānaṁ, ^snp3-5-4-6

Kathaṁ hutaṁ yajamānassa sujjhe”. ^snp3-5-4-7

“Yo yācayogo dānapati gahaṭṭho, ^snp3-5-5-1

(māghāti bhagavā) ^snp3-5-5-2

Puññatthiko yajati puññapekkho; ^snp3-5-5-3

Dadaṁ paresaṁ idha annapānaṁ, ^snp3-5-5-4

Ārādhaye dakkhiṇeyyebhi tādi”. ^snp3-5-5-5

“Yo yācayogo dānapati gahaṭṭho, ^snp3-5-6-1

(iti māgho māṇavo) ^snp3-5-6-2

Puññatthiko yajati puññapekkho; ^snp3-5-6-3

Dadaṁ paresaṁ idha annapānaṁ, ^snp3-5-6-4

Akkhāhi me bhagavā dakkhiṇeyye”. ^snp3-5-6-5

“Ye ve asattā vicaranti loke, ^snp3-5-7-1

Akiñcanā kevalino yatattā; ^snp3-5-7-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-5-7-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-5-7-4

Ye sabbasaṁyojanabandhanacchidā, ^snp3-5-8-1

Dantā vimuttā anīghā nirāsā; ^snp3-5-8-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-5-8-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-5-8-4

Ye sabbasaṁyojanavippamuttā, ^snp3-5-9-1

Dantā vimuttā anīghā nirāsā; ^snp3-5-9-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-5-9-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-5-9-4

Rāgañca dosañca pahāya mohaṁ, ^snp3-5-10-1

Khīṇāsavā vūsitabrahmacariyā; ^snp3-5-10-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-5-10-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-5-10-4

Yesu na māyā vasati na māno, ^snp3-5-11-1

Khīṇāsavā vūsitabrahmacariyā; ^snp3-5-11-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-5-11-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-5-11-4

Ye vītalobhā amamā nirāsā, ^snp3-5-12-1

Khīṇāsavā vūsitabrahmacariyā; ^snp3-5-12-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-5-12-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-5-12-4

Ye ve na taṇhāsu upātipannā, ^snp3-5-13-1

Vitareyya oghaṁ amamā caranti; ^snp3-5-13-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-5-13-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-5-13-4

Yesaṁ taṇhā natthi kuhiñci loke, ^snp3-5-14-1

Bhavābhavāya idha vā huraṁ vā; ^snp3-5-14-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-5-14-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-5-14-4

Ye kāme hitvā agahā caranti, ^snp3-5-15-1

Susaññatattā tasaraṁva ujjuṁ; ^snp3-5-15-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-5-15-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-5-15-4

Ye vītarāgā susamāhitindriyā, ^snp3-5-16-1

Candova rāhuggahaṇā pamuttā; ^snp3-5-16-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-5-16-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-5-16-4

Samitāvino vītarāgā akopā, ^snp3-5-17-1

Yesaṁ gatī natthidha vippahāya; ^snp3-5-17-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-5-17-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-5-17-4

Jahitvā jātimaraṇaṁ asesaṁ, ^snp3-5-18-1

Kathaṅkathiṁ sabbamupātivattā; ^snp3-5-18-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-5-18-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-5-18-4

Ye attadīpā vicaranti loke, ^snp3-5-19-1

Akiñcanā sabbadhi vippamuttā; ^snp3-5-19-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-5-19-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-5-19-4

Ye hettha jānanti yathā tathā idaṁ, ^snp3-5-20-1

Ayamantimā natthi punabbhavoti; ^snp3-5-20-2

Kālena tesu habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-5-20-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha. ^snp3-5-20-4

Yo vedagū jhānarato satīmā, ^snp3-5-21-1

Sambodhipatto saraṇaṁ bahūnaṁ; ^snp3-5-21-2

Kālena tamhi habyaṁ pavecche, ^snp3-5-21-3

Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekkho yajetha”. ^snp3-5-21-4

“Addhā amoghā mama pucchanā ahu, ^snp3-5-22-1

(iti māgho māṇavo) ^snp3-5-22-2

Akkhāsi me bhagavā dakkhiṇeyye; ^snp3-5-22-3

Tvañhettha jānāsi yathā tathā idaṁ, ^snp3-5-22-4

Tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo. ^snp3-5-22-5

Yo yācayogo dānapati gahaṭṭho, ^snp3-5-23-1

Puññatthiko yajati puññapekkho; ^snp3-5-23-2

Dadaṁ paresaṁ idha annapānaṁ, ^snp3-5-23-3

Akkhāhi me bhagavā yaññasampadaṁ”. ^snp3-5-23-4

“Yajassu yajamāno, ^snp3-5-24-1

(māghāti bhagavā) ^snp3-5-24-2

Sabbattha ca vippasādehi cittaṁ; ^snp3-5-24-3

Ārammaṇaṁ yajamānassa yañño, ^snp3-5-24-4

Ettha patiṭṭhāya jahāti dosaṁ. ^snp3-5-24-5

So vītarāgo pavineyya dosaṁ, ^snp3-5-25-1

Mettaṁ cittaṁ bhāvayamappamāṇaṁ; ^snp3-5-25-2

Rattindivaṁ satatamappamatto, ^snp3-5-25-3

Sabbā disā pharati appamaññaṁ”. ^snp3-5-25-4

“Ko sujjhati muccati bajjhatī ca, ^snp3-5-26-1

Kenattanā gacchati brahmalokaṁ; ^snp3-5-26-2

Ajānato me muni brūhi puṭṭho, ^snp3-5-26-3

Bhagavā hi me sakkhi brahmajjadiṭṭho; ^snp3-5-26-4

Tuvañhi no brahmasamosi saccaṁ, ^snp3-5-26-5

Kathaṁ upapajjati brahmalokaṁ jutima”. ^snp3-5-26-6

“Yo yajati tividhaṁ yaññasampadaṁ, ^snp3-5-27-1

(māghāti bhagavā) ^snp3-5-27-2

Ārādhaye dakkhiṇeyyebhi tādi; ^snp3-5-27-3

Evaṁ yajitvā sammā yācayogo, ^snp3-5-27-4

Upapajjati brahmalokanti brūmī”ti. ^snp3-5-27-5

Evaṁ vutte, māgho māṇavo bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-5-28-1

“abhikkantaṁ, bho gotama …pe… ^snp3-5-28-2

ajjatagge pāṇupetaṁ saraṇaṁ gatan”ti. ^snp3-5-28-3

Māghasuttaṁ pañcamaṁ. ^snp3-5-28-4

### Sabhiyasutta (Sutta Nipāta 3.6) ^snp3-6-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp3-6-1-1

ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. ^snp3-6-1-2

Tena kho pana samayena sabhiyassa paribbājakassa purāṇasālohitāya devatāya pañhā uddiṭṭhā honti: ^snp3-6-1-3

“yo te, sabhiya, samaṇo vā brāhmaṇo vā ime pañhe puṭṭho byākaroti tassa santike brahmacariyaṁ careyyāsī”ti. ^snp3-6-1-4

Atha kho sabhiyo paribbājako tassā devatāya santike te pañhe uggahetvā ye te samaṇabrāhmaṇā saṅghino gaṇino gaṇācariyā ñātā yasassino titthakarā sādhusammatā bahujanassa, seyyathidaṁ— ^snp3-6-2-1

pūraṇo kassapo makkhaligosālo ajito kesakambalo pakudho kaccāno sañcayo belaṭṭhaputto nigaṇṭho nāṭaputto— ^snp3-6-2-2

te upasaṅkamitvā te pañhe pucchati. ^snp3-6-2-3

Te sabhiyena paribbājakena pañhe puṭṭhā na sampāyanti; ^snp3-6-2-4

asampāyantā kopañca dosañca appaccayañca pātukaronti. ^snp3-6-2-5

Api ca sabhiyaṁyeva paribbājakaṁ paṭipucchanti. ^snp3-6-2-6

Atha kho sabhiyassa paribbājakassa etadahosi: ^snp3-6-3-1

“ye kho te bhonto samaṇabrāhmaṇā saṅghino gaṇino gaṇācariyā ñātā yasassino titthakarā sādhusammatā bahujanassa, seyyathidaṁ— ^snp3-6-3-2

pūraṇo kassapo …pe… nigaṇṭho nāṭaputto— ^snp3-6-3-3

te mayā pañhe puṭṭhā na sampāyanti, ^snp3-6-3-4

asampāyantā kopañca dosañca appaccayañca pātukaronti; ^snp3-6-3-5

api ca maññevettha paṭipucchanti. ^snp3-6-3-6

Yannūnāhaṁ hīnāyāvattitvā kāme paribhuñjeyyan”ti. ^snp3-6-3-7

Atha kho sabhiyassa paribbājakassa etadahosi: ^snp3-6-4-1

“ayampi kho samaṇo gotamo saṅghī ceva gaṇī ca gaṇācariyo ca ñāto yasassī titthakaro sādhusammato bahujanassa; ^snp3-6-4-2

yannūnāhaṁ samaṇaṁ gotamaṁ upasaṅkamitvā ime pañhe puccheyyan”ti. ^snp3-6-4-3

Atha kho sabhiyassa paribbājakassa etadahosi: ^snp3-6-5-1

“yepi kho te bhonto samaṇabrāhmaṇā jiṇṇā vuḍḍhā mahallakā addhagatā vayoanuppattā therā rattaññū cirapabbajitā saṅghino gaṇino gaṇācariyā ñātā yasassino titthakarā sādhusammatā bahujanassa, seyyathidaṁ— ^snp3-6-5-2

pūraṇo kassapo …pe… nigaṇṭho nāṭaputto— ^snp3-6-5-3

tepi mayā pañhe puṭṭhā na sampāyanti, ^snp3-6-5-4

asampāyantā kopañca dosañca appaccayañca pātukaronti, api ca maññevettha paṭipucchanti; ^snp3-6-5-5

kiṁ pana me samaṇo gotamo ime pañhe puṭṭho byākarissati. ^snp3-6-5-6

Samaṇo hi gotamo daharo ceva jātiyā, navo ca pabbajjāyā”ti. ^snp3-6-5-7

Atha kho sabhiyassa paribbājakassa etadahosi: ^snp3-6-6-1

“samaṇo kho daharoti na uññātabbo na paribhotabbo. ^snp3-6-6-2

Daharopi cesa samaṇo gotamo mahiddhiko hoti mahānubhāvo, yannūnāhaṁ samaṇaṁ gotamaṁ upasaṅkamitvā ime pañhe puccheyyan”ti. ^snp3-6-6-3

Atha kho sabhiyo paribbājako yena rājagahaṁ tena cārikaṁ pakkāmi. ^snp3-6-7-1

Anupubbena cārikaṁ caramāno yena rājagahaṁ veḷuvanaṁ kalandakanivāpo, yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṁ sammodi. ^snp3-6-7-2

Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. ^snp3-6-7-3

Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho sabhiyo paribbājako bhagavantaṁ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi— ^snp3-6-7-4

“Kaṅkhī vecikicchī āgamaṁ, ^snp3-6-8-1

(iti sabhiyo) ^snp3-6-8-2

Pañhe pucchituṁ abhikaṅkhamāno; ^snp3-6-8-3

Tesantakaro bhavāhi pañhe me puṭṭho, ^snp3-6-8-4

Anupubbaṁ anudhammaṁ byākarohi me”. ^snp3-6-8-5

“Dūrato āgatosi sabhiya, ^snp3-6-9-1

(iti bhagavā) ^snp3-6-9-2

Pañhe pucchituṁ abhikaṅkhamāno; ^snp3-6-9-3

Tesantakaro bhavāmi pañhe te puṭṭho, ^snp3-6-9-4

Anupubbaṁ anudhammaṁ byākaromi te. ^snp3-6-9-5

Puccha maṁ sabhiya pañhaṁ, ^snp3-6-10-1

Yaṁ kiñci manasicchasi; ^snp3-6-10-2

Tassa tasseva pañhassa, ^snp3-6-10-3

Ahaṁ antaṁ karomi te”ti. ^snp3-6-10-4

Atha kho sabhiyassa paribbājakassa etadahosi: ^snp3-6-11-1

“acchariyaṁ vata bho, abbhutaṁ vata bho. ^snp3-6-11-2

Yaṁ vatāhaṁ aññesu samaṇabrāhmaṇesu okāsakammamattampi nālatthaṁ taṁ me idaṁ samaṇena gotamena okāsakammaṁ katan”ti. ^snp3-6-11-3

Attamano pamudito udaggo pītisomanassajāto bhagavantaṁ pañhaṁ apucchi— ^snp3-6-11-4

“Kiṁpattinamāhu bhikkhunaṁ, ^snp3-6-12-1

(iti sabhiyo) ^snp3-6-12-2

Sorataṁ kena kathañca dantamāhu; ^snp3-6-12-3

Buddhoti kathaṁ pavuccati, ^snp3-6-12-4

Puṭṭho me bhagavā byākarohi”. ^snp3-6-12-5

“Pajjena katena attanā, ^snp3-6-13-1

(sabhiyāti bhagavā) ^snp3-6-13-2

Parinibbānagato vitiṇṇakaṅkho; ^snp3-6-13-3

Vibhavañca bhavañca vippahāya, ^snp3-6-13-4

Vusitavā khīṇapunabbhavo sa bhikkhu. ^snp3-6-13-5

Sabbattha upekkhako satimā, ^snp3-6-14-1

Na so hiṁsati kañci sabbaloke; ^snp3-6-14-2

Tiṇṇo samaṇo anāvilo, ^snp3-6-14-3

Ussadā yassa na santi sorato so. ^snp3-6-14-4

Yassindriyāni bhāvitāni, ^snp3-6-15-1

Ajjhattaṁ bahiddhā ca sabbaloke; ^snp3-6-15-2

Nibbijjha imaṁ parañca lokaṁ, ^snp3-6-15-3

Kālaṁ kaṅkhati bhāvito sa danto. ^snp3-6-15-4

Kappāni viceyya kevalāni, ^snp3-6-16-1

Saṁsāraṁ dubhayaṁ cutūpapātaṁ; ^snp3-6-16-2

Vigatarajamanaṅgaṇaṁ visuddhaṁ, ^snp3-6-16-3

Pattaṁ jātikhayaṁ tamāhu buddhan”ti. ^snp3-6-16-4

Atha kho sabhiyo paribbājako bhagavato bhāsitaṁ abhinanditvā anumoditvā attamano pamudito udaggo pītisomanassajāto bhagavantaṁ uttariṁ pañhaṁ apucchi— ^snp3-6-17-1

“Kiṁpattinamāhu brāhmaṇaṁ, ^snp3-6-18-1

(iti sabhiyo) ^snp3-6-18-2

Samaṇaṁ kena kathañca nhātakoti; ^snp3-6-18-3

Nāgoti kathaṁ pavuccati, ^snp3-6-18-4

Puṭṭho me bhagavā byākarohi”. ^snp3-6-18-5

“Bāhitvā sabbapāpakāni, ^snp3-6-19-1

(sabhiyāti bhagavā) ^snp3-6-19-2

Vimalo sādhusamāhito ṭhitatto; ^snp3-6-19-3

Saṁsāramaticca kevalī so, ^snp3-6-19-4

Asito tādi pavuccate sa brahmā. ^snp3-6-19-5

Samitāvi pahāya puññapāpaṁ, ^snp3-6-20-1

Virajo ñatvā imaṁ parañca lokaṁ; ^snp3-6-20-2

Jātimaraṇaṁ upātivatto, ^snp3-6-20-3

Samaṇo tādi pavuccate tathattā. ^snp3-6-20-4

Ninhāya sabbapāpakāni, ^snp3-6-21-1

Ajjhattaṁ bahiddhā ca sabbaloke; ^snp3-6-21-2

Devamanussesu kappiyesu, ^snp3-6-21-3

Kappaṁ neti tamāhu nhātakoti. ^snp3-6-21-4

Āguṁ na karoti kiñci loke, ^snp3-6-22-1

Sabbasaṁyoge visajja bandhanāni; ^snp3-6-22-2

Sabbattha na sajjatī vimutto, ^snp3-6-22-3

Nāgo tādi pavuccate tathattā”ti. ^snp3-6-22-4

Atha kho sabhiyo paribbājako …pe… bhagavantaṁ uttariṁ pañhaṁ apucchi— ^snp3-6-23-1

“Kaṁ khettajinaṁ vadanti buddhā, ^snp3-6-24-1

(iti sabhiyo) ^snp3-6-24-2

Kusalaṁ kena kathañca paṇḍitoti; ^snp3-6-24-3

Muni nāma kathaṁ pavuccati, ^snp3-6-24-4

Puṭṭho me bhagavā byākarohi”. ^snp3-6-24-5

“Khettāni viceyya kevalāni, ^snp3-6-25-1

(sabhiyāti bhagavā) ^snp3-6-25-2

Dibbaṁ mānusakañca brahmakhettaṁ; ^snp3-6-25-3

Sabbakhettamūlabandhanā pamutto, ^snp3-6-25-4

Khettajino tādi pavuccate tathattā. ^snp3-6-25-5

Kosāni viceyya kevalāni, ^snp3-6-26-1

Dibbaṁ mānusakañca brahmakosaṁ; ^snp3-6-26-2

Sabbakosamūlabandhanā pamutto, ^snp3-6-26-3

Kusalo tādi pavuccate tathattā. ^snp3-6-26-4

Dubhayāni viceyya paṇḍarāni, ^snp3-6-27-1

Ajjhattaṁ bahiddhā ca suddhipañño; ^snp3-6-27-2

Kaṇhaṁ sukkaṁ upātivatto, ^snp3-6-27-3

Paṇḍito tādi pavuccate tathattā. ^snp3-6-27-4

Asatañca satañca ñatvā dhammaṁ, ^snp3-6-28-1

Ajjhattaṁ bahiddhā ca sabbaloke; ^snp3-6-28-2

Devamanussehi pūjanīyo, ^snp3-6-28-3

Saṅgaṁ jālamaticca so munī”ti. ^snp3-6-28-4

Atha kho sabhiyo paribbājako …pe… bhagavantaṁ uttariṁ pañhaṁ apucchi— ^snp3-6-29-1

“Kiṁpattinamāhu vedaguṁ, ^snp3-6-30-1

(iti sabhiyo) ^snp3-6-30-2

Anuviditaṁ kena kathañca viriyavāti; ^snp3-6-30-3

Ājāniyo kinti nāma hoti, ^snp3-6-30-4

Puṭṭho me bhagavā byākarohi”. ^snp3-6-30-5

“Vedāni viceyya kevalāni, ^snp3-6-31-1

(sabhiyāti bhagavā) ^snp3-6-31-2

Samaṇānaṁ yānidhatthi brāhmaṇānaṁ; ^snp3-6-31-3

Sabbavedanāsu vītarāgo, ^snp3-6-31-4

Sabbaṁ vedamaticca vedagū so. ^snp3-6-31-5

Anuvicca papañcanāmarūpaṁ, ^snp3-6-32-1

Ajjhattaṁ bahiddhā ca rogamūlaṁ; ^snp3-6-32-2

Sabbarogamūlabandhanā pamutto, ^snp3-6-32-3

Anuvidito tādi pavuccate tathattā. ^snp3-6-32-4

Virato idha sabbapāpakehi, ^snp3-6-33-1

Nirayadukkhaṁ aticca viriyavāso; ^snp3-6-33-2

So vīriyavā padhānavā, ^snp3-6-33-3

Dhīro tādi pavuccate tathattā. ^snp3-6-33-4

Yassassu lunāni bandhanāni, ^snp3-6-34-1

Ajjhattaṁ bahiddhā ca saṅgamūlaṁ; ^snp3-6-34-2

Sabbasaṅgamūlabandhanā pamutto, ^snp3-6-34-3

Ājāniyo tādi pavuccate tathattā”ti. ^snp3-6-34-4

Atha kho sabhiyo paribbājako …pe… bhagavantaṁ uttariṁ pañhaṁ apucchi— ^snp3-6-35-1

“Kiṁpattinamāhu sottiyaṁ, ^snp3-6-36-1

(iti sabhiyo) ^snp3-6-36-2

Ariyaṁ kena kathañca caraṇavāti; ^snp3-6-36-3

Paribbājako kinti nāma hoti, ^snp3-6-36-4

Puṭṭho me bhagavā byākarohi”. ^snp3-6-36-5

“Sutvā sabbadhammaṁ abhiññāya loke, ^snp3-6-37-1

(sabhiyāti bhagavā) ^snp3-6-37-2

Sāvajjānavajjaṁ yadatthi kiñci; ^snp3-6-37-3

Abhibhuṁ akathaṅkathiṁ vimuttaṁ, ^snp3-6-37-4

Anighaṁ sabbadhimāhu sottiyoti. ^snp3-6-37-5

Chetvā āsavāni ālayāni, ^snp3-6-38-1

Vidvā so na upeti gabbhaseyyaṁ; ^snp3-6-38-2

Saññaṁ tividhaṁ panujja paṅkaṁ, ^snp3-6-38-3

Kappaṁ neti tamāhu ariyoti. ^snp3-6-38-4

Yo idha caraṇesu pattipatto, ^snp3-6-39-1

Kusalo sabbadā ājānāti dhammaṁ; ^snp3-6-39-2

Sabbattha na sajjati vimuttacitto, ^snp3-6-39-3

Paṭighā yassa na santi caraṇavā so. ^snp3-6-39-4

Dukkhavepakkaṁ yadatthi kammaṁ, ^snp3-6-40-1

Uddhamadho tiriyaṁ vāpi majjhe; ^snp3-6-40-2

Paribbājayitvā pariññacārī, ^snp3-6-40-3

Māyaṁ mānamathopi lobhakodhaṁ; ^snp3-6-40-4

Pariyantamakāsi nāmarūpaṁ, ^snp3-6-40-5

Taṁ paribbājakamāhu pattipattan”ti. ^snp3-6-40-6

Atha kho sabhiyo paribbājako bhagavato bhāsitaṁ abhinanditvā anumoditvā attamano pamudito udaggo pītisomanassajāto uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaṁsaṁ uttarāsaṅgaṁ karitvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṁ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṁ sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi: ^snp3-6-41-1

“Yāni ca tīṇi yāni ca saṭṭhi, ^snp3-6-42-1

Samaṇappavādasitāni bhūripañña; ^snp3-6-42-2

Saññakkharasaññanissitāni, ^snp3-6-42-3

Osaraṇāni vineyya oghatamagā. ^snp3-6-42-4

Antagūsi pāragū dukkhassa, ^snp3-6-43-1

Arahāsi sammāsambuddho khīṇāsavaṁ taṁ maññe; ^snp3-6-43-2

Jutimā mutimā pahūtapañño, ^snp3-6-43-3

Dukkhassantakara atāresi maṁ. ^snp3-6-43-4

Yaṁ me kaṅkhitamaññāsi, ^snp3-6-44-1

Vicikicchā maṁ tārayi namo te; ^snp3-6-44-2

Muni monapathesu pattipatta, ^snp3-6-44-3

Akhila ādiccabandhu soratosi. ^snp3-6-44-4

Yā me kaṅkhā pure āsi, ^snp3-6-45-1

Taṁ me byākāsi cakkhumā; ^snp3-6-45-2

Addhā munīsi sambuddho, ^snp3-6-45-3

Natthi nīvaraṇā tava. ^snp3-6-45-4

Upāyāsā ca te sabbe, ^snp3-6-46-1

Viddhastā vinaḷīkatā; ^snp3-6-46-2

Sītibhūto damappatto, ^snp3-6-46-3

Dhitimā saccanikkamo. ^snp3-6-46-4

Tassa te nāganāgassa, ^snp3-6-47-1

Mahāvīrassa bhāsato; ^snp3-6-47-2

Sabbe devānumodanti, ^snp3-6-47-3

Ubho nāradapabbatā. ^snp3-6-47-4

Namo te purisājañña, ^snp3-6-48-1

Namo te purisuttama; ^snp3-6-48-2

Sadevakasmiṁ lokasmiṁ, ^snp3-6-48-3

Natthi te paṭipuggalo. ^snp3-6-48-4

Tuvaṁ buddho tuvaṁ satthā, ^snp3-6-49-1

Tuvaṁ mārābhibhū muni; ^snp3-6-49-2

Tuvaṁ anusaye chetvā, ^snp3-6-49-3

Tiṇṇo tāresimaṁ pajaṁ. ^snp3-6-49-4

Upadhī te samatikkantā, ^snp3-6-50-1

Āsavā te padālitā; ^snp3-6-50-2

Sīhosi anupādāno, ^snp3-6-50-3

Pahīnabhayabheravo. ^snp3-6-50-4

Puṇḍarīkaṁ yathā vaggu, ^snp3-6-51-1

Toye na upalimpati; ^snp3-6-51-2

Evaṁ puññe ca pāpe ca, ^snp3-6-51-3

Ubhaye tvaṁ na limpasi; ^snp3-6-51-4

Pāde vīra pasārehi, ^snp3-6-51-5

Sabhiyo vandati satthuno”ti. ^snp3-6-51-6

Atha kho sabhiyo paribbājako bhagavato pādesu sirasā nipatitvā bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-6-52-1

“abhikkantaṁ, bhante …pe… ^snp3-6-52-2

esāhaṁ bhagavantaṁ saraṇaṁ gacchāmi dhammañca bhikkhusaṅghañca; ^snp3-6-52-3

labheyyāhaṁ, bhante, bhagavato santike pabbajjaṁ, labheyyaṁ upasampadan”ti. ^snp3-6-52-4

“Yo kho, sabhiya, aññatitthiyapubbo imasmiṁ dhammavinaye ākaṅkhati pabbajjaṁ, ākaṅkhati upasampadaṁ, so cattāro māse parivasati; catunnaṁ māsānaṁ accayena āraddhacittā bhikkhū pabbājenti, upasampādenti bhikkhubhāvāya. ^snp3-6-53-1

Api ca mettha puggalavemattatā viditā”ti. ^snp3-6-53-2

“Sace, bhante, aññatitthiyapubbā imasmiṁ dhammavinaye ākaṅkhantā pabbajjaṁ, ākaṅkhantā upasampadaṁ cattāro māse parivasanti, catunnaṁ māsānaṁ accayena āraddhacittā bhikkhū pabbājenti, upasampādenti bhikkhubhāvāya, ahaṁ cattāri vassāni parivasissāmi; catunnaṁ vassānaṁ accayena āraddhacittā bhikkhū pabbājentu upasampādentu bhikkhubhāvāyā”ti. ^snp3-6-54-1

Alattha kho sabhiyo paribbājako bhagavato santike pabbajjaṁ alattha upasampadaṁ …pe… ^snp3-6-54-2

aññataro kho panāyasmā sabhiyo arahataṁ ahosīti. ^snp3-6-54-3

Sabhiyasuttaṁ chaṭṭhaṁ. ^snp3-6-54-4

### Selasutta (Sutta Nipāta 3.7) ^snp3-7-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp3-7-1-1

ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā aṅguttarāpesu cārikaṁ caramāno mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena saddhiṁ aḍḍhateḷasehi bhikkhusatehi yena āpaṇaṁ nāma aṅguttarāpānaṁ nigamo tadavasari. ^snp3-7-1-2

Assosi kho keṇiyo jaṭilo: ^snp3-7-1-3

“samaṇo khalu, bho, gotamo sakyaputto sakyakulā pabbajito aṅguttarāpesu cārikaṁ caramāno mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena saddhiṁ aḍḍhateḷasehi bhikkhusatehi āpaṇaṁ anuppatto. ^snp3-7-1-4

Taṁ kho pana bhavantaṁ gotamaṁ evaṁ kalyāṇo kittisaddo abbhuggato: ^snp3-7-1-5

‘itipi so bhagavā arahaṁ sammāsambuddho vijjācaraṇasampanno sugato lokavidū anuttaro purisadammasārathi satthā devamanussānaṁ buddho bhagavā’ti. ^snp3-7-1-6

So imaṁ lokaṁ sadevakaṁ samārakaṁ sabrahmakaṁ sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiṁ pajaṁ sadevamanussaṁ sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā pavedeti. ^snp3-7-1-7

So dhammaṁ deseti ādikalyāṇaṁ majjhekalyāṇaṁ pariyosānakalyāṇaṁ sātthaṁ sabyañjanaṁ, kevalaparipuṇṇaṁ parisuddhaṁ brahmacariyaṁ pakāseti. ^snp3-7-1-8

Sādhu kho pana tathārūpānaṁ arahataṁ dassanaṁ hotī”ti. ^snp3-7-1-9

Atha kho keṇiyo jaṭilo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṁ sammodi. ^snp3-7-2-1

Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. ^snp3-7-2-2

Ekamantaṁ nisinnaṁ kho keṇiyaṁ jaṭilaṁ bhagavā dhammiyā kathāya sandassesi samādapesi samuttejesi sampahaṁsesi. ^snp3-7-2-3

Atha kho keṇiyo jaṭilo bhagavatā dhammiyā kathāya sandassito samādapito samuttejito sampahaṁsito bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-7-2-4

“adhivāsetu me bhavaṁ gotamo svātanāya bhattaṁ saddhiṁ bhikkhusaṅghenā”ti. ^snp3-7-2-5

Evaṁ vutte, bhagavā keṇiyaṁ jaṭilaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-7-2-6

“mahā kho, keṇiya, bhikkhusaṅgho aḍḍhateḷasāni bhikkhusatāni; tvañca brāhmaṇesu abhippasanno”ti. ^snp3-7-2-7

Dutiyampi kho keṇiyo jaṭilo bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-7-3-1

“kiñcāpi, bho gotama, mahā bhikkhusaṅgho aḍḍhateḷasāni bhikkhusatāni, ahañca brāhmaṇesu abhippasanno; ^snp3-7-3-2

adhivāsetu me bhavaṁ gotamo svātanāya bhattaṁ saddhiṁ bhikkhusaṅghenā”ti. ^snp3-7-3-3

Dutiyampi kho bhagavā keṇiyaṁ jaṭilaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-7-3-4

“mahā kho, keṇiya, bhikkhusaṅgho aḍḍhateḷasāni bhikkhusatāni; tvañca brāhmaṇesu abhippasanno”ti. ^snp3-7-3-5

Tatiyampi kho keṇiyo jaṭilo bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-7-4-1

“kiñcāpi, bho gotama, mahā bhikkhusaṅgho aḍḍhateḷasāni bhikkhusatāni, ahañca brāhmaṇesu abhippasanno, ^snp3-7-4-2

adhivāsetu me bhavaṁ gotamo svātanāya bhattaṁ saddhiṁ bhikkhusaṅghenā”ti. ^snp3-7-4-3

Adhivāsesi bhagavā tuṇhībhāvena. ^snp3-7-4-4

Atha kho keṇiyo jaṭilo bhagavato adhivāsanaṁ viditvā uṭṭhāyāsanā yena sako assamo tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā mittāmacce ñātisālohite āmantesi: ^snp3-7-4-5

“suṇantu me bhavanto mittāmaccā ñātisālohitā, ^snp3-7-4-6

samaṇo me gotamo nimantito svātanāya bhattaṁ saddhiṁ bhikkhusaṅghena, ^snp3-7-4-7

yena me kāyaveyyāvaṭikaṁ kareyyāthā”ti. ^snp3-7-4-8

“Evaṁ, bho”ti kho keṇiyassa jaṭilassa mittāmaccā ñātisālohitā keṇiyassa jaṭilassa paṭissutvā appekacce uddhanāni khaṇanti, appekacce kaṭṭhāni phālenti, appekacce bhājanāni dhovanti, appekacce udakamaṇikaṁ patiṭṭhāpenti, appekacce āsanāni paññāpenti. ^snp3-7-4-9

Keṇiyo pana jaṭilo sāmaṁyeva maṇḍalamāḷaṁ paṭiyādeti. ^snp3-7-4-10

Tena kho pana samayena selo brāhmaṇo āpaṇe paṭivasati, tiṇṇaṁ vedānaṁ pāragū sanighaṇḍukeṭubhānaṁ sākkharappabhedānaṁ itihāsapañcamānaṁ padako veyyākaraṇo lokāyatamahāpurisalakkhaṇesu anavayo, tīṇi ca māṇavakasatāni mante vāceti. ^snp3-7-5-1

Tena kho pana samayena keṇiyo jaṭilo sele brāhmaṇe abhippasanno hoti. ^snp3-7-6-1

Atha kho selo brāhmaṇo tīhi māṇavakasatehi parivuto jaṅghāvihāraṁ anucaṅkamamāno anuvicaramāno yena keṇiyassa jaṭilassa assamo tenupasaṅkami. ^snp3-7-6-2

Addasā kho selo brāhmaṇo keṇiyassa jaṭilassa assame appekacce uddhanāni khaṇante …pe… appekacce āsanāni paññapente, keṇiyaṁ pana jaṭilaṁ sāmaṁyeva maṇḍalamāḷaṁ paṭiyādentaṁ. ^snp3-7-6-3

Disvāna keṇiyaṁ jaṭilaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-7-6-4

“kiṁ nu kho bhoto keṇiyassa āvāho vā bhavissati, vivāho vā bhavissati, mahāyañño vā paccupaṭṭhito, rājā vā māgadho seniyo bimbisāro nimantito svātanāya saddhiṁ balakāyenā”ti? ^snp3-7-6-5

“Na me, bho sela, āvāho vā bhavissati vivāho vā, nāpi rājā māgadho seniyo bimbisāro nimantito svātanāya saddhiṁ balakāyena; ^snp3-7-7-1

api ca kho me mahāyañño paccupaṭṭhito. ^snp3-7-7-2

Atthi samaṇo gotamo sakyaputto sakyakulā pabbajito aṅguttarāpesu cārikaṁ caramāno mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena saddhiṁ aḍḍhateḷasehi bhikkhusatehi āpaṇaṁ anuppatto. ^snp3-7-7-3

Taṁ kho pana bhavantaṁ gotamaṁ …pe… ^snp3-7-7-4

buddho bhagavāti. ^snp3-7-7-5

So me nimantito svātanāya bhattaṁ saddhiṁ bhikkhusaṅghenā”ti. ^snp3-7-7-6

“Buddhoti, bho keṇiya, vadesi”? ^snp3-7-7-7

“Buddhoti, bho sela, vadāmi”. ^snp3-7-7-8

“Buddhoti, bho keṇiya, vadesi”? ^snp3-7-7-9

“Buddhoti, bho sela, vadāmī”ti. ^snp3-7-7-10

Atha kho selassa brāhmaṇassa etadahosi: ^snp3-7-8-1

“ghosopi kho eso dullabho lokasmiṁ, yadidaṁ buddhoti. ^snp3-7-8-2

Āgatāni kho panamhākaṁ mantesu dvattiṁsamahāpurisalakkhaṇāni, yehi samannāgatassa mahāpurisassa dveva gatiyo bhavanti anaññā. ^snp3-7-8-3

Sace agāraṁ ajjhāvasati rājā hoti cakkavattī dhammiko dhammarājā cāturanto vijitāvī janapadatthāvariyappatto sattaratanasamannāgato. ^snp3-7-8-4

Tassimāni satta ratanāni bhavanti, seyyathidaṁ— ^snp3-7-8-5

cakkaratanaṁ, hatthiratanaṁ, assaratanaṁ, maṇiratanaṁ, itthiratanaṁ, gahapatiratanaṁ, pariṇāyakaratanameva sattamaṁ. ^snp3-7-8-6

Parosahassaṁ kho panassa puttā bhavanti sūrā vīraṅgarūpā parasenappamaddanā. ^snp3-7-8-7

So imaṁ pathaviṁ sāgarapariyantaṁ adaṇḍena asatthena dhammena abhivijiya ajjhāvasati. ^snp3-7-8-8

Sace kho pana agārasmā anagāriyaṁ pabbajati, arahaṁ hoti sammāsambuddho loke vivaṭṭacchado. ^snp3-7-8-9

Kahaṁ pana, bho keṇiya, etarahi so bhavaṁ gotamo viharati arahaṁ sammāsambuddho”ti? ^snp3-7-8-10

Evaṁ vutte, keṇiyo jaṭilo dakkhiṇaṁ bāhuṁ paggahetvā selaṁ brāhmaṇaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-7-9-1

“yenesā, bho sela, nīlavanarājī”ti. ^snp3-7-9-2

Atha kho selo brāhmaṇo tīhi māṇavakasatehi saddhiṁ yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami. ^snp3-7-9-3

Atha kho selo brāhmaṇo te māṇavake āmantesi: ^snp3-7-9-4

“appasaddā bhonto āgacchantu, pade padaṁ nikkhipantā. ^snp3-7-9-5

Durāsadā hi te bhagavanto sīhāva ekacarā. ^snp3-7-9-6

Yadā cāhaṁ, bho, samaṇena gotamena saddhiṁ manteyyaṁ, mā me bhonto antarantarā kathaṁ opātetha; ^snp3-7-9-7

kathāpariyosānaṁ me bhavanto āgamentū”ti. ^snp3-7-9-8

Atha kho selo brāhmaṇo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṁ sammodi. ^snp3-7-10-1

Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. ^snp3-7-10-2

Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho selo brāhmaṇo bhagavato kāye dvattiṁsamahāpurisalakkhaṇāni samannesi. ^snp3-7-10-3

Addasā kho selo brāhmaṇo bhagavato kāye dvattiṁsamahāpurisalakkhaṇāni yebhuyyena ṭhapetvā dve. ^snp3-7-10-4

Dvīsu mahāpurisalakkhaṇesu kaṅkhati vicikicchati nādhimuccati na sampasīdati— ^snp3-7-10-5

kosohite ca vatthaguyhe pahūtajivhatāya cāti. ^snp3-7-10-6

Atha kho bhagavato etadahosi: ^snp3-7-11-1

“passati kho me ayaṁ selo brāhmaṇo dvattiṁsamahāpurisalakkhaṇāni yebhuyyena ṭhapetvā dve. ^snp3-7-11-2

Dvīsu mahāpurisalakkhaṇesu kaṅkhati vicikicchati nādhimuccati na sampasīdati— ^snp3-7-11-3

kosohite ca vatthaguyhe pahūtajivhatāya cā”ti. ^snp3-7-11-4

Atha kho bhagavā tathārūpaṁ iddhābhisaṅkhāraṁ abhisaṅkhāsi, yathā addasa selo brāhmaṇo bhagavato kosohitaṁ vatthaguyhaṁ. ^snp3-7-11-5

Atha kho bhagavā jivhaṁ ninnāmetvā ubhopi kaṇṇasotāni anumasi paṭimasi, ubhopi nāsikasotāni anumasi paṭimasi, kevalampi nalāṭamaṇḍalaṁ jivhāya chādesi. ^snp3-7-11-6

Atha kho selassa brāhmaṇassa etadahosi: ^snp3-7-12-1

“samannāgato kho samaṇo gotamo dvattiṁsamahāpurisalakkhaṇehi paripuṇṇehi, no aparipuṇṇehi. ^snp3-7-12-2

No ca kho naṁ jānāmi buddho vā no vā. ^snp3-7-12-3

Sutaṁ kho pana metaṁ brāhmaṇānaṁ vuḍḍhānaṁ mahallakānaṁ ācariyapācariyānaṁ bhāsamānānaṁ: ^snp3-7-12-4

‘ye te bhavanti arahanto sammāsambuddhā, te sake vaṇṇe bhaññamāne attānaṁ pātukarontī’ti. ^snp3-7-12-5

Yannūnāhaṁ samaṇaṁ gotamaṁ sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthaveyyan”ti. ^snp3-7-12-6

Atha kho selo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṁ sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi: ^snp3-7-12-7

“Paripuṇṇakāyo suruci, ^snp3-7-13-1

Sujāto cārudassano; ^snp3-7-13-2

Suvaṇṇavaṇṇosi bhagavā, ^snp3-7-13-3

Susukkadāṭhosi vīriyavā. ^snp3-7-13-4

Narassa hi sujātassa, ^snp3-7-14-1

ye bhavanti viyañjanā; ^snp3-7-14-2

Sabbe te tava kāyasmiṁ, ^snp3-7-14-3

mahāpurisalakkhaṇā. ^snp3-7-14-4

Pasannanetto sumukho, ^snp3-7-15-1

brahā uju patāpavā; ^snp3-7-15-2

Majjhe samaṇasaṅghassa, ^snp3-7-15-3

ādiccova virocasi. ^snp3-7-15-4

Kalyāṇadassano bhikkhu, ^snp3-7-16-1

kañcanasannibhattaco; ^snp3-7-16-2

Kiṁ te samaṇabhāvena, ^snp3-7-16-3

evaṁ uttamavaṇṇino. ^snp3-7-16-4

Rājā arahasi bhavituṁ, ^snp3-7-17-1

cakkavattī rathesabho; ^snp3-7-17-2

Cāturanto vijitāvī, ^snp3-7-17-3

jambusaṇḍassa issaro. ^snp3-7-17-4

Khattiyā bhogirājāno, ^snp3-7-18-1

anuyantā bhavantu te; ^snp3-7-18-2

Rājābhirājā manujindo, ^snp3-7-18-3

rajjaṁ kārehi gotama”. ^snp3-7-18-4

“Rājāhamasmi selāti, ^snp3-7-19-1

(bhagavā) ^snp3-7-19-2

Dhammarājā anuttaro; ^snp3-7-19-3

Dhammena cakkaṁ vattemi, ^snp3-7-19-4

Cakkaṁ appaṭivattiyaṁ”. ^snp3-7-19-5

“Sambuddho paṭijānāsi, ^snp3-7-20-1

(iti selo brāhmaṇo) ^snp3-7-20-2

Dhammarājā anuttaro; ^snp3-7-20-3

‘Dhammena cakkaṁ vattemi’, ^snp3-7-20-4

Iti bhāsasi gotama. ^snp3-7-20-5

Ko nu senāpati bhoto, ^snp3-7-21-1

Sāvako satthuranvayo; ^snp3-7-21-2

Ko te tamanuvatteti, ^snp3-7-21-3

Dhammacakkaṁ pavattitaṁ”. ^snp3-7-21-4

“Mayā pavattitaṁ cakkaṁ, ^snp3-7-22-1

(selāti bhagavā) ^snp3-7-22-2

Dhammacakkaṁ anuttaraṁ; ^snp3-7-22-3

Sāriputto anuvatteti, ^snp3-7-22-4

Anujāto tathāgataṁ. ^snp3-7-22-5

Abhiññeyyaṁ abhiññātaṁ, ^snp3-7-23-1

Bhāvetabbañca bhāvitaṁ; ^snp3-7-23-2

Pahātabbaṁ pahīnaṁ me, ^snp3-7-23-3

Tasmā buddhosmi brāhmaṇa. ^snp3-7-23-4

Vinayassu mayi kaṅkhaṁ, ^snp3-7-24-1

Adhimuccassu brāhmaṇa; ^snp3-7-24-2

Dullabhaṁ dassanaṁ hoti, ^snp3-7-24-3

Sambuddhānaṁ abhiṇhaso. ^snp3-7-24-4

Yesaṁ ve dullabho loke, ^snp3-7-25-1

Pātubhāvo abhiṇhaso; ^snp3-7-25-2

Sohaṁ brāhmaṇa sambuddho, ^snp3-7-25-3

Sallakatto anuttaro. ^snp3-7-25-4

Brahmabhūto atitulo, ^snp3-7-26-1

Mārasenappamaddano; ^snp3-7-26-2

Sabbāmitte vasīkatvā, ^snp3-7-26-3

Modāmi akutobhayo”. ^snp3-7-26-4

“Imaṁ bhavanto nisāmetha, ^snp3-7-27-1

Yathā bhāsati cakkhumā; ^snp3-7-27-2

Sallakatto mahāvīro, ^snp3-7-27-3

Sīhova nadatī vane. ^snp3-7-27-4

Brahmabhūtaṁ atitulaṁ, ^snp3-7-28-1

Mārasenappamaddanaṁ; ^snp3-7-28-2

Ko disvā nappasīdeyya, ^snp3-7-28-3

Api kaṇhābhijātiko. ^snp3-7-28-4

Yo maṁ icchati anvetu, ^snp3-7-29-1

Yo vā nicchati gacchatu; ^snp3-7-29-2

Idhāhaṁ pabbajissāmi, ^snp3-7-29-3

Varapaññassa santike”. ^snp3-7-29-4

“Evañce ruccati bhoto, ^snp3-7-30-1

Sammāsambuddhasāsane; ^snp3-7-30-2

Mayampi pabbajissāma, ^snp3-7-30-3

Varapaññassa santike”. ^snp3-7-30-4

Brāhmaṇā tisatā ime, ^snp3-7-31-1

Yācanti pañjalīkatā; ^snp3-7-31-2

“Brahmacariyaṁ carissāma, ^snp3-7-31-3

Bhagavā tava santike”. ^snp3-7-31-4

“Svākkhātaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, ^snp3-7-32-1

(selāti bhagavā) ^snp3-7-32-2

Sandiṭṭhikamakālikaṁ; ^snp3-7-32-3

Yattha amoghā pabbajjā, ^snp3-7-32-4

Appamattassa sikkhato”ti. ^snp3-7-32-5

Alattha kho selo brāhmaṇo sapariso bhagavato santike pabbajjaṁ, alattha upasampadaṁ. ^snp3-7-33-1

Atha kho keṇiyo jaṭilo tassā rattiyā accayena sake assame paṇītaṁ khādanīyaṁ bhojanīyaṁ paṭiyādāpetvā bhagavato kālaṁ ārocāpesi: ^snp3-7-33-2

“kālo, bho gotama, niṭṭhitaṁ bhattan”ti. ^snp3-7-33-3

Atha kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṁ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya yena keṇiyassa jaṭilassa assamo tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi saddhiṁ bhikkhusaṅghena. ^snp3-7-33-4

Atha kho keṇiyo jaṭilo buddhappamukhaṁ bhikkhusaṅghaṁ paṇītena khādanīyena bhojanīyena sahatthā santappesi sampavāresi. ^snp3-7-34-1

Atha kho keṇiyo jaṭilo bhagavantaṁ bhuttāviṁ onītapattapāṇiṁ aññataraṁ nīcaṁ āsanaṁ gahetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. ^snp3-7-34-2

Ekamantaṁ nisinnaṁ kho keṇiyaṁ jaṭilaṁ bhagavā imāhi gāthāhi anumodi: ^snp3-7-34-3

“Aggihuttamukhā yaññā, ^snp3-7-35-1

Sāvittī chandaso mukhaṁ; ^snp3-7-35-2

Rājā mukhaṁ manussānaṁ, ^snp3-7-35-3

Nadīnaṁ sāgaro mukhaṁ. ^snp3-7-35-4

Nakkhattānaṁ mukhaṁ cando, ^snp3-7-36-1

Ādicco tapataṁ mukhaṁ; ^snp3-7-36-2

Puññaṁ ākaṅkhamānānaṁ, ^snp3-7-36-3

Saṅgho ve yajataṁ mukhan”ti. ^snp3-7-36-4

Atha kho bhagavā keṇiyaṁ jaṭilaṁ imāhi gāthāhi anumoditvā uṭṭhāyāsanā pakkāmi. ^snp3-7-37-1

Atha kho āyasmā selo sapariso eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto nacirasseva …pe… ^snp3-7-37-2

aññataro kho panāyasmā selo sapariso arahataṁ ahosi. ^snp3-7-37-3

Atha kho āyasmā selo sapariso yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami, upasaṅkamitvā ekaṁsaṁ cīvaraṁ katvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṁ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṁ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi: ^snp3-7-38-1

“Yaṁ taṁ saraṇamāgamha, ^snp3-7-39-1

Ito aṭṭhami cakkhuma; ^snp3-7-39-2

Sattarattena bhagavā, ^snp3-7-39-3

Dantamha tava sāsane. ^snp3-7-39-4

Tuvaṁ buddho tuvaṁ satthā, ^snp3-7-40-1

Tuvaṁ mārābhibhū muni; ^snp3-7-40-2

Tuvaṁ anusaye chetvā, ^snp3-7-40-3

Tiṇṇo tāresimaṁ pajaṁ. ^snp3-7-40-4

Upadhī te samatikkantā, ^snp3-7-41-1

Āsavā te padālitā; ^snp3-7-41-2

Sīhosi anupādāno, ^snp3-7-41-3

Pahīnabhayabheravo. ^snp3-7-41-4

Bhikkhavo tisatā ime, ^snp3-7-42-1

Tiṭṭhanti pañjalīkatā; ^snp3-7-42-2

Pāde vīra pasārehi, ^snp3-7-42-3

Nāgā vandantu satthuno”ti. ^snp3-7-42-4

Selasuttaṁ sattamaṁ. ^snp3-7-42-5

### Sallasutta (Sutta Nipāta 3.8) ^snp3-8-0

Animittamanaññātaṁ, ^snp3-8-1-1

maccānaṁ idha jīvitaṁ; ^snp3-8-1-2

Kasirañca parittañca, ^snp3-8-1-3

tañca dukkhena saṁyutaṁ. ^snp3-8-1-4

Na hi so upakkamo atthi, ^snp3-8-2-1

yena jātā na miyyare; ^snp3-8-2-2

Jarampi patvā maraṇaṁ, ^snp3-8-2-3

evaṁdhammā hi pāṇino. ^snp3-8-2-4

Phalānamiva pakkānaṁ, ^snp3-8-3-1

pāto patanato bhayaṁ; ^snp3-8-3-2

Evaṁ jātāna maccānaṁ, ^snp3-8-3-3

niccaṁ maraṇato bhayaṁ. ^snp3-8-3-4

Yathāpi kumbhakārassa, ^snp3-8-4-1

katā mattikabhājanā; ^snp3-8-4-2

Sabbe bhedanapariyantā, ^snp3-8-4-3

evaṁ maccāna jīvitaṁ. ^snp3-8-4-4

Daharā ca mahantā ca, ^snp3-8-5-1

ye bālā ye ca paṇḍitā; ^snp3-8-5-2

Sabbe maccuvasaṁ yanti, ^snp3-8-5-3

sabbe maccuparāyaṇā. ^snp3-8-5-4

Tesaṁ maccuparetānaṁ, ^snp3-8-6-1

gacchataṁ paralokato; ^snp3-8-6-2

Na pitā tāyate puttaṁ, ^snp3-8-6-3

ñātī vā pana ñātake. ^snp3-8-6-4

Pekkhataṁyeva ñātīnaṁ, ^snp3-8-7-1

passa lālapataṁ puthu; ^snp3-8-7-2

Ekamekova maccānaṁ, ^snp3-8-7-3

govajjho viya nīyati. ^snp3-8-7-4

Evamabbhāhato loko, ^snp3-8-8-1

Maccunā ca jarāya ca; ^snp3-8-8-2

Tasmā dhīrā na socanti, ^snp3-8-8-3

Viditvā lokapariyāyaṁ. ^snp3-8-8-4

Yassa maggaṁ na jānāsi, ^snp3-8-9-1

āgatassa gatassa vā; ^snp3-8-9-2

Ubho ante asampassaṁ, ^snp3-8-9-3

niratthaṁ paridevasi. ^snp3-8-9-4

Paridevayamāno ce, ^snp3-8-10-1

Kiñcidatthaṁ udabbahe; ^snp3-8-10-2

Sammūḷho hiṁsamattānaṁ, ^snp3-8-10-3

Kayirā ce naṁ vicakkhaṇo. ^snp3-8-10-4

Na hi ruṇṇena sokena, ^snp3-8-11-1

Santiṁ pappoti cetaso; ^snp3-8-11-2

Bhiyyassuppajjate dukkhaṁ, ^snp3-8-11-3

Sarīraṁ cupahaññati. ^snp3-8-11-4

Kiso vivaṇṇo bhavati, ^snp3-8-12-1

Hiṁsamattānamattanā; ^snp3-8-12-2

Na tena petā pālenti, ^snp3-8-12-3

Niratthā paridevanā. ^snp3-8-12-4

Sokamappajahaṁ jantu, ^snp3-8-13-1

Bhiyyo dukkhaṁ nigacchati; ^snp3-8-13-2

Anutthunanto kālaṅkataṁ, ^snp3-8-13-3

Sokassa vasamanvagū. ^snp3-8-13-4

Aññepi passa gamine, ^snp3-8-14-1

Yathākammupage nare; ^snp3-8-14-2

Maccuno vasamāgamma, ^snp3-8-14-3

Phandantevidha pāṇino. ^snp3-8-14-4

Yena yena hi maññanti, ^snp3-8-15-1

Tato taṁ hoti aññathā; ^snp3-8-15-2

Etādiso vinābhāvo, ^snp3-8-15-3

Passa lokassa pariyāyaṁ. ^snp3-8-15-4

Api vassasataṁ jīve, ^snp3-8-16-1

Bhiyyo vā pana māṇavo; ^snp3-8-16-2

Ñātisaṅghā vinā hoti, ^snp3-8-16-3

Jahāti idha jīvitaṁ. ^snp3-8-16-4

Tasmā arahato sutvā, ^snp3-8-17-1

Vineyya paridevitaṁ; ^snp3-8-17-2

Petaṁ kālaṅkataṁ disvā, ^snp3-8-17-3

Neso labbhā mayā iti. ^snp3-8-17-4

Yathā saraṇamādittaṁ, ^snp3-8-18-1

Vārinā parinibbaye; ^snp3-8-18-2

Evampi dhīro sapañño, ^snp3-8-18-3

Paṇḍito kusalo naro; ^snp3-8-18-4

Khippamuppatitaṁ sokaṁ, ^snp3-8-18-5

Vāto tūlaṁva dhaṁsaye. ^snp3-8-18-6

Paridevaṁ pajappañca, ^snp3-8-19-1

Domanassañca attano; ^snp3-8-19-2

Attano sukhamesāno, ^snp3-8-19-3

Abbahe sallamattano. ^snp3-8-19-4

Abbūḷhasallo asito, ^snp3-8-20-1

santiṁ pappuyya cetaso; ^snp3-8-20-2

Sabbasokaṁ atikkanto, ^snp3-8-20-3

asoko hoti nibbutoti. ^snp3-8-20-4

Sallasuttaṁ aṭṭhamaṁ. ^snp3-8-20-5

### Vāseṭṭhasutta (Sutta Nipāta 3.9) ^snp3-9-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp3-9-1-1

ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā icchānaṅgale viharati icchānaṅgalavanasaṇḍe. ^snp3-9-1-2

Tena kho pana samayena sambahulā abhiññātā abhiññātā brāhmaṇamahāsālā icchānaṅgale paṭivasanti, seyyathidaṁ— ^snp3-9-1-3

caṅkī brāhmaṇo, tārukkho brāhmaṇo, pokkharasāti brāhmaṇo, jāṇussoṇi brāhmaṇo, todeyyo brāhmaṇo, aññe ca abhiññātā abhiññātā brāhmaṇamahāsālā. ^snp3-9-1-4

Atha kho vāseṭṭhabhāradvājānaṁ māṇavānaṁ jaṅghāvihāraṁ anucaṅkamantānaṁ anuvicarantānaṁ ayamantarākathā udapādi: ^snp3-9-1-5

“kathaṁ, bho, brāhmaṇo hotī”ti? ^snp3-9-1-6

Bhāradvājo māṇavo evamāha: ^snp3-9-2-1

“yato kho, bho, ubhato sujāto hoti mātito ca pitito ca saṁsuddhagahaṇiko yāva sattamā pitāmahayugā akkhitto anupakkuṭṭho jātivādena, ^snp3-9-2-2

ettāvatā kho bho brāhmaṇo hotī”ti. ^snp3-9-2-3

Vāseṭṭho māṇavo evamāha: ^snp3-9-3-1

“yato kho, bho, sīlavā ca hoti vatasampanno ca, ^snp3-9-3-2

ettāvatā kho, bho, brāhmaṇo hotī”ti. ^snp3-9-3-3

Neva kho asakkhi bhāradvājo māṇavo vāseṭṭhaṁ māṇavaṁ saññāpetuṁ, na pana asakkhi vāseṭṭho māṇavo bhāradvājaṁ māṇavaṁ saññāpetuṁ. ^snp3-9-3-4

Atha kho vāseṭṭho māṇavo bhāradvājaṁ māṇavaṁ āmantesi: ^snp3-9-4-1

“ayaṁ kho, bho bhāradvāja, samaṇo gotamo sakyaputto sakyakulā pabbajito icchānaṅgale viharati icchānaṅgalavanasaṇḍe; ^snp3-9-4-2

taṁ kho pana bhavantaṁ gotamaṁ evaṁ kalyāṇo kittisaddo abbhuggato: ^snp3-9-4-3

‘itipi …pe… buddho bhagavā’ti. ^snp3-9-4-4

Āyāma, bho bhāradvāja, yena samaṇo gotamo tenupasaṅkamissāma; upasaṅkamitvā samaṇaṁ gotamaṁ etamatthaṁ pucchissāma. ^snp3-9-4-5

Yathā no samaṇo gotamo byākarissati tathā naṁ dhāressāmā”ti. ^snp3-9-4-6

“Evaṁ, bho”ti kho bhāradvājo māṇavo vāseṭṭhassa māṇavassa paccassosi. ^snp3-9-4-7

Atha kho vāseṭṭhabhāradvājā māṇavā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṁsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṁ sammodiṁsu. ^snp3-9-5-1

Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdiṁsu. ^snp3-9-5-2

Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho vāseṭṭho māṇavo bhagavantaṁ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi: ^snp3-9-5-3

“Anuññātapaṭiññātā, ^snp3-9-6-1

tevijjā mayamasmubho; ^snp3-9-6-2

Ahaṁ pokkharasātissa, ^snp3-9-6-3

tārukkhassāyaṁ māṇavo. ^snp3-9-6-4

Tevijjānaṁ yadakkhātaṁ, ^snp3-9-7-1

Tatra kevalinosmase; ^snp3-9-7-2

Padakasma veyyākaraṇā, ^snp3-9-7-3

Jappe ācariyasādisā. ^snp3-9-7-4

Tesaṁ no jātivādasmiṁ, ^snp3-9-8-1

vivādo atthi gotama; ^snp3-9-8-2

Jātiyā brāhmaṇo hoti, ^snp3-9-8-3

bhāradvājo iti bhāsati; ^snp3-9-8-4

Ahañca kammunā brūmi, ^snp3-9-8-5

evaṁ jānāhi cakkhuma. ^snp3-9-8-6

Te na sakkoma saññāpetuṁ, ^snp3-9-9-1

aññamaññaṁ mayaṁ ubho; ^snp3-9-9-2

Bhavantaṁ puṭṭhumāgamhā, ^snp3-9-9-3

sambuddhaṁ iti vissutaṁ. ^snp3-9-9-4

Candaṁ yathā khayātītaṁ, ^snp3-9-10-1

pecca pañjalikā janā; ^snp3-9-10-2

Vandamānā namassanti, ^snp3-9-10-3

evaṁ lokasmi gotamaṁ. ^snp3-9-10-4

Cakkhuṁ loke samuppannaṁ, ^snp3-9-11-1

mayaṁ pucchāma gotamaṁ; ^snp3-9-11-2

Jātiyā brāhmaṇo hoti, ^snp3-9-11-3

udāhu bhavati kammunā; ^snp3-9-11-4

Ajānataṁ no pabrūhi, ^snp3-9-11-5

yathā jānemu brāhmaṇaṁ”. ^snp3-9-11-6

“Tesaṁ vo ahaṁ byakkhissaṁ, ^snp3-9-12-1

(vāseṭṭhāti bhagavā) ^snp3-9-12-2

Anupubbaṁ yathātathaṁ; ^snp3-9-12-3

Jātivibhaṅgaṁ pāṇānaṁ, ^snp3-9-12-4

Aññamaññā hi jātiyo. ^snp3-9-12-5

Tiṇarukkhepi jānātha, ^snp3-9-13-1

na cāpi paṭijānare; ^snp3-9-13-2

Liṅgaṁ jātimayaṁ tesaṁ, ^snp3-9-13-3

aññamaññā hi jātiyo. ^snp3-9-13-4

Tato kīṭe paṭaṅge ca, ^snp3-9-14-1

yāva kunthakipillike; ^snp3-9-14-2

Liṅgaṁ jātimayaṁ tesaṁ, ^snp3-9-14-3

aññamaññā hi jātiyo. ^snp3-9-14-4

Catuppadepi jānātha, ^snp3-9-15-1

Khuddake ca mahallake; ^snp3-9-15-2

Liṅgaṁ jātimayaṁ tesaṁ, ^snp3-9-15-3

Aññamaññā hi jātiyo. ^snp3-9-15-4

Pādūdarepi jānātha, ^snp3-9-16-1

Urage dīghapiṭṭhike; ^snp3-9-16-2

Liṅgaṁ jātimayaṁ tesaṁ, ^snp3-9-16-3

Aññamaññā hi jātiyo. ^snp3-9-16-4

Tato macchepi jānātha, ^snp3-9-17-1

Odake vārigocare; ^snp3-9-17-2

Liṅgaṁ jātimayaṁ tesaṁ, ^snp3-9-17-3

Aññamaññā hi jātiyo. ^snp3-9-17-4

Tato pakkhīpi jānātha, ^snp3-9-18-1

Pattayāne vihaṅgame; ^snp3-9-18-2

Liṅgaṁ jātimayaṁ tesaṁ, ^snp3-9-18-3

Aññamaññā hi jātiyo. ^snp3-9-18-4

Yathā etāsu jātīsu, ^snp3-9-19-1

Liṅgaṁ jātimayaṁ puthu; ^snp3-9-19-2

Evaṁ natthi manussesu, ^snp3-9-19-3

Liṅgaṁ jātimayaṁ puthu. ^snp3-9-19-4

Na kesehi na sīsena, ^snp3-9-20-1

Na kaṇṇehi na akkhibhi; ^snp3-9-20-2

Na mukhena na nāsāya, ^snp3-9-20-3

Na oṭṭhehi bhamūhi vā. ^snp3-9-20-4

Na gīvāya na aṁsehi, ^snp3-9-21-1

Na udarena na piṭṭhiyā; ^snp3-9-21-2

Na soṇiyā na urasā, ^snp3-9-21-3

Na sambādhe na methune. ^snp3-9-21-4

Na hatthehi na pādehi, ^snp3-9-22-1

Na jaṅghāhi na ūrūhi, ^snp3-9-22-3

Na vaṇṇena sarena vā; ^snp3-9-22-4

Liṅgaṁ jātimayaṁ neva, ^snp3-9-22-5

Yathā aññāsu jātisu. ^snp3-9-22-6

Paccattañca sarīresu, ^snp3-9-23-1

Manussesvetaṁ na vijjati; ^snp3-9-23-2

Yo hi koci manussesu, ^snp3-9-24-1

Kassako so na brāhmaṇo. ^snp3-9-24-4

Evaṁ vāseṭṭha jānāhi, ^snp3-9-28-3

Coro eso na brāhmaṇo. ^snp3-9-28-4

Evaṁ vāseṭṭha jānāhi, ^snp3-9-29-3

Yo hi koci manussesu, ^snp3-9-30-1

Evaṁ vāseṭṭha jānāhi, ^snp3-9-30-3

Yājako eso na brāhmaṇo. ^snp3-9-30-4

Yo hi koci manussesu, ^snp3-9-31-1

Evaṁ vāseṭṭha jānāhi, ^snp3-9-31-3

Rājā eso na brāhmaṇo. ^snp3-9-31-4

Na cāhaṁ brāhmaṇaṁ brūmi, ^snp3-9-32-1

Yonijaṁ mattisambhavaṁ; ^snp3-9-32-2

Bhovādi nāma so hoti, ^snp3-9-32-3

Sace hoti sakiñcano; ^snp3-9-32-4

Akiñcanaṁ anādānaṁ, ^snp3-9-32-5

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-32-6

Sabbasaṁyojanaṁ chetvā, ^snp3-9-33-1

Yo ve na paritassati; ^snp3-9-33-2

Saṅgātigaṁ visaṁyuttaṁ, ^snp3-9-33-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-33-4

Chetvā naddhiṁ varattañca, ^snp3-9-34-1

Ukkhittapalighaṁ buddhaṁ, ^snp3-9-34-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-34-4

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-35-4

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-36-4

Vāri pokkharapatteva, ^snp3-9-37-1

Yo na limpati kāmesu, ^snp3-9-37-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-38-4

Gambhīrapaññaṁ medhāviṁ, ^snp3-9-39-1
