Uttamatthamanuppattaṁ, ^snp3-9-39-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-39-4

Asaṁsaṭṭhaṁ gahaṭṭhehi, ^snp3-9-40-1

Anāgārehi cūbhayaṁ; ^snp3-9-40-2

Anokasārimappicchaṁ, ^snp3-9-40-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-40-4

Nidhāya daṇḍaṁ bhūtesu, ^snp3-9-41-1

Tasesu thāvaresu ca; ^snp3-9-41-2

Yo na hanti na ghāteti, ^snp3-9-41-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-41-4

Aviruddhaṁ viruddhesu, ^snp3-9-42-1

Attadaṇḍesu nibbutaṁ; ^snp3-9-42-2

Sādānesu anādānaṁ, ^snp3-9-42-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-42-4

Yassa rāgo ca doso ca, ^snp3-9-43-1

Māno makkho ca pātito; ^snp3-9-43-2

Sāsaporiva āraggā, ^snp3-9-43-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-43-4

Akakkasaṁ viññāpaniṁ, ^snp3-9-44-1

Giraṁ saccamudīraye; ^snp3-9-44-2

Yāya nābhisaje kañci, ^snp3-9-44-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-44-4

Yodha dīghaṁ va rassaṁ vā, ^snp3-9-45-1

Aṇuṁ thūlaṁ subhāsubhaṁ; ^snp3-9-45-2

Loke adinnaṁ nādiyati, ^snp3-9-45-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-45-4

Āsā yassa na vijjanti, ^snp3-9-46-1

Asmiṁ loke paramhi ca; ^snp3-9-46-2

Nirāsāsaṁ visaṁyuttaṁ, ^snp3-9-46-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-46-4

Yassālayā na vijjanti, ^snp3-9-47-1

Aññāya akathaṅkathī; ^snp3-9-47-2

Amatogadhamanuppattaṁ, ^snp3-9-47-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-47-4

Yodha puññañca pāpañca, ^snp3-9-48-1

Ubho saṅgamupaccagā; ^snp3-9-48-2

Asokaṁ virajaṁ suddhaṁ, ^snp3-9-48-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-48-4

Candaṁva vimalaṁ suddhaṁ, ^snp3-9-49-1

Vippasannamanāvilaṁ; ^snp3-9-49-2

Nandībhavaparikkhīṇaṁ, ^snp3-9-49-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-49-4

Yomaṁ palipathaṁ duggaṁ, ^snp3-9-50-1

Saṁsāraṁ mohamaccagā; ^snp3-9-50-2

Tiṇṇo pāraṅgato jhāyī, ^snp3-9-50-3

Anejo akathaṅkathī; ^snp3-9-50-4

Anupādāya nibbuto, ^snp3-9-50-5

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-50-6

Yodha kāme pahantvāna, ^snp3-9-51-1

Anāgāro paribbaje; ^snp3-9-51-2

Kāmabhavaparikkhīṇaṁ, ^snp3-9-51-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-51-4

Yodha taṇhaṁ pahantvāna, ^snp3-9-52-1

Anāgāro paribbaje; ^snp3-9-52-2

Taṇhābhavaparikkhīṇaṁ, ^snp3-9-52-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-52-4

Hitvā mānusakaṁ yogaṁ, ^snp3-9-53-1

Dibbaṁ yogaṁ upaccagā; ^snp3-9-53-2

Sabbayogavisaṁyuttaṁ, ^snp3-9-53-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-53-4

Hitvā ratiñca aratiṁ, ^snp3-9-54-1

Sītibhūtaṁ nirūpadhiṁ; ^snp3-9-54-2

Sabbalokābhibhuṁ vīraṁ, ^snp3-9-54-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-54-4

Cutiṁ yo vedi sattānaṁ, ^snp3-9-55-1

Upapattiñca sabbaso; ^snp3-9-55-2

Asattaṁ sugataṁ buddhaṁ, ^snp3-9-55-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-55-4

Yassa gatiṁ na jānanti, ^snp3-9-56-1

Devā gandhabbamānusā; ^snp3-9-56-2

Khīṇāsavaṁ arahantaṁ, ^snp3-9-56-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-56-4

Yassa pure ca pacchā ca, ^snp3-9-57-1

Majjhe ca natthi kiñcanaṁ; ^snp3-9-57-2

Akiñcanaṁ anādānaṁ, ^snp3-9-57-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-57-4

Usabhaṁ pavaraṁ vīraṁ, ^snp3-9-58-1

Mahesiṁ vijitāvinaṁ; ^snp3-9-58-2

Anejaṁ nhātakaṁ buddhaṁ, ^snp3-9-58-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-58-4

Pubbenivāsaṁ yo vedi, ^snp3-9-59-1

Saggāpāyañca passati; ^snp3-9-59-2

Atho jātikkhayaṁ patto, ^snp3-9-59-3

Tamahaṁ brūmi brāhmaṇaṁ. ^snp3-9-59-4

Samaññā hesā lokasmiṁ, ^snp3-9-60-1

Nāmagottaṁ pakappitaṁ; ^snp3-9-60-2

Sammuccā samudāgataṁ, ^snp3-9-60-3

Tattha tattha pakappitaṁ. ^snp3-9-60-4

Dīgharattamanusayitaṁ, ^snp3-9-61-1

Diṭṭhigatamajānataṁ; ^snp3-9-61-2

Ajānantā no pabruvanti, ^snp3-9-61-3

Jātiyā hoti brāhmaṇo. ^snp3-9-61-4

Na jaccā brāhmaṇo hoti, ^snp3-9-62-1

Na jaccā hoti abrāhmaṇo; ^snp3-9-62-2

Kammunā brāhmaṇo hoti, ^snp3-9-62-3

Kammunā hoti abrāhmaṇo. ^snp3-9-62-4

Kassako kammunā hoti, ^snp3-9-63-1

Sippiko hoti kammunā; ^snp3-9-63-2

Vāṇijo kammunā hoti, ^snp3-9-63-3

Pessiko hoti kammunā. ^snp3-9-63-4

Coropi kammunā hoti, ^snp3-9-64-1

Yodhājīvopi kammunā; ^snp3-9-64-2

Yājako kammunā hoti, ^snp3-9-64-3

Rājāpi hoti kammunā. ^snp3-9-64-4

Evametaṁ yathābhūtaṁ, ^snp3-9-65-1

Kammaṁ passanti paṇḍitā; ^snp3-9-65-2

Paṭiccasamuppādadassā, ^snp3-9-65-3

Kammavipākakovidā. ^snp3-9-65-4

Kammunā vattati loko, ^snp3-9-66-1

Kammunā vattati pajā; ^snp3-9-66-2

Kammanibandhanā sattā, ^snp3-9-66-3

Rathassāṇīva yāyato. ^snp3-9-66-4

Tapena brahmacariyena, ^snp3-9-67-1

Saṁyamena damena ca; ^snp3-9-67-2

Etena brāhmaṇo hoti, ^snp3-9-67-3

Etaṁ brāhmaṇamuttamaṁ. ^snp3-9-67-4

Tīhi vijjāhi sampanno, ^snp3-9-68-1

santo khīṇapunabbhavo; ^snp3-9-68-2

Evaṁ vāseṭṭha jānāhi, ^snp3-9-68-3

brahmā sakko vijānatan”ti. ^snp3-9-68-4

Evaṁ vutte, vāseṭṭhabhāradvājā māṇavā bhagavantaṁ etadavocuṁ: ^snp3-9-69-1

“abhikkantaṁ, bho gotama …pe… ^snp3-9-69-2

upāsake no bhavaṁ gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupete saraṇaṁ gate”ti. ^snp3-9-69-3

Vāseṭṭhasuttaṁ navamaṁ. ^snp3-9-69-4

### Kokālikasutta (Sutta Nipāta 3.10) ^snp3-10-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp3-10-1-1

ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. ^snp3-10-1-2

Atha kho kokāliko bhikkhu yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho kokāliko bhikkhu bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-10-1-3

“pāpicchā, bhante, sāriputtamoggallānā, pāpikānaṁ icchānaṁ vasaṁ gatā”ti. ^snp3-10-1-4

Evaṁ vutte, bhagavā kokālikaṁ bhikkhuṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-10-2-1

“mā hevaṁ, kokālika, mā hevaṁ, kokālika. ^snp3-10-2-2

Pasādehi, kokālika, sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṁ. ^snp3-10-2-3

Pesalā sāriputtamoggallānā”ti. ^snp3-10-2-4

Dutiyampi kho …pe… ^snp3-10-3-1

tatiyampi kho kokāliko bhikkhu bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-10-3-2

“kiñcāpi me, bhante, bhagavā saddhāyiko paccayiko, atha kho pāpicchāva sāriputtamoggallānā, pāpikānaṁ icchānaṁ vasaṁ gatā”ti. ^snp3-10-3-3

Tatiyampi kho bhagavā kokālikaṁ bhikkhuṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-10-3-4

“mā hevaṁ, kokālika, mā hevaṁ, kokālika. ^snp3-10-3-5

Pasādehi, kokālika, sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṁ. ^snp3-10-3-6

Pesalā sāriputtamoggallānā”ti. ^snp3-10-3-7

Atha kho kokāliko bhikkhu uṭṭhāyāsanā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṁ katvā pakkāmi. ^snp3-10-4-1

Acirappakkantassa ca kokālikassa bhikkhuno sāsapamattīhi piḷakāhi sabbo kāyo phuṭo ahosi; ^snp3-10-4-2

sāsapamattiyo hutvā muggamattiyo ahesuṁ; muggamattiyo hutvā kaḷāyamattiyo ahesuṁ; kaḷāyamattiyo hutvā kolaṭṭhimattiyo ahesuṁ; kolaṭṭhimattiyo hutvā kolamattiyo ahesuṁ; kolamattiyo hutvā āmalakamattiyo ahesuṁ; āmalakamattiyo hutvā beḷuvasalāṭukamattiyo ahesuṁ; beḷuvasalāṭukamattiyo hutvā billamattiyo ahesuṁ; billamattiyo hutvā pabhijjiṁsu; pubbañca lohitañca pagghariṁsu. ^snp3-10-4-3

Atha kho kokāliko bhikkhu tenevābādhena kālamakāsi. ^snp3-10-4-4

Kālaṅkato ca kokāliko bhikkhu padumaṁ nirayaṁ upapajji sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṁ āghātetvā. ^snp3-10-4-5

Atha kho brahmā sahampati abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇo kevalakappaṁ jetavanaṁ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṁ ṭhito kho brahmā sahampati bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-10-5-1

“kokāliko, bhante, bhikkhu kālaṅkato; ^snp3-10-5-2

kālaṅkato ca, bhante, kokāliko bhikkhu padumaṁ nirayaṁ upapanno sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṁ āghātetvā”ti. ^snp3-10-5-3

Idamavoca brahmā sahampati; ^snp3-10-5-4

idaṁ vatvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṁ katvā tatthevantaradhāyi. ^snp3-10-5-5

Atha kho bhagavā tassā rattiyā accayena bhikkhū āmantesi: ^snp3-10-6-1

“imaṁ, bhikkhave, rattiṁ brahmā sahampati abhikkantāya rattiyā …pe… ^snp3-10-6-2

idamavoca, bhikkhave, brahmā sahampati, idaṁ vatvā maṁ padakkhiṇaṁ katvā tatthevantaradhāyī”ti. ^snp3-10-6-3

Evaṁ vutte, aññataro bhikkhu bhagavantaṁ etadavoca: ^snp3-10-7-1

“kīvadīghaṁ nu kho, bhante, padume niraye āyuppamāṇan”ti? ^snp3-10-7-2

“Dīghaṁ kho, bhikkhu, padume niraye āyuppamāṇaṁ; ^snp3-10-7-3

taṁ na sukaraṁ saṅkhātuṁ ettakāni vassāni iti vā ettakāni vassasatāni iti vā ettakāni vassasahassāni iti vā ettakāni vassasatasahassāni iti vā”ti. ^snp3-10-7-4

“Sakkā pana, bhante, upamā kātun”ti? ^snp3-10-7-5

“Sakkā, bhikkhū”ti bhagavā avoca: ^snp3-10-7-6

“Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsatikhāriko kosalako tilavāho; tato puriso vassasatassa vassasatassa accayena ekamekaṁ tilaṁ uddhareyya. ^snp3-10-8-1

Khippataraṁ kho so bhikkhu vīsatikhāriko kosalako tilavāho iminā upakkamena parikkhayaṁ pariyādānaṁ gaccheyya, na tveva eko abbudo nirayo. ^snp3-10-8-2

Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati abbudā nirayā evameko nirabbudo nirayo. ^snp3-10-8-3

Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati nirabbudā nirayā evameko ababo nirayo. ^snp3-10-8-4

Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati ababā nirayā evameko aṭaṭo nirayo. ^snp3-10-8-5

Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati aṭaṭā nirayā evameko ahaho nirayo. ^snp3-10-8-6

Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati ahahā nirayā evameko kumudo nirayo. ^snp3-10-8-7

Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati kumudā nirayā evameko sogandhiko nirayo. ^snp3-10-8-8

Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati sogandhikā nirayā evameko uppalako nirayo. ^snp3-10-8-9

Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati uppalakā nirayā evameko puṇḍarīko nirayo. ^snp3-10-8-10

Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati puṇḍarīkā nirayā evameko padumo nirayo. ^snp3-10-8-11

Padumaṁ kho pana bhikkhu nirayaṁ kokāliko bhikkhu upapanno sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṁ āghātetvā”ti. ^snp3-10-8-12

Idamavoca bhagavā. ^snp3-10-8-13

Idaṁ vatvāna sugato athāparaṁ etadavoca satthā: ^snp3-10-8-14

“Purisassa hi jātassa, ^snp3-10-9-1

kuṭhārī jāyate mukhe; ^snp3-10-9-2

Yāya chindati attānaṁ, ^snp3-10-9-3

bālo dubbhāsitaṁ bhaṇaṁ. ^snp3-10-9-4

Yo nindiyaṁ pasaṁsati, ^snp3-10-10-1

Taṁ vā nindati yo pasaṁsiyo; ^snp3-10-10-2

Vicināti mukhena so kaliṁ, ^snp3-10-10-3

Kalinā tena sukhaṁ na vindati. ^snp3-10-10-4

Appamatto ayaṁ kali, ^snp3-10-11-1

Yo akkhesu dhanaparājayo; ^snp3-10-11-2

Sabbassāpi sahāpi attanā, ^snp3-10-11-3

Ayameva mahattaro kali; ^snp3-10-11-4

Yo sugatesu manaṁ padosaye. ^snp3-10-11-5

Sataṁ sahassānaṁ nirabbudānaṁ, ^snp3-10-12-1

Chattiṁsati pañca ca abbudāni; ^snp3-10-12-2

Yamariyagarahī nirayaṁ upeti, ^snp3-10-12-3

Vācaṁ manañca paṇidhāya pāpakaṁ. ^snp3-10-12-4

Abhūtavādī nirayaṁ upeti, ^snp3-10-13-1

Yo vāpi katvā na karomicāha; ^snp3-10-13-2

Ubhopi te pecca samā bhavanti, ^snp3-10-13-3

Nihīnakammā manujā parattha. ^snp3-10-13-4

Yo appaduṭṭhassa narassa dussati, ^snp3-10-14-1

Suddhassa posassa anaṅgaṇassa; ^snp3-10-14-2

Tameva bālaṁ pacceti pāpaṁ, ^snp3-10-14-3

Sukhumo rajo paṭivātaṁva khitto. ^snp3-10-14-4

Yo lobhaguṇe anuyutto, ^snp3-10-15-1

So vacasā paribhāsati aññe; ^snp3-10-15-2

Asaddho kadariyo avadaññū, ^snp3-10-15-3

Macchari pesuṇiyaṁ anuyutto. ^snp3-10-15-4

Mukhadugga vibhūta anariya, ^snp3-10-16-1

Bhūnahu pāpaka dukkaṭakāri; ^snp3-10-16-2

Purisanta kalī avajāta, ^snp3-10-16-3

Mā bahubhāṇidha nerayikosi. ^snp3-10-16-4

Rajamākirasī ahitāya, ^snp3-10-17-1

Sante garahasi kibbisakārī; ^snp3-10-17-2

Bahūni duccaritāni caritvā, ^snp3-10-17-3

Gacchasi kho papataṁ cirarattaṁ. ^snp3-10-17-4

Na hi nassati kassaci kammaṁ, ^snp3-10-18-1

Eti hataṁ labhateva suvāmi; ^snp3-10-18-2

Dukkhaṁ mando paraloke, ^snp3-10-18-3

Attani passati kibbisakārī. ^snp3-10-18-4

Ayosaṅkusamāhataṭṭhānaṁ, ^snp3-10-19-1

Tiṇhadhāramayasūlamupeti; ^snp3-10-19-2

Atha tattaayoguḷasannibhaṁ, ^snp3-10-19-3

Bhojanamatthi tathā patirūpaṁ. ^snp3-10-19-4

Na hi vaggu vadanti vadantā, ^snp3-10-20-1

Nābhijavanti na tāṇamupenti; ^snp3-10-20-2

Aṅgāre santhate sayanti, ^snp3-10-20-3

Ginisampajjalitaṁ pavisanti. ^snp3-10-20-4

Jālena ca onahiyāna, ^snp3-10-21-1

Tattha hananti ayomayakuṭebhi; ^snp3-10-21-2

Andhaṁva timisamāyanti, ^snp3-10-21-3

Taṁ vitatañhi yathā mahikāyo. ^snp3-10-21-4

Atha lohamayaṁ pana kumbhiṁ, ^snp3-10-22-1

Ginisampajjalitaṁ pavisanti; ^snp3-10-22-2

Paccanti hi tāsu cirarattaṁ, ^snp3-10-22-3

Agginisamāsu samuppilavāte. ^snp3-10-22-4

Atha pubbalohitamisse, ^snp3-10-23-1

Tattha kiṁ paccati kibbisakārī; ^snp3-10-23-2

Yaṁ yaṁ disakaṁ adhiseti, ^snp3-10-23-3

Tattha kilissati samphusamāno. ^snp3-10-23-4

Puḷavāvasathe salilasmiṁ, ^snp3-10-24-1

Tattha kiṁ paccati kibbisakārī; ^snp3-10-24-2

Gantuṁ na hi tīramapatthi, ^snp3-10-24-3

Sabbasamā hi samantakapallā. ^snp3-10-24-4

Asipattavanaṁ pana tiṇhaṁ, ^snp3-10-25-1

Taṁ pavisanti samucchidagattā; ^snp3-10-25-2

Jivhaṁ balisena gahetvā, ^snp3-10-25-3

Ārajayārajayā vihananti. ^snp3-10-25-4

Atha vetaraṇiṁ pana duggaṁ, ^snp3-10-26-1

Tiṇhadhārakhuradhāramupenti; ^snp3-10-26-2

Tattha mandā papatanti, ^snp3-10-26-3

Pāpakarā pāpāni karitvā. ^snp3-10-26-4

Khādanti hi tattha rudante, ^snp3-10-27-1

Sāmā sabalā kākolagaṇā ca; ^snp3-10-27-2

Soṇā siṅgālā paṭigiddhā, ^snp3-10-27-3

Kulalā vāyasā ca vitudanti. ^snp3-10-27-4

Kicchā vatayaṁ idha vutti, ^snp3-10-28-1

Yaṁ jano phusati kibbisakārī; ^snp3-10-28-2

Tasmā idha jīvitasese, ^snp3-10-28-3

Kiccakaro siyā naro na cappamajje. ^snp3-10-28-4

Te gaṇitā vidūhi tilavāhā, ^snp3-10-29-1

Ye padume niraye upanītā; ^snp3-10-29-2

Nahutāni hi koṭiyo pañca bhavanti, ^snp3-10-29-3

Dvādasa koṭisatāni punaññā. ^snp3-10-29-4

Yāva dukhā nirayā idha vuttā, ^snp3-10-30-1

Tatthapi tāva ciraṁ vasitabbaṁ; ^snp3-10-30-2

Tasmā sucipesalasādhuguṇesu, ^snp3-10-30-3

Vācaṁ manaṁ satataṁ parirakkhe”ti. ^snp3-10-30-4

Kokālikasuttaṁ dasamaṁ. ^snp3-10-30-5

### Nālakasutta (Sutta Nipāta 3.11) ^snp3-11-0

Ānandajāte tidasagaṇe patīte, ^snp3-11-1-1

Sakkañca indaṁ sucivasane ca deve; ^snp3-11-1-2

Dussaṁ gahetvā atiriva thomayante, ^snp3-11-1-3

Asito isi addasa divāvihāre. ^snp3-11-1-4

Disvāna deve muditamane udagge, ^snp3-11-2-1

Cittiṁ karitvāna idamavoca tattha; ^snp3-11-2-2

“Kiṁ devasaṅgho atiriva kalyarūpo, ^snp3-11-2-3

Dussaṁ gahetvā ramayatha kiṁ paṭicca. ^snp3-11-2-4

Yadāpi āsī asurehi saṅgamo, ^snp3-11-3-1

Jayo surānaṁ asurā parājitā; ^snp3-11-3-2

Tadāpi netādiso lomahaṁsano, ^snp3-11-3-3

Kimabbhutaṁ daṭṭhu marū pamoditā. ^snp3-11-3-4

Seḷenti gāyanti ca vādayanti ca, ^snp3-11-4-1

Bhujāni phoṭenti ca naccayanti ca; ^snp3-11-4-2

Pucchāmi vohaṁ merumuddhavāsine, ^snp3-11-4-3

Dhunātha me saṁsayaṁ khippa mārisā”. ^snp3-11-4-4

“So bodhisatto ratanavaro atulyo, ^snp3-11-5-1

Manussaloke hitasukhatthāya jāto; ^snp3-11-5-2

Sakyāna gāme janapade lumbineyye, ^snp3-11-5-3

Tenamha tuṭṭhā atiriva kalyarūpā. ^snp3-11-5-4

So sabbasattuttamo aggapuggalo, ^snp3-11-6-1

Narāsabho sabbapajānamuttamo; ^snp3-11-6-2

Vattessati cakkamisivhaye vane, ^snp3-11-6-3

Nadaṁva sīho balavā migābhibhū”. ^snp3-11-6-4

Taṁ saddaṁ sutvā turitamavasarī so, ^snp3-11-7-1

Suddhodanassa tada bhavanaṁ upāvisi; ^snp3-11-7-2

Nisajja tattha idamavocāsi sakye, ^snp3-11-7-3

“Kuhiṁ kumāro ahamapi daṭṭhukāmo”. ^snp3-11-7-4

Tato kumāraṁ jalitamiva suvaṇṇaṁ, ^snp3-11-8-1

Ukkāmukheva sukusalasampahaṭṭhaṁ; ^snp3-11-8-2

Daddallamānaṁ siriyā anomavaṇṇaṁ, ^snp3-11-8-3

Dassesu puttaṁ asitavhayassa sakyā. ^snp3-11-8-4

Disvā kumāraṁ sikhimiva pajjalantaṁ, ^snp3-11-9-1

Tārāsabhaṁva nabhasigamaṁ visuddhaṁ; ^snp3-11-9-2

Suriyaṁ tapantaṁ saradarivabbhamuttaṁ, ^snp3-11-9-3

Ānandajāto vipulamalattha pītiṁ. ^snp3-11-9-4

Anekasākhañca sahassamaṇḍalaṁ, ^snp3-11-10-1

Chattaṁ marū dhārayumantalikkhe; ^snp3-11-10-2

Suvaṇṇadaṇḍā vītipatanti cāmarā, ^snp3-11-10-3

Na dissare cāmarachattagāhakā. ^snp3-11-10-4

Disvā jaṭī kaṇhasirivhayo isi, ^snp3-11-11-1

Suvaṇṇanikkhaṁ viya paṇḍukambale; ^snp3-11-11-2

Setañca chattaṁ dhariyanta muddhani, ^snp3-11-11-3

Udaggacitto sumano paṭiggahe. ^snp3-11-11-4

Paṭiggahetvā pana sakyapuṅgavaṁ, ^snp3-11-12-1

Jigīsako lakkhaṇamantapāragū; ^snp3-11-12-2

Pasannacitto giramabbhudīrayi, ^snp3-11-12-3

“Anuttarāyaṁ dvipadānamuttamo”. ^snp3-11-12-4

Athattano gamanamanussaranto, ^snp3-11-13-1

Akalyarūpo gaḷayati assukāni; ^snp3-11-13-2

Disvāna sakyā isimavocuṁ rudantaṁ, ^snp3-11-13-3

“No ce kumāre bhavissati antarāyo”. ^snp3-11-13-4

Disvāna sakye isimavoca akalye, ^snp3-11-14-1

“Nāhaṁ kumāre ahitamanussarāmi; ^snp3-11-14-2

Na cāpimassa bhavissati antarāyo, ^snp3-11-14-3

Na orakāyaṁ adhimānasā bhavātha. ^snp3-11-14-4

Sambodhiyaggaṁ phusissatāyaṁ kumāro, ^snp3-11-15-1

So dhammacakkaṁ paramavisuddhadassī; ^snp3-11-15-2

Vattessatāyaṁ bahujanahitānukampī, ^snp3-11-15-3

Vitthārikassa bhavissati brahmacariyaṁ. ^snp3-11-15-4

Mamañca āyu na ciramidhāvaseso, ^snp3-11-16-1

Athantarā me bhavissati kālakiriyā; ^snp3-11-16-2

Sohaṁ na sossaṁ asamadhurassa dhammaṁ, ^snp3-11-16-3

Tenamhi aṭṭo byasanaṅgato aghāvī”. ^snp3-11-16-4

So sākiyānaṁ vipulaṁ janetvā pītiṁ, ^snp3-11-17-1

Antepuramhā niggamā brahmacārī; ^snp3-11-17-2

So bhāgineyyaṁ sayaṁ anukampamāno, ^snp3-11-17-3

Samādapesi asamadhurassa dhamme. ^snp3-11-17-4

“Buddhoti ghosaṁ yada parato suṇāsi, ^snp3-11-18-1

Sambodhipatto vivarati dhammamaggaṁ; ^snp3-11-18-2

Gantvāna tattha samayaṁ paripucchamāno, ^snp3-11-18-3

Carassu tasmiṁ bhagavati brahmacariyaṁ”. ^snp3-11-18-4

Tenānusiṭṭho hitamanena tādinā, ^snp3-11-19-1

Anāgate paramavisuddhadassinā; ^snp3-11-19-2

So nālako upacitapuññasañcayo, ^snp3-11-19-3

Jinaṁ patikkhaṁ parivasi rakkhitindriyo. ^snp3-11-19-4

Sutvāna ghosaṁ jinavaracakkavattane, ^snp3-11-20-1

Gantvāna disvā isinisabhaṁ pasanno; ^snp3-11-20-2

Moneyyaseṭṭhaṁ munipavaraṁ apucchi, ^snp3-11-20-3

Samāgate asitāvhayassa sāsaneti. ^snp3-11-20-4

Vatthugāthā niṭṭhitā. ^snp3-11-20-5

“Aññātametaṁ vacanaṁ, ^snp3-11-21-1

Asitassa yathātathaṁ; ^snp3-11-21-2

Taṁ taṁ gotama pucchāmi, ^snp3-11-21-3

Sabbadhammāna pāraguṁ. ^snp3-11-21-4

Anagāriyupetassa, ^snp3-11-22-1

Bhikkhācariyaṁ jigīsato; ^snp3-11-22-2

Muni pabrūhi me puṭṭho, ^snp3-11-22-3

Moneyyaṁ uttamaṁ padaṁ”. ^snp3-11-22-4

“Moneyyaṁ te upaññissaṁ, ^snp3-11-23-1

(iti bhagavā) ^snp3-11-23-2

Dukkaraṁ durabhisambhavaṁ; ^snp3-11-23-3

Handa te naṁ pavakkhāmi, ^snp3-11-23-4

Santhambhassu daḷho bhava. ^snp3-11-23-5

Samānabhāgaṁ kubbetha, ^snp3-11-24-1

Gāme akkuṭṭhavanditaṁ; ^snp3-11-24-2

Manopadosaṁ rakkheyya, ^snp3-11-24-3

Santo anuṇṇato care. ^snp3-11-24-4

Uccāvacā niccharanti, ^snp3-11-25-1

Dāye aggisikhūpamā; ^snp3-11-25-2

Nāriyo muniṁ palobhenti, ^snp3-11-25-3

Tā su taṁ mā palobhayuṁ. ^snp3-11-25-4

Virato methunā dhammā, ^snp3-11-26-1

Hitvā kāme paropare; ^snp3-11-26-2

Aviruddho asāratto, ^snp3-11-26-3

Pāṇesu tasathāvare. ^snp3-11-26-4

Yathā ahaṁ tathā ete, ^snp3-11-27-1

Yathā ete tathā ahaṁ; ^snp3-11-27-2

Attānaṁ upamaṁ katvā, ^snp3-11-27-3

Na haneyya na ghātaye. ^snp3-11-27-4

Hitvā icchañca lobhañca, ^snp3-11-28-1

Yattha satto puthujjano; ^snp3-11-28-2

Cakkhumā paṭipajjeyya, ^snp3-11-28-3

Tareyya narakaṁ imaṁ. ^snp3-11-28-4

Ūnūdaro mitāhāro, ^snp3-11-29-1

Appicchassa alolupo; ^snp3-11-29-2

Sadā icchāya nicchāto, ^snp3-11-29-3

Aniccho hoti nibbuto. ^snp3-11-29-4

Sa piṇḍacāraṁ caritvā, ^snp3-11-30-1

Vanantamabhihāraye; ^snp3-11-30-2

Upaṭṭhito rukkhamūlasmiṁ, ^snp3-11-30-3

Āsanūpagato muni. ^snp3-11-30-4

Sa jhānapasuto dhīro, ^snp3-11-31-1

Vanante ramito siyā; ^snp3-11-31-2

Jhāyetha rukkhamūlasmiṁ, ^snp3-11-31-3

Attānamabhitosayaṁ. ^snp3-11-31-4

Tato ratyā vivasāne, ^snp3-11-32-1

Gāmantamabhihāraye; ^snp3-11-32-2

Avhānaṁ nābhinandeyya, ^snp3-11-32-3

Abhihārañca gāmato. ^snp3-11-32-4

Na munī gāmamāgamma, ^snp3-11-33-1

Kulesu sahasā care; ^snp3-11-33-2

Ghāsesanaṁ chinnakatho, ^snp3-11-33-3

Na vācaṁ payutaṁ bhaṇe. ^snp3-11-33-4

Alatthaṁ yadidaṁ sādhu, ^snp3-11-34-1

Nālatthaṁ kusalaṁ iti; ^snp3-11-34-2

Ubhayeneva so tādī, ^snp3-11-34-3

Rukkhaṁvupanivattati. ^snp3-11-34-4

Sa pattapāṇi vicaranto, ^snp3-11-35-1

Amūgo mūgasammato; ^snp3-11-35-2

Appaṁ dānaṁ na hīḷeyya, ^snp3-11-35-3

Dātāraṁ nāvajāniyā. ^snp3-11-35-4

Uccāvacā hi paṭipadā, ^snp3-11-36-1

Samaṇena pakāsitā; ^snp3-11-36-2

Na pāraṁ diguṇaṁ yanti, ^snp3-11-36-3

Nayidaṁ ekaguṇaṁ mutaṁ. ^snp3-11-36-4

Yassa ca visatā natthi, ^snp3-11-37-1

Chinnasotassa bhikkhuno; ^snp3-11-37-2

Kiccākiccappahīnassa, ^snp3-11-37-3

Pariḷāho na vijjati. ^snp3-11-37-4

Moneyyaṁ te upaññissaṁ, ^snp3-11-38-1

Khuradhārūpamo bhave; ^snp3-11-38-2

Jivhāya tālumāhacca, ^snp3-11-38-3

Udare saññato siyā. ^snp3-11-38-4

Alīnacitto ca siyā, ^snp3-11-39-1

Na cāpi bahu cintaye; ^snp3-11-39-2

Nirāmagandho asito, ^snp3-11-39-3

Brahmacariyaparāyaṇo. ^snp3-11-39-4

Ekāsanassa sikkhetha, ^snp3-11-40-1

Samaṇūpāsanassa ca; ^snp3-11-40-2

Ekattaṁ monamakkhātaṁ, ^snp3-11-40-3

Eko ce abhiramissasi; ^snp3-11-40-4

Atha bhāhisi dasadisā. ^snp3-11-40-5

Sutvā dhīrānaṁ nighosaṁ, ^snp3-11-41-1

Jhāyīnaṁ kāmacāginaṁ; ^snp3-11-41-2

Tato hiriñca saddhañca, ^snp3-11-41-3

Bhiyyo kubbetha māmako. ^snp3-11-41-4

Taṁ nadīhi vijānātha, ^snp3-11-42-1

Sobbhesu padaresu ca; ^snp3-11-42-2

Saṇantā yanti kusobbhā, ^snp3-11-42-3

Tuṇhī yanti mahodadhī. ^snp3-11-42-4

Yadūnakaṁ taṁ saṇati, ^snp3-11-43-1

Yaṁ pūraṁ santameva taṁ; ^snp3-11-43-2

Aḍḍhakumbhūpamo bālo, ^snp3-11-43-3

Rahado pūrova paṇḍito. ^snp3-11-43-4

Yaṁ samaṇo bahuṁ bhāsati, ^snp3-11-44-1

Upetaṁ atthasañhitaṁ; ^snp3-11-44-2

Jānaṁ so dhammaṁ deseti, ^snp3-11-44-3

Jānaṁ so bahu bhāsati. ^snp3-11-44-4

Yo ca jānaṁ saṁyatatto, ^snp3-11-45-1

Jānaṁ na bahu bhāsati; ^snp3-11-45-2

Sa munī monamarahati, ^snp3-11-45-3

Sa munī monamajjhagā”ti. ^snp3-11-45-4

Nālakasuttaṁ ekādasamaṁ. ^snp3-11-45-5

### Dvayatānupassanāsutta (Sutta Nipāta 3.12) ^snp3-12-0

Evaṁ me sutaṁ— ^snp3-12-1-1

ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati pubbārāme migāramātupāsāde. ^snp3-12-1-2

Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā tadahuposathe pannarase puṇṇāya puṇṇamāya rattiyā bhikkhusaṅghaparivuto abbhokāse nisinno hoti. ^snp3-12-1-3

Atha kho bhagavā tuṇhībhūtaṁ tuṇhībhūtaṁ bhikkhusaṅghaṁ anuviloketvā bhikkhū āmantesi: ^snp3-12-1-4

“‘Ye te, bhikkhave, kusalā dhammā ariyā niyyānikā sambodhagāmino, tesaṁ vo, bhikkhave, kusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ ariyānaṁ niyyānikānaṁ sambodhagāmīnaṁ kā upanisā savanāyā’ti, iti ce, bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, te evamassu vacanīyā: ^snp3-12-2-1

‘yāvadeva dvayatānaṁ dhammānaṁ yathābhūtaṁ ñāṇāyā’ti. ^snp3-12-2-2

Kiñca dvayataṁ vadetha? ^snp3-12-2-3

Idaṁ dukkhaṁ, ayaṁ dukkhasamudayoti ayamekānupassanā. ^snp3-12-3-1

Ayaṁ dukkhanirodho, ayaṁ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadāti, ayaṁ dutiyānupassanā. ^snp3-12-3-2

Evaṁ sammā dvayatānupassino kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpino pahitattassa viharato dvinnaṁ phalānaṁ aññataraṁ phalaṁ pāṭikaṅkhaṁ— ^snp3-12-3-3

diṭṭheva dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese anāgāmitā”ti. ^snp3-12-3-4

Idamavoca bhagavā. ^snp3-12-4-1

Idaṁ vatvāna sugato athāparaṁ etadavoca satthā: ^snp3-12-4-2

“Ye dukkhaṁ nappajānanti, ^snp3-12-5-1

atho dukkhassa sambhavaṁ; ^snp3-12-5-2

Yattha ca sabbaso dukkhaṁ, ^snp3-12-5-3

asesaṁ uparujjhati; ^snp3-12-5-4

Tañca maggaṁ na jānanti, ^snp3-12-5-5

dukkhūpasamagāminaṁ. ^snp3-12-5-6

Cetovimuttihīnā te, ^snp3-12-6-1

Atho paññāvimuttiyā; ^snp3-12-6-2

Abhabbā te antakiriyāya, ^snp3-12-6-3

Te ve jātijarūpagā. ^snp3-12-6-4

Ye ca dukkhaṁ pajānanti, ^snp3-12-7-1

atho dukkhassa sambhavaṁ; ^snp3-12-7-2

Yattha ca sabbaso dukkhaṁ, ^snp3-12-7-3

asesaṁ uparujjhati; ^snp3-12-7-4

Tañca maggaṁ pajānanti, ^snp3-12-7-5

dukkhūpasamagāminaṁ. ^snp3-12-7-6

Cetovimuttisampannā, ^snp3-12-8-1

Atho paññāvimuttiyā; ^snp3-12-8-2

Bhabbā te antakiriyāya, ^snp3-12-8-3

Na te jātijarūpagāti. ^snp3-12-8-4

‘Siyā aññenapi pariyāyena sammā dvayatānupassanā’ti, iti ce, bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu; ^snp3-12-9-1

‘siyā’tissu vacanīyā. ^snp3-12-9-2

Kathañca siyā? ^snp3-12-9-3

Yaṁ kiñci dukkhaṁ sambhoti sabbaṁ upadhipaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. ^snp3-12-9-4

Upadhīnaṁ tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṁ dutiyānupassanā. ^snp3-12-9-5

Evaṁ sammā …pe… ^snp3-12-9-6

athāparaṁ etadavoca satthā: ^snp3-12-9-7

“Upadhinidānā pabhavanti dukkhā, ^snp3-12-10-1

Ye keci lokasmimanekarūpā; ^snp3-12-10-2

Yo ve avidvā upadhiṁ karoti, ^snp3-12-10-3

Punappunaṁ dukkhamupeti mando; ^snp3-12-10-4

Tasmā pajānaṁ upadhiṁ na kayirā, ^snp3-12-10-5

Dukkhassa jātippabhavānupassīti. ^snp3-12-10-6

avijjāyeva sā gati. ^snp3-12-12-4

“Yaṁ kiñci dukkhaṁ sambhoti, ^snp3-12-38-1

“Yaṁ kiñci dukkhaṁ sambhoti, ^snp3-12-42-1

Sabbaṁ iñjitapaccayā; ^snp3-12-42-2

Iñjitānaṁ nirodhena, ^snp3-12-42-3

Natthi dukkhassa sambhavo. ^snp3-12-42-4

Etamādīnavaṁ ñatvā, ^snp3-12-43-1

Saṅkhāre uparundhiya; ^snp3-12-43-4

Anejo anupādāno, ^snp3-12-43-5

Sato bhikkhu paribbajeti. ^snp3-12-43-6

‘Siyā aññenapi …pe… ^snp3-12-44-1

kathañca siyā? ^snp3-12-44-2

Nissitassa calitaṁ hotīti, ayamekānupassanā. ^snp3-12-44-3

Anissito na calatīti, ayaṁ dutiyānupassanā. ^snp3-12-44-4

Evaṁ sammā …pe… ^snp3-12-44-5

athāparaṁ etadavoca satthā: ^snp3-12-44-6

“Anissito na calati, ^snp3-12-45-1

Nissito ca upādiyaṁ; ^snp3-12-45-2

Itthabhāvaññathābhāvaṁ, ^snp3-12-45-3

Saṁsāraṁ nātivattati. ^snp3-12-45-4

Etamādīnavaṁ ñatvā, ^snp3-12-46-1

Nissayesu mahabbhayaṁ; ^snp3-12-46-2

Anissito anupādāno, ^snp3-12-46-3

Sato bhikkhu paribbajeti. ^snp3-12-46-4

‘Siyā aññenapi …pe… ^snp3-12-47-1

kathañca siyā? ^snp3-12-47-2

Rūpehi, bhikkhave, arūpā santatarāti, ayamekānupassanā. ^snp3-12-47-3

Arūpehi nirodho santataroti, ayaṁ dutiyānupassanā. ^snp3-12-47-4

Evaṁ sammā …pe… ^snp3-12-47-5

athāparaṁ etadavoca satthā: ^snp3-12-47-6

“Ye ca rūpūpagā sattā, ^snp3-12-48-1

Ye ca arūpaṭṭhāyino; ^snp3-12-48-2

Nirodhaṁ appajānantā, ^snp3-12-48-3

Āgantāro punabbhavaṁ. ^snp3-12-48-4

Ye ca rūpe pariññāya, ^snp3-12-49-1

Arūpesu asaṇṭhitā; ^snp3-12-49-2

Nirodhe ye vimuccanti, ^snp3-12-49-3

Te janā maccuhāyinoti. ^snp3-12-49-4

‘Siyā aññenapi …pe… ^snp3-12-50-1

kathañca siyā? ^snp3-12-50-2

Yaṁ, bhikkhave, sadevakassa lokassa samārakassa sabrahmakassa sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya idaṁ saccanti upanijjhāyitaṁ tadamariyānaṁ etaṁ musāti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya sudiṭṭhaṁ, ayamekānupassanā. ^snp3-12-50-3

Yaṁ, bhikkhave, sadevakassa …pe… sadevamanussāya idaṁ musāti upanijjhāyitaṁ, tadamariyānaṁ etaṁ saccanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya sudiṭṭhaṁ, ayaṁ dutiyānupassanā. ^snp3-12-50-4

Evaṁ sammā …pe… ^snp3-12-50-5

athāparaṁ etadavoca satthā: ^snp3-12-50-6

“Anattani attamāniṁ, ^snp3-12-51-1

Passa lokaṁ sadevakaṁ; ^snp3-12-51-2

Niviṭṭhaṁ nāmarūpasmiṁ, ^snp3-12-51-3

Idaṁ saccanti maññati. ^snp3-12-51-4

Yena yena hi maññanti, ^snp3-12-52-1

Tato taṁ hoti aññathā; ^snp3-12-52-2

Tañhi tassa musā hoti, ^snp3-12-52-3

Mosadhammañhi ittaraṁ. ^snp3-12-52-4

Amosadhammaṁ nibbānaṁ, ^snp3-12-53-1

Tadariyā saccato vidū; ^snp3-12-53-2

Te ve saccābhisamayā, ^snp3-12-53-3

Nicchātā parinibbutāti. ^snp3-12-53-4

‘Siyā aññenapi pariyāyena sammā dvayatānupassanā’ti, iti ce, bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu; ^snp3-12-54-1

‘siyā’tissu vacanīyā. ^snp3-12-54-2

Kathañca siyā? ^snp3-12-54-3

Yaṁ, bhikkhave, sadevakassa lokassa samārakassa sabrahmakassa sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya idaṁ sukhanti upanijjhāyitaṁ, tadamariyānaṁ etaṁ dukkhanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya sudiṭṭhaṁ, ayamekānupassanā. ^snp3-12-54-4

Yaṁ, bhikkhave, sadevakassa …pe… sadevamanussāya idaṁ dukkhanti upanijjhāyitaṁ tadamariyānaṁ etaṁ sukhanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya sudiṭṭhaṁ, ayaṁ dutiyānupassanā. ^snp3-12-54-5

Evaṁ sammā dvayatānupassino kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpino pahitattassa viharato dvinnaṁ phalānaṁ aññataraṁ phalaṁ pāṭikaṅkhaṁ— ^snp3-12-54-6

diṭṭheva dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese anāgāmitāti. ^snp3-12-54-7

Idamavoca bhagavā. ^snp3-12-54-8

Idaṁ vatvāna sugato athāparaṁ etadavoca satthā: ^snp3-12-54-9

“Rūpā saddā rasā gandhā, ^snp3-12-55-1

Phassā dhammā ca kevalā; ^snp3-12-55-2

Iṭṭhā kantā manāpā ca, ^snp3-12-55-3

Yāvatatthīti vuccati. ^snp3-12-55-4

Sadevakassa lokassa, ^snp3-12-56-1

Ete vo sukhasammatā; ^snp3-12-56-2

Yattha cete nirujjhanti, ^snp3-12-56-3

Taṁ nesaṁ dukkhasammataṁ. ^snp3-12-56-4

Sukhanti diṭṭhamariyehi, ^snp3-12-57-1

Sakkāyassuparodhanaṁ; ^snp3-12-57-2

Paccanīkamidaṁ hoti, ^snp3-12-57-3

Sabbalokena passataṁ. ^snp3-12-57-4

Yaṁ pare sukhato āhu, ^snp3-12-58-1

Tadariyā āhu dukkhato; ^snp3-12-58-2

Yaṁ pare dukkhato āhu, ^snp3-12-58-3

Tadariyā sukhato vidū. ^snp3-12-58-4

Passa dhammaṁ durājānaṁ, ^snp3-12-59-1

Sampamūḷhetthaviddasu; ^snp3-12-59-2

Nivutānaṁ tamo hoti, ^snp3-12-59-3

Andhakāro apassataṁ. ^snp3-12-59-4

Satañca vivaṭaṁ hoti, ^snp3-12-60-1

Āloko passatāmiva; ^snp3-12-60-2

Santike na vijānanti, ^snp3-12-60-3

Magā dhammassa kovidā. ^snp3-12-60-4

Bhavarāgaparetehi, ^snp3-12-61-1

Bhavasotānusāribhi; ^snp3-12-61-2

Māradheyyānupannehi, ^snp3-12-61-3

Nāyaṁ dhammo susambudho. ^snp3-12-61-4

Ko nu aññatra mariyehi, ^snp3-12-62-1

Padaṁ sambuddhumarahati; ^snp3-12-62-2

Yaṁ padaṁ sammadaññāya, ^snp3-12-62-3

Parinibbanti anāsavā”ti. ^snp3-12-62-4

Idamavoca bhagavā. ^snp3-12-63-1

Attamanā te bhikkhū bhagavato bhāsitaṁ abhinandunti. ^snp3-12-63-2

Imasmiñca pana veyyākaraṇasmiṁ bhaññamāne saṭṭhimattānaṁ bhikkhūnaṁ anupādāya āsavehi cittāni vimucciṁsūti. ^snp3-12-63-3

Dvayatānupassanāsuttaṁ dvādasamaṁ. ^snp3-12-63-4

Tassuddānaṁ ^snp3-12-64-0

Saccaṁ upadhi avijjā ca, ^snp3-12-64-1

saṅkhāre viññāṇapañcamaṁ; ^snp3-12-64-2

Phassavedaniyā taṇhā, ^snp3-12-64-3

upādānārambhaāhārā; ^snp3-12-64-4

Iñjitaṁ calitaṁ rūpaṁ, ^snp3-12-64-5

saccaṁ dukkhena soḷasāti. ^snp3-12-64-6

Mahāvaggo tatiyo. ^snp3-12-64-7

Tassuddānaṁ ^snp3-12-65-0

Pabbajjā ca padhānañca, ^snp3-12-65-1

subhāsitañca sundari; ^snp3-12-65-2

Māghasuttaṁ sabhiyo ca, ^snp3-12-65-3

selo sallañca vuccati. ^snp3-12-65-4

Vāseṭṭho cāpi kokāli, ^snp3-12-66-1

Nālako dvayatānupassanā; ^snp3-12-66-2

Dvādasetāni suttāni, ^snp3-12-66-3

Mahāvaggoti vuccatīti. ^snp3-12-66-4

## Vagga 4 ^vagga4-0

### Kāmasutta (Sutta Nipāta 4.1) ^snp4-1-0

Kāmaṁ kāmayamānassa, ^snp4-1-1-1

tassa ce taṁ samijjhati; ^snp4-1-1-2

Addhā pītimano hoti, ^snp4-1-1-3

laddhā macco yadicchati. ^snp4-1-1-4

Tassa ce kāmayānassa, ^snp4-1-2-1

chandajātassa jantuno; ^snp4-1-2-2

Te kāmā parihāyanti, ^snp4-1-2-3

sallaviddhova ruppati. ^snp4-1-2-4

Yo kāme parivajjeti, ^snp4-1-3-1

sappasseva padā siro; ^snp4-1-3-2

Somaṁ visattikaṁ loke, ^snp4-1-3-3

sato samativattati. ^snp4-1-3-4

Khettaṁ vatthuṁ hiraññaṁ vā, ^snp4-1-4-1

gavāssaṁ dāsaporisaṁ; ^snp4-1-4-2

Thiyo bandhū puthu kāme, ^snp4-1-4-3

yo naro anugijjhati. ^snp4-1-4-4

Abalā naṁ balīyanti, ^snp4-1-5-1

maddantenaṁ parissayā; ^snp4-1-5-2

Tato naṁ dukkhamanveti, ^snp4-1-5-3

nāvaṁ bhinnamivodakaṁ. ^snp4-1-5-4

Tasmā jantu sadā sato, ^snp4-1-6-1

Kāmāni parivajjaye; ^snp4-1-6-2

Te pahāya tare oghaṁ, ^snp4-1-6-3

Nāvaṁ sitvāva pāragūti. ^snp4-1-6-4

Kāmasuttaṁ paṭhamaṁ. ^snp4-1-6-5

### Guhaṭṭhakasutta (Sutta Nipāta 4.2) ^snp4-2-0

Satto guhāyaṁ bahunābhichanno, ^snp4-2-1-1

Tiṭṭhaṁ naro mohanasmiṁ pagāḷho; ^snp4-2-1-2

Dūre vivekā hi tathāvidho so, ^snp4-2-1-3

Kāmā hi loke na hi suppahāyā. ^snp4-2-1-4

Icchānidānā bhavasātabaddhā, ^snp4-2-2-1

Te duppamuñcā na hi aññamokkhā; ^snp4-2-2-2

Pacchā pure vāpi apekkhamānā, ^snp4-2-2-3

Ime va kāme purime va jappaṁ. ^snp4-2-2-4

Kāmesu giddhā pasutā pamūḷhā, ^snp4-2-3-1

Avadāniyā te visame niviṭṭhā; ^snp4-2-3-2

Dukkhūpanītā paridevayanti, ^snp4-2-3-3

Kiṁsū bhavissāma ito cutāse. ^snp4-2-3-4

Tasmā hi sikkhetha idheva jantu, ^snp4-2-4-1

Yaṁ kiñci jaññā visamanti loke; ^snp4-2-4-2

Na tassa hetū visamaṁ careyya, ^snp4-2-4-3

Appañhidaṁ jīvitamāhu dhīrā. ^snp4-2-4-4

Passāmi loke pariphandamānaṁ, ^snp4-2-5-1

Pajaṁ imaṁ taṇhagataṁ bhavesu; ^snp4-2-5-2

Hīnā narā maccumukhe lapanti, ^snp4-2-5-3

Avītataṇhāse bhavābhavesu. ^snp4-2-5-4

Mamāyite passatha phandamāne, ^snp4-2-6-1

Maccheva appodake khīṇasote; ^snp4-2-6-2

Etampi disvā amamo careyya, ^snp4-2-6-3

Bhavesu āsattimakubbamāno. ^snp4-2-6-4

Ubhosu antesu vineyya chandaṁ, ^snp4-2-7-1

Phassaṁ pariññāya anānugiddho; ^snp4-2-7-2

Yadattagarahī tadakubbamāno, ^snp4-2-7-3

Na lippatī diṭṭhasutesu dhīro. ^snp4-2-7-4

Saññaṁ pariññā vitareyya oghaṁ, ^snp4-2-8-1

Pariggahesu muni nopalitto; ^snp4-2-8-2

Abbūḷhasallo caramappamatto, ^snp4-2-8-3

Nāsīsatī lokamimaṁ parañcāti. ^snp4-2-8-4

Guhaṭṭhakasuttaṁ dutiyaṁ. ^snp4-2-8-5

### Duṭṭhaṭṭhakasutta (Sutta Nipāta 4.3) ^snp4-3-0

Vadanti ve duṭṭhamanāpi eke, ^snp4-3-1-1

Athopi ve saccamanā vadanti; ^snp4-3-1-2

Vādañca jātaṁ muni no upeti, ^snp4-3-1-3

Tasmā munī natthi khilo kuhiñci. ^snp4-3-1-4

Sakañhi diṭṭhiṁ kathamaccayeyya, ^snp4-3-2-1

Chandānunīto ruciyā niviṭṭho; ^snp4-3-2-2

Sayaṁ samattāni pakubbamāno, ^snp4-3-2-3

Yathā hi jāneyya tathā vadeyya. ^snp4-3-2-4

Yo attano sīlavatāni jantu, ^snp4-3-3-1

Anānupuṭṭhova paresa pāva; ^snp4-3-3-2

Anariyadhammaṁ kusalā tamāhu, ^snp4-3-3-3

Yo ātumānaṁ sayameva pāva. ^snp4-3-3-4

Santo ca bhikkhu abhinibbutatto, ^snp4-3-4-1

Itihanti sīlesu akatthamāno; ^snp4-3-4-2

Tamariyadhammaṁ kusalā vadanti, ^snp4-3-4-3

Yassussadā natthi kuhiñci loke. ^snp4-3-4-4

Pakappitā saṅkhatā yassa dhammā, ^snp4-3-5-1

Purakkhatā santi avīvadātā; ^snp4-3-5-2

Yadattani passati ānisaṁsaṁ, ^snp4-3-5-3

Taṁ nissito kuppapaṭiccasantiṁ. ^snp4-3-5-4

Diṭṭhīnivesā na hi svātivattā, ^snp4-3-6-1

Dhammesu niccheyya samuggahītaṁ; ^snp4-3-6-2

Tasmā naro tesu nivesanesu, ^snp4-3-6-3

Nirassatī ādiyatī ca dhammaṁ. ^snp4-3-6-4

Dhonassa hi natthi kuhiñci loke, ^snp4-3-7-1

Pakappitā diṭṭhi bhavābhavesu; ^snp4-3-7-2

Māyañca mānañca pahāya dhono, ^snp4-3-7-3

Sa kena gaccheyya anūpayo so. ^snp4-3-7-4

Upayo hi dhammesu upeti vādaṁ, ^snp4-3-8-1

Anūpayaṁ kena kathaṁ vadeyya; ^snp4-3-8-2

Attā nirattā na hi tassa atthi, ^snp4-3-8-3

Adhosi so diṭṭhimidheva sabbanti. ^snp4-3-8-4

Duṭṭhaṭṭhakasuttaṁ tatiyaṁ. ^snp4-3-8-5

### Suddhaṭṭhakasutta (Sutta Nipāta 4.4) ^snp4-4-0

Passāmi suddhaṁ paramaṁ arogaṁ, ^snp4-4-1-1

Diṭṭhena saṁsuddhi narassa hoti; ^snp4-4-1-2

Evābhijānaṁ paramanti ñatvā, ^snp4-4-1-3

Suddhānupassīti pacceti ñāṇaṁ. ^snp4-4-1-4

Diṭṭhena ce suddhi narassa hoti, ^snp4-4-2-1

Ñāṇena vā so pajahāti dukkhaṁ; ^snp4-4-2-2

Aññena so sujjhati sopadhīko, ^snp4-4-2-3

Diṭṭhī hi naṁ pāva tathā vadānaṁ. ^snp4-4-2-4

Na brāhmaṇo aññato suddhimāha, ^snp4-4-3-1

Diṭṭhe sute sīlavate mute vā; ^snp4-4-3-2

Puññe ca pāpe ca anūpalitto, ^snp4-4-3-3

Attañjaho nayidha pakubbamāno. ^snp4-4-3-4

Purimaṁ pahāya aparaṁ sitāse, ^snp4-4-4-1

Ejānugā te na taranti saṅgaṁ; ^snp4-4-4-2

Te uggahāyanti nirassajanti, ^snp4-4-4-3

Kapīva sākhaṁ pamuñcaṁ gahāyaṁ. ^snp4-4-4-4

Sayaṁ samādāya vatāni jantu, ^snp4-4-5-1

Uccāvacaṁ gacchati saññasatto; ^snp4-4-5-2

Vidvā ca vedehi samecca dhammaṁ, ^snp4-4-5-3

Na uccāvacaṁ gacchati bhūripañño. ^snp4-4-5-4

Sa sabbadhammesu visenibhūto, ^snp4-4-6-1

Yaṁ kiñci diṭṭhaṁ va sutaṁ mutaṁ vā; ^snp4-4-6-2

Tameva dassiṁ vivaṭaṁ carantaṁ, ^snp4-4-6-3

Kenīdha lokasmi vikappayeyya. ^snp4-4-6-4

Na kappayanti na purekkharonti, ^snp4-4-7-1

Accantasuddhīti na te vadanti; ^snp4-4-7-2

Ādānaganthaṁ gathitaṁ visajja, ^snp4-4-7-3

Āsaṁ na kubbanti kuhiñci loke. ^snp4-4-7-4

Sīmātigo brāhmaṇo tassa natthi, ^snp4-4-8-1

Ñatvā va disvā va samuggahītaṁ; ^snp4-4-8-2

Na rāgarāgī na virāgaratto, ^snp4-4-8-3

Tassīdha natthi paramuggahītanti. ^snp4-4-8-4

Suddhaṭṭhakasuttaṁ catutthaṁ. ^snp4-4-8-5

### Paramaṭṭhakasutta (Sutta Nipāta 4.5) ^snp4-5-0

Paramanti diṭṭhīsu paribbasāno, ^snp4-5-1-1

Yaduttari kurute jantu loke; ^snp4-5-1-2

Hīnāti aññe tato sabbamāha, ^snp4-5-1-3

Tasmā vivādāni avītivatto. ^snp4-5-1-4

Yadattanī passati ānisaṁsaṁ, ^snp4-5-2-1

Diṭṭhe sute sīlavate mute vā; ^snp4-5-2-2

Tadeva so tattha samuggahāya, ^snp4-5-2-3

Nihīnato passati sabbamaññaṁ. ^snp4-5-2-4

Taṁ vāpi ganthaṁ kusalā vadanti, ^snp4-5-3-1

Yaṁ nissito passati hīnamaññaṁ; ^snp4-5-3-2

Tasmā hi diṭṭhaṁ va sutaṁ mutaṁ vā, ^snp4-5-3-3

Sīlabbataṁ bhikkhu na nissayeyya. ^snp4-5-3-4

Diṭṭhimpi lokasmiṁ na kappayeyya, ^snp4-5-4-1

Ñāṇena vā sīlavatena vāpi; ^snp4-5-4-2

Samoti attānamanūpaneyya, ^snp4-5-4-3

Hīno na maññetha visesi vāpi. ^snp4-5-4-4

Attaṁ pahāya anupādiyāno, ^snp4-5-5-1

Ñāṇepi so nissayaṁ no karoti; ^snp4-5-5-2

Sa ve viyattesu na vaggasārī, ^snp4-5-5-3

Diṭṭhimpi so na pacceti kiñci. ^snp4-5-5-4

Yassūbhayante paṇidhīdha natthi, ^snp4-5-6-1

Bhavābhavāya idha vā huraṁ vā; ^snp4-5-6-2

Nivesanā tassa na santi keci, ^snp4-5-6-3

Dhammesu niccheyya samuggahītaṁ. ^snp4-5-6-4

Tassīdha diṭṭhe va sute mute vā, ^snp4-5-7-1

Pakappitā natthi aṇūpi saññā; ^snp4-5-7-2

Taṁ brāhmaṇaṁ diṭṭhimanādiyānaṁ, ^snp4-5-7-3

Kenīdha lokasmiṁ vikappayeyya. ^snp4-5-7-4

Na kappayanti na purekkharonti, ^snp4-5-8-1

Dhammāpi tesaṁ na paṭicchitāse; ^snp4-5-8-2

Na brāhmaṇo sīlavatena neyyo, ^snp4-5-8-3

Pāraṅgato na pacceti tādīti. ^snp4-5-8-4

Paramaṭṭhakasuttaṁ pañcamaṁ. ^snp4-5-8-5

### Jarāsutta (Sutta Nipāta 4.6) ^snp4-6-0

Appaṁ vata jīvitaṁ idaṁ, ^snp4-6-1-1

Oraṁ vassasatāpi miyyati; ^snp4-6-1-2

Yo cepi aticca jīvati, ^snp4-6-1-3

Atha kho so jarasāpi miyyati. ^snp4-6-1-4

Socanti janā mamāyite, ^snp4-6-2-1

Na hi santi niccā pariggahā; ^snp4-6-2-2

Vinābhāvasantamevidaṁ, ^snp4-6-2-3

Iti disvā nāgāramāvase. ^snp4-6-2-4

Maraṇenapi taṁ pahīyati, ^snp4-6-3-1

Yaṁ puriso mamidanti maññati; ^snp4-6-3-2

Etampi viditvā paṇḍito, ^snp4-6-3-3

Na mamattāya nametha māmako. ^snp4-6-3-4

Supinena yathāpi saṅgataṁ, ^snp4-6-4-1

Paṭibuddho puriso na passati; ^snp4-6-4-2

Evampi piyāyitaṁ janaṁ, ^snp4-6-4-3

Petaṁ kālaṅkataṁ na passati. ^snp4-6-4-4

Diṭṭhāpi sutāpi te janā, ^snp4-6-5-1

Yesaṁ nāmamidaṁ pavuccati; ^snp4-6-5-2

Nāmaṁyevāvasissati, ^snp4-6-5-3

Akkheyyaṁ petassa jantuno. ^snp4-6-5-4

Sokapparidevamaccharaṁ, ^snp4-6-6-1

Na jahanti giddhā mamāyite; ^snp4-6-6-2

Tasmā munayo pariggahaṁ, ^snp4-6-6-3

Hitvā acariṁsu khemadassino. ^snp4-6-6-4

Patilīnacarassa bhikkhuno, ^snp4-6-7-1

Bhajamānassa vivittamāsanaṁ; ^snp4-6-7-2

Sāmaggiyamāhu tassa taṁ, ^snp4-6-7-3

Yo attānaṁ bhavane na dassaye. ^snp4-6-7-4

Sabbattha munī anissito, ^snp4-6-8-1

Na piyaṁ kubbati nopi appiyaṁ; ^snp4-6-8-2

Tasmiṁ paridevamaccharaṁ, ^snp4-6-8-3

Paṇṇe vāri yathā na limpati. ^snp4-6-8-4

Udabindu yathāpi pokkhare, ^snp4-6-9-1

Padume vāri yathā na limpati; ^snp4-6-9-2

Evaṁ muni nopalimpati, ^snp4-6-9-3

Yadidaṁ diṭṭhasutaṁ mutesu vā. ^snp4-6-9-4

Dhono na hi tena maññati, ^snp4-6-10-1

Yadidaṁ diṭṭhasutaṁ mutesu vā; ^snp4-6-10-2

Nāññena visuddhimicchati, ^snp4-6-10-3

Na hi so rajjati no virajjatīti. ^snp4-6-10-4

Jarāsuttaṁ chaṭṭhaṁ. ^snp4-6-10-5

### Tissametteyyasutta (Sutta Nipāta 4.7) ^snp4-7-0

“Methunamanuyuttassa, ^snp4-7-1-1

(iccāyasmā tisso metteyyo) ^snp4-7-1-2

Vighātaṁ brūhi mārisa; ^snp4-7-1-3

Sutvāna tava sāsanaṁ, ^snp4-7-1-4

Viveke sikkhissāmase”. ^snp4-7-1-5

“Methunamanuyuttassa, ^snp4-7-2-1

(metteyyāti bhagavā) ^snp4-7-2-2

Mussate vāpi sāsanaṁ; ^snp4-7-2-3

Micchā ca paṭipajjati, ^snp4-7-2-4

Etaṁ tasmiṁ anāriyaṁ. ^snp4-7-2-5

Eko pubbe caritvāna, ^snp4-7-3-1

methunaṁ yo nisevati; ^snp4-7-3-2

Yānaṁ bhantaṁva taṁ loke, ^snp4-7-3-3

hīnamāhu puthujjanaṁ. ^snp4-7-3-4

Yaso kitti ca yā pubbe, ^snp4-7-4-1

hāyate vāpi tassa sā; ^snp4-7-4-2

Etampi disvā sikkhetha, ^snp4-7-4-3

methunaṁ vippahātave. ^snp4-7-4-4

Saṅkappehi pareto so, ^snp4-7-5-1

kapaṇo viya jhāyati; ^snp4-7-5-2

Sutvā paresaṁ nigghosaṁ, ^snp4-7-5-3

maṅku hoti tathāvidho. ^snp4-7-5-4

Atha satthāni kurute, ^snp4-7-6-1

paravādehi codito; ^snp4-7-6-2

Esa khvassa mahāgedho, ^snp4-7-6-3

mosavajjaṁ pagāhati. ^snp4-7-6-4

Paṇḍitoti samaññāto, ^snp4-7-7-1

ekacariyaṁ adhiṭṭhito; ^snp4-7-7-2

Athāpi methune yutto, ^snp4-7-7-3

mandova parikissati. ^snp4-7-7-4

Etamādīnavaṁ ñatvā, ^snp4-7-8-1

Muni pubbāpare idha; ^snp4-7-8-2

Ekacariyaṁ daḷhaṁ kayirā, ^snp4-7-8-3

Na nisevetha methunaṁ. ^snp4-7-8-4

Vivekaññeva sikkhetha, ^snp4-7-9-1

etaṁ ariyānamuttamaṁ; ^snp4-7-9-2

Na tena seṭṭho maññetha, ^snp4-7-9-3

sa ve nibbānasantike. ^snp4-7-9-4

Rittassa munino carato, ^snp4-7-10-1

Kāmesu anapekkhino; ^snp4-7-10-2

Oghatiṇṇassa pihayanti, ^snp4-7-10-3

Kāmesu gadhitā pajā”ti. ^snp4-7-10-4

Tissametteyyasuttaṁ sattamaṁ. ^snp4-7-10-5

### Pasūrasutta (Sutta Nipāta 4.8) ^snp4-8-0

Idheva suddhī iti vādayanti, ^snp4-8-1-1

Nāññesu dhammesu visuddhimāhu; ^snp4-8-1-2

Yaṁ nissitā tattha subhaṁ vadānā, ^snp4-8-1-3

Paccekasaccesu puthū niviṭṭhā. ^snp4-8-1-4

Te vādakāmā parisaṁ vigayha, ^snp4-8-2-1

Bālaṁ dahantī mithu aññamaññaṁ; ^snp4-8-2-2

Vadanti te aññasitā kathojjaṁ, ^snp4-8-2-3

Pasaṁsakāmā kusalā vadānā. ^snp4-8-2-4

Yutto kathāyaṁ parisāya majjhe, ^snp4-8-3-1

Pasaṁsamicchaṁ vinighāti hoti; ^snp4-8-3-2

Apāhatasmiṁ pana maṅku hoti, ^snp4-8-3-3

Nindāya so kuppati randhamesī. ^snp4-8-3-4

Yamassa vādaṁ parihīnamāhu, ^snp4-8-4-1

Apāhataṁ pañhavimaṁsakāse; ^snp4-8-4-2

Paridevati socati hīnavādo, ^snp4-8-4-3

Upaccagā manti anutthunāti. ^snp4-8-4-4

Ete vivādā samaṇesu jātā, ^snp4-8-5-1

Etesu ugghātinighāti hoti; ^snp4-8-5-2

Etampi disvā virame kathojjaṁ, ^snp4-8-5-3

Na haññadatthatthi pasaṁsalābhā. ^snp4-8-5-4

Pasaṁsito vā pana tattha hoti, ^snp4-8-6-1

Akkhāya vādaṁ parisāya majjhe; ^snp4-8-6-2

So hassatī unnamatī ca tena, ^snp4-8-6-3

Pappuyya tamatthaṁ yathā mano ahu. ^snp4-8-6-4

Yā unnatī sāssa vighātabhūmi, ^snp4-8-7-1

Mānātimānaṁ vadate paneso; ^snp4-8-7-2

Etampi disvā na vivādayetha, ^snp4-8-7-3

Na hi tena suddhiṁ kusalā vadanti. ^snp4-8-7-4

Sūro yathā rājakhādāya puṭṭho, ^snp4-8-8-1

Abhigajjameti paṭisūramicchaṁ; ^snp4-8-8-2

Yeneva so tena palehi sūra, ^snp4-8-8-3

Pubbeva natthi yadidaṁ yudhāya. ^snp4-8-8-4

Ye diṭṭhimuggayha vivādayanti, ^snp4-8-9-1

Idameva saccanti ca vādayanti; ^snp4-8-9-2

Te tvaṁ vadassū na hi tedha atthi, ^snp4-8-9-3

Vādamhi jāte paṭisenikattā. ^snp4-8-9-4

Visenikatvā pana ye caranti, ^snp4-8-10-1

Diṭṭhīhi diṭṭhiṁ avirujjhamānā; ^snp4-8-10-2

Tesu tvaṁ kiṁ labhetho pasūra, ^snp4-8-10-3

Yesīdha natthī paramuggahītaṁ. ^snp4-8-10-4

Atha tvaṁ pavitakkamāgamā, ^snp4-8-11-1

Manasā diṭṭhigatāni cintayanto; ^snp4-8-11-2

Dhonena yugaṁ samāgamā, ^snp4-8-11-3

Na hi tvaṁ sakkhasi sampayātaveti. ^snp4-8-11-4

Pasūrasuttaṁ aṭṭhamaṁ. ^snp4-8-11-5

### Māgaṇḍiyasutta (Sutta Nipāta 4.9) ^snp4-9-0

“Disvāna taṇhaṁ aratiṁ ragañca, ^snp4-9-1-1

Nāhosi chando api methunasmiṁ; ^snp4-9-1-2

Kimevidaṁ muttakarīsapuṇṇaṁ, ^snp4-9-1-3

Pādāpi naṁ samphusituṁ na icche”. ^snp4-9-1-4

“Etādisañce ratanaṁ na icchasi, ^snp4-9-2-1

Nāriṁ narindehi bahūhi patthitaṁ; ^snp4-9-2-2

Diṭṭhigataṁ sīlavataṁ nu jīvitaṁ, ^snp4-9-2-3

Bhavūpapattiñca vadesi kīdisaṁ”. ^snp4-9-2-4

“Idaṁ vadāmīti na tassa hoti, ^snp4-9-3-1

(māgaṇḍiyāti bhagavā) ^snp4-9-3-2

Dhammesu niccheyya samuggahītaṁ; ^snp4-9-3-3

Passañca diṭṭhīsu anuggahāya, ^snp4-9-3-4

Ajjhattasantiṁ pacinaṁ adassaṁ”. ^snp4-9-3-5

“Vinicchayā yāni pakappitāni, ^snp4-9-4-1

(iti māgaṇḍiyo) ^snp4-9-4-2

Te ve munī brūsi anuggahāya; ^snp4-9-4-3

Ajjhattasantīti yametamatthaṁ, ^snp4-9-4-4

Kathaṁ nu dhīrehi paveditaṁ taṁ”. ^snp4-9-4-5

“Na diṭṭhiyā na sutiyā na ñāṇena, ^snp4-9-5-1

(māgaṇḍiyāti bhagavā) ^snp4-9-5-2

Sīlabbatenāpi na suddhimāha; ^snp4-9-5-3

Adiṭṭhiyā assutiyā añāṇā, ^snp4-9-5-4

Asīlatā abbatā nopi tena; ^snp4-9-5-5

Ete ca nissajja anuggahāya, ^snp4-9-5-6

Santo anissāya bhavaṁ na jappe”. ^snp4-9-5-7

“No ce kira diṭṭhiyā na sutiyā na ñāṇena, ^snp4-9-6-1

(iti māgaṇḍiyo) ^snp4-9-6-2

Sīlabbatenāpi na suddhimāha; ^snp4-9-6-3

Adiṭṭhiyā assutiyā añāṇā, ^snp4-9-6-4

Asīlatā abbatā nopi tena; ^snp4-9-6-5

Maññāmahaṁ momuhameva dhammaṁ, ^snp4-9-6-6

Diṭṭhiyā eke paccenti suddhiṁ”. ^snp4-9-6-7

“Diṭṭhañca nissāya anupucchamāno, ^snp4-9-7-1

(māgaṇḍiyāti bhagavā) ^snp4-9-7-2

Samuggahītesu pamohamāgā; ^snp4-9-7-3

Ito ca nāddakkhi aṇumpi saññaṁ, ^snp4-9-7-4

Tasmā tuvaṁ momuhato dahāsi. ^snp4-9-7-5

Samo visesī uda vā nihīno, ^snp4-9-8-1

Yo maññati so vivadetha tena; ^snp4-9-8-2

Tīsu vidhāsu avikampamāno, ^snp4-9-8-3

Samo visesīti na tassa hoti. ^snp4-9-8-4

Saccanti so brāhmaṇo kiṁ vadeyya, ^snp4-9-9-1

Musāti vā so vivadetha kena; ^snp4-9-9-2

Yasmiṁ samaṁ visamaṁ vāpi natthi, ^snp4-9-9-3

Sa kena vādaṁ paṭisaṁyujeyya. ^snp4-9-9-4

Okaṁ pahāya aniketasārī, ^snp4-9-10-1

Gāme akubbaṁ muni santhavāni; ^snp4-9-10-2

Kāmehi ritto apurakkharāno, ^snp4-9-10-3

Kathaṁ na viggayha janena kayirā. ^snp4-9-10-4

Yehi vivitto vicareyya loke, ^snp4-9-11-1

Na tāni uggayha vadeyya nāgo; ^snp4-9-11-2

Jalambujaṁ kaṇḍakavārijaṁ yathā, ^snp4-9-11-3

Jalena paṅkena canūpalittaṁ; ^snp4-9-11-4

Evaṁ munī santivādo agiddho, ^snp4-9-11-5

Kāme ca loke ca anūpalitto. ^snp4-9-11-6

Na vedagū diṭṭhiyāyako na mutiyā, ^snp4-9-12-1

Sa mānameti na hi tammayo so; ^snp4-9-12-2

Na kammunā nopi sutena neyyo, ^snp4-9-12-3

Anūpanīto sa nivesanesu. ^snp4-9-12-4

Saññāvirattassa na santi ganthā, ^snp4-9-13-1

Paññāvimuttassa na santi mohā; ^snp4-9-13-2

Saññañca diṭṭhiñca ye aggahesuṁ, ^snp4-9-13-3

Te ghaṭṭayantā vicaranti loke”ti. ^snp4-9-13-4

Māgaṇḍiyasuttaṁ navamaṁ. ^snp4-9-13-5

### Purābhedasutta (Sutta Nipāta 4.10) ^snp4-10-0

“Kathaṁdassī kathaṁsīlo, ^snp4-10-1-1

upasantoti vuccati; ^snp4-10-1-2

Taṁ me gotama pabrūhi, ^snp4-10-1-3

pucchito uttamaṁ naraṁ”. ^snp4-10-1-4

“Vītataṇho purā bhedā, ^snp4-10-2-1

(iti bhagavā) ^snp4-10-2-2

Pubbamantamanissito; ^snp4-10-2-3

Vemajjhe nupasaṅkheyyo, ^snp4-10-2-4

Tassa natthi purakkhataṁ. ^snp4-10-2-5

Akkodhano asantāsī, ^snp4-10-3-1

avikatthī akukkuco; ^snp4-10-3-2

Mantabhāṇī anuddhato, ^snp4-10-3-3

sa ve vācāyato muni. ^snp4-10-3-4

Nirāsatti anāgate, ^snp4-10-4-1

atītaṁ nānusocati; ^snp4-10-4-2

Vivekadassī phassesu, ^snp4-10-4-3

diṭṭhīsu ca na nīyati. ^snp4-10-4-4

Patilīno akuhako, ^snp4-10-5-1

apihālu amaccharī; ^snp4-10-5-2

Appagabbho ajeguccho, ^snp4-10-5-3

pesuṇeyye ca no yuto. ^snp4-10-5-4

Sātiyesu anassāvī, ^snp4-10-6-1

atimāne ca no yuto; ^snp4-10-6-2

Saṇho ca paṭibhānavā, ^snp4-10-6-3

na saddho na virajjati. ^snp4-10-6-4

Lābhakamyā na sikkhati, ^snp4-10-7-1

alābhe ca na kuppati; ^snp4-10-7-2

Aviruddho ca taṇhāya, ^snp4-10-7-3

rasesu nānugijjhati. ^snp4-10-7-4

Upekkhako sadā sato, ^snp4-10-8-1

na loke maññate samaṁ; ^snp4-10-8-2

Na visesī na nīceyyo, ^snp4-10-8-3

tassa no santi ussadā. ^snp4-10-8-4

Yassa nissayanā natthi, ^snp4-10-9-1

ñatvā dhammaṁ anissito; ^snp4-10-9-2

Bhavāya vibhavāya vā, ^snp4-10-9-3

taṇhā yassa na vijjati. ^snp4-10-9-4

Taṁ brūmi upasantoti, ^snp4-10-10-1

Kāmesu anapekkhinaṁ; ^snp4-10-10-2

Ganthā tassa na vijjanti, ^snp4-10-10-3

Atarī so visattikaṁ. ^snp4-10-10-4

Na tassa puttā pasavo, ^snp4-10-11-1

Khettaṁ vatthuñca vijjati; ^snp4-10-11-2

Attā vāpi nirattā vā, ^snp4-10-11-3

Na tasmiṁ upalabbhati. ^snp4-10-11-4

Yena naṁ vajjuṁ puthujjanā, ^snp4-10-12-1

Atho samaṇabrāhmaṇā; ^snp4-10-12-2

Taṁ tassa apurakkhataṁ, ^snp4-10-12-3

Tasmā vādesu nejati. ^snp4-10-12-4

Vītagedho amaccharī, ^snp4-10-13-1

Na ussesu vadate muni; ^snp4-10-13-2

Na samesu na omesu, ^snp4-10-13-3

Kappaṁ neti akappiyo. ^snp4-10-13-4

Yassa loke sakaṁ natthi, ^snp4-10-14-1

Asatā ca na socati; ^snp4-10-14-2

Dhammesu ca na gacchati, ^snp4-10-14-3

Sa ve santoti vuccatī”ti. ^snp4-10-14-4

Purābhedasuttaṁ dasamaṁ. ^snp4-10-14-5

### Kalahavivādasutta (Sutta Nipāta 4.11) ^snp4-11-0

“Kutopahūtā kalahā vivādā, ^snp4-11-1-1

Paridevasokā sahamaccharā ca; ^snp4-11-1-2

Mānātimānā sahapesuṇā ca, ^snp4-11-1-3

Kutopahūtā te tadiṅgha brūhi”. ^snp4-11-1-4

“Piyappahūtā kalahā vivādā, ^snp4-11-2-1

Paridevasokā sahamaccharā ca; ^snp4-11-2-2

Mānātimānā sahapesuṇā ca, ^snp4-11-2-3

Maccherayuttā kalahā vivādā; ^snp4-11-2-4

Vivādajātesu ca pesuṇāni”. ^snp4-11-2-5

“Piyā su lokasmiṁ kutonidānā, ^snp4-11-3-1

Ye cāpi lobhā vicaranti loke; ^snp4-11-3-2

Āsā ca niṭṭhā ca kutonidānā, ^snp4-11-3-3

Ye samparāyāya narassa honti”. ^snp4-11-3-4

“Chandānidānāni piyāni loke, ^snp4-11-4-1

Ye cāpi lobhā vicaranti loke; ^snp4-11-4-2

Āsā ca niṭṭhā ca itonidānā, ^snp4-11-4-3

Ye samparāyāya narassa honti”. ^snp4-11-4-4

“Chando nu lokasmiṁ kutonidāno, ^snp4-11-5-1

Vinicchayā cāpi kutopahūtā; ^snp4-11-5-2

Kodho mosavajjañca kathaṅkathā ca, ^snp4-11-5-3

Ye vāpi dhammā samaṇena vuttā”. ^snp4-11-5-4

“Sātaṁ asātanti yamāhu loke, ^snp4-11-6-1

Tamūpanissāya pahoti chando; ^snp4-11-6-2

Rūpesu disvā vibhavaṁ bhavañca, ^snp4-11-6-3

Vinicchayaṁ kubbati jantu loke. ^snp4-11-6-4

Kodho mosavajjañca kathaṅkathā ca, ^snp4-11-7-1

Etepi dhammā dvayameva sante; ^snp4-11-7-2

Kathaṅkathī ñāṇapathāya sikkhe, ^snp4-11-7-3

Ñatvā pavuttā samaṇena dhammā”. ^snp4-11-7-4

“Sātaṁ asātañca kutonidānā, ^snp4-11-8-1

Kismiṁ asante na bhavanti hete; ^snp4-11-8-2

Vibhavaṁ bhavañcāpi yametamatthaṁ, ^snp4-11-8-3

Etaṁ me pabrūhi yatonidānaṁ”. ^snp4-11-8-4

“Phassanidānaṁ sātaṁ asātaṁ, ^snp4-11-9-1

Phasse asante na bhavanti hete; ^snp4-11-9-2

Vibhavaṁ bhavañcāpi yametamatthaṁ, ^snp4-11-9-3

Etaṁ te pabrūmi itonidānaṁ”. ^snp4-11-9-4

“Phasso nu lokasmi kutonidāno, ^snp4-11-10-1

Pariggahā cāpi kutopahūtā; ^snp4-11-10-2

Kismiṁ asante na mamattamatthi, ^snp4-11-10-3

Kismiṁ vibhūte na phusanti phassā”. ^snp4-11-10-4

“Nāmañca rūpañca paṭicca phasso, ^snp4-11-11-1

Icchānidānāni pariggahāni; ^snp4-11-11-2

Icchāyasantyā na mamattamatthi, ^snp4-11-11-3

Rūpe vibhūte na phusanti phassā”. ^snp4-11-11-4

“Kathaṁ sametassa vibhoti rūpaṁ, ^snp4-11-12-1

Sukhaṁ dukhañcāpi kathaṁ vibhoti; ^snp4-11-12-2

Etaṁ me pabrūhi yathā vibhoti, ^snp4-11-12-3

Taṁ jāniyāmāti me mano ahu”. ^snp4-11-12-4

“Na saññasaññī na visaññasaññī, ^snp4-11-13-1

Nopi asaññī na vibhūtasaññī; ^snp4-11-13-2

Evaṁ sametassa vibhoti rūpaṁ, ^snp4-11-13-3

Saññānidānā hi papañcasaṅkhā”. ^snp4-11-13-4

“Yaṁ taṁ apucchimha akittayī no, ^snp4-11-14-1

Aññaṁ taṁ pucchāma tadiṅgha brūhi; ^snp4-11-14-2

Ettāvataggaṁ nu vadanti heke, ^snp4-11-14-3

Yakkhassa suddhiṁ idha paṇḍitāse; ^snp4-11-14-4

Udāhu aññampi vadanti etto”. ^snp4-11-14-5

“Ettāvataggampi vadanti heke, ^snp4-11-15-1

Yakkhassa suddhiṁ idha paṇḍitāse; ^snp4-11-15-2

Tesaṁ paneke samayaṁ vadanti, ^snp4-11-15-3

Anupādisese kusalā vadānā. ^snp4-11-15-4

Ete ca ñatvā upanissitāti, ^snp4-11-16-1

Ñatvā munī nissaye so vimaṁsī; ^snp4-11-16-2

Ñatvā vimutto na vivādameti, ^snp4-11-16-3

Bhavābhavāya na sameti dhīro”ti. ^snp4-11-16-4

Kalahavivādasuttaṁ ekādasamaṁ. ^snp4-11-16-5

### Cūḷabyūhasutta (Sutta Nipāta 4.12) ^snp4-12-0

“Sakaṁsakaṁdiṭṭhiparibbasānā, ^snp4-12-1-1

Viggayha nānā kusalā vadanti; ^snp4-12-1-2

Yo evaṁ jānāti sa vedi dhammaṁ, ^snp4-12-1-3

Idaṁ paṭikkosamakevalī so. ^snp4-12-1-4

Evampi viggayha vivādayanti, ^snp4-12-2-1

Bālo paro akkusaloti cāhu; ^snp4-12-2-2

Sacco nu vādo katamo imesaṁ, ^snp4-12-2-3

Sabbeva hīme kusalāvadānā”. ^snp4-12-2-4

“Parassa ce dhammamanānujānaṁ, ^snp4-12-3-1

Bālomako hoti nihīnapañño; ^snp4-12-3-2

Sabbeva bālā sunihīnapaññā, ^snp4-12-3-3

Sabbevime diṭṭhiparibbasānā. ^snp4-12-3-4

Sandiṭṭhiyā ceva na vīvadātā, ^snp4-12-4-1

Saṁsuddhapaññā kusalā mutīmā; ^snp4-12-4-2

Na tesaṁ koci parihīnapañño, ^snp4-12-4-3

Diṭṭhī hi tesampi tathā samattā. ^snp4-12-4-4

Na vāhametaṁ tathiyanti brūmi, ^snp4-12-5-1

Yamāhu bālā mithu aññamaññaṁ; ^snp4-12-5-2

Sakaṁ sakaṁ diṭṭhimakaṁsu saccaṁ, ^snp4-12-5-3

Tasmā hi bāloti paraṁ dahanti”. ^snp4-12-5-4

“Yamāhu saccaṁ tathiyanti eke, ^snp4-12-6-1

Tamāhu aññe tucchaṁ musāti; ^snp4-12-6-2

Evampi vigayha vivādayanti, ^snp4-12-6-3

Kasmā na ekaṁ samaṇā vadanti”. ^snp4-12-6-4

“Ekañhi saccaṁ na dutīyamatthi, ^snp4-12-7-1

Yasmiṁ pajā no vivade pajānaṁ; ^snp4-12-7-2

Nānā te saccāni sayaṁ thunanti, ^snp4-12-7-3

Tasmā na ekaṁ samaṇā vadanti”. ^snp4-12-7-4

“Kasmā nu saccāni vadanti nānā, ^snp4-12-8-1

Pavādiyāse kusalāvadānā; ^snp4-12-8-2

Saccāni sutāni bahūni nānā, ^snp4-12-8-3

Udāhu te takkamanussaranti”. ^snp4-12-8-4

“Na heva saccāni bahūni nānā, ^snp4-12-9-1

Aññatra saññāya niccāni loke; ^snp4-12-9-2

Takkañca diṭṭhīsu pakappayitvā, ^snp4-12-9-3

Saccaṁ musāti dvayadhammamāhu. ^snp4-12-9-4

Diṭṭhe sute sīlavate mute vā, ^snp4-12-10-1

Ete ca nissāya vimānadassī; ^snp4-12-10-2

Vinicchaye ṭhatvā pahassamāno, ^snp4-12-10-3

Bālo paro akkusaloti cāha. ^snp4-12-10-4

Yeneva bāloti paraṁ dahāti, ^snp4-12-11-1

Tenātumānaṁ kusaloti cāha; ^snp4-12-11-2

Sayamattanā so kusalāvadāno, ^snp4-12-11-3

Aññaṁ vimāneti tadeva pāva. ^snp4-12-11-4

Atisāradiṭṭhiyā so samatto, ^snp4-12-12-1

Mānena matto paripuṇṇamānī; ^snp4-12-12-2

Sayameva sāmaṁ manasābhisitto, ^snp4-12-12-3

Diṭṭhī hi sā tassa tathā samattā. ^snp4-12-12-4

Parassa ce hi vacasā nihīno, ^snp4-12-13-1

Tumo sahā hoti nihīnapañño; ^snp4-12-13-2

Atha ce sayaṁ vedagū hoti dhīro, ^snp4-12-13-3

Na koci bālo samaṇesu atthi. ^snp4-12-13-4

Aññaṁ ito yābhivadanti dhammaṁ, ^snp4-12-14-1

Aparaddhā suddhimakevalī te; ^snp4-12-14-2

Evampi titthyā puthuso vadanti, ^snp4-12-14-3

Sandiṭṭhirāgena hi tebhirattā. ^snp4-12-14-4

Idheva suddhiṁ iti vādayanti, ^snp4-12-15-1

Nāññesu dhammesu visuddhimāhu; ^snp4-12-15-2

Evampi titthyā puthuso niviṭṭhā, ^snp4-12-15-3

Sakāyane tattha daḷhaṁ vadānā. ^snp4-12-15-4

Sakāyane vāpi daḷhaṁ vadāno, ^snp4-12-16-1

Kamettha bāloti paraṁ daheyya; ^snp4-12-16-2

Sayaṁva so medhagamāvaheyya, ^snp4-12-16-3

Paraṁ vadaṁ bālamasuddhidhammaṁ. ^snp4-12-16-4

Vinicchaye ṭhatvā sayaṁ pamāya, ^snp4-12-17-1

Uddhaṁsa lokasmiṁ vivādameti; ^snp4-12-17-2

Hitvāna sabbāni vinicchayāni, ^snp4-12-17-3

Na medhagaṁ kubbati jantu loke”ti. ^snp4-12-17-4

Cūḷabyūhasuttaṁ dvādasamaṁ. ^snp4-12-17-5

### Mahābyūhasutta (Sutta Nipāta 4.13) ^snp4-13-0

“Ye kecime diṭṭhiparibbasānā, ^snp4-13-1-1

Idameva saccanti vivādayanti; ^snp4-13-1-2

Sabbeva te nindamanvānayanti, ^snp4-13-1-3

Atho pasaṁsampi labhanti tattha”. ^snp4-13-1-4

“Appañhi etaṁ na alaṁ samāya, ^snp4-13-2-1

Duve vivādassa phalāni brūmi; ^snp4-13-2-2

Etampi disvā na vivādayetha, ^snp4-13-2-3

Khemābhipassaṁ avivādabhūmiṁ”. ^snp4-13-2-4

“Yā kācimā sammutiyo puthujjā, ^snp4-13-3-1

Sabbāva etā na upeti vidvā; ^snp4-13-3-2

Anūpayo so upayaṁ kimeyya, ^snp4-13-3-3

Diṭṭhe sute khantimakubbamāno”. ^snp4-13-3-4

“Sīluttamā saññamenāhu suddhiṁ, ^snp4-13-4-1

Vataṁ samādāya upaṭṭhitāse; ^snp4-13-4-2

Idheva sikkhema athassa suddhiṁ, ^snp4-13-4-3

Bhavūpanītā kusalāvadānā. ^snp4-13-4-4

Sace cuto sīlavatato hoti, ^snp4-13-5-1

Pavedhatī kamma virādhayitvā; ^snp4-13-5-2

Pajappatī patthayatī ca suddhiṁ, ^snp4-13-5-3

Satthāva hīno pavasaṁ gharamhā. ^snp4-13-5-4

Sīlabbataṁ vāpi pahāya sabbaṁ, ^snp4-13-6-1

Kammañca sāvajjanavajjametaṁ; ^snp4-13-6-2

Suddhiṁ asuddhinti apatthayāno, ^snp4-13-6-3

Virato care santimanuggahāya. ^snp4-13-6-4

Tamūpanissāya jigucchitaṁ vā, ^snp4-13-7-1

Atha vāpi diṭṭhaṁ va sutaṁ mutaṁ vā; ^snp4-13-7-2

Uddhaṁsarā suddhimanutthunanti, ^snp4-13-7-3

Avītataṇhāse bhavābhavesu. ^snp4-13-7-4

Patthayamānassa hi jappitāni, ^snp4-13-8-1

Pavedhitaṁ vāpi pakappitesu; ^snp4-13-8-2

Cutūpapāto idha yassa natthi, ^snp4-13-8-3

Sa kena vedheyya kuhiṁ va jappe”. ^snp4-13-8-4

“Yamāhu dhammaṁ paramanti eke, ^snp4-13-9-1

Tameva hīnanti panāhu aññe; ^snp4-13-9-2

Sacco nu vādo katamo imesaṁ, ^snp4-13-9-3

Sabbeva hīme kusalāvadānā”. ^snp4-13-9-4

“Sakañhi dhammaṁ paripuṇṇamāhu, ^snp4-13-10-1

Aññassa dhammaṁ pana hīnamāhu; ^snp4-13-10-2

Evampi viggayha vivādayanti, ^snp4-13-10-3

Sakaṁ sakaṁ sammutimāhu saccaṁ. ^snp4-13-10-4

Parassa ce vambhayitena hīno, ^snp4-13-11-1

Na koci dhammesu visesi assa; ^snp4-13-11-2

Puthū hi aññassa vadanti dhammaṁ, ^snp4-13-11-3

Nihīnato samhi daḷhaṁ vadānā. ^snp4-13-11-4

Saddhammapūjāpi nesaṁ tatheva, ^snp4-13-12-1

Yathā pasaṁsanti sakāyanāni; ^snp4-13-12-2

Sabbeva vādā tathiyā bhaveyyuṁ, ^snp4-13-12-3

Suddhī hi nesaṁ paccattameva. ^snp4-13-12-4

Na brāhmaṇassa paraneyyamatthi, ^snp4-13-13-1

Dhammesu niccheyya samuggahītaṁ; ^snp4-13-13-2

Tasmā vivādāni upātivatto, ^snp4-13-13-3

Na hi seṭṭhato passati dhammamaññaṁ. ^snp4-13-13-4

Jānāmi passāmi tatheva etaṁ, ^snp4-13-14-1

Diṭṭhiyā eke paccenti suddhiṁ; ^snp4-13-14-2

Addakkhi ce kiñhi tumassa tena, ^snp4-13-14-3

Atisitvā aññena vadanti suddhiṁ. ^snp4-13-14-4

Passaṁ naro dakkhati nāmarūpaṁ, ^snp4-13-15-1

Disvāna vā ñassati tānimeva; ^snp4-13-15-2

Kāmaṁ bahuṁ passatu appakaṁ vā, ^snp4-13-15-3

Na hi tena suddhiṁ kusalā vadanti. ^snp4-13-15-4

Nivissavādī na hi subbināyo, ^snp4-13-16-1

Pakappitaṁ diṭṭhi purakkharāno; ^snp4-13-16-2

Yaṁ nissito tattha subhaṁ vadāno, ^snp4-13-16-3

Suddhiṁ vado tattha tathaddasā so. ^snp4-13-16-4

Na brāhmaṇo kappamupeti saṅkhā, ^snp4-13-17-1

Na diṭṭhisārī napi ñāṇabandhu; ^snp4-13-17-2

Ñatvā ca so sammutiyo puthujjā, ^snp4-13-17-3

Upekkhatī uggahaṇanti maññe. ^snp4-13-17-4

Vissajja ganthāni munīdha loke, ^snp4-13-18-1

Vivādajātesu na vaggasārī; ^snp4-13-18-2

Santo asantesu upekkhako so, ^snp4-13-18-3

Anuggaho uggahaṇanti maññe. ^snp4-13-18-4

Pubbāsave hitvā nave akubbaṁ, ^snp4-13-19-1

Na chandagū nopi nivissavādī; ^snp4-13-19-2

Sa vippamutto diṭṭhigatehi dhīro, ^snp4-13-19-3

Na lippati loke anattagarahī. ^snp4-13-19-4

Sa sabbadhammesu visenibhūto, ^snp4-13-20-1

Yaṁ kiñci diṭṭhaṁ va sutaṁ mutaṁ vā; ^snp4-13-20-2

Sa pannabhāro muni vippamutto, ^snp4-13-20-3

Na kappiyo nūparato na patthiyo”ti. ^snp4-13-20-4

Mahābyūhasuttaṁ terasamaṁ. ^snp4-13-20-5

### Tuvaṭakasutta (Sutta Nipāta 4.14) ^snp4-14-0

“Pucchāmi taṁ ādiccabandhu, ^snp4-14-1-1

Vivekaṁ santipadañca mahesi; ^snp4-14-1-2

Kathaṁ disvā nibbāti bhikkhu, ^snp4-14-1-3

Anupādiyāno lokasmiṁ kiñci”. ^snp4-14-1-4

“Mūlaṁ papañcasaṅkhāya, ^snp4-14-2-1

(iti bhagavā) ^snp4-14-2-2

Mantā asmīti sabbamuparundhe; ^snp4-14-2-3

Yā kāci taṇhā ajjhattaṁ, ^snp4-14-2-4

Tāsaṁ vinayā sadā sato sikkhe. ^snp4-14-2-5

Yaṁ kiñci dhammamabhijaññā, ^snp4-14-3-1

Ajjhattaṁ atha vāpi bahiddhā; ^snp4-14-3-2

Na tena thāmaṁ kubbetha, ^snp4-14-3-3

Na hi sā nibbuti sataṁ vuttā. ^snp4-14-3-4

Seyyo na tena maññeyya, ^snp4-14-4-1

Nīceyyo atha vāpi sarikkho; ^snp4-14-4-2

Phuṭṭho anekarūpehi, ^snp4-14-4-3

Nātumānaṁ vikappayaṁ tiṭṭhe. ^snp4-14-4-4

Ajjhattamevupasame, ^snp4-14-5-1

Na aññato bhikkhu santimeseyya; ^snp4-14-5-2

Ajjhattaṁ upasantassa, ^snp4-14-5-3

Natthi attā kuto nirattā vā. ^snp4-14-5-4

Majjhe yathā samuddassa, ^snp4-14-6-1

Ūmi no jāyatī ṭhito hoti; ^snp4-14-6-2

Evaṁ ṭhito anejassa, ^snp4-14-6-3

Ussadaṁ bhikkhu na kareyya kuhiñci”. ^snp4-14-6-4

“Akittayī vivaṭacakkhu, ^snp4-14-7-1

Sakkhidhammaṁ parissayavinayaṁ; ^snp4-14-7-2

Paṭipadaṁ vadehi bhaddante, ^snp4-14-7-3

Pātimokkhaṁ atha vāpi samādhiṁ”. ^snp4-14-7-4

“Cakkhūhi neva lolassa, ^snp4-14-8-1

Gāmakathāya āvaraye sotaṁ; ^snp4-14-8-2

Rase ca nānugijjheyya, ^snp4-14-8-3

Na ca mamāyetha kiñci lokasmiṁ. ^snp4-14-8-4

Phassena yadā phuṭṭhassa, ^snp4-14-9-1

Paridevaṁ bhikkhu na kareyya kuhiñci; ^snp4-14-9-2

Bhavañca nābhijappeyya, ^snp4-14-9-3

Bheravesu ca na sampavedheyya. ^snp4-14-9-4

Annānamatho pānānaṁ, ^snp4-14-10-1

Khādanīyānaṁ athopi vatthānaṁ; ^snp4-14-10-2

Laddhā na sannidhiṁ kayirā, ^snp4-14-10-3

Na ca parittase tāni alabhamāno. ^snp4-14-10-4

Jhāyī na pādalolassa, ^snp4-14-11-1

Virame kukkuccā nappamajjeyya; ^snp4-14-11-2

Athāsanesu sayanesu, ^snp4-14-11-3

Appasaddesu bhikkhu vihareyya. ^snp4-14-11-4

Niddaṁ na bahulīkareyya, ^snp4-14-12-1

Jāgariyaṁ bhajeyya ātāpī; ^snp4-14-12-2

Tandiṁ māyaṁ hassaṁ khiḍḍaṁ, ^snp4-14-12-3

Methunaṁ vippajahe savibhūsaṁ. ^snp4-14-12-4

Āthabbaṇaṁ supinaṁ lakkhaṇaṁ, ^snp4-14-13-1

No vidahe athopi nakkhattaṁ; ^snp4-14-13-2

Virutañca gabbhakaraṇaṁ, ^snp4-14-13-3

Tikicchaṁ māmako na seveyya. ^snp4-14-13-4

Nindāya nappavedheyya, ^snp4-14-14-1

Na uṇṇameyya pasaṁsito bhikkhu; ^snp4-14-14-2

Lobhaṁ saha macchariyena, ^snp4-14-14-3

Kodhaṁ pesuṇiyañca panudeyya. ^snp4-14-14-4

Kayavikkaye na tiṭṭheyya, ^snp4-14-15-1

Upavādaṁ bhikkhu na kareyya kuhiñci; ^snp4-14-15-2

Gāme ca nābhisajjeyya, ^snp4-14-15-3

Lābhakamyā janaṁ na lapayeyya. ^snp4-14-15-4

Na ca katthitā siyā bhikkhu, ^snp4-14-16-1

Na ca vācaṁ payuttaṁ bhāseyya; ^snp4-14-16-2

Pāgabbhiyaṁ na sikkheyya, ^snp4-14-16-3

Kathaṁ viggāhikaṁ na kathayeyya. ^snp4-14-16-4

Mosavajje na nīyetha, ^snp4-14-17-1

Sampajāno saṭhāni na kayirā; ^snp4-14-17-2

Atha jīvitena paññāya, ^snp4-14-17-3

Sīlabbatena nāññamatimaññe. ^snp4-14-17-4

Sutvā rusito bahuṁ vācaṁ, ^snp4-14-18-1

Samaṇānaṁ vā puthujanānaṁ; ^snp4-14-18-2

Pharusena ne na paṭivajjā, ^snp4-14-18-3

Na hi santo paṭisenikaronti. ^snp4-14-18-4

Etañca dhammamaññāya, ^snp4-14-19-1

Vicinaṁ bhikkhu sadā sato sikkhe; ^snp4-14-19-2

Santīti nibbutiṁ ñatvā, ^snp4-14-19-3

Sāsane gotamassa na pamajjeyya. ^snp4-14-19-4

Abhibhū hi so anabhibhūto, ^snp4-14-20-1

Sakkhidhammamanītihamadassī; ^snp4-14-20-2

Tasmā hi tassa bhagavato sāsane, ^snp4-14-20-3

Appamatto sadā namassamanusikkhe”ti. ^snp4-14-20-4

Tuvaṭakasuttaṁ cuddasamaṁ. ^snp4-14-20-5

### Attadaṇḍasutta (Sutta Nipāta 4.15) ^snp4-15-0

“Attadaṇḍā bhayaṁ jātaṁ, ^snp4-15-1-1

janaṁ passatha medhagaṁ; ^snp4-15-1-2

Saṁvegaṁ kittayissāmi, ^snp4-15-1-3

yathā saṁvijitaṁ mayā. ^snp4-15-1-4

Phandamānaṁ pajaṁ disvā, ^snp4-15-2-1

macche appodake yathā; ^snp4-15-2-2

Aññamaññehi byāruddhe, ^snp4-15-2-3

disvā maṁ bhayamāvisi. ^snp4-15-2-4

Samantamasāro loko, ^snp4-15-3-1

disā sabbā sameritā; ^snp4-15-3-2

Icchaṁ bhavanamattano, ^snp4-15-3-3

nāddasāsiṁ anositaṁ. ^snp4-15-3-4

Osāne tveva byāruddhe, ^snp4-15-4-1

Disvā me aratī ahu; ^snp4-15-4-2

Athettha sallamaddakkhiṁ, ^snp4-15-4-3

Duddasaṁ hadayanissitaṁ. ^snp4-15-4-4

Yena sallena otiṇṇo, ^snp4-15-5-1

disā sabbā vidhāvati; ^snp4-15-5-2

Tameva sallamabbuyha, ^snp4-15-5-3

na dhāvati na sīdati. ^snp4-15-5-4

Tattha sikkhānugīyanti, ^snp4-15-6-1

yāni loke gadhitāni; ^snp4-15-6-2

Na tesu pasuto siyā, ^snp4-15-6-3

nibbijjha sabbaso kāme; ^snp4-15-6-4

Sikkhe nibbānamattano. ^snp4-15-6-5

Sacco siyā appagabbho, ^snp4-15-7-1

amāyo rittapesuṇo; ^snp4-15-7-2

Akkodhano lobhapāpaṁ, ^snp4-15-7-3

vevicchaṁ vitare muni. ^snp4-15-7-4

Niddaṁ tandiṁ sahe thīnaṁ, ^snp4-15-8-1

pamādena na saṁvase; ^snp4-15-8-2

Atimāne na tiṭṭheyya, ^snp4-15-8-3

nibbānamanaso naro. ^snp4-15-8-4

Mosavajje na nīyetha, ^snp4-15-9-1

rūpe snehaṁ na kubbaye; ^snp4-15-9-2

Mānañca parijāneyya, ^snp4-15-9-3

sāhasā virato care. ^snp4-15-9-4

Purāṇaṁ nābhinandeyya, ^snp4-15-10-1

Nave khantiṁ na kubbaye; ^snp4-15-10-2

Hiyyamāne na soceyya, ^snp4-15-10-3

Ākāsaṁ na sito siyā. ^snp4-15-10-4

Gedhaṁ brūmi mahoghoti, ^snp4-15-11-1

Ājavaṁ brūmi jappanaṁ; ^snp4-15-11-2

Ārammaṇaṁ pakappanaṁ, ^snp4-15-11-3

Kāmapaṅko duraccayo. ^snp4-15-11-4

Saccā avokkamma muni, ^snp4-15-12-1

Thale tiṭṭhati brāhmaṇo; ^snp4-15-12-2

Sabbaṁ so paṭinissajja, ^snp4-15-12-3

Sa ve santoti vuccati. ^snp4-15-12-4

Sa ve vidvā sa vedagū, ^snp4-15-13-1

Ñatvā dhammaṁ anissito; ^snp4-15-13-2

Sammā so loke iriyāno, ^snp4-15-13-3

Na pihetīdha kassaci. ^snp4-15-13-4

Yodha kāme accatari, ^snp4-15-14-1

Saṅgaṁ loke duraccayaṁ; ^snp4-15-14-2

Na so socati nājjheti, ^snp4-15-14-3

Chinnasoto abandhano. ^snp4-15-14-4

Yaṁ pubbe taṁ visosehi, ^snp4-15-15-1

Pacchā te māhu kiñcanaṁ; ^snp4-15-15-2

Majjhe ce no gahessasi, ^snp4-15-15-3

Upasanto carissasi. ^snp4-15-15-4

Sabbaso nāmarūpasmiṁ, ^snp4-15-16-1

Yassa natthi mamāyitaṁ; ^snp4-15-16-2

Asatā ca na socati, ^snp4-15-16-3

Sa ve loke na jīyati. ^snp4-15-16-4

Yassa natthi idaṁ meti, ^snp4-15-17-1

Paresaṁ vāpi kiñcanaṁ; ^snp4-15-17-2

Mamattaṁ so asaṁvindaṁ, ^snp4-15-17-3

Natthi meti na socati. ^snp4-15-17-4

Aniṭṭhurī ananugiddho, ^snp4-15-18-1

Anejo sabbadhī samo; ^snp4-15-18-2

Tamānisaṁsaṁ pabrūmi, ^snp4-15-18-3

Pucchito avikampinaṁ. ^snp4-15-18-4

Anejassa vijānato, ^snp4-15-19-1

Natthi kāci nisaṅkhati; ^snp4-15-19-2

Virato so viyārabbhā, ^snp4-15-19-3

Khemaṁ passati sabbadhi. ^snp4-15-19-4

Na samesu na omesu, ^snp4-15-20-1

Na ussesu vadate muni; ^snp4-15-20-2

Santo so vītamaccharo, ^snp4-15-20-3

Nādeti na nirassatī”ti. ^snp4-15-20-4

Attadaṇḍasuttaṁ pannarasamaṁ. ^snp4-15-20-5

### Sāriputtasutta (Sutta Nipāta 4.16) ^snp4-16-0

“Na me diṭṭho ito pubbe, ^snp4-16-1-1

(iccāyasmā sāriputto) ^snp4-16-1-2

Na suto uda kassaci; ^snp4-16-1-3

Evaṁ vagguvado satthā, ^snp4-16-1-4

Tusitā gaṇimāgato. ^snp4-16-1-5

Sadevakassa lokassa, ^snp4-16-2-1

yathā dissati cakkhumā; ^snp4-16-2-2

Sabbaṁ tamaṁ vinodetvā, ^snp4-16-2-3

ekova ratimajjhagā. ^snp4-16-2-4

Taṁ buddhaṁ asitaṁ tādiṁ, ^snp4-16-3-1

akuhaṁ gaṇimāgataṁ; ^snp4-16-3-2

Bahūnamidha baddhānaṁ, ^snp4-16-3-3

atthi pañhena āgamaṁ. ^snp4-16-3-4

Bhikkhuno vijigucchato, ^snp4-16-4-1

bhajato rittamāsanaṁ; ^snp4-16-4-2

Rukkhamūlaṁ susānaṁ vā, ^snp4-16-4-3

pabbatānaṁ guhāsu vā. ^snp4-16-4-4

Uccāvacesu sayanesu, ^snp4-16-5-1

kīvanto tattha bheravā; ^snp4-16-5-2

Yehi bhikkhu na vedheyya, ^snp4-16-5-3

nigghose sayanāsane. ^snp4-16-5-4

Katī parissayā loke, ^snp4-16-6-1

gacchato agataṁ disaṁ; ^snp4-16-6-2

Ye bhikkhu abhisambhave, ^snp4-16-6-3

pantamhi sayanāsane. ^snp4-16-6-4

Kyāssa byappathayo assu, ^snp4-16-7-1

kyāssassu idha gocarā; ^snp4-16-7-2

Kāni sīlabbatānāssu, ^snp4-16-7-3

pahitattassa bhikkhuno. ^snp4-16-7-4

Kaṁ so sikkhaṁ samādāya, ^snp4-16-8-1

ekodi nipako sato; ^snp4-16-8-2

Kammāro rajatasseva, ^snp4-16-8-3

niddhame malamattano”. ^snp4-16-8-4

“Vijigucchamānassa yadidaṁ phāsu, ^snp4-16-9-1

(sāriputtāti bhagavā) ^snp4-16-9-2

Rittāsanaṁ sayanaṁ sevato ce; ^snp4-16-9-3

Sambodhikāmassa yathānudhammaṁ, ^snp4-16-9-4

Taṁ te pavakkhāmi yathā pajānaṁ. ^snp4-16-9-5

Pañcannaṁ dhīro bhayānaṁ na bhāye, ^snp4-16-10-1

Bhikkhu sato sapariyantacārī; ^snp4-16-10-2

Ḍaṁsādhipātānaṁ sarīsapānaṁ, ^snp4-16-10-3

Manussaphassānaṁ catuppadānaṁ. ^snp4-16-10-4

Paradhammikānampi na santaseyya, ^snp4-16-11-1

Disvāpi tesaṁ bahubheravāni; ^snp4-16-11-2

Athāparāni abhisambhaveyya, ^snp4-16-11-3

Parissayāni kusalānuesī. ^snp4-16-11-4

Ātaṅkaphassena khudāya phuṭṭho, ^snp4-16-12-1

Sītaṁ athuṇhaṁ adhivāsayeyya; ^snp4-16-12-2

So tehi phuṭṭho bahudhā anoko, ^snp4-16-12-3

Viriyaṁ parakkammadaḷhaṁ kareyya. ^snp4-16-12-4

Theyyaṁ na kāre na musā bhaṇeyya, ^snp4-16-13-1

Mettāya phasse tasathāvarāni; ^snp4-16-13-2

Yadāvilattaṁ manaso vijaññā, ^snp4-16-13-3

Kaṇhassa pakkhoti vinodayeyya. ^snp4-16-13-4

Kodhātimānassa vasaṁ na gacche, ^snp4-16-14-1

Mūlampi tesaṁ palikhañña tiṭṭhe; ^snp4-16-14-2

Athappiyaṁ vā pana appiyaṁ vā, ^snp4-16-14-3

Addhā bhavanto abhisambhaveyya. ^snp4-16-14-4

Paññaṁ purakkhatvā kalyāṇapīti, ^snp4-16-15-1

Vikkhambhaye tāni parissayāni; ^snp4-16-15-2

Aratiṁ sahetha sayanamhi pante, ^snp4-16-15-3

Caturo sahetha paridevadhamme. ^snp4-16-15-4

Kiṁsū asissāmi kuva vā asissaṁ, ^snp4-16-16-1

Dukkhaṁ vata settha kvajja sessaṁ; ^snp4-16-16-2

Ete vitakke paridevaneyye, ^snp4-16-16-3

Vinayetha sekho aniketacārī. ^snp4-16-16-4

Annañca laddhā vasanañca kāle, ^snp4-16-17-1

Mattaṁ so jaññā idha tosanatthaṁ; ^snp4-16-17-2

So tesu gutto yatacāri gāme, ^snp4-16-17-3

Rusitopi vācaṁ pharusaṁ na vajjā. ^snp4-16-17-4

Okkhittacakkhu na ca pādalolo, ^snp4-16-18-1

Jhānānuyutto bahujāgarassa; ^snp4-16-18-2

Upekkhamārabbha samāhitatto, ^snp4-16-18-3

Takkāsayaṁ kukkucciyūpachinde. ^snp4-16-18-4

Cudito vacībhi satimābhinande, ^snp4-16-19-1

Sabrahmacārīsu khilaṁ pabhinde; ^snp4-16-19-2

Vācaṁ pamuñce kusalaṁ nātivelaṁ, ^snp4-16-19-3

Janavādadhammāya na cetayeyya. ^snp4-16-19-4

Athāparaṁ pañca rajāni loke, ^snp4-16-20-1

Yesaṁ satīmā vinayāya sikkhe; ^snp4-16-20-2

Rūpesu saddesu atho rasesu, ^snp4-16-20-3

Gandhesu phassesu sahetha rāgaṁ. ^snp4-16-20-4

Etesu dhammesu vineyya chandaṁ, ^snp4-16-21-1

Bhikkhu satimā suvimuttacitto; ^snp4-16-21-2

Kālena so sammā dhammaṁ parivīmaṁsamāno, ^snp4-16-21-3

Ekodibhūto vihane tamaṁ so”ti. ^snp4-16-21-4

Sāriputtasuttaṁ soḷasamaṁ. ^snp4-16-21-5

Aṭṭhakavaggo catuttho. ^snp4-16-21-6

Tassuddānaṁ ^snp4-16-22-0

Kāmaṁ guhañca duṭṭhā ca, ^snp4-16-22-1

suddhañca paramā jarā; ^snp4-16-22-2

Metteyyo ca pasūro ca, ^snp4-16-22-3

māgaṇḍi purābhedanaṁ. ^snp4-16-22-4

Kalahaṁ dve ca byūhāni, ^snp4-16-23-1

punadeva tuvaṭṭakaṁ; ^snp4-16-23-2

Attadaṇḍavaraṁ suttaṁ, ^snp4-16-23-3

therapuṭṭhena soḷasa; ^snp4-16-23-4

Iti etāni suttāni, ^snp4-16-23-5

sabbānaṭṭhakavaggikāti. ^snp4-16-23-6

## Vagga 5 ^vagga5-0

### Vatthugāthā (Sutta Nipāta 5.1) ^snp5-1-0

Kosalānaṁ purā rammā, ^snp5-1-1-1

agamā dakkhiṇāpathaṁ; ^snp5-1-1-2

Ākiñcaññaṁ patthayāno, ^snp5-1-1-3

brāhmaṇo mantapāragū. ^snp5-1-1-4

So assakassa visaye, ^snp5-1-2-1

aḷakassa samāsane; ^snp5-1-2-2

Vasi godhāvarīkūle, ^snp5-1-2-3

uñchena ca phalena ca. ^snp5-1-2-4

Tasseva upanissāya, ^snp5-1-3-1

gāmo ca vipulo ahu; ^snp5-1-3-2

Tato jātena āyena, ^snp5-1-3-3

mahāyaññamakappayi. ^snp5-1-3-4

Mahāyaññaṁ yajitvāna, ^snp5-1-4-1

puna pāvisi assamaṁ; ^snp5-1-4-2

Tasmiṁ paṭipaviṭṭhamhi, ^snp5-1-4-3

añño āgañchi brāhmaṇo. ^snp5-1-4-4

Ugghaṭṭapādo tasito, ^snp5-1-5-1

paṅkadanto rajassiro; ^snp5-1-5-2

So ca naṁ upasaṅkamma, ^snp5-1-5-3

satāni pañca yācati. ^snp5-1-5-4

Tamenaṁ bāvarī disvā, ^snp5-1-6-1

āsanena nimantayi; ^snp5-1-6-2

Sukhañca kusalaṁ pucchi, ^snp5-1-6-3

idaṁ vacanamabravi. ^snp5-1-6-4

“Yaṁ kho mama deyyadhammaṁ, ^snp5-1-7-1

Sabbaṁ visajjitaṁ mayā; ^snp5-1-7-2

Anujānāhi me brahme, ^snp5-1-7-3

Natthi pañcasatāni me”. ^snp5-1-7-4

“Sace me yācamānassa, ^snp5-1-8-1

bhavaṁ nānupadassati; ^snp5-1-8-2

Sattame divase tuyhaṁ, ^snp5-1-8-3

muddhā phalatu sattadhā”. ^snp5-1-8-4

Abhisaṅkharitvā kuhako, ^snp5-1-9-1

bheravaṁ so akittayi; ^snp5-1-9-2

Tassa taṁ vacanaṁ sutvā, ^snp5-1-9-3

bāvarī dukkhito ahu. ^snp5-1-9-4

Ussussati anāhāro, ^snp5-1-10-1

Sokasallasamappito; ^snp5-1-10-2

Athopi evaṁ cittassa, ^snp5-1-10-3

Jhāne na ramatī mano. ^snp5-1-10-4

Utrastaṁ dukkhitaṁ disvā, ^snp5-1-11-1

Devatā atthakāminī; ^snp5-1-11-2

Bāvariṁ upasaṅkamma, ^snp5-1-11-3

Idaṁ vacanamabravi. ^snp5-1-11-4

“Na so muddhaṁ pajānāti, ^snp5-1-12-1

Kuhako so dhanatthiko; ^snp5-1-12-2

Muddhani muddhapāte vā, ^snp5-1-12-3

Ñāṇaṁ tassa na vijjati”. ^snp5-1-12-4

“Bhotī carahi jānāsi, ^snp5-1-13-1

Taṁ me akkhāhi pucchitā; ^snp5-1-13-2

Muddhaṁ muddhādhipātañca, ^snp5-1-13-3

Taṁ suṇoma vaco tava”. ^snp5-1-13-4

“Ahampetaṁ na jānāmi, ^snp5-1-14-1

Ñāṇamettha na vijjati; ^snp5-1-14-2

Muddhani muddhādhipāte ca, ^snp5-1-14-3

Jinānaṁ hettha dassanaṁ”. ^snp5-1-14-4

“Atha ko carahi jānāti, ^snp5-1-15-1

Asmiṁ pathavimaṇḍale; ^snp5-1-15-2

Muddhaṁ muddhādhipātañca, ^snp5-1-15-3

Taṁ me akkhāhi devate”. ^snp5-1-15-4

“Purā kapilavatthumhā, ^snp5-1-16-1

Nikkhanto lokanāyako; ^snp5-1-16-2

Apacco okkākarājassa, ^snp5-1-16-3

Sakyaputto pabhaṅkaro. ^snp5-1-16-4

So hi brāhmaṇa sambuddho, ^snp5-1-17-1

Sabbadhammāna pāragū; ^snp5-1-17-2

Sabbābhiññābalappatto, ^snp5-1-17-3

Sabbadhammesu cakkhumā; ^snp5-1-17-4

Sabbakammakkhayaṁ patto, ^snp5-1-17-5

Vimutto upadhikkhaye. ^snp5-1-17-6

Buddho so bhagavā loke, ^snp5-1-18-1

Dhammaṁ deseti cakkhumā; ^snp5-1-18-2

Taṁ tvaṁ gantvāna pucchassu, ^snp5-1-18-3

So te taṁ byākarissati”. ^snp5-1-18-4

Sambuddhoti vaco sutvā, ^snp5-1-19-1

Udaggo bāvarī ahu; ^snp5-1-19-2

Sokassa tanuko āsi, ^snp5-1-19-3

Pītiñca vipulaṁ labhi. ^snp5-1-19-4

So bāvarī attamano udaggo, ^snp5-1-20-1

Taṁ devataṁ pucchati vedajāto; ^snp5-1-20-2

“Katamamhi gāme nigamamhi vā pana, ^snp5-1-20-3

Katamamhi vā janapade lokanātho; ^snp5-1-20-4

Yattha gantvāna passemu, ^snp5-1-20-5

Sambuddhaṁ dvipaduttamaṁ”. ^snp5-1-20-6

“Sāvatthiyaṁ kosalamandire jino, ^snp5-1-21-1

Pahūtapañño varabhūrimedhaso; ^snp5-1-21-2

So sakyaputto vidhuro anāsavo, ^snp5-1-21-3

Muddhādhipātassa vidū narāsabho”. ^snp5-1-21-4

Tato āmantayī sisse, ^snp5-1-22-1

Brāhmaṇe mantapārage; ^snp5-1-22-2

“Etha māṇavā akkhissaṁ, ^snp5-1-22-3

Suṇātha vacanaṁ mama. ^snp5-1-22-4

Yasseso dullabho loke, ^snp5-1-23-1

Pātubhāvo abhiṇhaso; ^snp5-1-23-2

Svājja lokamhi uppanno, ^snp5-1-23-3

Sambuddho iti vissuto; ^snp5-1-23-4

Khippaṁ gantvāna sāvatthiṁ, ^snp5-1-23-5

Passavho dvipaduttamaṁ”. ^snp5-1-23-6

“Kathaṁ carahi jānemu, ^snp5-1-24-1

Disvā buddhoti brāhmaṇa; ^snp5-1-24-2

Ajānataṁ no pabrūhi, ^snp5-1-24-3

Yathā jānemu taṁ mayaṁ”. ^snp5-1-24-4

“Āgatāni hi mantesu, ^snp5-1-25-1

Mahāpurisalakkhaṇā; ^snp5-1-25-2

Dvattiṁsāni ca byākkhātā, ^snp5-1-25-3

Samattā anupubbaso. ^snp5-1-25-4

Yassete honti gattesu, ^snp5-1-26-1

Mahāpurisalakkhaṇā; ^snp5-1-26-2

Dveyeva tassa gatiyo, ^snp5-1-26-3

Tatiyā hi na vijjati. ^snp5-1-26-4

Sace agāraṁ āvasati, ^snp5-1-27-1

Vijeyya pathaviṁ imaṁ; ^snp5-1-27-2

Adaṇḍena asatthena, ^snp5-1-27-3

Dhammena manusāsati. ^snp5-1-27-4

Sace ca so pabbajati, ^snp5-1-28-1

Agārā anagāriyaṁ; ^snp5-1-28-2

Vivaṭṭacchado sambuddho, ^snp5-1-28-3

Arahā bhavati anuttaro. ^snp5-1-28-4

Jātiṁ gottañca lakkhaṇaṁ, ^snp5-1-29-1

Mante sisse punāpare; ^snp5-1-29-2

Muddhaṁ muddhādhipātañca, ^snp5-1-29-3

Manasāyeva pucchatha. ^snp5-1-29-4

Anāvaraṇadassāvī, ^snp5-1-30-1

Yadi buddho bhavissati; ^snp5-1-30-2

Manasā pucchite pañhe, ^snp5-1-30-3

Vācāya vissajessati”. ^snp5-1-30-4

Bāvarissa vaco sutvā, ^snp5-1-31-1

Sissā soḷasa brāhmaṇā; ^snp5-1-31-2

Ajito tissametteyyo, ^snp5-1-31-3

Puṇṇako atha mettagū. ^snp5-1-31-4

Dhotako upasīvo ca, ^snp5-1-32-1

Nando ca atha hemako; ^snp5-1-32-2

Todeyya-kappā dubhayo, ^snp5-1-32-3

Jatukaṇṇī ca paṇḍito. ^snp5-1-32-4

Bhadrāvudho udayo ca, ^snp5-1-33-1

Posālo cāpi brāhmaṇo; ^snp5-1-33-2

Mogharājā ca medhāvī, ^snp5-1-33-3

Piṅgiyo ca mahāisi. ^snp5-1-33-4

Paccekagaṇino sabbe, ^snp5-1-34-1

Sabbalokassa vissutā; ^snp5-1-34-2

Jhāyī jhānaratā dhīrā, ^snp5-1-34-3

Pubbavāsanavāsitā. ^snp5-1-34-4

Bāvariṁ abhivādetvā, ^snp5-1-35-1

Katvā ca naṁ padakkhiṇaṁ; ^snp5-1-35-2

Jaṭājinadharā sabbe, ^snp5-1-35-3

Pakkāmuṁ uttarāmukhā. ^snp5-1-35-4

Aḷakassa patiṭṭhānaṁ, ^snp5-1-36-1

Purimāhissatiṁ tadā; ^snp5-1-36-2

Ujjeniñcāpi gonaddhaṁ, ^snp5-1-36-3

Vedisaṁ vanasavhayaṁ. ^snp5-1-36-4

Kosambiñcāpi sāketaṁ, ^snp5-1-37-1

Sāvatthiñca puruttamaṁ; ^snp5-1-37-2

Setabyaṁ kapilavatthuṁ, ^snp5-1-37-3

Kusinārañca mandiraṁ. ^snp5-1-37-4

Pāvañca bhoganagaraṁ, ^snp5-1-38-1

Vesāliṁ māgadhaṁ puraṁ; ^snp5-1-38-2

Pāsāṇakaṁ cetiyañca, ^snp5-1-38-3

Ramaṇīyaṁ manoramaṁ. ^snp5-1-38-4

Tasitovudakaṁ sītaṁ, ^snp5-1-39-1

Mahālābhaṁva vāṇijo; ^snp5-1-39-2

Chāyaṁ ghammābhitattova, ^snp5-1-39-3

Turitā pabbatamāruhuṁ. ^snp5-1-39-4

Bhagavā tamhi samaye, ^snp5-1-40-1

Bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato; ^snp5-1-40-2

Bhikkhūnaṁ dhammaṁ deseti, ^snp5-1-40-3

Sīhova nadatī vane. ^snp5-1-40-4

Ajito addasa buddhaṁ, ^snp5-1-41-1

Sataraṁsiṁva bhāṇumaṁ; ^snp5-1-41-2

Candaṁ yathā pannarase, ^snp5-1-41-3

Pāripūriṁ upāgataṁ. ^snp5-1-41-4

Athassa gatte disvāna, ^snp5-1-42-1

Paripūrañca byañjanaṁ; ^snp5-1-42-2

Ekamantaṁ ṭhito haṭṭho, ^snp5-1-42-3

Manopañhe apucchatha. ^snp5-1-42-4

“Ādissa jammanaṁ brūhi, ^snp5-1-43-1

Gottaṁ brūhi salakkhaṇaṁ; ^snp5-1-43-2

Mantesu pāramiṁ brūhi, ^snp5-1-43-3

Kati vāceti brāhmaṇo”. ^snp5-1-43-4

“Vīsaṁ vassasataṁ āyu, ^snp5-1-44-1

So ca gottena bāvarī; ^snp5-1-44-2

Tīṇissa lakkhaṇā gatte, ^snp5-1-44-3

Tiṇṇaṁ vedāna pāragū. ^snp5-1-44-4

Lakkhaṇe itihāse ca, ^snp5-1-45-1

Sanighaṇḍusakeṭubhe; ^snp5-1-45-2

Pañcasatāni vāceti, ^snp5-1-45-3

Sadhamme pāramiṁ gato”. ^snp5-1-45-4

“Lakkhaṇānaṁ pavicayaṁ, ^snp5-1-46-1

Bāvarissa naruttama; ^snp5-1-46-2

Kaṅkhacchida pakāsehi, ^snp5-1-46-3

Mā no kaṅkhāyitaṁ ahu”. ^snp5-1-46-4

“Mukhaṁ jivhāya chādeti, ^snp5-1-47-1

Uṇṇassa bhamukantare; ^snp5-1-47-2

Kosohitaṁ vatthaguyhaṁ, ^snp5-1-47-3

Evaṁ jānāhi māṇava”. ^snp5-1-47-4

Pucchañhi kiñci asuṇanto, ^snp5-1-48-1

Sutvā pañhe viyākate; ^snp5-1-48-2

Vicinteti jano sabbo, ^snp5-1-48-3

Vedajāto katañjalī. ^snp5-1-48-4

“Ko nu devo vā brahmā vā, ^snp5-1-49-1

Indo vāpi sujampati; ^snp5-1-49-2

Manasā pucchite pañhe, ^snp5-1-49-3

Kametaṁ paṭibhāsati”. ^snp5-1-49-4

“Muddhaṁ muddhādhipātañca, ^snp5-1-50-1

Bāvarī paripucchati; ^snp5-1-50-2

Taṁ byākarohi bhagavā, ^snp5-1-50-3

Kaṅkhaṁ vinaya no ise”. ^snp5-1-50-4

“Avijjā muddhāti jānāhi, ^snp5-1-51-1

Vijjā muddhādhipātinī; ^snp5-1-51-2

Saddhāsatisamādhīhi, ^snp5-1-51-3

Chandaviriyena saṁyutā”. ^snp5-1-51-4

Tato vedena mahatā, ^snp5-1-52-1

Santhambhitvāna māṇavo; ^snp5-1-52-2

Ekaṁsaṁ ajinaṁ katvā, ^snp5-1-52-3

Pādesu sirasā pati. ^snp5-1-52-4

“Bāvarī brāhmaṇo bhoto, ^snp5-1-53-1

Saha sissehi mārisa; ^snp5-1-53-2

Udaggacitto sumano, ^snp5-1-53-3

Pāde vandati cakkhuma”. ^snp5-1-53-4

“Sukhito bāvarī hotu, ^snp5-1-54-1

Saha sissehi brāhmaṇo; ^snp5-1-54-2

Tvañcāpi sukhito hohi, ^snp5-1-54-3

Ciraṁ jīvāhi māṇava. ^snp5-1-54-4

Bāvarissa ca tuyhaṁ vā, ^snp5-1-55-1

Sabbesaṁ sabbasaṁsayaṁ; ^snp5-1-55-2

Katāvakāsā pucchavho, ^snp5-1-55-3

Yaṁ kiñci manasicchatha”. ^snp5-1-55-4

Sambuddhena katokāso, ^snp5-1-56-1

Nisīditvāna pañjalī; ^snp5-1-56-2

Ajito paṭhamaṁ pañhaṁ, ^snp5-1-56-3

Tattha pucchi tathāgataṁ. ^snp5-1-56-4

Vatthugāthā niṭṭhitā. ^snp5-1-56-5

### Ajitamāṇavapucchā (Sutta Nipāta 5.2) ^snp5-2-0

“Kenassu nivuto loko, ^snp5-2-1-1

(iccāyasmā ajito) ^snp5-2-1-2

Kenassu nappakāsati; ^snp5-2-1-3

Kissābhilepanaṁ brūsi, ^snp5-2-1-4

Kiṁsu tassa mahabbhayaṁ”. ^snp5-2-1-5

“Avijjāya nivuto loko, ^snp5-2-2-1

(ajitāti bhagavā) ^snp5-2-2-2

Vevicchā pamādā nappakāsati; ^snp5-2-2-3

Jappābhilepanaṁ brūmi, ^snp5-2-2-4

Dukkhamassa mahabbhayaṁ”. ^snp5-2-2-5

“Savanti sabbadhi sotā, ^snp5-2-3-1

(iccāyasmā ajito) ^snp5-2-3-2

Sotānaṁ kiṁ nivāraṇaṁ; ^snp5-2-3-3

Sotānaṁ saṁvaraṁ brūhi, ^snp5-2-3-4

Kena sotā pidhiyyare”. ^snp5-2-3-5

“Yāni sotāni lokasmiṁ, ^snp5-2-4-1

(ajitāti bhagavā) ^snp5-2-4-2

Sati tesaṁ nivāraṇaṁ; ^snp5-2-4-3

Sotānaṁ saṁvaraṁ brūmi, ^snp5-2-4-4

Paññāyete pidhiyyare”. ^snp5-2-4-5

“Paññā ceva sati yañca, ^snp5-2-5-1

(iccāyasmā ajito) ^snp5-2-5-2

Nāmarūpañca mārisa; ^snp5-2-5-3

Etaṁ me puṭṭho pabrūhi, ^snp5-2-5-4

Katthetaṁ uparujjhati”. ^snp5-2-5-5

“Yametaṁ pañhaṁ apucchi, ^snp5-2-6-1

ajita taṁ vadāmi te; ^snp5-2-6-2

Yattha nāmañca rūpañca, ^snp5-2-6-3

asesaṁ uparujjhati; ^snp5-2-6-4

Viññāṇassa nirodhena, ^snp5-2-6-5

etthetaṁ uparujjhati”. ^snp5-2-6-6

“Ye ca saṅkhātadhammāse, ^snp5-2-7-1

ye ca sekhā puthū idha; ^snp5-2-7-2

Tesaṁ me nipako iriyaṁ, ^snp5-2-7-3

puṭṭho pabrūhi mārisa”. ^snp5-2-7-4

“Kāmesu nābhigijjheyya, ^snp5-2-8-1

Manasānāvilo siyā; ^snp5-2-8-2

Kusalo sabbadhammānaṁ, ^snp5-2-8-3

Sato bhikkhu paribbaje”ti. ^snp5-2-8-4

Ajitamāṇavapucchā paṭhamā. ^snp5-2-8-5

### Tissametteyyamāṇavapucchā (Sutta Nipāta 5.3) ^snp5-3-0

“Kodha santusito loke, ^snp5-3-1-1

(iccāyasmā tissametteyyo) ^snp5-3-1-2

Kassa no santi iñjitā; ^snp5-3-1-3

Ko ubhantamabhiññāya, ^snp5-3-1-4

Majjhe mantā na lippati; ^snp5-3-1-5

Kaṁ brūsi mahāpurisoti, ^snp5-3-1-6

Ko idha sibbinimaccagā”. ^snp5-3-1-7

“Kāmesu brahmacariyavā, ^snp5-3-2-1

(metteyyāti bhagavā) ^snp5-3-2-2

Vītataṇho sadā sato; ^snp5-3-2-3

Saṅkhāya nibbuto bhikkhu, ^snp5-3-2-4

Tassa no santi iñjitā. ^snp5-3-2-5

So ubhantamabhiññāya, ^snp5-3-3-1

Majjhe mantā na lippati; ^snp5-3-3-2

Taṁ brūmi mahāpurisoti, ^snp5-3-3-3

So idha sibbinimaccagā”ti. ^snp5-3-3-4

Tissametteyyamāṇavapucchā dutiyā. ^snp5-3-3-5

### Puṇṇakamāṇavapucchā (Sutta Nipāta 5.4) ^snp5-4-0

“Anejaṁ mūladassāviṁ, ^snp5-4-1-1

(iccāyasmā puṇṇako) ^snp5-4-1-2

Atthi pañhena āgamaṁ; ^snp5-4-1-3

Kiṁ nissitā isayo manujā, ^snp5-4-1-4

Khattiyā brāhmaṇā devatānaṁ; ^snp5-4-1-5

Yaññamakappayiṁsu puthūdha loke, ^snp5-4-1-6

Pucchāmi taṁ bhagavā brūhi me taṁ”. ^snp5-4-1-7

“Ye kecime isayo manujā, ^snp5-4-2-1

(puṇṇakāti bhagavā) ^snp5-4-2-2

Khattiyā brāhmaṇā devatānaṁ; ^snp5-4-2-3

Yaññamakappayiṁsu puthūdha loke, ^snp5-4-2-4

Āsīsamānā puṇṇaka itthattaṁ; ^snp5-4-2-5

Jaraṁ sitā yaññamakappayiṁsu”. ^snp5-4-2-6

“Ye kecime isayo manujā, ^snp5-4-3-1

(iccāyasmā puṇṇako) ^snp5-4-3-2

Khattiyā brāhmaṇā devatānaṁ; ^snp5-4-3-3

Yaññamakappayiṁsu puthūdha loke, ^snp5-4-3-4

Kaccissu te bhagavā yaññapathe appamattā; ^snp5-4-3-5

Atāruṁ jātiñca jarañca mārisa, ^snp5-4-3-6

Pucchāmi taṁ bhagavā brūhi me taṁ”. ^snp5-4-3-7

“Āsīsanti thomayanti abhijappanti juhanti, ^snp5-4-4-1

(puṇṇakāti bhagavā) ^snp5-4-4-2

Kāmābhijappanti paṭicca lābhaṁ; ^snp5-4-4-3

Te yājayogā bhavarāgarattā, ^snp5-4-4-4

Nātariṁsu jātijaranti brūmi”. ^snp5-4-4-5

“Te ce nātariṁsu yājayogā, ^snp5-4-5-1

(iccāyasmā puṇṇako) ^snp5-4-5-2

Yaññehi jātiñca jarañca mārisa; ^snp5-4-5-3

Atha ko carahi devamanussaloke, ^snp5-4-5-4

Atāri jātiñca jarañca mārisa; ^snp5-4-5-5

Pucchāmi taṁ bhagavā brūhi me taṁ”. ^snp5-4-5-6

“Saṅkhāya lokasmi paroparāni, ^snp5-4-6-1

(puṇṇakāti bhagavā) ^snp5-4-6-2

Yassiñjitaṁ natthi kuhiñci loke; ^snp5-4-6-3

Santo vidhūmo anīgho nirāso, ^snp5-4-6-4

Atāri so jātijaranti brūmī”ti. ^snp5-4-6-5

Puṇṇakamāṇavapucchā tatiyā. ^snp5-4-6-6

### Mettagūmāṇavapucchā (Sutta Nipāta 5.5) ^snp5-5-0

“Pucchāmi taṁ bhagavā brūhi me taṁ, ^snp5-5-1-1

(iccāyasmā mettagū) ^snp5-5-1-2

Maññāmi taṁ vedaguṁ bhāvitattaṁ; ^snp5-5-1-3

Kuto nu dukkhā samudāgatā ime, ^snp5-5-1-4

Ye keci lokasmimanekarūpā”. ^snp5-5-1-5

“Dukkhassa ve maṁ pabhavaṁ apucchasi, ^snp5-5-2-1

(mettagūti bhagavā) ^snp5-5-2-2

Taṁ te pavakkhāmi yathā pajānaṁ; ^snp5-5-2-3

Upadhinidānā pabhavanti dukkhā, ^snp5-5-2-4

Ye keci lokasmimanekarūpā. ^snp5-5-2-5

Yo ve avidvā upadhiṁ karoti, ^snp5-5-3-1

Punappunaṁ dukkhamupeti mando; ^snp5-5-3-2

Tasmā pajānaṁ upadhiṁ na kayirā, ^snp5-5-3-3

Dukkhassa jātippabhavānupassī”. ^snp5-5-3-4

“Yaṁ taṁ apucchimha akittayī no, ^snp5-5-4-1
