Aññaṁ taṁ pucchāma tadiṅgha brūhi; ^snp5-5-4-2

Kathaṁ nu dhīrā vitaranti oghaṁ, ^snp5-5-4-3

Jātiṁ jaraṁ sokapariddavañca; ^snp5-5-4-4

Taṁ me muni sādhu viyākarohi, ^snp5-5-4-5

Tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo”. ^snp5-5-4-6

“Kittayissāmi te dhammaṁ, ^snp5-5-5-1

(mettagūti bhagavā) ^snp5-5-5-2

Diṭṭhe dhamme anītihaṁ; ^snp5-5-5-3

Yaṁ viditvā sato caraṁ, ^snp5-5-5-4

Tare loke visattikaṁ”. ^snp5-5-5-5

“Tañcāhaṁ abhinandāmi, ^snp5-5-6-1

mahesi dhammamuttamaṁ; ^snp5-5-6-2

Yaṁ viditvā sato caraṁ, ^snp5-5-6-3

tare loke visattikaṁ”. ^snp5-5-6-4

“Yaṁ kiñci sampajānāsi, ^snp5-5-7-1

(mettagūti bhagavā) ^snp5-5-7-2

Uddhaṁ adho tiriyañcāpi majjhe; ^snp5-5-7-3

Etesu nandiñca nivesanañca, ^snp5-5-7-4

Panujja viññāṇaṁ bhave na tiṭṭhe. ^snp5-5-7-5

Evaṁvihārī sato appamatto, ^snp5-5-8-1

Bhikkhu caraṁ hitvā mamāyitāni; ^snp5-5-8-2

Jātiṁ jaraṁ sokapariddavañca, ^snp5-5-8-3

Idheva vidvā pajaheyya dukkhaṁ”. ^snp5-5-8-4

“Etābhinandāmi vaco mahesino, ^snp5-5-9-1

Sukittitaṁ gotamanūpadhīkaṁ; ^snp5-5-9-2

Addhā hi bhagavā pahāsi dukkhaṁ, ^snp5-5-9-3

Tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo. ^snp5-5-9-4

Te cāpi nūnappajaheyyu dukkhaṁ, ^snp5-5-10-1

Ye tvaṁ muni aṭṭhitaṁ ovadeyya; ^snp5-5-10-2

Taṁ taṁ namassāmi samecca nāga, ^snp5-5-10-3

Appeva maṁ bhagavā aṭṭhitaṁ ovadeyya”. ^snp5-5-10-4

“Yaṁ brāhmaṇaṁ vedagumābhijaññā, ^snp5-5-11-1

Akiñcanaṁ kāmabhave asattaṁ; ^snp5-5-11-2

Addhā hi so oghamimaṁ atāri, ^snp5-5-11-3

Tiṇṇo ca pāraṁ akhilo akaṅkho. ^snp5-5-11-4

Vidvā ca yo vedagū naro idha, ^snp5-5-12-1

Bhavābhave saṅgamimaṁ visajja; ^snp5-5-12-2

So vītataṇho anīgho nirāso, ^snp5-5-12-3

Atāri so jātijaranti brūmī”ti. ^snp5-5-12-4

Mettagūmāṇavapucchā catutthī. ^snp5-5-12-5

### Dhotakamāṇavapucchā (Sutta Nipāta 5.6) ^snp5-6-0

“Pucchāmi taṁ bhagavā brūhi metaṁ, ^snp5-6-1-1

(iccāyasmā dhotako) ^snp5-6-1-2

Vācābhikaṅkhāmi mahesi tuyhaṁ; ^snp5-6-1-3

Tava sutvāna nigghosaṁ, ^snp5-6-1-4

Sikkhe nibbānamattano”. ^snp5-6-1-5

“Tenahātappaṁ karohi, ^snp5-6-2-1

(dhotakāti bhagavā) ^snp5-6-2-2

Idheva nipako sato; ^snp5-6-2-3

Ito sutvāna nigghosaṁ, ^snp5-6-2-4

Sikkhe nibbānamattano”. ^snp5-6-2-5

“Passāmahaṁ devamanussaloke, ^snp5-6-3-1

Akiñcanaṁ brāhmaṇamiriyamānaṁ; ^snp5-6-3-2

Taṁ taṁ namassāmi samantacakkhu, ^snp5-6-3-3

Pamuñca maṁ sakka kathaṅkathāhi”. ^snp5-6-3-4

“Nāhaṁ sahissāmi pamocanāya, ^snp5-6-4-1

Kathaṅkathiṁ dhotaka kañci loke; ^snp5-6-4-2

Dhammañca seṭṭhaṁ abhijānamāno, ^snp5-6-4-3

Evaṁ tuvaṁ oghamimaṁ taresi”. ^snp5-6-4-4

“Anusāsa brahme karuṇāyamāno, ^snp5-6-5-1

Vivekadhammaṁ yamahaṁ vijaññaṁ; ^snp5-6-5-2

Yathāhaṁ ākāsova abyāpajjamāno, ^snp5-6-5-3

Idheva santo asito careyyaṁ”. ^snp5-6-5-4

“Kittayissāmi te santiṁ, ^snp5-6-6-1

(dhotakāti bhagavā) ^snp5-6-6-2

Diṭṭhe dhamme anītihaṁ; ^snp5-6-6-3

Yaṁ viditvā sato caraṁ, ^snp5-6-6-4

Tare loke visattikaṁ”. ^snp5-6-6-5

“Tañcāhaṁ abhinandāmi, ^snp5-6-7-1

mahesi santimuttamaṁ; ^snp5-6-7-2

Yaṁ viditvā sato caraṁ, ^snp5-6-7-3

tare loke visattikaṁ”. ^snp5-6-7-4

“Yaṁ kiñci sampajānāsi, ^snp5-6-8-1

(dhotakāti bhagavā) ^snp5-6-8-2

Uddhaṁ adho tiriyañcāpi majjhe; ^snp5-6-8-3

Etaṁ viditvā saṅgoti loke, ^snp5-6-8-4

Bhavābhavāya mākāsi taṇhan”ti. ^snp5-6-8-5

Dhotakamāṇavapucchā pañcamī. ^snp5-6-8-6

### Upasīvamāṇavapucchā (Sutta Nipāta 5.7) ^snp5-7-0

“Eko ahaṁ sakka mahantamoghaṁ, ^snp5-7-1-1

(iccāyasmā upasīvo) ^snp5-7-1-2

Anissito no visahāmi tārituṁ; ^snp5-7-1-3

Ārammaṇaṁ brūhi samantacakkhu, ^snp5-7-1-4

Yaṁ nissito oghamimaṁ tareyyaṁ”. ^snp5-7-1-5

“Ākiñcaññaṁ pekkhamāno satimā, ^snp5-7-2-1

(upasīvāti bhagavā) ^snp5-7-2-2

Natthīti nissāya tarassu oghaṁ; ^snp5-7-2-3

Kāme pahāya virato kathāhi, ^snp5-7-2-4

Taṇhakkhayaṁ nattamahābhipassa”. ^snp5-7-2-5

“Sabbesu kāmesu yo vītarāgo, ^snp5-7-3-1

(iccāyasmā upasīvo) ^snp5-7-3-2

Ākiñcaññaṁ nissito hitvā maññaṁ; ^snp5-7-3-3

Saññāvimokkhe parame vimutto, ^snp5-7-3-4

Tiṭṭhe nu so tattha anānuyāyī”. ^snp5-7-3-5

“Sabbesu kāmesu yo vītarāgo, ^snp5-7-4-1

(upasīvāti bhagavā) ^snp5-7-4-2

Ākiñcaññaṁ nissito hitvā maññaṁ; ^snp5-7-4-3

Saññāvimokkhe parame vimutto, ^snp5-7-4-4

Tiṭṭheyya so tattha anānuyāyī”. ^snp5-7-4-5

“Tiṭṭhe ce so tattha anānuyāyī, ^snp5-7-5-1

Pūgampi vassānaṁ samantacakkhu; ^snp5-7-5-2

Tattheva so sītisiyā vimutto, ^snp5-7-5-3

Cavetha viññāṇaṁ tathāvidhassa”. ^snp5-7-5-4

“Accī yathā vātavegena khittā, ^snp5-7-6-1

(upasīvāti bhagavā) ^snp5-7-6-2

Atthaṁ paleti na upeti saṅkhaṁ; ^snp5-7-6-3

Evaṁ munī nāmakāyā vimutto, ^snp5-7-6-4

Atthaṁ paleti na upeti saṅkhaṁ”. ^snp5-7-6-5

“Atthaṅgato so uda vā so natthi, ^snp5-7-7-1

Udāhu ve sassatiyā arogo; ^snp5-7-7-2

Taṁ me munī sādhu viyākarohi, ^snp5-7-7-3

Tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo”. ^snp5-7-7-4

“Atthaṅgatassa na pamāṇamatthi, ^snp5-7-8-1

(upasīvāti bhagavā) ^snp5-7-8-2

Yena naṁ vajjuṁ taṁ tassa natthi; ^snp5-7-8-3

Sabbesu dhammesu samohatesu, ^snp5-7-8-4

Samūhatā vādapathāpi sabbe”ti. ^snp5-7-8-5

Upasīvamāṇavapucchā chaṭṭhī. ^snp5-7-8-6

### Nandamāṇavapucchā (Sutta Nipāta 5.8) ^snp5-8-0

“Santi loke munayo, ^snp5-8-1-1

(iccāyasmā nando) ^snp5-8-1-2

Janā vadanti tayidaṁ kathaṁsu; ^snp5-8-1-3

Ñāṇūpapannaṁ no muniṁ vadanti, ^snp5-8-1-4

Udāhu ve jīvitenūpapannaṁ”. ^snp5-8-1-5

“Na diṭṭhiyā na sutiyā na ñāṇena, (…) ^snp5-8-2-1

Munīdha nanda kusalā vadanti; ^snp5-8-2-2

Visenikatvā anīghā nirāsā, ^snp5-8-2-3

Caranti ye te munayoti brūmi”. ^snp5-8-2-4

“Ye kecime samaṇabrāhmaṇāse, ^snp5-8-3-1

(iccāyasmā nando) ^snp5-8-3-2

Diṭṭhassutenāpi vadanti suddhiṁ; ^snp5-8-3-3

Sīlabbatenāpi vadanti suddhiṁ, ^snp5-8-3-4

Anekarūpena vadanti suddhiṁ. ^snp5-8-3-5

Kaccissu te bhagavā tattha yatā carantā, ^snp5-8-3-6

Atāru jātiñca jarañca mārisa; ^snp5-8-3-7

Pucchāmi taṁ bhagavā brūhi me taṁ”. ^snp5-8-3-8

“Ye kecime samaṇabrāhmaṇāse, ^snp5-8-4-1

(nandāti bhagavā) ^snp5-8-4-2

Diṭṭhassutenāpi vadanti suddhiṁ; ^snp5-8-4-3

Sīlabbatenāpi vadanti suddhiṁ, ^snp5-8-4-4

Anekarūpena vadanti suddhiṁ; ^snp5-8-4-5

Kiñcāpi te tattha yatā caranti, ^snp5-8-4-6

Nātariṁsu jātijaranti brūmi”. ^snp5-8-4-7

“Ye kecime samaṇabrāhmaṇāse, ^snp5-8-5-1

(iccāyasmā nando) ^snp5-8-5-2

Diṭṭhassutenāpi vadanti suddhiṁ; ^snp5-8-5-3

Sīlabbatenāpi vadanti suddhiṁ, ^snp5-8-5-4

Anekarūpena vadanti suddhiṁ. ^snp5-8-5-5

Te ce muni brūsi anoghatiṇṇe, ^snp5-8-5-6

Atha ko carahi devamanussaloke; ^snp5-8-5-7

Atāri jātiñca jarañca mārisa, ^snp5-8-5-8

Pucchāmi taṁ bhagavā brūhi me taṁ”. ^snp5-8-5-9

“Nāhaṁ sabbe samaṇabrāhmaṇāse, ^snp5-8-6-1

(nandāti bhagavā) ^snp5-8-6-2

Jātijarāya nivutāti brūmi; ^snp5-8-6-3

Ye sīdha diṭṭhaṁ va sutaṁ mutaṁ vā, ^snp5-8-6-4

Sīlabbataṁ vāpi pahāya sabbaṁ. ^snp5-8-6-5

Anekarūpampi pahāya sabbaṁ, ^snp5-8-6-6

Taṇhaṁ pariññāya anāsavāse; ^snp5-8-6-7

Te ve narā oghatiṇṇāti brūmi”. ^snp5-8-6-8

“Etābhinandāmi vaco mahesino, ^snp5-8-7-1

Sukittitaṁ gotamanūpadhīkaṁ; ^snp5-8-7-2

Ye sīdha diṭṭhaṁ va sutaṁ mutaṁ vā, ^snp5-8-7-3

Sīlabbataṁ vāpi pahāya sabbaṁ. ^snp5-8-7-4

Anekarūpampi pahāya sabbaṁ, ^snp5-8-7-5

Taṇhaṁ pariññāya anāsavāse; ^snp5-8-7-6

Ahampi te oghatiṇṇāti brūmī”ti. ^snp5-8-7-7

Nandamāṇavapucchā sattamā. ^snp5-8-7-8

### Hemakamāṇavapucchā (Sutta Nipāta 5.9) ^snp5-9-0

“Ye me pubbe viyākaṁsu, ^snp5-9-1-1

(iccāyasmā hemako) ^snp5-9-1-2

Huraṁ gotamasāsanā; ^snp5-9-1-3

Iccāsi iti bhavissati, ^snp5-9-1-4

Sabbaṁ taṁ itihītihaṁ; ^snp5-9-1-5

Sabbaṁ taṁ takkavaḍḍhanaṁ, ^snp5-9-1-6

Nāhaṁ tattha abhiramiṁ. ^snp5-9-1-7

Tvañca me dhammamakkhāhi, ^snp5-9-2-1

taṇhānigghātanaṁ muni; ^snp5-9-2-2

Yaṁ viditvā sato caraṁ, ^snp5-9-2-3

tare loke visattikaṁ”. ^snp5-9-2-4

“Idha diṭṭhasutamutaviññātesu, ^snp5-9-3-1

Piyarūpesu hemaka; ^snp5-9-3-2

Chandarāgavinodanaṁ, ^snp5-9-3-3

Nibbānapadamaccutaṁ. ^snp5-9-3-4

Etadaññāya ye satā, ^snp5-9-4-1

Diṭṭhadhammābhinibbutā; ^snp5-9-4-2

Upasantā ca te sadā, ^snp5-9-4-3

Tiṇṇā loke visattikan”ti. ^snp5-9-4-4

Hemakamāṇavapucchā aṭṭhamā. ^snp5-9-4-5

### Todeyyamāṇavapucchā (Sutta Nipāta 5.10) ^snp5-10-0

“Yasmiṁ kāmā na vasanti, ^snp5-10-1-1

(iccāyasmā todeyyo) ^snp5-10-1-2

Taṇhā yassa na vijjati; ^snp5-10-1-3

Kathaṅkathā ca yo tiṇṇo, ^snp5-10-1-4

Vimokkho tassa kīdiso”. ^snp5-10-1-5

“Yasmiṁ kāmā na vasanti, ^snp5-10-2-1

(todeyyāti bhagavā) ^snp5-10-2-2

Taṇhā yassa na vijjati; ^snp5-10-2-3

Kathaṅkathā ca yo tiṇṇo, ^snp5-10-2-4

Vimokkho tassa nāparo”. ^snp5-10-2-5

“Nirāsaso so uda āsasāno, ^snp5-10-3-1

Paññāṇavā so uda paññakappī; ^snp5-10-3-2

Muniṁ ahaṁ sakka yathā vijaññaṁ, ^snp5-10-3-3

Taṁ me viyācikkha samantacakkhu”. ^snp5-10-3-4

“Nirāsaso so na ca āsasāno, ^snp5-10-4-1

Paññāṇavā so na ca paññakappī; ^snp5-10-4-2

Evampi todeyya muniṁ vijāna, ^snp5-10-4-3

Akiñcanaṁ kāmabhave asattan”ti. ^snp5-10-4-4

Todeyyamāṇavapucchā navamā. ^snp5-10-4-5

### Kappamāṇavapucchā (Sutta Nipāta 5.11) ^snp5-11-0

“Majjhe sarasmiṁ tiṭṭhataṁ, ^snp5-11-1-1

(iccāyasmā kappo) ^snp5-11-1-2

Oghe jāte mahabbhaye; ^snp5-11-1-3

Jarāmaccuparetānaṁ, ^snp5-11-1-4

Dīpaṁ pabrūhi mārisa; ^snp5-11-1-5

Tvañca me dīpamakkhāhi, ^snp5-11-1-6

Yathāyidaṁ nāparaṁ siyā”. ^snp5-11-1-7

“Majjhe sarasmiṁ tiṭṭhataṁ, ^snp5-11-2-1

(kappāti bhagavā) ^snp5-11-2-2

Oghe jāte mahabbhaye; ^snp5-11-2-3

Jarāmaccuparetānaṁ, ^snp5-11-2-4

Dīpaṁ pabrūmi kappa te. ^snp5-11-2-5

Akiñcanaṁ anādānaṁ, ^snp5-11-3-1

etaṁ dīpaṁ anāparaṁ; ^snp5-11-3-2

Nibbānaṁ iti naṁ brūmi, ^snp5-11-3-3

jarāmaccuparikkhayaṁ. ^snp5-11-3-4

Etadaññāya ye satā, ^snp5-11-4-1

Diṭṭhadhammābhinibbutā; ^snp5-11-4-2

Na te māravasānugā, ^snp5-11-4-3

Na te mārassa paddhagū”ti. ^snp5-11-4-4

Kappamāṇavapucchā dasamā. ^snp5-11-4-5

### Jatukaṇṇimāṇavapucchā (Sutta Nipāta 5.12) ^snp5-12-0

“Sutvānahaṁ vīramakāmakāmiṁ, ^snp5-12-1-1

(iccāyasmā jatukaṇṇi) ^snp5-12-1-2

Oghātigaṁ puṭṭhumakāmamāgamaṁ; ^snp5-12-1-3

Santipadaṁ brūhi sahajanetta, ^snp5-12-1-4

Yathātacchaṁ bhagavā brūhi metaṁ. ^snp5-12-1-5

Bhagavā hi kāme abhibhuyya iriyati, ^snp5-12-2-1

Ādiccova pathaviṁ tejī tejasā; ^snp5-12-2-2

Parittapaññassa me bhūripañña, ^snp5-12-2-3

Ācikkha dhammaṁ yamahaṁ vijaññaṁ; ^snp5-12-2-4

Jātijarāya idha vippahānaṁ”. ^snp5-12-2-5

“Kāmesu vinaya gedhaṁ, ^snp5-12-3-1

(jatukaṇṇīti bhagavā) ^snp5-12-3-2

Nekkhammaṁ daṭṭhu khemato; ^snp5-12-3-3

Uggahītaṁ nirattaṁ vā, ^snp5-12-3-4

Mā te vijjittha kiñcanaṁ. ^snp5-12-3-5

Yaṁ pubbe taṁ visosehi, ^snp5-12-4-1

pacchā te māhu kiñcanaṁ; ^snp5-12-4-2

Majjhe ce no gahessasi, ^snp5-12-4-3

upasanto carissasi. ^snp5-12-4-4

Sabbaso nāmarūpasmiṁ, ^snp5-12-5-1

Vītagedhassa brāhmaṇa; ^snp5-12-5-2

Āsavāssa na vijjanti, ^snp5-12-5-3

Yehi maccuvasaṁ vaje”ti. ^snp5-12-5-4

Jatukaṇṇimāṇavapucchā ekādasamā. ^snp5-12-5-5

### Bhadrāvudhamāṇavapucchā (Sutta Nipāta 5.13) ^snp5-13-0

“Okañjahaṁ taṇhacchidaṁ anejaṁ, ^snp5-13-1-1

(iccāyasmā bhadrāvudho) ^snp5-13-1-2

Nandiñjahaṁ oghatiṇṇaṁ vimuttaṁ; ^snp5-13-1-3

Kappañjahaṁ abhiyāce sumedhaṁ, ^snp5-13-1-4

Sutvāna nāgassa apanamissanti ito. ^snp5-13-1-5

Nānājanā janapadehi saṅgatā, ^snp5-13-2-1

Tava vīra vākyaṁ abhikaṅkhamānā; ^snp5-13-2-2

Tesaṁ tuvaṁ sādhu viyākarohi, ^snp5-13-2-3

Tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo”. ^snp5-13-2-4

“Ādānataṇhaṁ vinayetha sabbaṁ, ^snp5-13-3-1

(bhadrāvudhāti bhagavā ^snp5-13-3-2

Uddhaṁ adho tiriyañcāpi majjhe; ^snp5-13-3-3

Yaṁ yañhi lokasmimupādiyanti, ^snp5-13-3-4

Teneva māro anveti jantuṁ. ^snp5-13-3-5

Tasmā pajānaṁ na upādiyetha, ^snp5-13-4-1

Bhikkhu sato kiñcanaṁ sabbaloke; ^snp5-13-4-2

Ādānasatte iti pekkhamāno, ^snp5-13-4-3

Pajaṁ imaṁ maccudheyye visattan”ti. ^snp5-13-4-4

Bhadrāvudhamāṇavapucchā dvādasamā. ^snp5-13-4-5

### Udayamāṇavapucchā (Sutta Nipāta 5.14) ^snp5-14-0

“Jhāyiṁ virajamāsīnaṁ, ^snp5-14-1-1

(iccāyasmā udayo) ^snp5-14-1-2

Katakiccaṁ anāsavaṁ; ^snp5-14-1-3

Pāraguṁ sabbadhammānaṁ, ^snp5-14-1-4

Atthi pañhena āgamaṁ; ^snp5-14-1-5

Aññāvimokkhaṁ pabrūhi, ^snp5-14-1-6

Avijjāya pabhedanaṁ”. ^snp5-14-1-7

“Pahānaṁ kāmacchandānaṁ, ^snp5-14-2-1

(udayāti bhagavā) ^snp5-14-2-2

Domanassāna cūbhayaṁ; ^snp5-14-2-3

Thinassa ca panūdanaṁ, ^snp5-14-2-4

Kukkuccānaṁ nivāraṇaṁ. ^snp5-14-2-5

Upekkhāsatisaṁsuddhaṁ, ^snp5-14-3-1

dhammatakkapurejavaṁ; ^snp5-14-3-2

Aññāvimokkhaṁ pabrūmi, ^snp5-14-3-3

avijjāya pabhedanaṁ”. ^snp5-14-3-4

“Kiṁsu saṁyojano loko, ^snp5-14-4-1

kiṁsu tassa vicāraṇaṁ; ^snp5-14-4-2

Kissassa vippahānena, ^snp5-14-4-3

nibbānaṁ iti vuccati”. ^snp5-14-4-4

“Nandisaṁyojano loko, ^snp5-14-5-1

vitakkassa vicāraṇaṁ; ^snp5-14-5-2

Taṇhāya vippahānena, ^snp5-14-5-3

nibbānaṁ iti vuccati”. ^snp5-14-5-4

“Kathaṁ satassa carato, ^snp5-14-6-1

viññāṇaṁ uparujjhati; ^snp5-14-6-2

Bhagavantaṁ puṭṭhumāgamma, ^snp5-14-6-3

taṁ suṇoma vaco tava”. ^snp5-14-6-4

“Ajjhattañca bahiddhā ca, ^snp5-14-7-1

Vedanaṁ nābhinandato; ^snp5-14-7-2

Evaṁ satassa carato, ^snp5-14-7-3

Viññāṇaṁ uparujjhatī”ti. ^snp5-14-7-4

Udayamāṇavapucchā terasamā. ^snp5-14-7-5

### Posālamāṇavapucchā (Sutta Nipāta 5.15) ^snp5-15-0

“Yo atītaṁ ādisati, ^snp5-15-1-1

(iccāyasmā posālo) ^snp5-15-1-2

Anejo chinnasaṁsayo; ^snp5-15-1-3

Pāraguṁ sabbadhammānaṁ, ^snp5-15-1-4

Atthi pañhena āgamaṁ. ^snp5-15-1-5

Vibhūtarūpasaññissa, ^snp5-15-2-1

sabbakāyappahāyino; ^snp5-15-2-2

Ajjhattañca bahiddhā ca, ^snp5-15-2-3

natthi kiñcīti passato; ^snp5-15-2-4

Ñāṇaṁ sakkānupucchāmi, ^snp5-15-2-5

kathaṁ neyyo tathāvidho”. ^snp5-15-2-6

“Viññāṇaṭṭhitiyo sabbā, ^snp5-15-3-1

(posālāti bhagavā) ^snp5-15-3-2

Abhijānaṁ tathāgato; ^snp5-15-3-3

Tiṭṭhantamenaṁ jānāti, ^snp5-15-3-4

Vimuttaṁ tapparāyaṇaṁ. ^snp5-15-3-5

Ākiñcaññasambhavaṁ ñatvā, ^snp5-15-4-1

Nandī saṁyojanaṁ iti; ^snp5-15-4-2

Evametaṁ abhiññāya, ^snp5-15-4-3

Tato tattha vipassati; ^snp5-15-4-4

Etaṁ ñāṇaṁ tathaṁ tassa, ^snp5-15-4-5

Brāhmaṇassa vusīmato”ti. ^snp5-15-4-6

Posālamāṇavapucchā cuddasamā. ^snp5-15-4-7

### Mogharājamāṇavapucchā (Sutta Nipāta 5.16) ^snp5-16-0

“Dvāhaṁ sakkaṁ apucchissaṁ, ^snp5-16-1-1

(iccāyasmā mogharājā) ^snp5-16-1-2

Na me byākāsi cakkhumā; ^snp5-16-1-3

Yāvatatiyañca devīsi, ^snp5-16-1-4

Byākarotīti me sutaṁ. ^snp5-16-1-5

Ayaṁ loko paro loko, ^snp5-16-2-1

brahmaloko sadevako; ^snp5-16-2-2

Diṭṭhiṁ te nābhijānāti, ^snp5-16-2-3

gotamassa yasassino. ^snp5-16-2-4

Evaṁ abhikkantadassāviṁ, ^snp5-16-3-1

atthi pañhena āgamaṁ; ^snp5-16-3-2

Kathaṁ lokaṁ avekkhantaṁ, ^snp5-16-3-3

maccurājā na passati”. ^snp5-16-3-4

“Suññato lokaṁ avekkhassu, ^snp5-16-4-1

Mogharāja sadā sato; ^snp5-16-4-2

Attānudiṭṭhiṁ ūhacca, ^snp5-16-4-3

Evaṁ maccutaro siyā; ^snp5-16-4-4

Evaṁ lokaṁ avekkhantaṁ, ^snp5-16-4-5

Maccurājā na passatī”ti. ^snp5-16-4-6

Mogharājamāṇavapucchā pannarasamā. ^snp5-16-4-7

### Piṅgiyamāṇavapucchā (Sutta Nipāta 5.17) ^snp5-17-0

“Jiṇṇohamasmi abalo vītavaṇṇo, ^snp5-17-1-1

(iccāyasmā piṅgiyo) ^snp5-17-1-2

Nettā na suddhā savanaṁ na phāsu; ^snp5-17-1-3

Māhaṁ nassaṁ momuho antarāva, ^snp5-17-1-4

Ācikkha dhammaṁ yamahaṁ vijaññaṁ; ^snp5-17-1-5

Jātijarāya idha vippahānaṁ”. ^snp5-17-1-6

“Disvāna rūpesu vihaññamāne, ^snp5-17-2-1

(piṅgiyāti bhagavā) ^snp5-17-2-2

Ruppanti rūpesu janā pamattā; ^snp5-17-2-3

Tasmā tuvaṁ piṅgiya appamatto, ^snp5-17-2-4

Jahassu rūpaṁ apunabbhavāya”. ^snp5-17-2-5

“Disā catasso vidisā catasso, ^snp5-17-3-1

Uddhaṁ adho dasa disā imāyo; ^snp5-17-3-2

Na tuyhaṁ adiṭṭhaṁ asutaṁ amutaṁ, ^snp5-17-3-3

Atho aviññātaṁ kiñcanamatthi loke; ^snp5-17-3-4

Ācikkha dhammaṁ yamahaṁ vijaññaṁ, ^snp5-17-3-5

Jātijarāya idha vippahānaṁ”. ^snp5-17-3-6

“Taṇhādhipanne manuje pekkhamāno, ^snp5-17-4-1

(piṅgiyāti bhagavā) ^snp5-17-4-2

Santāpajāte jarasā parete; ^snp5-17-4-3

Tasmā tuvaṁ piṅgiya appamatto, ^snp5-17-4-4

Jahassu taṇhaṁ apunabbhavāyā”ti. ^snp5-17-4-5

Piṅgiyamāṇavapucchā soḷasamā. ^snp5-17-4-6

### Pārāyanatthutigāthā (Sutta Nipāta 5.18) ^snp5-18-0

Idamavoca bhagavā magadhesu viharanto pāsāṇake cetiye, ^snp5-18-1-1

paricārakasoḷasānaṁ brāhmaṇānaṁ ajjhiṭṭho puṭṭho puṭṭho pañhaṁ byākāsi. ^snp5-18-1-2

Ekamekassa cepi pañhassa atthamaññāya dhammamaññāya dhammānudhammaṁ paṭipajjeyya, gaccheyyeva jarāmaraṇassa pāraṁ. ^snp5-18-1-3

Pāraṅgamanīyā ime dhammāti, tasmā imassa dhammapariyāyassa pārāyananteva adhivacanaṁ. ^snp5-18-1-4

Ajito tissametteyyo, ^snp5-18-2-1

puṇṇako atha mettagū; ^snp5-18-2-2

Dhotako upasīvo ca, ^snp5-18-2-3

nando ca atha hemako. ^snp5-18-2-4

Todeyya-kappā dubhayo, ^snp5-18-3-1

jatukaṇṇī ca paṇḍito; ^snp5-18-3-2

Bhadrāvudho udayo ca, ^snp5-18-3-3

posālo cāpi brāhmaṇo; ^snp5-18-3-4

Mogharājā ca medhāvī, ^snp5-18-3-5

piṅgiyo ca mahāisi. ^snp5-18-3-6

Ete buddhaṁ upāgacchuṁ, ^snp5-18-4-1

sampannacaraṇaṁ isiṁ; ^snp5-18-4-2

Pucchantā nipuṇe pañhe, ^snp5-18-4-3

buddhaseṭṭhaṁ upāgamuṁ. ^snp5-18-4-4

Tesaṁ buddho pabyākāsi, ^snp5-18-5-1

pañhe puṭṭho yathātathaṁ; ^snp5-18-5-2

Pañhānaṁ veyyākaraṇena, ^snp5-18-5-3

tosesi brāhmaṇe muni. ^snp5-18-5-4

Te tositā cakkhumatā, ^snp5-18-6-1

buddhenādiccabandhunā; ^snp5-18-6-2

Brahmacariyamacariṁsu, ^snp5-18-6-3

varapaññassa santike. ^snp5-18-6-4

Ekamekassa pañhassa, ^snp5-18-7-1

yathā buddhena desitaṁ; ^snp5-18-7-2

Tathā yo paṭipajjeyya, ^snp5-18-7-3

gacche pāraṁ apārato. ^snp5-18-7-4

Apārā pāraṁ gaccheyya, ^snp5-18-8-1

bhāvento maggamuttamaṁ; ^snp5-18-8-2

Maggo so pāraṁ gamanāya, ^snp5-18-8-3

tasmā pārāyanaṁ iti. ^snp5-18-8-4

### Pārāyanānugītigāthā (Sutta Nipāta 5.19) ^snp5-19-0

“Pārāyanamanugāyissaṁ, ^snp5-19-1-1

(iccāyasmā piṅgiyo) ^snp5-19-1-2

Yathāddakkhi tathākkhāsi; ^snp5-19-1-3

Vimalo bhūrimedhaso, ^snp5-19-1-4

Nikkāmo nibbano nāgo; ^snp5-19-1-5

Kissa hetu musā bhaṇe. ^snp5-19-1-6

Pahīnamalamohassa, ^snp5-19-2-1

mānamakkhappahāyino; ^snp5-19-2-2

Handāhaṁ kittayissāmi, ^snp5-19-2-3

giraṁ vaṇṇūpasañhitaṁ. ^snp5-19-2-4

Tamonudo buddho samantacakkhu, ^snp5-19-3-1

Lokantagū sabbabhavātivatto; ^snp5-19-3-2

Anāsavo sabbadukkhappahīno, ^snp5-19-3-3

Saccavhayo brahme upāsito me. ^snp5-19-3-4

Dijo yathā kubbanakaṁ pahāya, ^snp5-19-4-1

Bahupphalaṁ kānanamāvaseyya; ^snp5-19-4-2

Evampahaṁ appadasse pahāya, ^snp5-19-4-3

Mahodadhiṁ haṁsoriva ajjhapatto. ^snp5-19-4-4

Ye me pubbe viyākaṁsu, ^snp5-19-5-1

Huraṁ gotamasāsanā; ^snp5-19-5-2

Iccāsi iti bhavissati, ^snp5-19-5-3

Sabbaṁ taṁ itihītihaṁ; ^snp5-19-5-4

Sabbaṁ taṁ takkavaḍḍhanaṁ. ^snp5-19-5-5

Eko tamanudāsino, ^snp5-19-6-1

jutimā so pabhaṅkaro; ^snp5-19-6-2

Gotamo bhūripaññāṇo, ^snp5-19-6-3

gotamo bhūrimedhaso. ^snp5-19-6-4

Yo me dhammamadesesi, ^snp5-19-7-1

Sandiṭṭhikamakālikaṁ; ^snp5-19-7-2

Taṇhakkhayamanītikaṁ, ^snp5-19-7-3

Yassa natthi upamā kvaci”. ^snp5-19-7-4

“Kiṁ nu tamhā vippavasasi, ^snp5-19-8-1

muhuttamapi piṅgiya; ^snp5-19-8-2

Gotamā bhūripaññāṇā, ^snp5-19-8-3

gotamā bhūrimedhasā. ^snp5-19-8-4

Yo te dhammamadesesi, ^snp5-19-9-1

Sandiṭṭhikamakālikaṁ; ^snp5-19-9-2

Taṇhakkhayamanītikaṁ, ^snp5-19-9-3

Yassa natthi upamā kvaci”. ^snp5-19-9-4

“Nāhaṁ tamhā vippavasāmi, ^snp5-19-10-1

Muhuttamapi brāhmaṇa; ^snp5-19-10-2

Gotamā bhūripaññāṇā, ^snp5-19-10-3

Gotamā bhūrimedhasā. ^snp5-19-10-4

Yo me dhammamadesesi, ^snp5-19-11-1

Sandiṭṭhikamakālikaṁ; ^snp5-19-11-2

Taṇhakkhayamanītikaṁ, ^snp5-19-11-3

Yassa natthi upamā kvaci. ^snp5-19-11-4

Passāmi naṁ manasā cakkhunāva, ^snp5-19-12-1

Rattindivaṁ brāhmaṇa appamatto; ^snp5-19-12-2

Namassamāno vivasemi rattiṁ, ^snp5-19-12-3

Teneva maññāmi avippavāsaṁ. ^snp5-19-12-4

Saddhā ca pīti ca mano sati ca, ^snp5-19-13-1

Nāpentime gotamasāsanamhā; ^snp5-19-13-2

Yaṁ yaṁ disaṁ vajati bhūripañño, ^snp5-19-13-3

Sa tena teneva natohamasmi. ^snp5-19-13-4

Jiṇṇassa me dubbalathāmakassa, ^snp5-19-14-1

Teneva kāyo na paleti tattha; ^snp5-19-14-2

Saṅkappayantāya vajāmi niccaṁ, ^snp5-19-14-3

Mano hi me brāhmaṇa tena yutto. ^snp5-19-14-4

Paṅke sayāno pariphandamāno, ^snp5-19-15-1

Dīpā dīpaṁ upaplaviṁ; ^snp5-19-15-2

Athaddasāsiṁ sambuddhaṁ, ^snp5-19-15-3

Oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṁ”. ^snp5-19-15-4

“Yathā ahū vakkali muttasaddho, ^snp5-19-16-1

Bhadrāvudho āḷavigotamo ca; ^snp5-19-16-2

Evamevaṁ tvampi pamuñcassu saddhaṁ, ^snp5-19-16-3

Gamissasi tvaṁ piṅgiya maccudheyyassa pāraṁ”. ^snp5-19-16-4

“Esa bhiyyo pasīdāmi, ^snp5-19-17-1

Sutvāna munino vaco; ^snp5-19-17-2

Vivaṭṭacchado sambuddho, ^snp5-19-17-3

Akhilo paṭibhānavā. ^snp5-19-17-4

Adhideve abhiññāya, ^snp5-19-18-1

Sabbaṁ vedi varovaraṁ; ^snp5-19-18-2

Pañhānantakaro satthā, ^snp5-19-18-3

Kaṅkhīnaṁ paṭijānataṁ. ^snp5-19-18-4

Asaṁhīraṁ asaṅkuppaṁ, ^snp5-19-19-1

Yassa natthi upamā kvaci; ^snp5-19-19-2

Addhā gamissāmi na mettha kaṅkhā, ^snp5-19-19-3

Evaṁ maṁ dhārehi adhimuttacittan”ti. ^snp5-19-19-4

Pārāyanavaggo pañcamo. ^snp5-19-19-5

Suttuddānaṁ ^snp5-19-19-6

Urago dhaniyopi ca, ^snp5-19-20-1

Khaggavisāṇo kasi ca; ^snp5-19-20-2

Cundo bhavo punadeva, ^snp5-19-20-3

Vasalo ca karaṇīyañca; ^snp5-19-20-4

Hemavato atha yakkho, ^snp5-19-20-5

Vijayasuttaṁ munisuttavaranti. ^snp5-19-20-6

Paṭhamakaṭṭhavaro varavaggo, ^snp5-19-21-1

Dvādasasuttadharo suvibhatto; ^snp5-19-21-2

Desito cakkhumatā vimalena, ^snp5-19-21-3

Suyyati vaggavaro uragoti. ^snp5-19-21-4

Ratanāmagandho hirimaṅgalanāmo, ^snp5-19-22-1

Sucilomakapilo ca brāhmaṇadhammo; ^snp5-19-22-2

Nāvā kiṁsīlauṭṭhahano ca, ^snp5-19-22-3

Rāhulo ca punapi vaṅgīso. ^snp5-19-22-4

Sammāparibbājanīyopi cettha, ^snp5-19-23-1

Dhammikasuttavaro suvibhatto; ^snp5-19-23-2

Cuddasasuttadharo dutiyamhi, ^snp5-19-23-3

Cūḷakavaggavaroti tamāhu. ^snp5-19-23-4

Pabbajjapadhānasubhāsitanāmo, ^snp5-19-24-1

Pūraḷāso punadeva māgho ca; ^snp5-19-24-2

Sabhiyaṁ keṇiyameva sallanāmo, ^snp5-19-24-3

Vāseṭṭhavaro kālikopi ca. ^snp5-19-24-4

Nālakasuttavaro suvibhatto, ^snp5-19-25-1

Taṁ anupassī tathā punadeva; ^snp5-19-25-2

Dvādasasuttadharo tatiyamhi, ^snp5-19-25-3

Suyyati vaggavaro mahānāmo. ^snp5-19-25-4

Kāmaguhaṭṭhakaduṭṭhakanāmā, ^snp5-19-26-1

Suddhavaro paramaṭṭhakanāmo; ^snp5-19-26-2

Jarā mettiyavaro suvibhatto, ^snp5-19-26-3

Pasūramāgaṇḍiyā purābhedo. ^snp5-19-26-4

Kalahavivādo ubho viyuhā ca, ^snp5-19-27-1

Tuvaṭakaattadaṇḍasāriputtā; ^snp5-19-27-2

Soḷasasuttadharo catutthamhi, ^snp5-19-27-3

Aṭṭhakavaggavaroti tamāhu. ^snp5-19-27-4

Magadhe janapade ramaṇīye, ^snp5-19-28-1

Desavare katapuññanivese; ^snp5-19-28-2

Pāsāṇakacetiyavare suvibhatte, ^snp5-19-28-3

Vasi bhagavā gaṇaseṭṭho. ^snp5-19-28-4

Ubhayavāsamāgatiyamhi, ^snp5-19-29-1

Dvādasayojaniyā parisāya; ^snp5-19-29-2

Soḷasabrāhmaṇānaṁ kira puṭṭho, ^snp5-19-29-3

Pucchāya soḷasapañhakammiyā; ^snp5-19-29-4

Nippakāsayi dhammamadāsi. ^snp5-19-29-5

Atthapakāsakabyañjanapuṇṇaṁ, ^snp5-19-30-1

Dhammamadesesi parakhemajaniyaṁ; ^snp5-19-30-2

Lokahitāya jino dvipadaggo, ^snp5-19-30-3

Suttavaraṁ bahudhammavicitraṁ; ^snp5-19-30-4

Sabbakilesapamocanahetuṁ, ^snp5-19-30-5

Desayi suttavaraṁ dvipadaggo. ^snp5-19-30-6

Byañjanamatthapadaṁ samayuttaṁ, ^snp5-19-31-1

Akkharasaññitaopamagāḷhaṁ; ^snp5-19-31-2

Lokavicāraṇañāṇapabhaggaṁ, ^snp5-19-31-3

Desayi suttavaraṁ dvipadaggo. ^snp5-19-31-4

Rāgamale amalaṁ vimalaggaṁ, ^snp5-19-32-1

Dosamale amalaṁ vimalaggaṁ; ^snp5-19-32-2

Mohamale amalaṁ vimalaggaṁ, ^snp5-19-32-3

Lokavicāraṇañāṇapabhaggaṁ; ^snp5-19-32-4

Desayi suttavaraṁ dvipadaggo. ^snp5-19-32-5

Klesamale amalaṁ vimalaggaṁ, ^snp5-19-33-1

Duccaritamale amalaṁ vimalaggaṁ; ^snp5-19-33-2

Lokavicāraṇañāṇapabhaggaṁ, ^snp5-19-33-3

Desayi suttavaraṁ dvipadaggo. ^snp5-19-33-4

Āsavabandhanayogākilesaṁ, ^snp5-19-34-1

Nīvaraṇāni ca tīṇi malāni; ^snp5-19-34-2

Tassa kilesapamocanahetuṁ, ^snp5-19-34-3

Desayi suttavaraṁ dvipadaggo. ^snp5-19-34-4

Nimmalasabbakilesapanūdaṁ, ^snp5-19-35-1

Rāgavirāgamanejamasokaṁ; ^snp5-19-35-2

Santapaṇītasududdasadhammaṁ, ^snp5-19-35-3

Desayi suttavaraṁ dvipadaggo. ^snp5-19-35-4

Rāgañca dosakamabhañjitasantaṁ, ^snp5-19-36-1

Yonicatuggatipañcaviññāṇaṁ; ^snp5-19-36-2

Taṇhāratacchadanatāṇalatāpamokkhaṁ, ^snp5-19-36-3

Desayi suttavaraṁ dvipadaggo. ^snp5-19-36-4

Gambhīraduddasasaṇhanipuṇaṁ, ^snp5-19-37-1

Paṇḍitavedaniyaṁ nipuṇatthaṁ; ^snp5-19-37-2

Lokavicāraṇañāṇapabhaggaṁ, ^snp5-19-37-3

Desayi suttavaraṁ dvipadaggo. ^snp5-19-37-4

Navaṅgakusumamālagīveyyaṁ, ^snp5-19-38-1

Indriyajhānavimokkhavibhattaṁ; ^snp5-19-38-2

Aṭṭhaṅgamaggadharaṁ varayānaṁ, ^snp5-19-38-3

Desayi suttavaraṁ dvipadaggo. ^snp5-19-38-4

Somupamaṁ vimalaṁ parisuddhaṁ, ^snp5-19-39-1

Aṇṇavamūpamaratanasucittaṁ; ^snp5-19-39-2

Pupphasamaṁ ravimūpamatejaṁ, ^snp5-19-39-3

Desayi suttavaraṁ dvipadaggo. ^snp5-19-39-4

Khemasivaṁ sukhasītalasantaṁ, ^snp5-19-40-1

Maccutatāṇaparaṁ paramatthaṁ; ^snp5-19-40-2

Tassa sunibbutadassanahetuṁ, ^snp5-19-40-3

Desayi suttavaraṁ dvipadaggoti. ^snp5-19-40-4

Suttanipātapāḷi samattā. ^snp5-19-40-5
